===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDataFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage.StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage.StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchDataFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "data";
  public static final String DATASETS = "datasets";
  public static final String DATASET_VIEW = "dataset-view";
  public static final String DATASET_LIVE = "dataset-live";
  public static final String S3_BROWSER = "s3-browser";
  public static final String S3_QUERY = "s3-query";
  public static final String STREAMS = "streams";
  public static final String ENTRY_DATASETS = "data.datasets";
  public static final String ENTRY_STREAMS = "data.streams";
  public static final String ENTRY_S3_BROWSER = "data.s3browser";
  public static final String ENTRY_S3_QUERY = "data.s3query";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchDatasetsScreenConfig datasets;
  private final StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig datasetView;
  private final StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig datasetLive;
  private final StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig s3Browser;
  private final StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig s3Query;
  private final StitchStreamsScreenConfig streams;

  private StitchDataFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.datasets = builder.datasetsBuilder.build();
    this.datasetView = builder.datasetViewBuilder.build();
    this.datasetLive = builder.datasetLiveBuilder.build();
    this.s3Browser = builder.s3BrowserBuilder.build();
    this.s3Query = builder.s3QueryBuilder.build();
    this.streams = builder.streamsBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchDatasetsScreenConfig datasets() {
    return datasets;
  }

  public StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig s3Browser() {
    return s3Browser;
  }

  public StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig datasetView() {
    return datasetView;
  }

  public StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig datasetLive() {
    return datasetLive;
  }

  public StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig s3Query() {
    return s3Query;
  }

  public StitchStreamsScreenConfig streams() {
    return streams;
  }

  public Optional<StitchDatasetsScreenConfig> datasetsScreen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return DATASETS.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(datasets) : Optional.empty();
  }

  public Optional<StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return S3_BROWSER.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(s3Browser) : Optional.empty();
  }

  public Optional<StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig> s3QueryScreen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return S3_QUERY.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(s3Query) : Optional.empty();
  }

  public Optional<StitchStreamsScreenConfig> streamsScreen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return STREAMS.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(streams) : Optional.empty();
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    List<StitchMenuEntry> entries = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
    if (datasets.enabled()) {
      entries.add(
          StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_DATASETS)
              .withLabel(datasets.label())
              .withRoutePath(datasets.routePath())
              .withOrder(datasets.order())
              .build());
    }
    if (streams.enabled()) {
      entries.add(
          StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_STREAMS)
              .withLabel(streams.label())
              .withRoutePath(streams.routePath())
              .withOrder(streams.order())
              .build());
    }
    if (s3Browser.enabled()) {
      entries.add(
          StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_S3_BROWSER)
              .withLabel(s3Browser.label())
              .withRoutePath(s3Browser.routePath())
              .withOrder(s3Browser.order())
              .build());
    }
    if (s3Query.enabled()) {
      entries.add(
          StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_S3_QUERY)
              .withLabel(s3Query.label())
              .withRoutePath(s3Query.routePath())
              .withOrder(s3Query.order())
              .build());
    }
    return List.copyOf(entries);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Data";
    private int order = 40;
    private final StitchDatasetsScreenConfig.Builder datasetsBuilder =
        StitchDatasetsScreenConfig.builder(DATASETS);
    private final StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig.Builder datasetViewBuilder =
        StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig.builder(DATASET_VIEW);
    private final StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig.Builder datasetLiveBuilder =
        StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig.builder(DATASET_LIVE);
    private final StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig.Builder s3BrowserBuilder =
        StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig.builder(S3_BROWSER);
    private final StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig.Builder s3QueryBuilder =
        StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig.builder(S3_QUERY);
    private final StitchStreamsScreenConfig.Builder streamsBuilder =
        StitchStreamsScreenConfig.builder(STREAMS);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder datasets(Consumer<StitchDatasetsScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(datasetsBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder datasetView(Consumer<StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(datasetViewBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder datasetLive(Consumer<StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(datasetLiveBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder s3Browser(Consumer<StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(s3BrowserBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder s3Query(Consumer<StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(s3QueryBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder streams(Consumer<StitchStreamsScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(streamsBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDataFeature build() {
      return new StitchDataFeature(this);
    }
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetDetails.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;

public record StitchDatasetDetails(
    String datasetId,
    String group,
    String namespace,
    String name,
    Map<String, String> fields,
    Object sourceObject) {

  public StitchDatasetDetails {
    datasetId = normalize(datasetId);
    group = normalize(group);
    namespace = normalize(namespace);
    name = normalize(name);
    fields = fields == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(fields));
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetLiveProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.Future;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicLong;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightStream;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.FieldVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VectorSchemaRoot;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.DateUnit;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.ArrowType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularStreamOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularStreamSubscription;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.RemoteTabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceInstanceResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.StreamFilterSqlValidator;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableDelta;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConflationMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchSubscriptionScope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchDatasetLiveProvider {
  private static final String SUBSCRIPTION_PREFIX = "stitch-live";
  private static final Set<String> SEQUENCE_COLUMNS =
      Set.of("_seq", "seq", "sequence", "change_seq", "last_seq", "checkpoint_seq");

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchDatasetsProvider datasetsProvider;
  private final String sessionGroup;
  private final String sessionAppName;
  private final String sessionInstance;
  private final String sessionEnv;
  private final String sessionRegion;
  private final String sessionSite;
  private final Path serviceTrustCert;
  private volatile ServiceInstanceResolver dynamicServiceResolver;

  public StitchDatasetLiveProvider(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchDatasetsProvider datasetsProvider) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.datasetsProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(datasetsProvider, "datasetsProvider");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.sessionGroup =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getGroup(), "platform");
    this.sessionAppName =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getAppName(), "stitch");
    this.sessionInstance =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getInstance(), "instance");
    this.sessionEnv = Strings.trimToNull(session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getEnv());
    this.sessionRegion =
        Strings.trimToNull(session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getRegion());
    this.sessionSite = Strings.trimToNull(session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getSite());
    this.serviceTrustCert = session.trustCert();
  }

  public Optional<DatasetLiveContext> loadContext(String datasetResourceId) {
    DatasetId datasetId = parseDatasetId(datasetResourceId);
    if (datasetId == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    StitchDatasetsRow row =
        datasetsProvider.loadRows().stream()
            .filter(value -> value != null && datasetId.toString().equals(value.id()))
            .findFirst()
            .orElse(null);
    if (row == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    DefinitionDataset definition =
        datasetsProvider
            .loadDetails(row.id())
            .map(StitchDatasetDetails::sourceObject)
            .filter(DefinitionDataset.class::isInstance)
            .map(DefinitionDataset.class::cast)
            .orElse(null);
    String accessMode = resolveAccessMode(definition, row.mode());
    return Optional.of(
        new DatasetLiveContext(
            row.id(),
            row.group(),
            row.namespace(),
            row.name(),
            row.datasetType(),
            row.sourceType(),
            row.mode(),
            row.schema(),
            row.sourceHint(),
            primaryKeys(definition),
            accessMode,
            "PUBLIC".equals(accessMode),
            row.liveServiceId(),
            row.liveServiceDisplay(),
            row.liveSupported(),
            row.liveUnavailableReason()));
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaultUpdatePolicy() {
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(StitchRealtimeConflationMode.LATEST_ONLY)
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(200)
        .withMaxBatchSize(16)
        .withMaxQueueSize(512)
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(30_000)
        .build();
  }

  public LiveSubscriptionOptions defaultOptions(DatasetLiveContext context) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    LiveTableMode mode = context.primaryKeys().isEmpty() ? LiveTableMode.HISTORY : LiveTableMode.ACTIVE;
    return new LiveSubscriptionOptions(
        TabularStreamOptions.Start.LATEST, 50, 250, "", mode, 500, context.publicAccess());
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionScope defaultScope(DatasetLiveContext context) {
    return context != null && context.publicAccess()
        ? StitchSubscriptionScope.PUBLIC
        : StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeSource<StitchLiveTableDelta<LiveRow, String>> sourceFor(
      DatasetLiveContext context, LiveSubscriptionOptions options) {
    DatasetLiveContext liveContext = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    LiveSubscriptionOptions liveOptions =
        (options == null ? defaultOptions(liveContext) : options).normalized(liveContext.publicAccess());
    validateContext(liveContext);
    String subject = currentSubject();

    return sink -> {
      Objects.requireNonNull(sink, "listener");
      AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
      AtomicBoolean unsubscribed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
      ExecutorService executor =
          Executors.newSingleThreadExecutor(
              task -> {
                Thread thread =
                    new Thread(
                        task,
                        "stitch-dataset-live-"
                            + liveContext.group()
                            + "-"
                            + liveContext.namespace()
                            + "-"
                            + liveContext.name());
                thread.setDaemon(true);
                return thread;
              });
      sink.onSubscribed();
      sink.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.snapshot(StitchLiveTableDelta.snapshot(List.of())));
      Future<?> future =
          executor.submit(
              () -> {
                try {
                  runStreamLoop(liveContext, liveOptions, subject, sink, closed);
                } catch (Throwable error) {
                  if (!closed.get()) {
                    sink.onError(error, true);
                  }
                } finally {
                  if (unsubscribed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
                    sink.onUnsubscribed();
                  }
                }
              });
      return () -> {
        if (!closed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
          return;
        }
        future.cancel(true);
        executor.shutdownNow();
        if (unsubscribed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
          sink.onUnsubscribed();
        }
      };
    };
  }

  private void validateContext(DatasetLiveContext context) {
    if (!context.liveSupported()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(context.liveUnavailableReason()),
              "Live viewing is not supported for this dataset."));
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(context.liveServiceId()) == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("No live query service is available for this dataset.");
    }
  }

  private void runStreamLoop(
      DatasetLiveContext context,
      LiveSubscriptionOptions options,
      String subject,
      StitchRealtimeSource.Listener<StitchLiveTableDelta<LiveRow, String>> sink,
      AtomicBoolean closed)
      throws Exception {
    DatasetAccumulator accumulator = new DatasetAccumulator(context.primaryKeys(), options.mode(), options.maxRows());
    try (TabularStreamSubscription subscription = openSubscription(context, options, subject)) {
      FlightStream stream = subscription.stream();
      while (!closed.get() && !Thread.currentThread().isInterrupted()) {
        if (!stream.next()) {
          return;
        }
        Batch batch = toBatch(stream.getRoot());
        if (batch.rows().isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<LiveRow, String>> update :
            accumulator.apply(batch.rows(), batch.maxSequence(), batch.observedAt())) {
          sink.onUpdate(update);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private TabularStreamSubscription openSubscription(
      DatasetLiveContext context, LiveSubscriptionOptions options, String subject) {
    DatasetId datasetId = DatasetId.parse(context.datasetId());
    ServiceRef serviceRef = parseServiceRef(context.liveServiceId());
    if ("direct".equals(serviceRef.name())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Live dataset subscription requires a remote query service.");
    }
    TabularStreamOptions streamOptions = toStreamOptions(context, options);
    try (RemoteTabularManager tabular = newRemoteTabularManager(serviceRef)) {
      return runAsSubject(subject, () -> tabular.subscribeDataset(datasetId, streamOptions));
    }
  }

  private static TabularStreamOptions toStreamOptions(
      DatasetLiveContext context, LiveSubscriptionOptions options) {
    return TabularStreamOptions.builder()
        .withStart(options.startMode())
        .withBatchMaxRows(options.batchMaxRows())
        .withFlushMillis(options.flushMillis())
        .withSubscriptionId(SUBSCRIPTION_PREFIX + ":" + context.datasetId())
        .withFilter(StreamFilterSqlValidator.validate(options.filterSql()))
        .withPublic(context.publicAccess())
        .build();
  }

  private static Batch toBatch(VectorSchemaRoot root) {
    if (root == null || root.getRowCount() <= 0) {
      return new Batch(List.of(), null, Instant.now());
    }
    List<String> columns = columnNames(root);
    int sequenceColumn = sequenceIndex(columns);
    List<FieldVector> vectors = root.getFieldVectors();
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>(root.getRowCount());
    Long maxSequence = null;

    for (int rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < root.getRowCount(); rowIndex++) {
      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> row = new LinkedHashMap<>(vectors.size());
      for (int col = 0; col < vectors.size(); col++) {
        FieldVector vector = vectors.get(col);
        Object value = vector.getObject(rowIndex);
        if (col == sequenceColumn) {
          Long sequence = toLong(value);
          if (sequence != null) {
            maxSequence = maxSequence == null ? sequence : Math.max(maxSequence, sequence);
          }
        }
        String column = col < columns.size() ? columns.get(col) : "COL_" + (col + 1);
        row.put(column, convertArrowValue(vector, value));
      }
      rows.add(Map.copyOf(row));
    }
    return new Batch(List.copyOf(rows), maxSequence, Instant.now());
  }

  private static List<String> columnNames(VectorSchemaRoot root) {
    if (root.getSchema() == null || root.getSchema().getFields() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> names = new ArrayList<>(root.getSchema().getFields().size());
    root.getSchema().getFields().forEach(field -> names.add(field.getName()));
    return List.copyOf(names);
  }

  private static int sequenceIndex(List<String> columns) {
    for (int i = 0; i < columns.size(); i++) {
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(columns.get(i));
      if (name != null && SEQUENCE_COLUMNS.contains(name.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        return i;
      }
    }
    return -1;
  }

  private static Object convertArrowValue(FieldVector vector, Object value) {
    if (vector == null || value == null) {
      return value;
    }
    ArrowType type = vector.getField() == null ? null : vector.getField().getType();
    if (type instanceof ArrowType.Date date && value instanceof Number number) {
      if (date.getUnit() == DateUnit.DAY) {
        return LocalDate.ofEpochDay(number.longValue());
      }
      if (date.getUnit() == DateUnit.MILLISECOND) {
        return Instant.ofEpochMilli(number.longValue()).atZone(ZoneOffset.UTC).toLocalDate();
      }
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static Long toLong(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (value instanceof Number number) {
      return number.longValue();
    }
    try {
      return Long.parseLong(String.valueOf(value).trim());
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private ServiceRef parseServiceRef(String serviceResourceId) {
    String resource = Strings.trimToNull(serviceResourceId);
    if (resource == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Live dataset service id is missing.");
    }
    if (!resource.startsWith("service:")) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Live dataset service id must use canonical service:group/name format.");
    }
    String token = resource.substring("service:".length());
    int slash = token.indexOf('/');
    if (slash <= 0 || slash >= token.length() - 1) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Live dataset service id is malformed: " + resource);
    }
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(token.substring(0, slash));
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(token.substring(slash + 1));
    if (group == null || name == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Live dataset service id is malformed: " + resource);
    }
    return new ServiceRef(group, name);
  }

  private RemoteTabularManager newRemoteTabularManager(ServiceRef serviceRef) {
    ServiceRunOptions.Builder runOptions = ServiceRunOptions.builder().withGroup(serviceRef.group());
    if (serviceTrustCert != null) {
      runOptions.withTlsTrustCert(serviceTrustCert).withTlsClientTrustCert(serviceTrustCert);
    }
    DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions =
        DataOptions.ServiceOptions.builder()
            .withEnabled(true)
            .withQueryService(serviceRef.name())
            .withServiceOptions(runOptions.build())
            .build();
    return new RemoteTabularManager(
        session,
        session.internal().discoveryCache(),
        sessionGroup,
        sessionAppName,
        sessionInstance,
        sessionEnv,
        sessionRegion,
        sessionSite,
        serviceOptions,
        session.kerberosPrincipal(),
        session.kerberosKeytab(),
        resolveDynamicServiceResolver());
  }

  private ServiceInstanceResolver resolveDynamicServiceResolver() {
    ServiceInstanceResolver existing = dynamicServiceResolver;
    if (existing != null) {
      return existing;
    }
    synchronized (this) {
      existing = dynamicServiceResolver;
      if (existing != null) {
        return existing;
      }
      ServiceInstanceResolver fromSession = session.serviceInstanceResolverIfInitialized();
      if (fromSession != null) {
        dynamicServiceResolver = fromSession;
        return fromSession;
      }
      if (session.internal().controlPlaneConnection() == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Session control plane is not initialized");
      }
      ServiceInstanceResolver created =
          new ServiceInstanceResolver(session.internal().controlPlaneConnection(), session.statusScheduler());
      dynamicServiceResolver = created;
      return created;
    }
  }

  private String currentSubject() {
    return StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
  }

  private static DatasetId parseDatasetId(String datasetResourceId) {
    try {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(datasetResourceId);
      return normalized == null ? null : DatasetId.parse(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static List<String> primaryKeys(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.binding() == null || definition.binding().duckdb() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> configured = definition.binding().duckdb().primaryKey();
    if (configured == null || configured.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> keys = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String key : configured) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (normalized != null) {
        keys.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    return keys.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(keys);
  }

  private static String resolveAccessMode(DefinitionDataset definition, String mode) {
    if (!"DUCKDB_ACTIVE".equals(Strings.trimToEmpty(mode))) {
      return "PRIVATE";
    }
    DefinitionDataset required = Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(required.effectiveAccessMode(), "definition.effectiveAccessMode");
  }

  private static <T> T runAsSubject(String subject, java.util.function.Supplier<T> callback) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.runAsSubject(subject, callback);
  }

  private record Batch(List<Map<String, Object>> rows, Long maxSequence, Instant observedAt) {}

  private record ServiceRef(String group, String name) {}

  private static final class DatasetAccumulator {
    private final List<String> primaryKeys;
    private final boolean activeMode;
    private final int maxRows;
    private final LinkedHashMap<String, LiveRow> activeRows = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    private final ArrayDeque<LiveRow> historyRows = new ArrayDeque<>();
    private final AtomicLong historyId = new AtomicLong(0L);

    private DatasetAccumulator(List<String> primaryKeys, LiveTableMode mode, int maxRows) {
      this.primaryKeys = primaryKeys == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(primaryKeys);
      this.activeMode = mode == LiveTableMode.ACTIVE && !this.primaryKeys.isEmpty();
      this.maxRows = Math.max(50, maxRows);
    }

    private List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<LiveRow, String>>> apply(
        List<Map<String, Object>> rows, Long maxSequence, Instant observedAt) {
      if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<LiveRow> upserts = new ArrayList<>(rows.size());
      List<String> removals = new ArrayList<>();
      Map<String, List<String>> changedCells = new LinkedHashMap<>();

      for (Map<String, Object> values : rows) {
        String rowId = activeMode ? primaryKeyRowId(values) : "row-" + historyId.incrementAndGet();
        LiveRow row = new LiveRow(rowId, values, maxSequence, observedAt);
        upserts.add(row);
        changedCells.put(rowId, List.copyOf(values.keySet()));
        if (activeMode) {
          activeRows.put(rowId, row);
        } else {
          historyRows.addFirst(row);
        }
      }

      if (activeMode) {
        while (activeRows.size() > maxRows) {
          String oldest = activeRows.keySet().iterator().next();
          activeRows.remove(oldest);
          removals.add(oldest);
        }
      } else {
        while (historyRows.size() > maxRows) {
          removals.add(historyRows.removeLast().rowId());
        }
      }
      return toUpdates(upserts, removals, changedCells);
    }

    private List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<LiveRow, String>>> toUpdates(
        List<LiveRow> upserts, List<String> removals, Map<String, List<String>> changedCells) {
      List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<LiveRow, String>>> updates = new ArrayList<>(2);
      if (!upserts.isEmpty()) {
        updates.add(
            StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(
                new StitchLiveTableDelta<>(
                    StitchLiveTableDelta.Type.UPSERT, upserts, List.of(), changedCells)));
      }
      if (!removals.isEmpty()) {
        updates.add(StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(StitchLiveTableDelta.remove(removals)));
      }
      return updates;
    }

    private String primaryKeyRowId(Map<String, Object> values) {
      StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
      for (int i = 0; i < primaryKeys.size(); i++) {
        if (i > 0) {
          builder.append('\u001f');
        }
        builder.append(String.valueOf(values.get(primaryKeys.get(i))));
      }
      String rowId = Strings.trimToNull(builder.toString());
      return rowId == null ? "pk-" + historyId.incrementAndGet() : rowId;
    }
  }

  public record DatasetLiveContext(
      String datasetId,
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String name,
      String datasetType,
      String sourceType,
      String mode,
      String schema,
      String sourceHint,
      List<String> primaryKeys,
      String accessMode,
      boolean publicAccess,
      String liveServiceId,
      String liveServiceDisplay,
      boolean liveSupported,
      String liveUnavailableReason) {
    public DatasetLiveContext {
      primaryKeys = primaryKeys == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(primaryKeys);
    }
  }

  public enum LiveTableMode {
    ACTIVE,
    HISTORY
  }

  public record LiveSubscriptionOptions(
      TabularStreamOptions.Start startMode,
      int batchMaxRows,
      int flushMillis,
      String filterSql,
      LiveTableMode mode,
      int maxRows,
      boolean publicAccess) {
    public LiveSubscriptionOptions {
      startMode = startMode == null ? TabularStreamOptions.Start.LATEST : startMode;
      batchMaxRows = Math.max(1, batchMaxRows <= 0 ? 50 : batchMaxRows);
      flushMillis = Math.max(1, flushMillis <= 0 ? 250 : flushMillis);
      filterSql = Strings.trimToEmpty(filterSql);
      mode = mode == null ? LiveTableMode.ACTIVE : mode;
      maxRows = Math.max(50, maxRows <= 0 ? 500 : maxRows);
    }

    public LiveSubscriptionOptions normalized(boolean effectivePublicAccess) {
      return new LiveSubscriptionOptions(
          startMode, batchMaxRows, flushMillis, filterSql, mode, maxRows, effectivePublicAccess);
    }
  }

  public record LiveRow(String rowId, Map<String, Object> values, Long sequence, Instant observedAt) {
    public LiveRow {
      rowId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rowId), "row");
      values = values == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(values);
      observedAt = observedAt == null ? Instant.now() : observedAt;
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.DetachEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularStreamOptions;

import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConflationMode;

import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

@Route(value = StitchDatasetLiveScreen.ROUTE_PATH, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchDatasetLiveScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  public static final String ROUTE_PATH = "data/datasets/live";
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_DATASET_ID = "datasetId";

  private static final List<Integer> BATCH_ROWS = List.of(10, 25, 50, 100, 256);
  private static final List<Integer> FLUSH_MS = List.of(50, 100, 250, 500);
  private static final List<Integer> MAX_ROWS = List.of(200, 500, 1000, 2000);
  private static final List<Integer> DISPATCH_MS = List.of(50, 100, 200, 500);
  private static final List<Integer> FLASH_SECONDS = List.of(1, 2, 5, 10);

  private final StitchDatasetLiveProvider provider;
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry;

  private final StitchSection contextSection = new StitchSection("Dataset Context");
  private final StitchSection controlsSection = new StitchSection("Live Controls");
  private final FormLayout contextForm = new FormLayout();
  private final FormLayout controlsForm = new FormLayout();
  private final Span changeSummary = new Span("Changed rows: 0 | changed cells: 0");
  private final StitchLiveTableShell<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow, String> liveTable =
      new StitchLiveTableShell<>();

  private final Select<TabularStreamOptions.Start> startMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Start Mode",
          "Live stream start mode",
          TabularStreamOptions.Start.values(),
          TabularStreamOptions.Start::name);
  private final Select<Integer> batchMaxRows =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Batch Rows", "Live stream batch row count", BATCH_ROWS, String::valueOf);
  private final Select<Integer> flushMillis =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Flush ms", "Live stream flush interval milliseconds", FLUSH_MS, String::valueOf);
  private final TextField filterSql = textField("Filter SQL", "Live stream SQL filter");
  private final Select<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveTableMode> tableMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Table Mode",
          "Live table mode",
          StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveTableMode.values(),
          StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveTableMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> maxRows =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select("Max Rows", "Maximum live rows", MAX_ROWS, String::valueOf);
  private final Select<StitchRealtimeConflationMode> conflationMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Conflation",
          "Realtime conflation mode",
          StitchRealtimeConflationMode.values(),
          StitchRealtimeConflationMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> dispatchIntervalMs =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Dispatch ms",
          "Realtime dispatch interval milliseconds",
          DISPATCH_MS,
          String::valueOf);
  private final Select<StitchLiveTableHighlightMode> highlightMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Highlight",
          "Live table highlight mode",
          StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.values(),
          StitchLiveTableHighlightMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> flashWindowSeconds =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Flash Seconds",
          "Temporary highlight duration seconds",
          FLASH_SECONDS,
          String::valueOf);
  private final Button applyControls =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("APPLY", "Apply live control changes");

  private StitchDatasetLiveProvider.DatasetLiveContext context;
  private List<String> configuredColumns = List.of();
  private StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<
          StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow, String>>
      controller;
  private AutoCloseable controllerBinding = () -> {};
  private AutoCloseable registryBinding = () -> {};

  public StitchDatasetLiveScreen(
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchDatasetLiveProvider provider,
      StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), provider, realtimeRegistry);
  }

  protected StitchDatasetLiveScreen(
      StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig config,
      StitchDatasetLiveProvider provider,
      StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(config.pageSubtitle(), ""));
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.realtimeRegistry = Objects.requireNonNull(realtimeRegistry, "realtimeRegistry");
    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    configureContextSection();
    configureControlsSection();
    configureLiveTable();
    configurePageActions();

    addToBody(contextSection, controlsSection, liveTable);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, liveTable);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String datasetId = StitchStreamViewSupport.queryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_DATASET_ID);
    if (datasetId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Dataset Not Selected",
          "Open this screen from Data -> Datasets using the Live action.");
      return;
    }
    loadDataset(datasetId, false);
  }

  @Override
  protected void onDetach(DetachEvent detachEvent) {
    closeController();
    super.onDetach(detachEvent);
  }

  private void configureContextSection() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureContextForm(contextForm);
    contextSection.addToBody(contextForm);
  }

  private void configureControlsSection() {
    filterSql.setWidthFull();
    filterSql.setPlaceholder("e.g. symbol = 'AAPL'");

    highlightMode.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          liveTable.setHighlightMode(event.getValue());
          liveTable.clearHighlights();
          liveTable.refreshGrid();
          updateChangeSummary();
        });
    flashWindowSeconds.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          Integer seconds = event.getValue();
          if (seconds != null) {
            liveTable.setFlashWindow(Duration.ofSeconds(seconds));
          }
        });

    applyControls.addClickListener(event -> applyControlChanges());
    controlsForm.setWidthFull();
    controlsForm.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("40em", 2),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("70em", 4));
    controlsForm.add(
        startMode,
        batchMaxRows,
        flushMillis,
        filterSql,
        tableMode,
        maxRows,
        conflationMode,
        dispatchIntervalMs,
        highlightMode,
        flashWindowSeconds);
    controlsSection.addToBody(controlsForm, new HorizontalLayout(applyControls), changeSummary);
  }

  private void configureLiveTable() {
    liveTable.withRowIdResolver(StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow::rowId);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureLiveTableShell(
        liveTable,
        "No live rows",
        "Start the subscription to receive updates.",
        "Live dataset grid",
        true,
        true,
        () -> {
          liveTable.clearHighlights();
          liveTable.refreshGrid();
          updateChangeSummary();
        });
    configureGridColumns(List.of());
  }

  private void configurePageActions() {
    Button refresh =
        StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("REFRESH", "Refresh live dataset screen");
    refresh.addClickListener(event -> loadDataset(datasetId(), false));
    addPageAction(refresh);
  }

  private void loadDataset(String requestedDatasetId, boolean autoStart) {
    String datasetId = Strings.trimToNull(requestedDatasetId);
    if (datasetId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Dataset Not Selected",
          "Open this screen from Data -> Datasets using the Live action.");
      return;
    }
    StitchDatasetLiveProvider.DatasetLiveContext loaded =
        provider.loadContext(datasetId).orElse(null);
    if (loaded == null) {
      applyEmptyState("Dataset Not Found", "The requested dataset could not be resolved.");
      return;
    }
    context = loaded;
    syncControlDefaults();
    updateContextForm();
    if (!loaded.liveSupported()) {
      applyEmptyState("Live Not Available", loaded.liveUnavailableReason());
      return;
    }
    bindController(autoStart);
  }

  private void applyControlChanges() {
    boolean wasActive = controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state());
    bindController(wasActive);
  }

  private void bindController(boolean autoStart) {
    if (context == null || !context.liveSupported()) {
      return;
    }
    closeController();
    liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
    configureGridColumns(List.of());
    try {
      controller =
          new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
              provider.sourceFor(context, optionsFromControls()),
              policyFromControls(),
              provider.defaultScope(context),
              getUI().orElse(null));
      controllerBinding = liveTable.bindController(controller, this::onLiveUpdates);
      registryBinding =
          realtimeRegistry.register(
              "Data Datasets Live",
              context.group() + " / " + context.namespace() + " / " + context.name(),
              controller,
              getUI().orElse(null));
      liveTable.statusBar().setMessage("");
      if (autoStart) {
        controller.start();
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Live Setup Failed",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Live dataset setup failed."));
    }
  }

  private void closeController() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(registryBinding);
    registryBinding = () -> {};
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(controllerBinding);
    controllerBinding = () -> {};
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.close();
      controller = null;
    }
  }

  private void onLiveUpdates(
      List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow, String>>>
          updates) {
    List<String> columns = collectColumns(configuredColumns, updates);
    if (!Objects.equals(columns, configuredColumns)) {
      configureGridColumns(columns);
    }
    liveTable.pruneTransientHighlights();
    liveTable.refreshGrid();
    updateChangeSummary();
  }

  private void configureGridColumns(List<String> columns) {
    configuredColumns = columns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(columns);
    Grid<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow> grid = liveTable.resultsView().grid();
    grid.removeAllColumns();

    grid.addColumn(row -> row != null && liveTable.changeTracker().isRowChanged(row.rowId()) ? "*" : "")
        .setHeader("Changed")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(false);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null ? "-" : Strings.firstNonBlank(row.rowId(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Row Id")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null || row.sequence() == null ? "-" : String.valueOf(row.sequence()))
        .setHeader("Seq")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null || row.observedAt() == null ? "-" : row.observedAt().toString())
        .setHeader("Observed")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);

    for (String column : configuredColumns) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      grid.addColumn(row -> formattedCell(row, key))
          .setHeader(key)
          .setAutoWidth(true)
          .setSortable(false)
          .setResizable(true);
    }
  }

  private String formattedCell(StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow row, String key) {
    if (row == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return StitchStreamViewSupport.trackedCellValue(liveTable, row.rowId(), key, row.values().get(key));
  }

  private void updateContextForm() {
    if (context == null) {
      StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, Map.of());
      return;
    }
    Map<String, String> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("Group", context.group());
    fields.put("Namespace", context.namespace());
    fields.put("Name", context.name());
    fields.put("Type", context.datasetType());
    fields.put("Source", context.sourceType());
    fields.put("Mode", context.mode());
    fields.put("Schema", context.schema());
    fields.put("Live Service", context.liveServiceDisplay());
    fields.put("Access", context.accessMode());
    fields.put(
        "Primary Keys",
        context.primaryKeys().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(", ", context.primaryKeys()));
    fields.put("Source Hint", context.sourceHint());
    StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, fields);
    setPageSubtitle(
        context.group()
            + "/"
            + context.namespace()
            + "/"
            + context.name()
            + " - Realtime dataset viewing");
  }

  private void applyEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    closeController();
    liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
    configureGridColumns(List.of());
    liveTable.clearHighlights();
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmptyState(title, Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    liveTable.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
    liveTable.statusBar().setMessage(Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    updateChangeSummary();
  }

  private StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveSubscriptionOptions optionsFromControls() {
    return new StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveSubscriptionOptions(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(startMode.getValue(), TabularStreamOptions.Start.LATEST),
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(batchMaxRows.getValue(), 50),
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(flushMillis.getValue(), 250),
        Strings.trimToEmpty(filterSql.getValue()),
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
            tableMode.getValue(), StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveTableMode.ACTIVE),
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxRows.getValue(), 500),
        context != null && context.publicAccess());
  }

  private StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyFromControls() {
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaults = provider.defaultUpdatePolicy();
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(conflationMode.getValue(), defaults.conflationMode()))
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                dispatchIntervalMs.getValue(), defaults.dispatchIntervalMillis()))
        .withMaxBatchSize(defaults.maxBatchSize())
        .withMaxQueueSize(defaults.maxQueueSize())
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(defaults.staleTimeoutMillis())
        .build();
  }

  private void syncControlDefaults() {
    if (context == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveSubscriptionOptions defaults = provider.defaultOptions(context);
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyDefaults = provider.defaultUpdatePolicy();
    startMode.setValue(defaults.startMode());
    batchMaxRows.setValue(defaults.batchMaxRows());
    flushMillis.setValue(defaults.flushMillis());
    filterSql.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(defaults.filterSql()));
    tableMode.setValue(defaults.mode());
    maxRows.setValue(defaults.maxRows());
    conflationMode.setValue(policyDefaults.conflationMode());
    dispatchIntervalMs.setValue(policyDefaults.dispatchIntervalMillis());
    highlightMode.setValue(StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT);
    flashWindowSeconds.setValue(2);
  }

  private void updateChangeSummary() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.updateChangeSummary(changeSummary, liveTable);
    int changedRows = liveTable.changedRowsCount();
    int changedCells = liveTable.changedCellsCount();
    liveTable.controls().clearEnabled(changedRows > 0 || changedCells > 0);
  }

  private String datasetId() {
    return context == null ? null : context.datasetId();
  }

  private static List<String> collectColumns(
      List<String> current,
      List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow, String>>>
          updates) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> columns = new LinkedHashSet<>(current == null ? List.of() : current);
    if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
      return List.copyOf(columns);
    }
    for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow, String>> update :
        updates) {
      if (update == null || update.payload() == null || update.payload().rows() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (StitchDatasetLiveProvider.LiveRow row : update.payload().rows()) {
        if (row != null && row.values() != null) {
          columns.addAll(row.values().keySet());
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(columns);
  }

  private static StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::datasetLive)
        .filter(StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private static TextField textField(String label, String ariaLabel) {
    TextField field = new TextField(label);
    field.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    return field;
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

public final class StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.routePath = "data/datasets/live";
      this.pageTitle = "Data - Dataset Live";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Realtime dataset viewing for supported live datasets.";
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchDatasetLiveScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetProviderSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data.DataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchDatasetProviderSupport {
  private StitchDatasetProviderSupport() {}

  public static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  public static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return "";
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      String normalized = normalize(value);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        return normalized;
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  public static String truncate(String value, int maxLength) {
    String normalized = normalize(value);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    if (normalized.length() <= Math.max(1, maxLength)) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, Math.max(1, maxLength) - 3) + "...";
  }

  public static String joinParts(List<String> parts) {
    if (parts == null || parts.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>(parts.size());
    for (String part : parts) {
      String value = normalize(part);
      if (!value.isBlank() && !value.endsWith("=")) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(" | ", normalized);
  }

  public static boolean isDirectServiceId(String serviceId, String directId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(serviceId);
    return normalized != null && Strings.firstNonBlank(directId, "").equals(normalized);
  }

  public static boolean isServiceStateAvailable(String state) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(state);
    return normalized != null && ("ONLINE".equals(normalized) || "STALE".equals(normalized));
  }

  public static String serviceKey(String group, String name) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedName == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalizedGroup + "/" + normalizedName;
  }

  public static String datasetKey(String namespace, String name) {
    String normalizedNamespace = Strings.trimToNull(namespace);
    String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    if (normalizedNamespace == null || normalizedName == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalizedNamespace + "/" + normalizedName;
  }

  public static String groupedDatasetKey(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String key = datasetKey(namespace, name);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || key == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalizedGroup + "/" + key;
  }

  public static boolean isS3Uri(String uri) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(uri);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String lower = normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.startsWith("s3://") || lower.startsWith("s3a://") || lower.startsWith("s3n://");
  }

  public static <T> T runAsSubject(String subject, Supplier<T> callback) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(callback, "callback");
    String normalizedSubject = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    if (normalizedSubject == null) {
      return callback.get();
    }
    UserPrincipal previous = UserContext.get().orElse(null);
    UserContext.set(new UserPrincipal(normalizedSubject, Map.of()));
    try {
      return callback.get();
    } finally {
      if (previous == null) {
        UserContext.clear();
      } else {
        UserContext.set(previous);
      }
    }
  }

  public static String datasetId(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    return DataEntitlements.canonicalDatasetResourceId(group, namespace, name);
  }

  public static long recencyEpoch(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    long updated = parseEpoch(envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    if (updated > Long.MIN_VALUE) {
      return updated;
    }
    return parseEpoch(envelope.createdTimeUtc());
  }

  public static long parseEpoch(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized).toEpochMilli();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
  }

  public static String indexKey(String value) {
    return normalize(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}
