package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport;

public class StitchDatasetsDetailsDialog extends StitchDialog {
  public StitchDatasetsDetailsDialog(StitchDatasetDetails details) {
    super("Dataset Details");
    Objects.requireNonNull(details, "details");

    String target = StitchDetailsDialogSupport.joinPath(details.group(), details.namespace(), details.name());
    setDialogTitle("Dataset Details - " + target);

    Map<String, String> labels = labels();
    Map<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(details.fields());

    addToBody(StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(orderedKeys(values), values, labels));
    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> details.sourceObject() == null ? details : details.sourceObject());
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> labels() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> labels = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    labels.put("enabled", "Enabled");
    labels.put("group", "Group");
    labels.put("namespace", "Namespace");
    labels.put("name", "Name");
    labels.put("datasetId", "Dataset Id");
    labels.put("type", "Type");
    labels.put("sourceType", "Source Type");
    labels.put("mode", "Mode");
    labels.put("accessMode", "Access Mode");
    labels.put("schema", "Schema");
    labels.put("sourceHint", "Source Hint");
    labels.put("binding", "Binding");
    labels.put("primaryKeys", "Primary Keys");
    labels.put("updatedUtc", "Updated (UTC)");
    labels.put("createdUtc", "Created (UTC)");
    labels.put("description", "Description");
    labels.put("dependencies", "Dependencies");
    return Map.copyOf(labels);
  }

  private static List<String> orderedKeys(Map<String, String> values) {
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.orderedKeys(
        null,
        List.of(
            "enabled",
            "group",
            "namespace",
            "name",
            "datasetId",
            "type",
            "sourceType",
            "mode",
            "accessMode",
            "schema",
            "sourceHint",
            "binding",
            "primaryKeys",
            "updatedUtc",
            "createdUtc",
            "description",
            "dependencies"),
        values);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.access.AccessManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularTableMetadata;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.RemoteTabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceInstanceResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchDatasetsProvider {
  private static final int QUERY_PREVIEW_MAX = 140;
  private static final String DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID = "direct";
  private static final String DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_DISPLAY = "DIRECT";

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final AccessManager accessManager;
  private final String sessionGroup;
  private final String sessionAppName;
  private final String sessionInstance;
  private final String sessionEnv;
  private final String sessionRegion;
  private final String sessionSite;
  private final Path serviceTrustCert;
  private volatile ServiceInstanceResolver dynamicServiceResolver;

  public StitchDatasetsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.accessManager = this.session.access();
    this.sessionGroup =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getGroup(),
            "platform");
    this.sessionAppName =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getAppName(),
            "stitch");
    this.sessionInstance =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getInstance(),
            "instance");
    this.sessionEnv =
        Strings.trimToNull(this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getEnv());
    this.sessionRegion =
        Strings.trimToNull(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getRegion());
    this.sessionSite =
        Strings.trimToNull(this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getSite());
    this.serviceTrustCert = this.session.trustCert();
  }

  public List<StitchDatasetsRow> loadRows() {
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = discoveryCache();
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Map<String, DatasetRef> indexed = indexDatasets(discoveryCache);
    if (indexed.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, String> schemaHintsByDataset = indexSchemaHints(discoveryCache);
    String subject = currentSubject();

    List<StitchDatasetsRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(indexed.size());
    for (DatasetRef ref : indexed.values()) {
      rows.add(toRow(ref, schemaHintsByDataset, subject));
    }
    rows.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(StitchDatasetsRow::group, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchDatasetsRow::namespace, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchDatasetsRow::name, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  public Optional<StitchDatasetDetails> loadDetails(String datasetId) {
    String normalizedId = normalize(datasetId);
    if (normalizedId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = discoveryCache();
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }

    Map<String, DatasetRef> indexed = indexDatasets(discoveryCache);
    DatasetRef ref = indexed.get(StitchDatasetProviderSupport.indexKey(normalizedId));
    if (ref == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    Map<String, String> schemaHintsByDataset = indexSchemaHints(discoveryCache);
    return Optional.of(toDetails(ref, schemaHintsByDataset));
  }

  private StitchDatasetsRow toRow(
      DatasetRef ref,
      Map<String, String> schemaHintsByDataset,
      String subject) {
    DefinitionDataset definition = ref.definition();
    ViewSupport viewSupport = resolveViewSupport(ref.datasetId(), definition, subject);
    LiveSupport liveSupport = resolveLiveSupport(ref.datasetId(), definition, subject);
    return new StitchDatasetsRow(
        ref.datasetId(),
        isEnabled(definition),
        ref.group(),
        ref.namespace(),
        ref.name(),
        datasetType(definition),
        sourceType(definition),
        datasetMode(definition),
        schemaHint(ref, schemaHintsByDataset),
        sourceHint(definition),
        viewSupport.supported(),
        viewSupport.reason(),
        viewSupport.queryServiceId(),
        viewSupport.queryServiceDisplay(),
        liveSupport.supported(),
        liveSupport.reason(),
        liveSupport.serviceId(),
        liveSupport.serviceDisplay());
  }

  private StitchDatasetDetails toDetails(DatasetRef ref, Map<String, String> schemaHintsByDataset) {
    DefinitionDataset definition = ref.definition();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("enabled", isEnabled(definition) ? "ENABLED" : "DISABLED");
    fields.put("group", ref.group());
    fields.put("namespace", ref.namespace());
    fields.put("name", ref.name());
    fields.put("datasetId", ref.datasetId());
    fields.put("type", datasetType(definition));
    fields.put("sourceType", sourceType(definition));
    fields.put("mode", datasetMode(definition));
    fields.put("accessMode", accessMode(definition));
    fields.put("schema", schemaHint(ref, schemaHintsByDataset));
    fields.put("sourceHint", sourceHint(definition));
    fields.put("binding", bindingDetails(definition));
    fields.put("primaryKeys", primaryKeys(definition));
    fields.put("updatedUtc", normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc()));
    fields.put("createdUtc", normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.createdTimeUtc()));

    String description = semanticDescription(definition);
    if (!description.isBlank()) {
      fields.put("description", description);
    }
    String dependencies = viewDependencies(definition);
    if (!dependencies.isBlank()) {
      fields.put("dependencies", dependencies);
    }

    return new StitchDatasetDetails(
        ref.datasetId(),
        ref.group(),
        ref.namespace(),
        ref.name(),
        fields,
        definition);
  }

  private Map<String, DatasetRef> indexDatasets(DiscoveryCache discoveryCache) {
    Map<String, DatasetRef> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<Definition> definitions = discoveryCache.allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    for (Definition definition : definitions) {
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionDataset dataset)) {
        continue;
      }
      DatasetRef parsed = toDatasetRef(dataset);
      String key = StitchDatasetProviderSupport.indexKey(parsed.datasetId());
      DatasetRef current = indexed.get(key);
      if (current == null || parsed.recencyEpochMs() > current.recencyEpochMs()) {
        indexed.put(key, parsed);
      }
    }
    return indexed.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(indexed);
  }

  private static DatasetRef toDatasetRef(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    String group = requireDefinitionValue(envelope.group(), "dataset.envelope.group");
    String namespace = requireDefinitionValue(definition.namespace(), "dataset.namespace");
    String envelopeName = requireDefinitionValue(envelope.name(), "dataset.envelope.name");
    String datasetName = envelopeName;
    int slash = envelopeName.indexOf('/');
    if (slash <= 0 || slash >= envelopeName.length() - 1) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dataset.envelope.name must be namespace/name: " + envelopeName);
    }
    String namespaceFromEnvelope = requireDefinitionValue(
        envelopeName.substring(0, slash), "dataset.envelope.name.namespace");
    if (!namespace.equals(namespaceFromEnvelope)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dataset.namespace must match envelope namespace: " + namespace + " vs " + namespaceFromEnvelope);
    }
    datasetName = requireDefinitionValue(
        envelopeName.substring(slash + 1), "dataset.envelope.name.dataset");
    String datasetId = StitchDatasetProviderSupport.datasetId(group, namespace, datasetName);
    long recency = StitchDatasetProviderSupport.recencyEpoch(envelope);
    return new DatasetRef(datasetId, group, namespace, datasetName, definition, recency);
  }

  private static String datasetType(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    return Objects.requireNonNull(definition.type(), "dataset.type").name();
  }

  private static String sourceType(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    if (definition.view() != null) {
      return "VIEW";
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    if (binding == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dataset.binding is required when dataset.view is absent");
    }
    if (binding.duckdb() != null) {
      return "DUCKDB";
    }
    if (binding.parquet() != null) {
      return "PARQUET";
    }
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      return "ODBC";
    }
    if (binding.external() != null) {
      return "EXTERNAL";
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("dataset.binding type is not supported");
  }

  private static String datasetMode(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (definition.view() != null && definition.view().target() != null) {
      String targetType = normalize(definition.view().target().targetType());
      if (!targetType.isBlank()) {
        return targetType;
      }
    }
    if (definition.binding() != null && definition.binding().duckdb() != null) {
      String duckdbTargetType = normalize(definition.binding().duckdb().targetType());
      if (!duckdbTargetType.isBlank()) {
        return duckdbTargetType;
      }
    }
    return accessMode(definition);
  }

  private static boolean supportsDirectQuery(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.binding() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (definition.binding().odbc() != null) {
      return true;
    }
    if (definition.binding().parquet() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    DefinitionDataset.ParquetBinding parquet = definition.binding().parquet();
    String uri = Strings.trimToNull(parquet.uri());
    if (isS3Uri(uri)) {
      return true;
    }
    String connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(parquet.connectionName());
    return connectionName != null;
  }

  private ViewSupport resolveViewSupport(
      String datasetId,
      DefinitionDataset definition,
      String subject) {
    String mode = datasetMode(definition);
    if ("DUCKDB_ACTIVE".equals(mode)) {
      return new ViewSupport(
          false,
          "Live dataset mode is not supported in this phase. Non-live table viewing only.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    if (!accessManager.canQueryDataset(subject, datasetId)) {
      return new ViewSupport(
          false,
          "This dataset is not queryable in standard non-live mode for the current subject.",
          null,
          null);
    }

    AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute route =
        resolveRouteForDataset(datasetId, definition, subject);
    if (route == null) {
      if (supportsDirectQuery(definition)) {
        return new ViewSupport(true, "", DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID, DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_DISPLAY);
      }
      return new ViewSupport(
          false,
          "No online query service is mapped for this dataset.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    return new ViewSupport(
        true,
        "",
        normalize(route.serviceId()),
        normalize(route.serviceDisplay()));
  }

  private LiveSupport resolveLiveSupport(
      String datasetId,
      DefinitionDataset definition,
      String subject) {
    String mode = datasetMode(definition);
    if (!"DUCKDB_ACTIVE".equals(mode)) {
      return new LiveSupport(
          false,
          "Live viewing is supported only for DUCKDB_ACTIVE datasets in this phase.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    if (!accessManager.canQueryDataset(subject, datasetId)) {
      return new LiveSupport(
          false,
          "This dataset is not queryable in live mode for the current subject.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute route =
        resolveRouteForDataset(datasetId, definition, subject);
    if (route == null) {
      return new LiveSupport(
          false,
          "No online query service is mapped for live dataset streaming.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    if (isDirectServiceId(route.serviceId())) {
      return new LiveSupport(
          false,
          "Direct query bindings do not support live subscriptions.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    if (!supportsLiveServiceType(route.serviceType())) {
      return new LiveSupport(
          false,
          "The mapped query service does not support dataset live subscriptions.",
          null,
          null);
    }
    return new LiveSupport(
        true,
        "",
        normalize(route.serviceId()),
        normalize(route.serviceDisplay()));
  }

  private static String accessMode(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalize(definition.effectiveAccessMode());
  }

  private static String sourceHint(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (definition.view() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      if (definition.view().target() != null) {
        parts.add("target=" + firstNonBlank(definition.view().target().duckdbTableName(), definition.view().target().parquetPath()));
      }
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(definition.view().querySql())) {
        parts.add("query=" + truncate(definition.view().querySql(), QUERY_PREVIEW_MAX));
      }
      return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
    }

    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    if (binding == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (binding.duckdb() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(binding.duckdb().relationName(), binding.duckdb().databasePath(), binding.duckdb().parquetHistoryPath());
    }
    if (binding.parquet() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(binding.parquet().uri(), binding.parquet().connectionName(), binding.parquet().glob());
    }
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(binding.odbc().tableName(), binding.odbc().querySql(), binding.odbc().connectionName());
    }
    if (binding.external() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(binding.external().reference(), binding.external().externalType());
    }
    return "";
  }

  private static String schemaHint(DatasetRef ref, Map<String, String> schemaHintsByDataset) {
    if (ref == null || ref.definition() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String fromView =
        normalize(ref.definition().view() == null ? null : ref.definition().view().schemaName());
    if (!fromView.isBlank()) {
      return fromView;
    }
    if (schemaHintsByDataset == null || schemaHintsByDataset.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalize(schemaHintsByDataset.get(StitchDatasetProviderSupport.indexKey(ref.datasetId())));
  }

  private static String bindingDetails(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (definition.view() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      if (definition.view().target() != null) {
        parts.add("targetType=" + normalize(definition.view().target().targetType()));
        parts.add("targetTable=" + normalize(definition.view().target().duckdbTableName()));
        parts.add("targetPath=" + normalize(definition.view().target().parquetPath()));
      }
      parts.add("querySql=" + truncate(definition.view().querySql(), QUERY_PREVIEW_MAX));
      return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    if (binding == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (binding.duckdb() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      parts.add("relation=" + normalize(binding.duckdb().relationName()));
      parts.add("targetType=" + normalize(binding.duckdb().targetType()));
      parts.add("memory=" + String.valueOf(Boolean.TRUE.equals(binding.duckdb().memory())));
      parts.add("databasePath=" + normalize(binding.duckdb().databasePath()));
      return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
    }
    if (binding.parquet() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      parts.add("uri=" + normalize(binding.parquet().uri()));
      parts.add("glob=" + normalize(binding.parquet().glob()));
      parts.add("connection=" + normalize(binding.parquet().connectionName()));
      return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
    }
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      parts.add("connection=" + normalize(binding.odbc().connectionName()));
      parts.add(
          "databaseType="
              + normalize(
                  binding.odbc().databaseType() == null ? null : binding.odbc().databaseType().name()));
      parts.add("schema=" + normalize(binding.odbc().schemaName()));
      parts.add("table=" + normalize(binding.odbc().tableName()));
      parts.add("querySql=" + truncate(binding.odbc().querySql(), QUERY_PREVIEW_MAX));
      return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
    }
    if (binding.external() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      parts.add("externalType=" + normalize(binding.external().externalType()));
      parts.add("reference=" + normalize(binding.external().reference()));
      return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
    }
    return "";
  }

  private static String primaryKeys(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.binding() == null || definition.binding().duckdb() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> configured = definition.binding().duckdb().primaryKey();
    if (configured == null || configured.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>(configured.size());
    for (String key : configured) {
      String value = normalize(key);
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(", ", normalized);
  }

  private static String semanticDescription(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.semantic() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String description = normalize(definition.semantic().description());
    if (description.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("TODO:")) {
      return "";
    }
    return description;
  }

  private static String viewDependencies(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.view() == null || definition.view().dependencies() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> dependencies = definition.view().dependencies();
    if (dependencies.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String dependency : dependencies) {
      String value = normalize(dependency);
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(", ", normalized);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> indexSchemaHints(DiscoveryCache discoveryCache) {
    List<Definition> definitions = discoveryCache.allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, String> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Definition definition : definitions) {
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionIngest ingest)) {
        continue;
      }
      String datasetId = normalize(ingest.datasetId());
      String schema = normalize(ingest.outputSchemaId());
      if (datasetId.isBlank() || schema.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      indexed.putIfAbsent(StitchDatasetProviderSupport.indexKey(datasetId), schema);
    }
    return indexed.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(indexed);
  }

  private static boolean isEnabled(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return !Boolean.FALSE.equals(definition.envelope().enabled());
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    return session.internal().discoveryCache();
  }

  private String currentSubject() {
    return StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
  }

  private static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.firstNonBlank(values);
  }

  private static String truncate(String value, int maxLength) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.truncate(value, maxLength);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.normalize(value);
  }

  private AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute resolveRouteForDataset(
      String datasetId, DefinitionDataset definition, String subject) {
    AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute route =
        accessManager.datasetQueryRoute(subject, datasetId).orElse(null);
    if (route != null && isDirectServiceId(route.serviceId()) && !supportsDirectQuery(definition)) {
      route = null;
    }
    if (route != null && route.online()) {
      return route;
    }
    return null;
  }

  private Map<String, DatasetServiceSelection> resolveDatasetServiceSelections(
      Iterable<DatasetRef> datasets) {
    if (datasets == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    List<DatasetRef> refs = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DatasetRef ref : datasets) {
      if (ref != null) {
        refs.add(ref);
      }
    }
    if (refs.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }

    List<ServiceReference> services = listAvailableArrowServices();
    if (services.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }

    Map<String, DatasetServiceCandidate> candidatesByServiceId = new HashMap<>();
    Map<String, List<DatasetServiceCandidate>> candidatesByDatasetId = new HashMap<>();
    for (DatasetRef ref : refs) {
      candidatesByDatasetId.put(ref.datasetId(), new ArrayList<>());
    }
    Map<String, Set<String>> supportedByServiceId = new HashMap<>();
    for (ServiceReference serviceRef : services) {
      supportedByServiceId.put(serviceRef.serviceId(), fetchSupportedDatasetKeys(serviceRef));
    }

    for (DatasetRef ref : refs) {
      String datasetKey = datasetKey(ref.namespace(), ref.name());
      String groupedKey = groupedDatasetKey(ref.group(), ref.namespace(), ref.name());
      if (datasetKey == null) {
        continue;
      }
      candidatesByServiceId.clear();
      for (ServiceReference serviceRef : services) {
        Set<String> supported = supportedByServiceId.get(serviceRef.serviceId());
        if (supported.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        if (!supported.contains(groupedKey) && !supported.contains(datasetKey)) {
          continue;
        }
        candidatesByServiceId.putIfAbsent(
            serviceRef.serviceId(),
            new DatasetServiceCandidate(
                serviceRef.serviceId(),
                serviceRef.serviceDisplay(),
                serviceRef.serviceType(),
                ref.group().equals(serviceRef.group())));
      }
      if (!candidatesByServiceId.isEmpty()) {
        candidatesByDatasetId
            .computeIfAbsent(ref.datasetId(), ignored -> new ArrayList<>())
            .addAll(candidatesByServiceId.values());
      }
    }

    Map<String, DatasetServiceSelection> selections = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, List<DatasetServiceCandidate>> entry : candidatesByDatasetId.entrySet()) {
      List<DatasetServiceCandidate> candidates = entry.getValue();
      if (candidates == null || candidates.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      DatasetServiceCandidate selected =
          candidates.stream().min(this::compareServiceCandidates).orElse(null);
      if (selected == null) {
        continue;
      }
      int serviceCount = candidates.size();
      String display =
          serviceCount > 1
              ? selected.serviceDisplay() + " (+" + (serviceCount - 1) + ")"
              : selected.serviceDisplay();
      selections.put(
          entry.getKey(),
          new DatasetServiceSelection(
              selected.serviceId(), display, selected.serviceType(), serviceCount));
    }
    return selections.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(selections);
  }

  private int compareServiceCandidates(
      DatasetServiceCandidate left, DatasetServiceCandidate right) {
    int leftGroup = left.sameGroup() ? 0 : 1;
    int rightGroup = right.sameGroup() ? 0 : 1;
    if (leftGroup != rightGroup) {
      return Integer.compare(leftGroup, rightGroup);
    }
    int leftType = serviceTypeRank(left.serviceType());
    int rightType = serviceTypeRank(right.serviceType());
    if (leftType != rightType) {
      return Integer.compare(leftType, rightType);
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(left.serviceDisplay(), "")
        .compareToIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(right.serviceDisplay(), ""));
  }

  private int serviceTypeRank(DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType) {
    if (serviceType == null) {
      return 99;
    }
    return switch (serviceType) {
      case ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL -> 0;
      case ARROW_FLIGHT -> 1;
      default -> 99;
    };
  }

  private List<ServiceReference> listAvailableArrowServices() {
    Set<String> onlineKeys = onlineServiceKeys();
    if (onlineKeys.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ServiceReference> resolved = new ArrayList<>();
    List<Definition> definitions = discoveryCache().allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    for (Definition definition : definitions) {
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionService service) || service.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (Boolean.FALSE.equals(service.envelope().enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionService.ServiceType type = service.serviceType();
      if (type != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL
          && type != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT) {
        continue;
      }
      String group = Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().group());
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().name());
      if (group == null || name == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("service.envelope.group/name are required");
      }
      if (!onlineKeys.contains(serviceKey(group, name))) {
        continue;
      }
      String serviceId = Strings.requireNonBlank(service.resourceId(), "service.resourceId");
      resolved.add(new ServiceReference(group, name, serviceId, type, group + "/" + name));
    }
    resolved.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(
                (ServiceReference value) -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.group(), ""),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(
                value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.serviceName(), ""),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(resolved);
  }

  private Set<String> onlineServiceKeys() {
    ServiceStatusCache cache = session.internal().serviceStatusCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    Set<String> keys = new HashSet<>();
    for (ServiceStatusRow row : cache.snapshot()) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String state = Strings.trimToNull(row.state());
      if (!isServiceStateAvailable(state)) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = serviceKey(row.group(), row.name());
      if (key != null) {
        keys.add(key);
      }
    }
    return keys;
  }

  private Set<String> fetchSupportedDatasetKeys(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    if (serviceRef == null || serviceRef.serviceType() != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    try (RemoteTabularManager tabular = newRemoteTabularManager(serviceRef)) {
      List<TabularTableMetadata> tables = runAsSubject(currentSubject(), tabular::listTables);
      if (tables == null || tables.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      Set<String> supported = new HashSet<>();
      for (TabularTableMetadata table : tables) {
        if (table == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String datasetKey = datasetKey(table.schemaName(), table.tableName());
        if (datasetKey != null) {
          supported.add(datasetKey);
        }
        String grouped = groupedDatasetKey(serviceRef.group(), table.schemaName(), table.tableName());
        if (grouped != null) {
          supported.add(grouped);
        }
      }
      return supported.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(supported);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Set.of();
    }
  }

  private RemoteTabularManager newRemoteTabularManager(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions = serviceOptionsFor(serviceRef);
    ServiceInstanceResolver resolver = resolveDynamicServiceResolver();
    return new RemoteTabularManager(
        session,
        discoveryCache(),
        sessionGroup,
        sessionAppName,
        sessionInstance,
        sessionEnv,
        sessionRegion,
        sessionSite,
        serviceOptions,
        session.kerberosPrincipal(),
        session.kerberosKeytab(),
        resolver);
  }

  private DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptionsFor(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    ServiceRunOptions.Builder optionsBuilder = ServiceRunOptions.builder().withGroup(serviceRef.group());
    if (serviceTrustCert != null) {
      optionsBuilder.withTlsTrustCert(serviceTrustCert).withTlsClientTrustCert(serviceTrustCert);
    }
    return DataOptions.ServiceOptions.builder()
        .withEnabled(true)
        .withQueryService(serviceRef.serviceName())
        .withServiceOptions(optionsBuilder.build())
        .build();
  }

  private ServiceInstanceResolver resolveDynamicServiceResolver() {
    ServiceInstanceResolver existing = dynamicServiceResolver;
    if (existing != null) {
      return existing;
    }
    synchronized (this) {
      existing = dynamicServiceResolver;
      if (existing != null) {
        return existing;
      }
      ServiceInstanceResolver fromSession = session.serviceInstanceResolverIfInitialized();
      if (fromSession != null) {
        dynamicServiceResolver = fromSession;
        return fromSession;
      }
      if (session.internal().controlPlaneConnection() == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Session control plane is not initialized");
      }
      ServiceInstanceResolver created =
          new ServiceInstanceResolver(session.internal().controlPlaneConnection(), session.statusScheduler());
      dynamicServiceResolver = created;
      return created;
    }
  }

  private static boolean isDirectServiceId(String serviceId) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.isDirectServiceId(
        serviceId, DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID);
  }

  private static boolean isServiceStateAvailable(String state) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.isServiceStateAvailable(state);
  }

  private static String serviceKey(String group, String name) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.serviceKey(group, name);
  }

  private static String datasetKey(String namespace, String name) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.datasetKey(namespace, name);
  }

  private static String groupedDatasetKey(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.groupedDatasetKey(group, namespace, name);
  }

  private static boolean isS3Uri(String uri) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.isS3Uri(uri);
  }

  private static boolean supportsLiveServiceType(String serviceType) {
    return "ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL".equals(serviceType) || "ARROW_FLIGHT".equals(serviceType);
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope requireEnvelope(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition").envelope();
    if (envelope == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dataset.envelope is required");
    }
    return envelope;
  }

  private static String requireDefinitionValue(String value, String field) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(value, field);
  }

  private static <T> T runAsSubject(String subject, java.util.function.Supplier<T> callback) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.runAsSubject(subject, callback);
  }

  private record DatasetRef(
      String datasetId,
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String name,
      DefinitionDataset definition,
      long recencyEpochMs) {}

  private record ViewSupport(
      boolean supported, String reason, String queryServiceId, String queryServiceDisplay) {}

  private record LiveSupport(
      boolean supported, String reason, String serviceId, String serviceDisplay) {}

  private record ServiceReference(
      String group,
      String serviceName,
      String serviceId,
      DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType,
      String serviceDisplay) {}

  private record DatasetServiceCandidate(
      String serviceId, String serviceDisplay, DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType, boolean sameGroup) {}

  private record DatasetServiceSelection(
      String serviceId, String serviceDisplay, DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType, int serviceCount) {}
}
