package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

public record StitchDatasetsRow(
    String id,
    boolean enabled,
    String group,
    String namespace,
    String name,
    String datasetType,
    String sourceType,
    String mode,
    String schema,
    String sourceHint,
    boolean viewSupported,
    String viewUnavailableReason,
    String queryServiceId,
    String queryServiceDisplay,
    boolean liveSupported,
    String liveUnavailableReason,
    String liveServiceId,
    String liveServiceDisplay) {

  public StitchDatasetsRow {
    id = normalize(id);
    group = normalize(group);
    namespace = normalize(namespace);
    name = normalize(name);
    datasetType = normalize(datasetType);
    sourceType = normalize(sourceType);
    mode = normalize(mode);
    schema = normalize(schema);
    sourceHint = normalize(sourceHint);
    viewUnavailableReason = normalize(viewUnavailableReason);
    queryServiceId = normalize(queryServiceId);
    queryServiceDisplay = normalize(queryServiceDisplay);
    liveUnavailableReason = normalize(liveUnavailableReason);
    liveServiceId = normalize(liveServiceId);
    liveServiceDisplay = normalize(liveServiceDisplay);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetsScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.QueryParameters;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchBooleanToggle;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component.StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchGroupedResultsPage;

public class StitchDatasetsScreen extends StitchGroupedResultsPage<StitchDatasetsRow> {
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchDatasetsProvider provider;

  public StitchDatasetsScreen(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchDatasetsScreenConfig config,
      StitchDatasetsProvider provider) {
    super(
        runtimeContext,
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle(),
        "Type to filter results...",
        "Search dataset rows");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");

    resultsView().grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset results grid");
    initializeResultsScreen(
        "No datasets", "No matching dataset definitions were found.", "Refresh dataset rows");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchDatasetsRow> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Enabled", this::enabledToggle)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.ENABLED)
            .key("enabled")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("8.1rem")
            .resizable(false)
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(StitchGridColumn.group("Group", StitchDatasetsRow::group).key("group"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Namespace", StitchDatasetsRow::namespace)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("namespace"));
    grid.addColumn(StitchGridColumn.name("Name", StitchDatasetsRow::name).key("name"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Type", StitchDatasetsRow::datasetType)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("datasetType"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Source", StitchDatasetsRow::sourceType)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("sourceType"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Mode", StitchDatasetsRow::mode)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("mode"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Schema", StitchDatasetsRow::schema)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("schema"));

    if (grid.getColumnByKey("datasets-actions") == null) {
      StitchRowActions<StitchDatasetsRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
      rowActions.addAction(
          StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.INFO_CIRCLE_O, "Details", this::openDetails));
      rowActions.addAction(
          StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.TABLE, "View Data", this::openDatasetView));
      rowActions.addAction(
          StitchRowActions.Action.icon(
              VaadinIcon.SHIELD, "Entitlements", this::openDatasetEntitlements));
      rowActions.addColumn(grid).setKey("datasets-actions");
    }
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchDatasetsRow> loadRows() {
    return provider.loadRows();
  }

  @Override
  protected Comparator<StitchDatasetsRow> rowComparator() {
    return Comparator.comparing(StitchDatasetsRow::group, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(StitchDatasetsRow::namespace, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(StitchDatasetsRow::name, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
  }

  @Override
  protected String groupValue(StitchDatasetsRow row) {
    return row == null ? null : row.group();
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesSearch(StitchDatasetsRow row, String query) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return contains(row.group(), query)
        || contains(row.namespace(), query)
        || contains(row.name(), query)
        || contains(row.datasetType(), query)
        || contains(row.sourceType(), query)
        || contains(row.mode(), query)
        || contains(row.schema(), query)
        || contains(row.sourceHint(), query);
  }

  private void openDetails(StitchDatasetsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    provider
        .loadDetails(row.id())
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            details -> new StitchDatasetsDetailsDialog(details).open(),
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Dataset not found",
                    "Unable to load dataset details for "
                        + row.group()
                        + "/"
                        + row.namespace()
                        + "/"
                        + row.name()));
  }

  private void openDatasetView(StitchDatasetsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!row.viewSupported()) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "View Not Available",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(row.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This dataset does not support standard non-live table viewing in this phase."));
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null) {
      return;
    }
    ui.navigate(
        StitchDatasetViewScreen.ROUTE_PATH,
        QueryParameters.simple(Map.of(StitchDatasetViewScreen.QUERY_PARAM_DATASET_ID, row.id())));
  }

  private void openDatasetEntitlements(StitchDatasetsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (row.group().isBlank() || row.namespace().isBlank() || row.name().isBlank()) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Entitlements Not Available",
          "Dataset entitlements require group, namespace, and name.");
      return;
    }
    new StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog(runtimeContext, row.group(), row.namespace(), row.name()).open();
  }

  private StitchBooleanToggle enabledToggle(StitchDatasetsRow row) {
    boolean enabled = row != null && row.enabled();
    StitchBooleanToggle toggle = new StitchBooleanToggle("Enabled", enabled);
    toggle.setLabel("");
    toggle.setReadOnly(true);
    toggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled");
    return toggle;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetsScreenConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

public final class StitchDatasetsScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchDatasetsScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "Datasets";
      this.routePath = "data/datasets";
      this.pageTitle = "Data - Datasets";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Browse dataset definitions and inspect dataset metadata.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDatasetsScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchDatasetsScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetsView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

@Route(value = "data/datasets", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchDatasetsView extends StitchDatasetsScreen {
  public StitchDatasetsView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, Stitch stitch, StitchDatasetsProvider provider) {
    super(runtimeContext, requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  private static StitchDatasetsScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::datasets)
        .filter(StitchDatasetsScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetViewProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.access.AccessManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularTableMetadata;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.RemoteRowManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.RemoteTabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.TabularManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceInstanceResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public class StitchDatasetViewProvider {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchDatasetViewProvider.class);
  private static final String DATASET_SQL_MARKER = "${DATASET}";
  private static final String DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID = "direct";
  private static final String DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_DISPLAY = "DIRECT";

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final AccessManager accessManager;
  private final String sessionGroup;
  private final String sessionAppName;
  private final String sessionInstance;
  private final String sessionEnv;
  private final String sessionRegion;
  private final String sessionSite;
  private final Path serviceTrustCert;
  private volatile ServiceInstanceResolver dynamicServiceResolver;

  public StitchDatasetViewProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.accessManager = this.session.access();
    this.sessionGroup =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getGroup(),
            "platform");
    this.sessionAppName =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getAppName(),
            "stitch");
    this.sessionInstance =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getInstance(),
            "instance");
    this.sessionEnv =
        Strings.trimToNull(this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getEnv());
    this.sessionRegion =
        Strings.trimToNull(
            this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getRegion());
    this.sessionSite =
        Strings.trimToNull(this.session.context() == null ? null : this.session.context().getSite());
    this.serviceTrustCert = this.session.trustCert();
  }

  public Optional<DatasetViewContext> loadContext(String datasetResourceId) {
    DatasetId datasetId = parseDatasetId(datasetResourceId);
    if (datasetId == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    DefinitionDataset definition =
        findDefinition(datasetId.group(), datasetId.namespace(), datasetId.name()).orElse(null);
    if (definition == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.of(toContext(datasetId, definition));
  }

  public DatasetViewPage loadPage(String datasetResourceId, int pageIndex, int pageSize) {
    DatasetId datasetId =
        Objects.requireNonNull(parseDatasetId(datasetResourceId), "datasetResourceId");
    DefinitionDataset definition =
        findDefinition(datasetId.group(), datasetId.namespace(), datasetId.name())
            .orElseThrow(
                () ->
                    new IllegalArgumentException(
                        "Dataset not found: "
                            + datasetId.group()
                            + "/"
                            + datasetId.namespace()
                            + "/"
                            + datasetId.name()));
    DatasetViewContext context = toContext(datasetId, definition);
    if (!context.viewSupported()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(context.viewUnavailableReason());
    }

    int resolvedPageSize = Math.max(1, Math.min(pageSize <= 0 ? 25 : pageSize, 200));
    int requestedPageIndex = Math.max(0, pageIndex);

    ServiceReference serviceRef = resolveServiceReference(context.queryServiceId());
    long totalRows = countRows(datasetId, serviceRef);
    int maxPageIndex = totalRows == 0 ? 0 : (int) ((totalRows - 1L) / resolvedPageSize);
    int effectivePageIndex = Math.min(requestedPageIndex, maxPageIndex);
    int offset = effectivePageIndex * resolvedPageSize;

    String rowsSql = "select * from ${DATASET} limit " + resolvedPageSize + " offset " + offset;
    RowResult rowsResult = queryRows(datasetId, rowsSql, serviceRef);
    List<String> columns = rowsResult.columns();
    if (columns == null || columns.isEmpty()) {
      columns = loadColumns(datasetId, serviceRef);
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = toRowMaps(columns, rowsResult.rows());

    return new DatasetViewPage(
        context,
        List.copyOf(columns == null ? List.of() : columns),
        rows,
        totalRows,
        effectivePageIndex,
        resolvedPageSize);
  }

  private DatasetViewContext toContext(DatasetId datasetId, DefinitionDataset definition) {
    String datasetCanonical = datasetId.toString();
    String mode = datasetMode(definition);
    String subject = currentSubject();
    String schema = resolveSchemaName(datasetId.group(), datasetId.namespace(), datasetId.name());
    if (schema.isBlank()) {
      schema = normalize(definition.view() == null ? null : definition.view().schemaName());
    }

    if ("DUCKDB_ACTIVE".equals(mode)) {
      return new DatasetViewContext(
          datasetCanonical,
          datasetId.group(),
          datasetId.namespace(),
          datasetId.name(),
          datasetType(definition),
          sourceType(definition),
          mode,
          schema,
          sourceHint(definition),
          "",
          "",
          false,
          "Live dataset mode is out of scope in this phase. Only non-live table view is supported.");
    }

    if (!accessManager.canQueryDataset(subject, datasetCanonical)) {
      return new DatasetViewContext(
          datasetCanonical,
          datasetId.group(),
          datasetId.namespace(),
          datasetId.name(),
          datasetType(definition),
          sourceType(definition),
          mode,
          schema,
          sourceHint(definition),
          "",
          "",
          false,
          "This dataset is not queryable in standard non-live mode for the current subject.");
    }

    AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute route = resolveRouteForDataset(datasetId, definition, subject);
    if (route == null) {
      if (supportsDirectQuery(definition)) {
        return new DatasetViewContext(
            datasetCanonical,
            datasetId.group(),
            datasetId.namespace(),
            datasetId.name(),
            datasetType(definition),
            sourceType(definition),
            mode,
            schema,
            sourceHint(definition),
            DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID,
            DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_DISPLAY,
            true,
            "");
      }
      return new DatasetViewContext(
          datasetCanonical,
          datasetId.group(),
          datasetId.namespace(),
          datasetId.name(),
          datasetType(definition),
          sourceType(definition),
          mode,
          schema,
          sourceHint(definition),
          "",
          "",
          false,
          "No online query service is mapped for this dataset.");
    }

    return new DatasetViewContext(
        datasetCanonical,
        datasetId.group(),
        datasetId.namespace(),
        datasetId.name(),
        datasetType(definition),
        sourceType(definition),
        mode,
        schema,
        sourceHint(definition),
        Strings.requireNonBlank(route.serviceId(), "dataset.route.serviceId"),
        Strings.requireNonBlank(route.serviceDisplay(), "dataset.route.serviceDisplay"),
        true,
        "");
  }

  private RowResult queryRows(DatasetId datasetId, String sql, ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    String subject = currentSubject();
    String resolvedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    if (serviceRef.direct()) {
      String directSql = rewriteDirectDatasetSql(resolvedSql, datasetId);
      try {
        return runAsSubject(
            subject,
            () -> {
              if (datasetId != null) {
                TabularManager directTabular = session.data().direct().tabular();
                if (directTabular instanceof TabularManagerImpl directManager) {
                  directManager.installDataset(datasetId.toString());
                }
              }
              return session.data().direct().rows().querySql(directSql);
            });
      } catch (RuntimeException error) {
        LOGGER.error(
            "[Stitch][Data][DatasetView][queryRows][direct][failed] datasetId={} subject={} sql={} message={}",
            datasetId,
            subject,
            directSql,
            Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()),
            error);
        throw error;
      }
    }
    String serviceSql = rewriteServiceDatasetSql(resolvedSql, datasetId);
    try (RowManager rows = newRemoteRowManager(serviceRef)) {
      try {
        return runAsSubject(subject, () -> rows.querySql(serviceSql));
      } catch (RuntimeException error) {
        LOGGER.error(
            "[Stitch][Data][DatasetView][queryRows][service][failed] datasetId={} serviceId={} subject={} sql={} message={}",
            datasetId,
            serviceRef.serviceId(),
            subject,
            serviceSql,
            Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()),
            error);
        throw error;
      }
    }
  }

  private long countRows(DatasetId datasetId, ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    RowResult result = queryRows(datasetId, "select count(*) as __row_count from ${DATASET}", serviceRef);
    if (result.rows() == null || result.rows().isEmpty() || result.rows().get(0).isEmpty()) {
      return 0L;
    }
    Object value = result.rows().get(0).get(0);
    if (value instanceof Number number) {
      return number.longValue();
    }
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(String.valueOf(value));
    if (text == null) {
      return 0L;
    }
    return Long.parseLong(text);
  }

  private List<String> loadColumns(DatasetId datasetId, ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    RowResult schemaOnly = queryRows(datasetId, "select * from ${DATASET} limit 0", serviceRef);
    List<String> columns = schemaOnly.columns();
    if (columns != null && !columns.isEmpty()) {
      return List.copyOf(columns);
    }
    RowResult singleRow = queryRows(datasetId, "select * from ${DATASET} limit 1", serviceRef);
    List<String> fallback = singleRow.columns();
    return fallback == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(fallback);
  }

  private ServiceReference resolveServiceReference(String queryServiceId) {
    return parseServiceReference(queryServiceId);
  }

  private ServiceReference parseServiceReference(String serviceResourceId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(serviceResourceId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset query service id is missing.");
    }
    if (isDirectServiceId(normalized)) {
      return directServiceReference();
    }
    if (!normalized.startsWith("service:")) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset query service id must use canonical service:group/name format.");
    }
    String token = normalized.substring("service:".length());
    int slash = token.indexOf('/');
    if (slash <= 0 || slash >= token.length() - 1) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset query service id is malformed: " + normalized);
    }
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(token.substring(0, slash));
    String serviceName = Strings.trimToNull(token.substring(slash + 1));
    if (group == null || serviceName == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset query service id is malformed: " + normalized);
    }
    DefinitionService definition =
        discoveryCache()
            .get(DefinitionService.class, group, serviceName)
            .orElseThrow(
                () ->
                    new IllegalStateException(
                        "Dataset query service not found: " + group + "/" + serviceName));
    DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType = definition.serviceType();
    String canonical = Strings.requireNonBlank(definition.resourceId(), "service.resourceId");
    return new ServiceReference(group, serviceName, canonical, serviceType, group + "/" + serviceName, false);
  }

  private ServiceReference directServiceReference() {
    String group = sessionGroup;
    return new ServiceReference(
        group,
        DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID,
        DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID,
        null,
        DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_DISPLAY,
        true);
  }

  private RowManager newRemoteRowManager(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions = serviceOptionsFor(serviceRef);
    ServiceInstanceResolver resolver = resolveDynamicServiceResolver();
    DiscoveryCache cache = discoveryCache();
    RemoteTabularManager tabular =
        new RemoteTabularManager(
            session,
            cache,
            sessionGroup,
            sessionAppName,
            sessionInstance,
            sessionEnv,
            sessionRegion,
            sessionSite,
            serviceOptions,
            session.kerberosPrincipal(),
            session.kerberosKeytab(),
            resolver);
    return new RemoteRowManager(
        session,
        tabular,
        cache,
        sessionGroup,
        sessionAppName,
        sessionInstance,
        sessionEnv,
        sessionRegion,
        sessionSite,
        serviceOptions,
        session.kerberosPrincipal(),
        session.kerberosKeytab(),
        resolver);
  }

  private RemoteTabularManager newRemoteTabularManager(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions = serviceOptionsFor(serviceRef);
    ServiceInstanceResolver resolver = resolveDynamicServiceResolver();
    return new RemoteTabularManager(
        session,
        discoveryCache(),
        sessionGroup,
        sessionAppName,
        sessionInstance,
        sessionEnv,
        sessionRegion,
        sessionSite,
        serviceOptions,
        session.kerberosPrincipal(),
        session.kerberosKeytab(),
        resolver);
  }

  private DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptionsFor(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    ServiceRunOptions.Builder optionsBuilder = ServiceRunOptions.builder().withGroup(serviceRef.group());
    if (serviceTrustCert != null) {
      optionsBuilder.withTlsTrustCert(serviceTrustCert).withTlsClientTrustCert(serviceTrustCert);
    }
    return DataOptions.ServiceOptions.builder()
        .withEnabled(true)
        .withQueryService(serviceRef.serviceName())
        .withServiceOptions(optionsBuilder.build())
        .build();
  }

  private ServiceInstanceResolver resolveDynamicServiceResolver() {
    ServiceInstanceResolver existing = dynamicServiceResolver;
    if (existing != null) {
      return existing;
    }
    synchronized (this) {
      existing = dynamicServiceResolver;
      if (existing != null) {
        return existing;
      }
      ServiceInstanceResolver fromSession = session.serviceInstanceResolverIfInitialized();
      if (fromSession != null) {
        dynamicServiceResolver = fromSession;
        return fromSession;
      }
      if (session.internal().controlPlaneConnection() == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Session control plane is not initialized");
      }
      ServiceInstanceResolver created =
          new ServiceInstanceResolver(session.internal().controlPlaneConnection(), session.statusScheduler());
      dynamicServiceResolver = created;
      return created;
    }
  }

  private String resolveSchemaName(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    DefinitionDataset definition =
        findDefinition(
                Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group"),
                Strings.requireNonBlank(namespace, "namespace"),
                Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "name"))
            .orElse(null);
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String viewSchema = normalize(definition.view() == null ? null : definition.view().schemaName());
    if (!viewSchema.isBlank()) {
      return viewSchema;
    }
    String datasetId = DatasetId.of(group, namespace, name).toString();
    for (DefinitionIngest ingest : discoveryCache().list(DefinitionIngest.class, group)) {
      if (ingest == null || ingest.envelope() == null || Boolean.FALSE.equals(ingest.envelope().enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!datasetId.equals(normalize(ingest.datasetId()))) {
        continue;
      }
      String schema = normalize(ingest.outputSchemaId());
      if (!schema.isBlank()) {
        return schema;
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  private Optional<DefinitionDataset> findDefinition(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    String envelopeName = namespace + "/" + name;
    return discoveryCache().get(DefinitionDataset.class, group, envelopeName);
  }

  private static DatasetId parseDatasetId(String datasetResourceId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(datasetResourceId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return DatasetId.parse(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private String currentSubject() {
    return StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
  }

  private static String datasetType(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    return Objects.requireNonNull(definition.type(), "dataset.type").name();
  }

  private static String sourceType(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    if (definition.view() != null) {
      return "VIEW";
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    if (binding == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dataset.binding is required when dataset.view is absent");
    }
    if (binding.duckdb() != null) {
      return "DUCKDB";
    }
    if (binding.parquet() != null) {
      return "PARQUET";
    }
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      return "ODBC";
    }
    if (binding.external() != null) {
      return "EXTERNAL";
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("dataset.binding type is not supported");
  }

  private static String datasetMode(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (definition.view() != null && definition.view().target() != null) {
      String targetType = normalize(definition.view().target().targetType());
      if (!targetType.isBlank()) {
        return targetType;
      }
    }
    if (definition.binding() != null && definition.binding().duckdb() != null) {
      String duckdbTargetType = normalize(definition.binding().duckdb().targetType());
      if (!duckdbTargetType.isBlank()) {
        return duckdbTargetType;
      }
    }
    return normalize(definition.effectiveAccessMode());
  }

  private static boolean supportsDirectQuery(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.binding() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (definition.binding().odbc() != null) {
      return true;
    }
    if (definition.binding().parquet() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    DefinitionDataset.ParquetBinding parquet = definition.binding().parquet();
    String uri = Strings.trimToNull(parquet.uri());
    if (isS3Uri(uri)) {
      return true;
    }
    String connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(parquet.connectionName());
    return connectionName != null;
  }

  private static String sourceHint(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (definition.view() != null) {
      List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
      if (definition.view().target() != null) {
        parts.add(
            "target="
                + firstNonBlank(
                    definition.view().target().duckdbTableName(),
                    definition.view().target().parquetPath()));
      }
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(definition.view().querySql())) {
        parts.add("query=" + truncate(definition.view().querySql(), 140));
      }
      return joinParts(parts);
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    if (binding == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (binding.duckdb() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(
          binding.duckdb().relationName(),
          binding.duckdb().databasePath(),
          binding.duckdb().parquetHistoryPath());
    }
    if (binding.parquet() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(
          binding.parquet().uri(), binding.parquet().connectionName(), binding.parquet().glob());
    }
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(
          binding.odbc().tableName(), binding.odbc().querySql(), binding.odbc().connectionName());
    }
    if (binding.external() != null) {
      return firstNonBlank(binding.external().reference(), binding.external().externalType());
    }
    return "";
  }

  private static List<Map<String, Object>> toRowMaps(List<String> columns, List<List<Object>> rows) {
    if (columns == null || columns.isEmpty() || rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> mapped = new ArrayList<>(rows.size());
    for (List<Object> row : rows) {
      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(columns.size());
      for (int index = 0; index < columns.size(); index++) {
        Object value = row != null && index < row.size() ? row.get(index) : null;
        values.put(columns.get(index), value);
      }
      mapped.add(Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(values)));
    }
    return List.copyOf(mapped);
  }

  private static String rewriteDirectDatasetSql(String sql, DatasetId datasetId) {
    String normalizedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    Objects.requireNonNull(datasetId, "datasetId");
    if (!normalizedSql.contains(DATASET_SQL_MARKER)) {
      return normalizedSql;
    }
    String token = quoteIdentifier(datasetId.namespace()) + "." + quoteIdentifier(datasetId.name());
    return normalizedSql.replace(DATASET_SQL_MARKER, token);
  }

  private static String rewriteServiceDatasetSql(String sql, DatasetId datasetId) {
    String normalizedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    Objects.requireNonNull(datasetId, "datasetId");
    if (!normalizedSql.contains(DATASET_SQL_MARKER)) {
      return normalizedSql;
    }
    String token = quoteIdentifier(datasetId.namespace()) + "." + quoteIdentifier(datasetId.name());
    return normalizedSql.replace(DATASET_SQL_MARKER, token);
  }

  private static String quoteIdentifier(String identifier) {
    return "\"" + identifier.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.normalize(value);
  }

  private static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.firstNonBlank(values);
  }

  private static String truncate(String value, int maxLength) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.truncate(value, maxLength);
  }

  private static String joinParts(List<String> parts) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.joinParts(parts);
  }

  private static boolean isDirectServiceId(String serviceId) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.isDirectServiceId(
        serviceId, DIRECT_QUERY_SERVICE_ID);
  }

  private AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute resolveRouteForDataset(
      DatasetId datasetId, DefinitionDataset definition, String subject) {
    String datasetResourceId = datasetId == null ? null : datasetId.toString();
    if (datasetResourceId == null) {
      return null;
    }
    AccessManager.DatasetServiceRoute route =
        accessManager.datasetQueryRoute(subject, datasetResourceId).orElse(null);
    if (route != null && isDirectServiceId(route.serviceId()) && !supportsDirectQuery(definition)) {
      route = null;
    }
    if (route != null && route.online()) {
      return route;
    }
    return null;
  }

  private DatasetServiceSelection resolveDatasetServiceSelection(DatasetId datasetId) {
    if (datasetId == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String datasetKey = datasetKey(datasetId.namespace(), datasetId.name());
    String groupedKey = groupedDatasetKey(datasetId.group(), datasetId.namespace(), datasetId.name());
    if (datasetKey == null) {
      return null;
    }

    List<ServiceReference> services = listAvailableArrowServices();
    if (services.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }

    Map<String, DatasetServiceCandidate> candidatesByServiceId = new HashMap<>();
    for (ServiceReference serviceRef : services) {
      Set<String> supported = fetchSupportedDatasetKeys(serviceRef);
      if (supported.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      boolean supports = supported.contains(groupedKey) || supported.contains(datasetKey);
      if (!supports) {
        continue;
      }
      candidatesByServiceId.putIfAbsent(
          serviceRef.serviceId(),
          new DatasetServiceCandidate(
              serviceRef.serviceId(),
              serviceRef.serviceDisplay(),
              serviceRef.serviceType(),
              datasetId.group().equals(serviceRef.group())));
    }
    if (candidatesByServiceId.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    List<DatasetServiceCandidate> candidates = List.copyOf(candidatesByServiceId.values());
    DatasetServiceCandidate selected =
        candidates.stream().min(this::compareServiceCandidates).orElse(null);
    if (selected == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int serviceCount = candidates.size();
    String display =
        serviceCount > 1
            ? selected.serviceDisplay() + " (+" + (serviceCount - 1) + ")"
            : selected.serviceDisplay();
    return new DatasetServiceSelection(
        selected.serviceId(), display, selected.serviceType(), serviceCount);
  }

  private int compareServiceCandidates(
      DatasetServiceCandidate left, DatasetServiceCandidate right) {
    int leftGroup = left.sameGroup() ? 0 : 1;
    int rightGroup = right.sameGroup() ? 0 : 1;
    if (leftGroup != rightGroup) {
      return Integer.compare(leftGroup, rightGroup);
    }
    int leftType = serviceTypeRank(left.serviceType());
    int rightType = serviceTypeRank(right.serviceType());
    if (leftType != rightType) {
      return Integer.compare(leftType, rightType);
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(left.serviceDisplay(), "")
        .compareToIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(right.serviceDisplay(), ""));
  }

  private int serviceTypeRank(DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType) {
    if (serviceType == null) {
      return 99;
    }
    return switch (serviceType) {
      case ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL -> 0;
      case ARROW_FLIGHT -> 1;
      default -> 99;
    };
  }

  private List<ServiceReference> listAvailableArrowServices() {
    Set<String> onlineKeys = onlineServiceKeys();
    if (onlineKeys.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ServiceReference> resolved = new ArrayList<>();
    List<org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition> definitions =
        discoveryCache().allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    for (org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition definition : definitions) {
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionService service) || service.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (Boolean.FALSE.equals(service.envelope().enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType = service.serviceType();
      if (serviceType != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL
          && serviceType != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT) {
        continue;
      }
      String group = Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().group());
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().name());
      if (group == null || name == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("service.envelope.group/name are required");
      }
      if (!onlineKeys.contains(serviceKey(group, name))) {
        continue;
      }
      String serviceId = Strings.requireNonBlank(service.resourceId(), "service.resourceId");
      resolved.add(new ServiceReference(group, name, serviceId, serviceType, group + "/" + name, false));
    }
    resolved.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(
                (ServiceReference value) -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.group(), ""),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(
                value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.serviceName(), ""),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(resolved);
  }

  private Set<String> onlineServiceKeys() {
    ServiceStatusCache cache = session.internal().serviceStatusCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    Set<String> keys = new HashSet<>();
    for (ServiceStatusRow row : cache.snapshot()) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String state = Strings.trimToNull(row.state());
      if (!isServiceStateAvailable(state)) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = serviceKey(row.group(), row.name());
      if (key != null) {
        keys.add(key);
      }
    }
    return keys;
  }

  private Set<String> fetchSupportedDatasetKeys(ServiceReference serviceRef) {
    if (serviceRef == null || serviceRef.serviceType() != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    try (RemoteTabularManager tabular = newRemoteTabularManager(serviceRef)) {
      List<TabularTableMetadata> tables = runAsSubject(currentSubject(), tabular::listTables);
      if (tables == null || tables.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      Set<String> supported = new HashSet<>();
      for (TabularTableMetadata table : tables) {
        if (table == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = datasetKey(table.schemaName(), table.tableName());
        if (key != null) {
          supported.add(key);
        }
        String grouped = groupedDatasetKey(serviceRef.group(), table.schemaName(), table.tableName());
        if (grouped != null) {
          supported.add(grouped);
        }
      }
      return supported.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(supported);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Set.of();
    }
  }

  private static boolean isServiceStateAvailable(String state) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.isServiceStateAvailable(state);
  }

  private static String serviceKey(String group, String name) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.serviceKey(group, name);
  }

  private static String datasetKey(String namespace, String name) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.datasetKey(namespace, name);
  }

  private static String groupedDatasetKey(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.groupedDatasetKey(group, namespace, name);
  }

  private static boolean isS3Uri(String uri) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.isS3Uri(uri);
  }

  private static <T> T runAsSubject(String subject, java.util.function.Supplier<T> callback) {
    return StitchDatasetProviderSupport.runAsSubject(subject, callback);
  }

  public record DatasetViewContext(
      String datasetId,
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String name,
      String datasetType,
      String sourceType,
      String mode,
      String schema,
      String sourceHint,
      String queryServiceId,
      String queryServiceDisplay,
      boolean viewSupported,
      String viewUnavailableReason) {}

  public record DatasetViewPage(
      DatasetViewContext context,
      List<String> columns,
      List<Map<String, Object>> rows,
      long totalRows,
      int pageIndex,
      int pageSize) {}

  private record ServiceReference(
      String group,
      String serviceName,
      String serviceId,
      DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType,
      String serviceDisplay,
      boolean direct) {}

  private record DatasetServiceCandidate(
      String serviceId, String serviceDisplay, DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType, boolean sameGroup) {}

  private record DatasetServiceSelection(
      String serviceId, String serviceDisplay, DefinitionService.ServiceType serviceType, int serviceCount) {}
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchDatasetViewScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

@Route(value = StitchDatasetViewScreen.ROUTE_PATH, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchDatasetViewScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  public static final String ROUTE_PATH = "data/datasets/view";
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_DATASET_ID = "datasetId";

  private final StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig config;
  private final StitchDatasetViewProvider provider;
  private final StitchSection contextSection = new StitchSection("Dataset Context");
  private final FormLayout contextForm = new FormLayout();
  private final StitchResultsView<Map<String, Object>> results = new StitchResultsView<>();

  private String datasetId;
  private int pageIndex;
  private int pageSize = 25;
  private long totalRows;
  private List<String> configuredColumns = List.of();
  private StitchDatasetViewProvider.DatasetViewContext currentContext;

  public StitchDatasetViewScreen(
      Stitch stitch, StitchDatasetViewProvider provider) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  private StitchDatasetViewScreen(
      StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig config, StitchDatasetViewProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle());
    this.config = config;
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    configureContextSection();
    configureResults();

    Button refresh = new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshPage());
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refresh);
    refresh.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh dataset table rows");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh dataset table rows");
    addPageAction(refresh);

    addToBody(contextSection, results);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String requestedDatasetId =
        firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_DATASET_ID);
    if (requestedDatasetId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Dataset Not Selected",
          "Open this view from Data -> Datasets using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    loadDataset(requestedDatasetId, true);
  }

  private void configureContextSection() {
    contextForm.setWidthFull();
    contextForm.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("48em", 2));
    contextSection.addToBody(contextForm);
  }

  private void configureResults() {
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setHeight(null);
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(25, 50, 100, 200);
    results.setPageSize(pageSize);
    results.setResultCountVisible(false);
    results.setEmptyState("No rows", "No rows found for this dataset.");
    results
        .pagination()
        .onPrevious(
            () -> {
              if (pageIndex <= 0) {
                return;
              }
              pageIndex--;
              refreshPage();
            })
        .onNext(
            () -> {
              if (!canAdvancePage()) {
                return;
              }
              pageIndex++;
              refreshPage();
            })
        .onPageSizeChange(
            value -> {
              int requested = value == null ? 25 : value;
              if (requested == pageSize) {
                return;
              }
              pageSize = requested;
              pageIndex = 0;
              refreshPage();
            });
    StitchGrid<Map<String, Object>> grid = results.grid();
    grid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset table rows");
    grid.setSelectionMode(Grid.SelectionMode.NONE);
  }

  private void loadDataset(String requestedDatasetId, boolean resetPaging) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(requestedDatasetId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Dataset Not Selected",
          "Open this view from Data -> Datasets using the View action.");
      return;
    }

    StitchDatasetViewProvider.DatasetViewContext context =
        provider.loadContext(normalized).orElse(null);
    if (context == null) {
      applyEmptyState("Dataset Not Found", "The requested dataset could not be resolved.");
      return;
    }

    this.datasetId = context.datasetId();
    this.currentContext = context;
    if (resetPaging) {
      this.pageIndex = 0;
    }
    updateContextForm(context);
    refreshPage();
  }

  private void refreshPage() {
    if (datasetId == null || currentContext == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Dataset Not Selected",
          "Open this view from Data -> Datasets using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    if (!currentContext.viewSupported()) {
      applyEmptyState("View Not Available", currentContext.viewUnavailableReason());
      return;
    }

    try {
      StitchDatasetViewProvider.DatasetViewPage page =
          provider.loadPage(datasetId, pageIndex, pageSize);
      currentContext = page.context();
      configureGridColumns(page.columns());
      results.setItems(page.rows());
      results.setEmpty(page.rows().isEmpty());
      updatePagingState(page.totalRows(), page.pageIndex(), page.pageSize());
      updateContextForm(page.context());
    } catch (Exception error) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Unable To Load Dataset Rows",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()),
              "The dataset table could not be loaded."));
    }
  }

  private void configureGridColumns(List<String> columns) {
    List<String> resolved = columns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(columns);
    if (Objects.equals(configuredColumns, resolved)) {
      return;
    }
    StitchGrid<Map<String, Object>> grid = results.grid();
    grid.removeAllColumns();
    int index = 0;
    for (String column : resolved) {
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (name == null) {
        continue;
      }
      final String key = name;
      grid.addColumn(
          StitchGridColumn.<Map<String, Object>>text(name, row -> formatValue(row == null ? null : row.get(key)))
              .key("col_" + index++)
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
              .enumLikeBadges(false)
              .sortable(false));
    }
    configuredColumns = resolved;
  }

  private void updateContextForm(StitchDatasetViewProvider.DatasetViewContext context) {
    contextForm.removeAll();
    addContextValue("Group", context.group());
    addContextValue("Namespace", context.namespace());
    addContextValue("Name", context.name());
    addContextValue("Type", context.datasetType());
    addContextValue("Source", context.sourceType());
    addContextValue("Mode", context.mode());
    addContextValue("Schema", context.schema());
    addContextValue("Query Service", context.queryServiceDisplay());
    addContextValue("Source Hint", context.sourceHint());
    setPageSubtitle(
        context.group()
            + "/"
            + context.namespace()
            + "/"
            + context.name()
            + " - Read-only table view");
  }

  private void addContextValue(String label, String value) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    Span content = new Span(resolved == null ? "-" : resolved);
    content.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label + " value");
    contextForm.addFormItem(content, label);
  }

  private void updatePagingState(long total, int currentPageIndex, int currentPageSize) {
    totalRows = Math.max(0L, total);
    pageIndex = Math.max(0, currentPageIndex);
    pageSize = Math.max(1, currentPageSize <= 0 ? pageSize : currentPageSize);
    if (results.pagination().pageSize() != pageSize) {
      results.pagination().setPageSize(pageSize);
    }
    int pages = totalRows == 0 ? 1 : (int) Math.ceil((double) totalRows / pageSize);
    int boundedPage = totalRows == 0 ? 0 : Math.min(pageIndex, Math.max(0, pages - 1));
    results.pagination().setPageState(boundedPage, pages, (int) totalRows);
  }

  private boolean canAdvancePage() {
    if (totalRows <= 0) {
      return false;
    }
    int pages = (int) Math.ceil((double) totalRows / pageSize);
    return pageIndex < pages - 1;
  }

  private void applyEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    configuredColumns = List.of();
    results.grid().removeAllColumns();
    results.setItems(List.of());
    results.setEmptyState(title, message);
    results.setEmpty(true);
    updatePagingState(0, 0, pageSize);
  }

  private static String formatValue(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    if (value instanceof byte[] bytes) {
      int max = Math.min(bytes.length, 12);
      StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder("0x");
      for (int i = 0; i < max; i++) {
        builder.append(String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%02x", bytes[i]));
      }
      if (bytes.length > max) {
        builder.append("...");
      }
      return builder.toString();
    }
    return String.valueOf(value);
  }

  private static String firstQueryParam(BeforeEnterEvent event, String key) {
    if (event == null || key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    List<String> values = event.getLocation().getQueryParameters().getParameters().get(key);
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(values.get(0));
  }

  private static StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::datasetView)
        .filter(StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}
