package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

public final class StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.routePath = "data/datasets/view";
      this.pageTitle = "Data - Dataset View";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Read-only dataset table browsing for queryable datasets.";
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchDatasetViewScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchStreamDefinitionSupport {
  private StitchStreamDefinitionSupport() {}

  public static String schemaRef(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(
        Strings.trimToNull(definition.schemaId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(definition.schemaKey()),
        "-");
  }

  public static String sourceHint(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.address() == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>(3);
    if (Strings.trimToNull(definition.address().topic()) != null) {
      parts.add("topic=" + Strings.trimToNull(definition.address().topic()));
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(definition.address().channel()) != null) {
      parts.add("channel=" + Strings.trimToNull(definition.address().channel()));
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(definition.address().streamId()) != null) {
      parts.add("addressStreamId=" + Strings.trimToNull(definition.address().streamId()));
    }
    return parts.isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(" | ", parts);
  }

  public static List<String> schemaColumns(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.schema() == null || definition.schema().fields() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> columns = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (DefinitionStream.Column field : definition.schema().fields()) {
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(field == null ? null : field.name());
      if (name != null) {
        columns.add(name);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(columns);
  }

  public static List<String> keyFields(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null
        || definition.semantic() == null
        || definition.semantic().dataShape() == null
        || definition.semantic().dataShape().keyFields() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> keys = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String key : definition.semantic().dataShape().keyFields()) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (value != null) {
        keys.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(keys);
  }

  public static String summarizeRefs(List<String> refs) {
    if (refs == null || refs.isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String ref : refs) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(ref);
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    int limit = Math.min(3, normalized.size());
    String joined = String.join(", ", normalized.subList(0, limit));
    int extra = normalized.size() - limit;
    return extra > 0 ? joined + " (+" + extra + ")" : joined;
  }

  public static boolean isEnabled(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return !Boolean.FALSE.equals(definition.envelope().enabled());
  }

  public static String classify(DefinitionStream definition) {
    boolean hasFields =
        definition != null
            && definition.schema() != null
            && definition.schema().fields() != null
            && !definition.schema().fields().isEmpty();
    boolean hasMessageType = Strings.trimToNull(definition == null ? null : definition.messageType()) != null;
    if (hasFields && hasMessageType) {
      return "HYBRID";
    }
    if (hasFields) {
      return "TABULAR";
    }
    return "EVENT";
  }

  public static String liveStatus(
      String streamClass, String eventStatus, String tabularStatus, String hybridStatus) {
    return switch (streamClass) {
      case "TABULAR" -> tabularStatus;
      case "HYBRID" -> hybridStatus;
      default -> eventStatus;
    };
  }

  public static String validateTabularStructure(
      DefinitionStream definition,
      String unsupportedSerdeStatus,
      String noKeysStatus,
      String missingKeysStatus) {
    if (!isTabularSerdeSupported(definition)) {
      return unsupportedSerdeStatus;
    }
    List<String> keys = keyFields(definition);
    if (keys.isEmpty()) {
      return noKeysStatus;
    }
    if (!schemaContainsAllKeys(definition, keys)) {
      return missingKeysStatus;
    }
    return null;
  }

  public static boolean isTabularSerdeSupported(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.serde() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return definition.serde() == DefinitionStream.SerdeType.JSON
        || definition.serde() == DefinitionStream.SerdeType.NVFIX
        || definition.serde() == DefinitionStream.SerdeType.BYTES;
  }

  public static boolean schemaContainsAllKeys(DefinitionStream definition, List<String> keys) {
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    Set<String> schema = new LinkedHashSet<>(schemaColumns(definition));
    for (String key : keys) {
      if (!schema.contains(key)) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  public static String primaryConnectionRef(DefinitionStream definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.connectionRefs() == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String ref : definition.connectionRefs()) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(ref);
      if (value != null) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public static String enumName(Enum<?> value) {
    return value == null ? "UNKNOWN" : value.name();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamDetails.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;

public record StitchStreamDetails(
    String streamId,
    String group,
    String namespace,
    String name,
    Map<String, String> fields,
    Object sourceObject) {

  public StitchStreamDetails {
    streamId = normalize(streamId);
    group = normalize(group);
    namespace = normalize(namespace);
    name = normalize(name);
    fields = fields == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(fields));
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamDetailsDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport;

public class StitchStreamDetailsDialog extends StitchDialog {
  public StitchStreamDetailsDialog(StitchStreamDetails details) {
    super("Stream Details");
    Objects.requireNonNull(details, "details");

    String target = StitchDetailsDialogSupport.joinPath(details.group(), details.namespace(), details.name());
    setDialogTitle("Stream Details - " + target);

    Map<String, String> labels = labels();
    Map<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(details.fields());

    addToBody(StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(orderedKeys(values), values, labels));
    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> details.sourceObject() == null ? details : details.sourceObject());
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> labels() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> labels = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    labels.put("enabled", "Enabled");
    labels.put("group", "Group");
    labels.put("namespace", "Namespace");
    labels.put("name", "Name");
    labels.put("streamId", "Stream Id");
    labels.put("classification", "Classification");
    labels.put("transport", "Transport");
    labels.put("serde", "Serde");
    labels.put("messageType", "Message Type");
    labels.put("schemaRef", "Schema");
    labels.put("sourceHint", "Source");
    labels.put("lifecycle", "Lifecycle");
    labels.put("updatedUtc", "Updated (UTC)");
    labels.put("createdUtc", "Created (UTC)");
    labels.put("connectionRefs", "Connections");
    labels.put("dependencyRefs", "Dependencies");
    labels.put("viewStatus", "View Status");
    labels.put("liveStatus", "Live Status");
    return Map.copyOf(labels);
  }

  private static List<String> orderedKeys(Map<String, String> values) {
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.orderedKeys(
        null,
        List.of(
            "enabled",
            "group",
            "namespace",
            "name",
            "streamId",
            "classification",
            "transport",
            "serde",
            "messageType",
            "schemaRef",
            "sourceHint",
            "lifecycle",
            "updatedUtc",
            "createdUtc",
            "connectionRefs",
            "dependencyRefs",
            "viewStatus",
            "liveStatus"),
        values);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamEventViewScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.DetachEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchEventLogShell;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConflationMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

@Route(value = StitchStreamEventViewScreen.ROUTE_PATH, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStreamEventViewScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  public static final String ROUTE_PATH = "data/streams/view";
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_STREAM_ID = "streamId";

  private static final List<Integer> DISPATCH_MS = List.of(50, 100, 200, 500);
  private static final List<Integer> MAX_EVENTS = List.of(100, 250, 500, 1000, 2000);

  private final StitchStreamsProvider provider;
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry;
  private final StitchSection contextSection = new StitchSection("Stream Context");
  private final StitchSection controlsSection = new StitchSection("Event View Controls");
  private final FormLayout contextForm = new FormLayout();
  private final StitchEventLogShell<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> eventLog =
      new StitchEventLogShell<>();
  private final Select<StitchRealtimeConflationMode> conflationMode = new Select<>();
  private final Select<Integer> dispatchIntervalMs = new Select<>();
  private final Select<Integer> maxRetainedEvents = new Select<>();

  private StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEventContext context;
  private StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> controller;
  private AutoCloseable shellBinding = () -> {};
  private AutoCloseable registryBinding = () -> {};

  public StitchStreamEventViewScreen(
      Stitch stitch, StitchStreamsProvider provider, StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    super(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.requireConfig(stitch).pageTitle() + " - View",
        "Realtime event-stream viewer");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.realtimeRegistry = Objects.requireNonNull(realtimeRegistry, "realtimeRegistry");

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    configureContextSection();
    configureControlsSection();
    configureEventLog();
    configureRefreshAction();
    syncControlDefaults();

    addToBody(contextSection, controlsSection, eventLog);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, eventLog);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String streamId = StitchStreamViewSupport.queryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_STREAM_ID);
    if (streamId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Stream Not Selected", "Open this screen from Data -> Streams using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    loadStream(streamId, true);
  }

  @Override
  protected void onDetach(DetachEvent detachEvent) {
    closeController();
    super.onDetach(detachEvent);
  }

  private void configureControlsLayout() {
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setWidthFull();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("36em", 2),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("60em", 4));
    form.add(conflationMode, dispatchIntervalMs, maxRetainedEvents);

    Button apply =
        StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("APPLY", "Apply event viewer control changes");
    apply.addClickListener(event -> applyControlChanges());
    controlsSection.addToBody(form, new HorizontalLayout(apply));
  }

  private void configureContextSection() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureContextForm(contextForm);
    contextSection.addToBody(contextForm);
  }

  private void configureControlsSection() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
        "Conflation",
        "Realtime conflation mode",
        List.of(StitchRealtimeConflationMode.values()),
        StitchRealtimeConflationMode::name,
        conflationMode);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
        "Dispatch ms",
        "Realtime dispatch interval milliseconds",
        DISPATCH_MS,
        String::valueOf,
        dispatchIntervalMs);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
        "Max Events",
        "Maximum retained events in the viewer",
        MAX_EVENTS,
        String::valueOf,
        maxRetainedEvents);
    configureControlsLayout();
  }

  private void configureEventLog() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureEventLogShell(
        eventLog,
        "No events",
        "Start the subscription to receive events.",
        "Stream event log grid",
        true,
        true);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamEventColumns(eventLog);
  }

  private void configureRefreshAction() {
    Button refresh =
        StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("REFRESH", "Refresh stream event viewer");
    refresh.addClickListener(
        event ->
            loadStream(
                currentStreamId(),
                controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state())));
    addPageAction(refresh);
  }

  private void syncControlDefaults() {
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaults = provider.defaultEventPolicy();
    conflationMode.setValue(defaults.conflationMode());
    dispatchIntervalMs.setValue(defaults.dispatchIntervalMillis());
    maxRetainedEvents.setValue(500);
    eventLog.setMaxEvents(500);
  }

  private void loadStream(String requestedStreamId, boolean autoStart) {
    String streamId = Strings.trimToNull(requestedStreamId);
    if (streamId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Stream Not Selected", "Open this screen from Data -> Streams using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEventContext loaded = provider.loadEventContext(streamId).orElse(null);
    if (loaded == null) {
      applyEmptyState("Stream Not Found", "The requested stream could not be resolved.");
      return;
    }
    context = loaded;
    updateContextForm(loaded);
    if (!loaded.viewSupported()) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "View Not Available",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(loaded.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream does not support event viewing in this phase."));
      return;
    }
    bindController(autoStart);
  }

  private void bindController(boolean autoStart) {
    if (context == null || !context.viewSupported()) {
      return;
    }
    closeController();
    eventLog.clearEvents();
    eventLog.setMaxEvents(StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxRetainedEvents.getValue(), 500));
    try {
      controller =
          new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
              provider.eventSourceFor(context),
              policyFromControls(),
              provider.defaultEventScope(context),
              getUI().orElse(null));
      shellBinding = eventLog.bindController(controller);
      registryBinding =
          realtimeRegistry.register(
              "Data Streams View",
              context.group() + " / " + context.namespace() + " / " + context.name(),
              controller,
              getUI().orElse(null));
      eventLog.statusBar().setMessage("");
      if (autoStart) {
        controller.start();
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Event Viewer Setup Failed",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Unable to initialize stream event viewer."));
    }
  }

  private void applyControlChanges() {
    eventLog.setMaxEvents(StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxRetainedEvents.getValue(), 500));
    if (context != null && context.viewSupported()) {
      bindController(controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state()));
    }
  }

  private void closeController() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(registryBinding);
    registryBinding = () -> {};
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(shellBinding);
    shellBinding = () -> {};
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.close();
      controller = null;
    }
  }

  private StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyFromControls() {
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaults = provider.defaultEventPolicy();
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                conflationMode.getValue(), defaults.conflationMode()))
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                dispatchIntervalMs.getValue(), defaults.dispatchIntervalMillis()))
        .withMaxBatchSize(defaults.maxBatchSize())
        .withMaxQueueSize(defaults.maxQueueSize())
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(defaults.staleTimeoutMillis())
        .build();
  }

  private void updateContextForm(StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEventContext value) {
    if (value == null) {
      StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, Map.of());
      return;
    }
    Map<String, String> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("Group", value.group());
    fields.put("Namespace", value.namespace());
    fields.put("Name", value.name());
    fields.put("Stream Id", value.streamId());
    fields.put("Class", value.streamClass());
    fields.put("Transport", value.transport());
    fields.put("Serde", value.serde());
    fields.put("Message Type", value.messageType());
    fields.put("Topic", value.topic());
    fields.put("Connection", value.connectionRef());
    fields.put("Source", value.sourceHint());
    StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, fields);
    setPageSubtitle(
        value.group() + "/" + value.namespace() + "/" + value.name() + " - Realtime event stream viewer");
  }

  private void applyEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    closeController();
    eventLog.clearEvents();
    eventLog.resultsView().setEmptyState(title, Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    eventLog.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
    eventLog.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
    eventLog.statusBar().setMessage(Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
  }

  private String currentStreamId() {
    return context == null ? null : context.streamId();
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamHybridViewScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.DetachEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.tabs.Tab;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.tabs.Tabs;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchEventLogShell;

import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableShell;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConflationMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchSubscriptionControls;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

@Route(value = StitchStreamHybridViewScreen.ROUTE_PATH, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStreamHybridViewScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  public static final String ROUTE_PATH = "data/streams/view/hybrid";
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_STREAM_ID = "streamId";

  private static final List<Integer> MAX_ROWS = List.of(200, 500, 1000, 2000);
  private static final List<Integer> MAX_EVENTS = List.of(100, 250, 500, 1000, 2000);
  private static final List<Integer> DISPATCH_MS = List.of(50, 100, 200, 500);
  private static final List<Integer> FLASH_SECONDS = List.of(1, 2, 5, 10);

  private final StitchStreamsProvider provider;
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry;
  private final StitchSection contextSection = new StitchSection("Stream Context");
  private final StitchSection controlsSection = new StitchSection("Hybrid View Controls");
  private final FormLayout contextForm = new FormLayout();
  private final FormLayout controlsForm = new FormLayout();
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar = new StitchRealtimeStatusBar();
  private final StitchSubscriptionControls subscriptionControls = new StitchSubscriptionControls();
  private final StitchEventLogShell<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> eventLog =
      new StitchEventLogShell<>();
  private final StitchLiveTableShell<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String> liveTable =
      new StitchLiveTableShell<>();
  private final Select<Integer> maxEvents =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Max Events", "Maximum retained events", MAX_EVENTS, String::valueOf);
  private final Select<Integer> maxRows =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Max Rows", "Maximum retained table rows", MAX_ROWS, String::valueOf);
  private final Select<StitchRealtimeConflationMode> conflationMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Conflation",
          "Realtime conflation mode",
          StitchRealtimeConflationMode.values(),
          StitchRealtimeConflationMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> dispatchIntervalMs =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Dispatch ms",
          "Realtime dispatch interval milliseconds",
          DISPATCH_MS,
          String::valueOf);
  private final Select<StitchLiveTableHighlightMode> highlightMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Highlight",
          "Live table highlight mode",
          StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.values(),
          StitchLiveTableHighlightMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> flashWindowSeconds =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Flash Seconds",
          "Temporary highlight duration seconds",
          FLASH_SECONDS,
          String::valueOf);
  private final Span changeSummary = new Span("Changed rows: 0 | changed cells: 0");
  private final Button applyControls =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("APPLY", "Apply hybrid stream control changes");
  private final Tabs viewTabs = new Tabs();
  private final Tab eventTab = new Tab("Event View");
  private final Tab tabularTab = new Tab("Tabular View");
  private final Div viewerContainer = new Div();
  private final Div eventPane = new Div();
  private final Div tabularPane = new Div();

  private StitchStreamsProvider.StreamHybridContext context;
  private StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate> controller;
  private AutoCloseable updatesBinding = () -> {};
  private AutoCloseable registryBinding = () -> {};
  private Registration statusBinding = () -> {};
  private Registration controlsBinding = () -> {};

  public StitchStreamHybridViewScreen(
      Stitch stitch, StitchStreamsProvider provider, StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    super(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.requireConfig(stitch).pageTitle() + " - View",
        "Realtime hybrid-stream viewer");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.realtimeRegistry = Objects.requireNonNull(realtimeRegistry, "realtimeRegistry");

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    configureContextSection();
    configureControlsSection();
    configureRealtimeSurface();
    configureEventPane();
    configureTabularPane();
    configureViewerTabs();
    configurePageActions();

    addToBody(contextSection, controlsSection, statusBar, subscriptionControls, viewTabs, viewerContainer);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, viewerContainer);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String streamId = StitchStreamViewSupport.queryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_STREAM_ID);
    if (streamId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Stream Not Selected", "Open this screen from Data -> Streams using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    loadStream(streamId, true);
  }

  @Override
  protected void onDetach(DetachEvent detachEvent) {
    closeController();
    super.onDetach(detachEvent);
  }

  private void configureContextSection() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureContextForm(contextForm);
    contextSection.addToBody(contextForm);
  }

  private void configureControlsSection() {
    controlsForm.setWidthFull();
    controlsForm.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("36em", 2),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("60em", 6));
    controlsForm.add(maxEvents, maxRows, conflationMode, dispatchIntervalMs, highlightMode, flashWindowSeconds);

    highlightMode.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          liveTable.setHighlightMode(
              StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                  event.getValue(), StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.NONE));
          liveTable.clearHighlights();
          liveTable.refreshGrid();
          updateChangeSummary();
        });
    flashWindowSeconds.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          Integer seconds = event.getValue();
          if (seconds != null) {
            liveTable.setFlashWindow(Duration.ofSeconds(seconds));
            liveTable.pruneTransientHighlights();
            liveTable.refreshGrid();
            updateChangeSummary();
          }
        });
    maxEvents.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          Integer value = event.getValue();
          if (value != null) {
            eventLog.setMaxEvents(value);
          }
          updateClearState();
        });

    applyControls.addClickListener(event -> applyControlChanges());
    controlsSection.addToBody(controlsForm, new HorizontalLayout(applyControls), changeSummary);
  }

  private void configureRealtimeSurface() {
    statusBar.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Hybrid stream realtime status");
    subscriptionControls.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Hybrid stream subscription controls");
    subscriptionControls.onClear(this::clearTransientState);
  }

  private void configureEventPane() {
    eventPane.setSizeFull();
    eventPane.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");

    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureEventLogShell(
        eventLog,
        "No events",
        "Start the subscription to receive events.",
        "Hybrid stream event log grid",
        false,
        false);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamEventColumns(eventLog);

    eventPane.add(eventLog);
  }

  private void configureTabularPane() {
    tabularPane.setSizeFull();
    tabularPane.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");

    liveTable.withRowIdResolver(StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow::rowId);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureLiveTableShell(
        liveTable,
        "No live rows",
        "Start the subscription to receive updates.",
        "Hybrid stream tabular grid",
        false,
        false,
        null);

    configureTabularGridColumns();
    tabularPane.add(liveTable);
  }

  private void configureViewerTabs() {
    viewTabs.add(eventTab, tabularTab);
    viewTabs.setWidthFull();
    viewTabs.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Hybrid stream viewer mode");
    viewTabs.addSelectedChangeListener(event -> updateVisiblePane());

    viewerContainer.setSizeFull();
    viewerContainer.getStyle().set("display", "flex");
    viewerContainer.getStyle().set("flex-direction", "column");
    viewerContainer.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    eventPane.getStyle().set("flex", "1");
    tabularPane.getStyle().set("flex", "1");
    viewerContainer.add(eventPane, tabularPane);

    viewTabs.setSelectedTab(eventTab);
    updateVisiblePane();
  }

  private void configurePageActions() {
    Button refresh =
        StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("REFRESH", "Refresh hybrid stream viewer");
    refresh.addClickListener(
        event ->
            loadStream(
                streamId(),
                controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state())));
    addPageAction(refresh);
  }

  private void loadStream(String requestedStreamId, boolean autoStart) {
    String streamId = Strings.trimToNull(requestedStreamId);
    if (streamId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Stream Not Selected", "Open this screen from Data -> Streams using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    StitchStreamsProvider.StreamHybridContext loaded = provider.loadHybridContext(streamId).orElse(null);
    if (loaded == null) {
      applyEmptyState("Stream Not Found", "The requested stream could not be resolved.");
      return;
    }
    context = loaded;
    syncControlDefaults();
    updateContextForm();
    if (!loaded.viewSupported()) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "View Not Available",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(loaded.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream does not support hybrid viewing in this phase."));
      return;
    }
    bindController(autoStart);
  }

  private void bindController(boolean autoStart) {
    if (context == null || !context.viewSupported()) {
      return;
    }
    closeController();
    eventLog.clearEvents();
    eventLog.setMaxEvents(StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxEvents.getValue(), 500));
    liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
    configureTabularGridColumns();
    updateChangeSummary();
    updateClearState();
    try {
      controller =
          new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
              provider.hybridSourceFor(context, optionsFromControls()),
              policyFromControls(),
              provider.defaultHybridScope(context),
              getUI().orElse(null));
      statusBinding = statusBar.bind(controller);
      controlsBinding = subscriptionControls.bind(controller);
      updatesBinding = controller.addListener(new HybridUpdatesListener());
      registryBinding =
          realtimeRegistry.register(
              "Data Streams Hybrid View",
              context.group() + " / " + context.namespace() + " / " + context.name(),
              controller,
              getUI().orElse(null));
      statusBar.setMessage("");
      if (autoStart) {
        controller.start();
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Hybrid Viewer Setup Failed",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Hybrid stream setup failed."));
    }
  }

  private void applyControlChanges() {
    boolean wasActive =
        controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state());
    bindController(wasActive);
  }

  private void closeController() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(registryBinding);
    registryBinding = () -> {};
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(updatesBinding);
    updatesBinding = () -> {};
    statusBinding.remove();
    statusBinding = () -> {};
    controlsBinding.remove();
    controlsBinding = () -> {};
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.close();
      controller = null;
    }
  }

  private void clearTransientState() {
    eventLog.clearEvents();
    liveTable.clearHighlights();
    liveTable.refreshGrid();
    updateChangeSummary();
    updateClearState();
  }

  private void updateVisiblePane() {
    boolean eventSelected = viewTabs.getSelectedTab() == eventTab;
    eventPane.setVisible(eventSelected);
    tabularPane.setVisible(!eventSelected);
  }

  private void configureTabularGridColumns() {
    List<String> dataColumns = context == null ? List.of() : context.schemaColumns();
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamTabularColumns(
        liveTable,
        dataColumns,
        "Event (UTC)",
        "Observed (UTC)",
        StitchStreamViewSupport::formatUtc);
  }

  private void updateContextForm() {
    if (context == null) {
      StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, Map.of());
      return;
    }
    Map<String, String> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("Group", context.group());
    fields.put("Namespace", context.namespace());
    fields.put("Name", context.name());
    fields.put("Stream Id", context.streamId());
    fields.put("Class", context.streamClass());
    fields.put("Transport", context.transport());
    fields.put("Serde", context.serde());
    fields.put("Message Type", context.messageType());
    fields.put("Topic", context.topic());
    fields.put("Connection", context.connectionRef());
    fields.put(
        "Key Fields",
        context.keyFields().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(", ", context.keyFields()));
    fields.put(
        "Schema Columns",
        context.schemaColumns().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.valueOf(context.schemaColumns().size()));
    fields.put("Source", context.sourceHint());
    StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, fields);
    setPageSubtitle(
        context.group()
            + "/"
            + context.namespace()
            + "/"
            + context.name()
            + " - Realtime hybrid stream viewer");
  }

  private void applyEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    closeController();
    eventLog.clearEvents();
    eventLog.resultsView().setEmptyState(title, Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    eventLog.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
    eventLog.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
    liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
    configureTabularGridColumns();
    liveTable.clearHighlights();
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmptyState(title, Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    liveTable.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
    statusBar.setMessage(Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    updateChangeSummary();
    updateClearState();
  }

  private void syncControlDefaults() {
    if (context == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchStreamsProvider.TabularViewOptions defaults = provider.defaultHybridOptions(context);
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyDefaults = provider.defaultHybridPolicy();
    maxEvents.setValue(500);
    maxRows.setValue(defaults.maxRows());
    conflationMode.setValue(policyDefaults.conflationMode());
    dispatchIntervalMs.setValue(policyDefaults.dispatchIntervalMillis());
    highlightMode.setValue(StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT);
    flashWindowSeconds.setValue(2);
    eventLog.setMaxEvents(StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxEvents.getValue(), 500));
    liveTable.setHighlightMode(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
            highlightMode.getValue(), StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.NONE));
    liveTable.setFlashWindow(
        Duration.ofSeconds(StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(flashWindowSeconds.getValue(), 2)));
    updateChangeSummary();
    updateClearState();
  }

  private StitchStreamsProvider.TabularViewOptions optionsFromControls() {
    return new StitchStreamsProvider.TabularViewOptions(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxRows.getValue(), 500));
  }

  private StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyFromControls() {
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaults = provider.defaultHybridPolicy();
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                conflationMode.getValue(), defaults.conflationMode()))
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                dispatchIntervalMs.getValue(), defaults.dispatchIntervalMillis()))
        .withMaxBatchSize(defaults.maxBatchSize())
        .withMaxQueueSize(defaults.maxQueueSize())
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(defaults.staleTimeoutMillis())
        .build();
  }

  private void updateChangeSummary() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.updateChangeSummary(changeSummary, liveTable);
  }

  private void updateClearState() {
    subscriptionControls.clearEnabled(
        !eventLog.events().isEmpty() || liveTable.changedRowsCount() > 0 || liveTable.changedCellsCount() > 0);
  }

  private String streamId() {
    return context == null ? null : context.streamId();
  }

  private final class HybridUpdatesListener
      implements StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Listener<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate> {
    @Override
    public void onUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate>> updates) {
      if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
        return;
      }
      List<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> append = new ArrayList<>();
      for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate> update : updates) {
        if (update == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (update.kind() == StitchRealtimeUpdate.Kind.SNAPSHOT) {
          eventLog.clearEvents();
          liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
        }
        StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate payload = update.payload();
        if (payload == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (payload.event() != null) {
          append.add(payload.event());
        }
        if (payload.tabularDelta() != null) {
          liveTable.applyDelta(payload.tabularDelta());
        }
      }
      if (!append.isEmpty()) {
        eventLog.appendAll(append);
      }
      liveTable.pruneTransientHighlights();
      liveTable.refreshGrid();
      updateChangeSummary();
      updateClearState();
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamPayloadSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class StitchStreamPayloadSupport {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();
  private static final List<String> OPERATION_HEADERS =
      List.of("op", "operation", "action", "eventType", "event");
  private static final Set<String> REMOVE_OPERATIONS =
      Set.of("delete", "removed", "remove", "del", "d", "tombstone");

  private StitchStreamPayloadSupport() {}

  static List<Map<String, Object>> decodePayloadRows(byte[] payload, String serde) {
    if (payload == null || payload.length == 0) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String normalizedSerde = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(serde), "UNKNOWN");
    if ("NVFIX".equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedSerde)) {
      return decodeDelimitedRow(payload);
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> json = decodeJsonRows(payload);
    return json.isEmpty() && "BYTES".equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedSerde)
        ? decodeDelimitedRow(payload)
        : json;
  }

  @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
  static List<Map<String, Object>> decodeJsonRows(byte[] payload) {
    try {
      Object parsed = MAPPER.readValue(payload, Object.class);
      if (parsed instanceof Map<?, ?> map) {
        Map<String, Object> row = normalizeKeys(map);
        return row.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.of(row);
      }
      if (!(parsed instanceof List<?> rows)) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<Map<String, Object>> out = new ArrayList<>();
      for (Object item : rows) {
        if (item instanceof Map<?, ?> map) {
          Map<String, Object> row = normalizeKeys(map);
          if (!row.isEmpty()) {
            out.add(row);
          }
        }
      }
      return out.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(out);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return List.of();
    }
  }

  static Map<String, Object> normalizeKeys(Map<?, ?> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<?, ?> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey() == null ? null : String.valueOf(entry.getKey()));
      if (key != null) {
        out.put(key, entry.getValue());
      }
    }
    return out.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(out);
  }

  static List<Map<String, Object>> decodeDelimitedRow(byte[] payload) {
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(new String(payload, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    if (text == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    char delimiter = text.indexOf('\u0001') >= 0 ? '\u0001' : '|';
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> row = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String token : text.split(java.util.regex.Pattern.quote(String.valueOf(delimiter)))) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      int eq = value.indexOf('=');
      if (eq <= 0 || eq >= value.length() - 1) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(value.substring(0, eq));
      if (key != null) {
        row.put(key, Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value.substring(eq + 1)), ""));
      }
    }
    return row.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.of(Map.copyOf(row));
  }

  static LinkedHashMap<String, Object> projectTabularValues(
      StitchStreamsProvider.StreamTabularContext context, Map<String, Object> source) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> projected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (context == null || source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return projected;
    }
    Map<String, Object> byLower = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    source.forEach(
        (key, value) -> {
          String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
          if (normalized != null) {
            byLower.putIfAbsent(normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), value);
          }
        });
    for (String column : context.schemaColumns()) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Object value = source.containsKey(key) ? source.get(key) : byLower.get(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      if (value != null || source.containsKey(key)) {
        projected.put(key, value);
      }
    }
    return projected;
  }

  static String operationFromHeaders(Map<String, String> headers) {
    return findOperation(headers);
  }

  static String operationFromValues(Map<String, Object> values) {
    return findOperation(values);
  }

  static void removeOperationFields(Map<String, Object> values) {
    values.keySet().removeIf(StitchStreamPayloadSupport::isOperationField);
  }

  static boolean isRemoveOperation(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized != null && REMOVE_OPERATIONS.contains(normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
  }

  static String rowIdFor(List<String> keyFields, Map<String, Object> values) {
    if (keyFields == null || keyFields.isEmpty() || values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    StringBuilder rowId = new StringBuilder();
    for (String rawKey : keyFields) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(rawKey);
      Object value = key == null ? null : values.get(key);
      if (key == null || value == null) {
        return null;
      }
      if (!rowId.isEmpty()) {
        rowId.append('\u001f');
      }
      rowId.append(value);
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(rowId.toString());
  }

  static Map<String, String> headersAsText(Map<String, byte[]> headers) {
    if (headers == null || headers.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    headers.forEach(
        (key, value) -> {
          String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
          if (normalizedKey != null) {
            values.put(normalizedKey, headerValue(value));
          }
        });
    return values.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  static String payloadPreview(byte[] payload) {
    if (payload == null || payload.length == 0) {
      return "-";
    }
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(new String(payload, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    if (text != null) {
      return truncate(text.replace('\n', ' ').replace('\r', ' '), 240);
    }
    int max = Math.min(payload.length, 16);
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder("0x");
    for (int i = 0; i < max; i++) {
      builder.append(String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%02x", payload[i]));
    }
    if (payload.length > max) {
      builder.append("...");
    }
    return builder + " (" + payload.length + " bytes)";
  }

  static String truncate(String value, int limit) {
    if (value == null || value.length() <= limit) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(value, "");
    }
    return value.substring(0, Math.max(0, limit - 3)) + "...";
  }

  static Instant toInstant(long epochMillis) {
    long value = epochMillis <= 0L ? System.currentTimeMillis() : epochMillis;
    try {
      return Instant.ofEpochMilli(value);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Instant.now();
    }
  }

  static byte[] cloneBytes(byte[] value) {
    return value == null ? new byte[0] : value.clone();
  }

  static long recencyEpoch(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    long updated = parseEpoch(envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    return updated > Long.MIN_VALUE ? updated : parseEpoch(envelope.createdTimeUtc());
  }

  static long parseEpoch(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized).toEpochMilli();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
  }

  static String indexKey(String value) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String headerValue(byte[] value) {
    if (value == null || value.length == 0) {
      return "";
    }
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(new String(value, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    return text != null ? truncate(text, 180) : "base64:" + Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(value);
  }

  private static String findOperation(Map<?, ?> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<?, ?> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey() == null ? null : String.valueOf(entry.getKey()));
      if (key != null && isOperationField(key)) {
        return Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue() == null ? null : String.valueOf(entry.getValue()));
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static boolean isOperationField(String key) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String op : OPERATION_HEADERS) {
      if (normalized.equalsIgnoreCase(op)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamsLiveDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.dialog.Dialog;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchEventLogShell;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableDelta;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableShell;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConnectionState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;

final class StitchStreamsLiveDialog extends Dialog {
  private final StitchStreamsProvider provider;
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry;
  private final StitchStreamsRow row;

  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final VerticalLayout contentHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchEventLogShell<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> eventLog =
      new StitchEventLogShell<>();
  private final StitchLiveTableShell<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String> liveTable =
      new StitchLiveTableShell<>();

  private final Button startButton = headerAction("START");
  private final Button stopButton = headerAction("STOP");
  private final Button clearButton = headerAction("CLEAR");
  private final Button jsonButton = headerAction("JSON");
  private final Button closeButton = headerAction("CLOSE");

  private ViewMode viewMode = ViewMode.UNSUPPORTED;
  private String unavailableReason;
  private String lastError;
  private StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEventContext eventContext;
  private StitchStreamsProvider.StreamTabularContext tabularContext;
  private StitchStreamsProvider.StreamHybridContext hybridContext;
  private StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> controller;
  private AutoCloseable streamBinding = () -> {};
  private AutoCloseable observerBinding = () -> {};
  private AutoCloseable registryBinding = () -> {};
  private Registration statusBinding = () -> {};

  StitchStreamsLiveDialog(
      StitchStreamsProvider provider,
      StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry,
      StitchStreamsRow row) {
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.realtimeRegistry = Objects.requireNonNull(realtimeRegistry, "realtimeRegistry");
    this.row = Objects.requireNonNull(row, "row");

    configureDialogChrome();
    configureRealtimeViews();
    resolveContext();
    composeBody();
    configureHeaderActions();
    refreshSummary();
    refreshActionState();

    addOpenedChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isOpened()) {
            closeResources();
          }
        });
  }

  private void configureDialogChrome() {
    addClassName("stitch-dialog");
    addClassName("stitch-streams-live-dialog");
    getElement().getThemeList().add("stitch-dialog");
    setWidth("94vw");
    setMaxWidth("1500px");
    setHeight("88vh");
    setTop("4vh");
    setCloseOnEsc(true);
    setCloseOnOutsideClick(false);

    HorizontalLayout header = new HorizontalLayout();
    header.setWidthFull();
    header.setPadding(false);
    header.setSpacing(false);
    header.addClassName("stitch-dialog-header");

    Span title =
        new Span(
            "Stream - "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(
                    Strings.trimToNull(row.name()),
                    Strings.trimToNull(row.streamClass()),
                    "Unknown"));
    title.addClassName("stitch-dialog-title");

    Div spacer = new Div();
    spacer.getStyle().set("flex", "1 1 auto");

    HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout();
    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(true);
    actions.addClassName("stitch-dialog-header-actions");
    actions.addClassName("stitch-dialog-actions");
    actions.add(startButton, stopButton, clearButton, jsonButton, closeButton);

    header.add(title, spacer, actions);
    header.expand(spacer);

    contentHost.setSizeFull();
    contentHost.setPadding(false);
    contentHost.setSpacing(true);
    contentHost.addClassName("stitch-dialog-body");
    contentHost.addClassName("stitch-streams-live-dialog-body");

    add(header, contentHost);
  }

  private void configureRealtimeViews() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureEventLogShell(
        eventLog,
        "No live stream events",
        "Press START to subscribe.",
        "Stream event grid",
        true,
        false);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamEventColumns(eventLog);
    eventLog.addClassName("stitch-streams-live-event-log");
    eventLog.controls().setVisible(false);

    liveTable.withRowIdResolver(StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow::rowId);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureLiveTableShell(
        liveTable,
        "No live stream rows",
        "Press START to subscribe.",
        "Stream live rows grid",
        true,
        false,
        null);
    liveTable.addClassName("stitch-streams-live-grid");
    liveTable.controls().setVisible(false);
  }

  private void resolveContext() {
    String streamClass =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(row.streamClass()), "").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    switch (streamClass) {
      case "EVENT" -> {
        viewMode = ViewMode.EVENT;
        eventContext = provider.loadEventContext(row.id()).orElse(null);
        if (eventContext == null) {
          unavailableReason = "The selected stream could not be resolved.";
          return;
        }
        if (!eventContext.viewSupported()) {
          unavailableReason =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  Strings.trimToNull(eventContext.viewUnavailableReason()),
                  "Event viewing is not supported for this stream.");
        }
      }
      case "TABULAR" -> {
        viewMode = ViewMode.TABULAR;
        tabularContext = provider.loadTabularContext(row.id()).orElse(null);
        if (tabularContext == null) {
          unavailableReason = "The selected stream could not be resolved.";
          return;
        }
        StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamTabularColumns(
            liveTable,
            tabularContext.schemaColumns(),
            "Event (UTC)",
            "Observed (UTC)",
            StitchStreamViewSupport::formatUtc);
        if (!tabularContext.viewSupported()) {
          unavailableReason =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  Strings.trimToNull(tabularContext.viewUnavailableReason()),
                  "Tabular viewing is not supported for this stream.");
        }
      }
      case "HYBRID" -> {
        viewMode = ViewMode.HYBRID;
        hybridContext = provider.loadHybridContext(row.id()).orElse(null);
        if (hybridContext == null) {
          unavailableReason = "The selected stream could not be resolved.";
          return;
        }
        StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamTabularColumns(
            liveTable,
            hybridContext.schemaColumns(),
            "Event (UTC)",
            "Observed (UTC)",
            StitchStreamViewSupport::formatUtc);
        if (!hybridContext.viewSupported()) {
          unavailableReason =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  Strings.trimToNull(hybridContext.viewUnavailableReason()),
                  "Hybrid viewing is not supported for this stream.");
        }
      }
      default -> {
        viewMode = ViewMode.UNSUPPORTED;
        unavailableReason = "Unsupported stream mode: " + Strings.firstNonBlank(streamClass, "UNKNOWN");
      }
    }
  }

  private void composeBody() {
    contentHost.removeAll();
    contentHost.add(summaryStrip, liveComponent());
    contentHost.setFlexGrow(1, liveComponent());
    applyUnavailableState();
  }

  private Component liveComponent() {
    return switch (viewMode) {
      case EVENT -> eventLog;
      case TABULAR, HYBRID -> liveTable;
      case UNSUPPORTED -> liveTable;
    };
  }

  private void applyUnavailableState() {
    String reason = Strings.trimToNull(unavailableReason);
    if (reason == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (viewMode == ViewMode.EVENT) {
      eventLog.resultsView().setEmptyState("View Not Available", reason);
      eventLog.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
      eventLog.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
      eventLog.statusBar().setMessage(reason);
    } else {
      liveTable.resultsView().setEmptyState("View Not Available", reason);
      liveTable.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
      liveTable.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
      liveTable.statusBar().setMessage(reason);
    }
  }

  private void configureHeaderActions() {
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(startButton);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(stopButton);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(clearButton);
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(jsonButton);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(closeButton);

    startButton.addClickListener(event -> startStreaming());
    stopButton.addClickListener(event -> stopStreaming());
    clearButton.addClickListener(event -> clearStreaming());
    jsonButton.addClickListener(event -> openJson());
    closeButton.addClickListener(event -> close());
  }

  private void startStreaming() {
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(unavailableReason)) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      ensureController();
      if (controller != null) {
        controller.start();
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      lastError = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Unable to start stream.");
    }
    refreshSummary();
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void stopStreaming() {
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.stop();
    }
    refreshSummary();
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void clearStreaming() {
    if (viewMode == ViewMode.EVENT) {
      eventLog.clearEvents();
    } else {
      liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
      liveTable.clearHighlights();
      liveTable.refreshGrid();
    }
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void openJson() {
    new StitchJsonDialog("Stream JSON - " + Strings.firstNonBlank(row.name(), "Stream"), jsonPayload())
        .open();
  }

  private void ensureController() {
    if (controller != null) {
      return;
    }
    closeResources();
    switch (viewMode) {
      case EVENT -> bindEventController();
      case TABULAR -> bindTabularController();
      case HYBRID -> bindHybridController();
      case UNSUPPORTED -> {
        // No controller.
      }
    }
    refreshSummary();
    refreshActionState();
  }

  private void bindEventController() {
    if (eventContext == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> resolved =
        new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
            provider.eventSourceFor(eventContext),
            provider.defaultEventPolicy(),
            provider.defaultEventScope(eventContext),
            getUI().orElse(null));
    streamBinding = eventLog.bindController(resolved);
    observerBinding = observeController(resolved);
    registryBinding = registerController(resolved);
    controller = resolved;
  }

  private void bindTabularController() {
    if (tabularContext == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<
            StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String>>
        resolved =
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
                provider.tabularSourceFor(
                    tabularContext, provider.defaultTabularOptions(tabularContext)),
                provider.defaultTabularPolicy(),
                provider.defaultTabularScope(tabularContext),
                getUI().orElse(null));
    streamBinding =
        liveTable.bindController(
            resolved,
            updates -> {
              liveTable.pruneTransientHighlights();
              liveTable.refreshGrid();
            });
    observerBinding = observeController(resolved);
    registryBinding = registerController(resolved);
    controller = resolved;
  }

  private void bindHybridController() {
    if (hybridContext == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate> resolved =
        new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
            provider.hybridSourceFor(hybridContext, provider.defaultHybridOptions(hybridContext)),
            provider.defaultHybridPolicy(),
            provider.defaultHybridScope(hybridContext),
            getUI().orElse(null));
    statusBinding = liveTable.statusBar().bind(resolved);
    streamBinding =
        resolved.addListener(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Listener<>() {
              @Override
              public void onUpdates(
                  List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate>> updates) {
                if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
                  return;
                }
                runUi(
                    () -> {
                      for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate> update : updates) {
                        if (update == null) {
                          continue;
                        }
                        if (update.kind() == StitchRealtimeUpdate.Kind.SNAPSHOT) {
                          liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
                        }
                        StitchStreamsProvider.HybridStreamUpdate payload = update.payload();
                        if (payload != null && payload.tabularDelta() != null) {
                          liveTable.applyDelta(payload.tabularDelta());
                        }
                      }
                      liveTable.pruneTransientHighlights();
                      liveTable.refreshGrid();
                    });
              }
            });
    observerBinding = observeController(resolved);
    registryBinding = registerController(resolved);
    controller = resolved;
  }

  private AutoCloseable registerController(StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    try {
      return realtimeRegistry.register(
          "Data Streams",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(row.group()) + " / " + Strings.trimToNull(row.namespace()) + " / " + row.name(),
              row.name()),
          value,
          getUI().orElse(null));
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return () -> {};
    }
  }

  private AutoCloseable observeController(StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    try {
      return value.addObserver(
          new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Observer() {
            @Override
            public void onStateChanged(
                StitchRealtimeConnectionState state,
                org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {
              lastError = null;
              refreshSummary();
              refreshActionState();
            }

            @Override
            public void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {
              lastError = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error == null ? null : error.getMessage()), null);
              refreshSummary();
              refreshActionState();
            }
          });
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return () -> {};
    }
  }

  private void refreshSummary() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Group", row.group());
    values.put("Namespace", row.namespace());
    values.put("Stream", row.name());
    values.put("Mode", StitchStreamsScreen.modeLabel(row));
    values.put("Schema", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(row.schemaRef()), "-"));
    values.put("Status", statusLabel());
    summaryStrip.setItems(values);
  }

  private String statusLabel() {
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(unavailableReason)) {
      return "ERROR";
    }
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState state =
        controller == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED : controller.state();
    if (lastError != null) {
      return state.name() + " - " + lastError;
    }
    return state.name();
  }

  private void refreshActionState() {
    boolean unavailable = Strings.isNotBlank(unavailableReason);
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState state =
        controller == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED : controller.state();
    boolean active =
        state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED
            || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING
            || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE;
    startButton.setEnabled(!unavailable && !active);
    stopButton.setEnabled(!unavailable && active);
    clearButton.setEnabled(true);
  }

  private Object jsonPayload() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> json = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    json.put("stream", row);
    json.put("mode", viewMode.name());
    json.put("state", controller == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED.name() : controller.state().name());
    if (eventContext != null) {
      json.put("context", eventContext);
      json.put("events", eventLog.events().stream().limit(250).toList());
    }
    if (tabularContext != null) {
      json.put("context", tabularContext);
      json.put("rows", liveTable.rows().stream().limit(500).toList());
    }
    if (hybridContext != null) {
      json.put("context", hybridContext);
      json.put("rows", liveTable.rows().stream().limit(500).toList());
    }
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(unavailableReason)) {
      json.put("unavailableReason", unavailableReason);
    }
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(lastError)) {
      json.put("lastError", lastError);
    }
    return json;
  }

  private void closeResources() {
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(registryBinding);
    registryBinding = () -> {};
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(observerBinding);
    observerBinding = () -> {};
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(streamBinding);
    streamBinding = () -> {};
    if (statusBinding != null) {
      statusBinding.remove();
      statusBinding = () -> {};
    }
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.close();
      controller = null;
    }
  }

  private static Button headerAction(String label) {
    Button button = new Button(label);
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-action-button");
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", label);
    return button;
  }

  private void runUi(Runnable action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null || !ui.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    ui.access(action::run);
  }

  private enum ViewMode {
    EVENT,
    TABULAR,
    HYBRID,
    UNSUPPORTED
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;
