public class StitchStreamsProvider {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_EVENT_SUPPORTED = "Supported in Phase 2 event viewer.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_SUPPORTED = "Supported in Phase 3 tabular viewer.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_SUPPORTED = "Supported in Phase 4 hybrid viewer.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_EVENT_ONLY =
      "This stream is EVENT; open it with the event stream viewer.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_ONLY =
      "This stream is TABULAR; open it with the tabular stream viewer.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_ONLY =
      "This stream is HYBRID; open it with the hybrid stream viewer.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_DISABLED = "Stream is disabled.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_GROUP_MISMATCH =
      "Stream group differs from the current session group.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_NO_TOPIC = "Stream topic is not configured.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_NO_CONNECTION = "No stream connection reference configured.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_UNSUPPORTED_TRANSPORT = "Only AMPS streams are supported.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_NO_KEYS =
      "TABULAR stream must define semantic.dataShape.keyFields.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_KEY_MISSING =
      "TABULAR stream key fields must exist in the stream schema.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_SERDE =
      "TABULAR stream viewer currently supports JSON, NVFIX, or BYTES serde.";
  private static final String VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_NO_MESSAGE_TYPE =
      "HYBRID stream must define messageType.";
  private static final String LIVE_EVENT_STATUS = "Planned for Phase 3 (event stream live action).";
  private static final String LIVE_TABULAR_STATUS =
      "Planned for a later phase (tabular stream live action).";
  private static final String LIVE_HYBRID_STATUS =
      "Planned for a later phase (hybrid stream live action).";

  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final String sessionGroup;

  public StitchStreamsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.sessionGroup =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getGroup()),
            "platform");
  }

  public List<StitchStreamsRow> loadRows() {
    Map<String, StreamRef> indexed = indexStreams();
    if (indexed.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchStreamsRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(indexed.size());
    for (StreamRef ref : indexed.values()) {
      rows.add(toRow(ref));
    }
    rows.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(StitchStreamsRow::group, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchStreamsRow::namespace, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchStreamsRow::name, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  public Optional<StitchStreamDetails> loadDetails(String streamId) {
    return resolveRef(streamId).map(this::toDetails);
  }

  public Optional<StreamEventContext> loadEventContext(String streamId) {
    return resolveRef(streamId)
        .map(
            ref -> {
              StreamContextBase base = contextBase(ref);
              return base.toEventContext(resolveEventViewCapability(ref, base.streamClass()));
            });
  }

  public Optional<StreamTabularContext> loadTabularContext(String streamId) {
    return resolveRef(streamId)
        .map(
            ref -> {
              StreamContextBase base = contextBase(ref);
              return base.toTabularContext(resolveTabularViewCapability(ref, base.streamClass()));
            });
  }

  public Optional<StreamHybridContext> loadHybridContext(String streamId) {
    return resolveRef(streamId)
        .map(
            ref -> {
              StreamContextBase base = contextBase(ref);
              return base.toHybridContext(resolveHybridViewCapability(ref, base.streamClass()));
            });
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaultEventPolicy() {
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(StitchRealtimeConflationMode.LATEST_ONLY)
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(200)
        .withMaxBatchSize(32)
        .withMaxQueueSize(1024)
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(30_000)
        .build();
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionScope defaultEventScope(StreamEventContext context) {
    return StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaultTabularPolicy() {
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(StitchRealtimeConflationMode.LATEST_ONLY)
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(200)
        .withMaxBatchSize(16)
        .withMaxQueueSize(512)
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(30_000)
        .build();
  }

  public TabularViewOptions defaultTabularOptions(StreamTabularContext context) {
    return new TabularViewOptions(500);
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionScope defaultTabularScope(StreamTabularContext context) {
    return StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaultHybridPolicy() {
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(StitchRealtimeConflationMode.LATEST_ONLY)
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(200)
        .withMaxBatchSize(24)
        .withMaxQueueSize(1024)
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(30_000)
        .build();
  }

  public TabularViewOptions defaultHybridOptions(StreamHybridContext context) {
    return new TabularViewOptions(500);
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionScope defaultHybridScope(StreamHybridContext context) {
    return StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeSource<StreamEvent> eventSourceFor(StreamEventContext context) {
    StreamEventContext required = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    if (!required.viewSupported()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(required.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream does not support event viewing in this phase."));
    }
    AtomicLong sequence = new AtomicLong(0L);
    return streamBytesSource(
        required.streamId(),
        listener -> listener.onSubscribed(),
        (listener, message) -> {
          try {
            listener.onUpdate(
                StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(
                    toStreamEvent(sequence.incrementAndGet(), required, message)));
          } catch (Throwable error) {
            listener.onError(error, false);
          }
        });
  }

  public StitchRealtimeSource<StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String>>
      tabularSourceFor(StreamTabularContext context, TabularViewOptions options) {
    StreamTabularContext required = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    TabularViewOptions normalized =
        (options == null ? defaultTabularOptions(required) : options).normalized();
    if (!required.viewSupported()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(required.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream does not support tabular viewing in this phase."));
    }
    AtomicLong sequence = new AtomicLong(0L);
    TabularAccumulator accumulator = new TabularAccumulator(normalized.maxRows());
    return streamBytesSource(
        required.streamId(),
        listener -> {
          listener.onSubscribed();
          listener.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.snapshot(StitchLiveTableDelta.snapshot(List.of())));
        },
        (listener, message) -> {
          try {
            List<TabularMutation> mutations = decodeTabularMutations(sequence, required, message);
            if (mutations.isEmpty()) {
              return;
            }
            for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String>> update :
                accumulator.apply(mutations)) {
              listener.onUpdate(update);
            }
          } catch (Throwable error) {
            listener.onError(error, true);
          }
        });
  }

  public StitchRealtimeSource<HybridStreamUpdate> hybridSourceFor(
      StreamHybridContext context, TabularViewOptions options) {
    StreamHybridContext required = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    TabularViewOptions normalized =
        (options == null ? defaultHybridOptions(required) : options).normalized();
    if (!required.viewSupported()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(required.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream does not support hybrid viewing in this phase."));
    }
    StreamEventContext eventContext = asEventContext(required);
    StreamTabularContext tabularContext = asTabularContext(required);
    AtomicLong sequence = new AtomicLong(0L);
    TabularAccumulator accumulator = new TabularAccumulator(normalized.maxRows());
    return streamBytesSource(
        required.streamId(),
        listener -> {
          listener.onSubscribed();
          listener.onUpdate(
              StitchRealtimeUpdate.snapshot(
                  HybridStreamUpdate.snapshot(StitchLiveTableDelta.snapshot(List.of()))));
        },
        (listener, message) -> {
          try {
            StreamEvent event = toStreamEvent(sequence.incrementAndGet(), eventContext, message);
            listener.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(HybridStreamUpdate.event(event)));
            List<TabularMutation> mutations = decodeTabularMutations(sequence, tabularContext, message);
            if (mutations.isEmpty()) {
              return;
            }
            for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String>> update :
                accumulator.apply(mutations)) {
              if (update == null || update.payload() == null) {
                continue;
              }
              listener.onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(HybridStreamUpdate.tabular(update.payload())));
            }
          } catch (Throwable error) {
            listener.onError(error, true);
          }
        });
  }

  private <T> StitchRealtimeSource<T> streamBytesSource(
      String streamId,
      Consumer<StitchRealtimeSource.Listener<T>> onStarted,
      StreamMessageHandler<T> messageHandler) {
    String requiredStreamId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(streamId), "");
    return sink -> {
      Objects.requireNonNull(sink, "listener");
      AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
      AtomicBoolean unsubscribed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
      Stream runtime = null;
      StreamSubscription subscription = null;
      try {
        runtime = session.streams().start(requiredStreamId);
        Stream activeRuntime = runtime;
        if (onStarted != null) {
          onStarted.accept(sink);
        }
        subscription =
            activeRuntime.subscribeBytes(
                message -> {
                  if (closed.get()) {
                    return;
                  }
                  messageHandler.onMessage(sink, message);
                });
      } catch (Exception error) {
        StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(subscription);
        StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(runtime);
        throw error;
      }
      Stream finalRuntime = runtime;
      StreamSubscription finalSubscription = subscription;
      return () -> {
        if (!closed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
          return;
        }
        StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(finalSubscription);
        StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(finalRuntime);
        if (unsubscribed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
          sink.onUnsubscribed();
        }
      };
    };
  }

  public Object payloadDialogValue(StreamEvent event) {
    if (event == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("sequence", event.sequence());
    payload.put("observedAtUtc", event.observedAtUtc());
    payload.put("eventTimeUtc", event.eventTimeUtc());
    payload.put("streamId", event.streamId());
    payload.put("topic", event.topic());
    payload.put("serde", event.serde());
    payload.put("messageType", event.messageType());
    payload.put("summary", event.summary());
    payload.put("headers", event.headers());
    payload.put("payloadPreview", event.payloadPreview());
    payload.put("payloadBytes", event.payload().length);
    payload.put(
        "payloadBase64",
        event.payload().length == 0 ? "" : Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(event.payload()));
    try {
      if ("JSON".equals(event.serde()) && event.payload().length > 0) {
        payload.put("payloadJson", MAPPER.readTree(event.payload()));
      }
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
    }
    return Map.copyOf(payload);
  }

  public Object payloadDialogValue(TabularStreamRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("rowId", row.rowId());
    payload.put("sequence", row.sequence());
    payload.put("observedAtUtc", row.observedAtUtc());
    payload.put("eventTimeUtc", row.eventTimeUtc());
    payload.put("streamId", row.streamId());
    payload.put("topic", row.topic());
    payload.put("operation", row.operation());
    payload.put("headers", row.headers());
    payload.put("values", row.values());
    payload.put("payloadPreview", row.payloadPreview());
    payload.put("payloadBytes", row.payload().length);
    payload.put(
        "payloadBase64",
        row.payload().length == 0 ? "" : Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(row.payload()));
    try {
      if (row.payload().length > 0) {
        payload.put("payloadJson", MAPPER.readTree(row.payload()));
      }
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
    }
    return Map.copyOf(payload);
  }

  private StitchStreamsRow toRow(StreamRef ref) {
    DefinitionStream definition = ref.definition();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    String streamClass = classify(definition);
    ViewCapability view = resolveViewCapability(ref, streamClass);
    return new StitchStreamsRow(
        ref.streamId(),
        isEnabled(definition),
        ref.group(),
        ref.namespace(),
        ref.name(),
        streamClass,
        enumName(definition.transport()),
        enumName(definition.serde()),
        Strings.trimToNull(definition.messageType()),
        schemaRef(definition),
        sourceHint(definition),
        requireDefinitionValue(envelope.lifecycleStatus(), "stream.envelope.lifecycleStatus"),
        requireDefinitionValue(envelope.updatedTimeUtc(), "stream.envelope.updatedTimeUtc"),
        view.supported(),
        view.reason(),
        false,
        liveStatus(streamClass));
  }

  private StitchStreamDetails toDetails(StreamRef ref) {
    DefinitionStream definition = ref.definition();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    String streamClass = classify(definition);
    ViewCapability view = resolveViewCapability(ref, streamClass);
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("enabled", isEnabled(definition) ? "ENABLED" : "DISABLED");
    fields.put("group", ref.group());
    fields.put("namespace", ref.namespace());
    fields.put("name", ref.name());
    fields.put("streamId", ref.streamId());
    fields.put("classification", streamClass);
    fields.put("transport", enumName(definition.transport()));
    fields.put("serde", enumName(definition.serde()));
    fields.put("messageType", Strings.trimToNull(definition.messageType()));
    fields.put("schemaRef", schemaRef(definition));
    fields.put("sourceHint", sourceHint(definition));
    fields.put("lifecycle", requireDefinitionValue(envelope.lifecycleStatus(), "stream.envelope.lifecycleStatus"));
    fields.put("updatedUtc", requireDefinitionValue(envelope.updatedTimeUtc(), "stream.envelope.updatedTimeUtc"));
    fields.put("createdUtc", requireDefinitionValue(envelope.createdTimeUtc(), "stream.envelope.createdTimeUtc"));
    fields.put("connectionRefs", summarizeRefs(definition.connectionRefs()));
    fields.put("dependencyRefs", summarizeRefs(definition.dependencyRefs()));
    fields.put("viewStatus", view.reason());
    fields.put("liveStatus", liveStatus(streamClass));
    return new StitchStreamDetails(
        ref.streamId(), ref.group(), ref.namespace(), ref.name(), fields, definition);
  }

  private Map<String, StreamRef> indexStreams() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, StreamRef> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<DefinitionStream> streams = cache.list(DefinitionStream.class);
    if (streams == null || streams.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    for (DefinitionStream definition : streams) {
      StreamRef ref = toStreamRef(definition);
      String key = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.indexKey(ref.streamId());
      StreamRef current = indexed.get(key);
      if (current == null || ref.recencyEpochMs() > current.recencyEpochMs()) {
        indexed.put(key, ref);
      }
    }
    return indexed.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(indexed);
  }

  private Optional<StreamRef> resolveRef(String streamId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(streamId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.ofNullable(indexStreams().get(StitchStreamPayloadSupport.indexKey(normalized)));
  }

  private static StreamContextBase contextBase(StreamRef ref) {
    StreamRef requiredRef = Objects.requireNonNull(ref, "ref");
    DefinitionStream definition = Objects.requireNonNull(requiredRef.definition(), "ref.definition");
    return new StreamContextBase(
        requiredRef.streamId(),
        requiredRef.group(),
        requiredRef.namespace(),
        requiredRef.name(),
        classify(definition),
        enumName(definition.transport()),
        enumName(definition.serde()),
        Strings.trimToNull(definition.messageType()),
        requireTopic(definition),
        sourceHint(definition),
        requireConnectionRef(definition),
        schemaColumns(definition),
        keyFields(definition));
  }

  private static StreamRef toStreamRef(DefinitionStream definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    String group = requireDefinitionValue(envelope.group(), "stream.envelope.group");
    String namespace = requireDefinitionValue(definition.namespace(), "stream.namespace");
    String name = requireDefinitionValue(envelope.name(), "stream.envelope.name");
    String streamId = requireDefinitionValue(definition.streamId(), "stream.streamId");
    return new StreamRef(
        streamId, group, namespace, name, definition, StitchStreamPayloadSupport.recencyEpoch(envelope));
  }

    return StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.liveStatus(
        streamClass, LIVE_EVENT_STATUS, LIVE_TABULAR_STATUS, LIVE_HYBRID_STATUS);

  private ViewCapability resolveViewCapability(StreamRef ref, String streamClass) {
    return switch (streamClass) {
      case "EVENT" -> resolveEventViewCapability(ref, streamClass);
      case "TABULAR" -> resolveTabularViewCapability(ref, streamClass);
      case "HYBRID" -> resolveHybridViewCapability(ref, streamClass);
      default -> new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_EVENT_ONLY);
    };
  }

  private ViewCapability resolveEventViewCapability(StreamRef ref, String streamClass) {
    String common = validateCommonViewSupport(ref);
    if (common != null) {
      return new ViewCapability(false, common);
    }
    if (!"EVENT".equals(streamClass)) {
      if ("HYBRID".equals(streamClass)) {
        return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_ONLY);
      }
      return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_ONLY);
    }
    return new ViewCapability(true, VIEW_STATUS_EVENT_SUPPORTED);
  }

  private ViewCapability resolveTabularViewCapability(StreamRef ref, String streamClass) {
    String common = validateCommonViewSupport(ref);
    if (common != null) {
      return new ViewCapability(false, common);
    }
    DefinitionStream definition = ref == null ? null : ref.definition();
    if (!"TABULAR".equals(streamClass)) {
      if ("HYBRID".equals(streamClass)) {
        return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_ONLY);
      }
      return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_EVENT_ONLY);
    }
    String tabularValidation = validateTabularStructure(definition);
    if (tabularValidation != null) {
      return new ViewCapability(false, tabularValidation);
    }
    return new ViewCapability(true, VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_SUPPORTED);
  }

  private ViewCapability resolveHybridViewCapability(StreamRef ref, String streamClass) {
    String common = validateCommonViewSupport(ref);
    if (common != null) {
      return new ViewCapability(false, common);
    }
    DefinitionStream definition = ref == null ? null : ref.definition();
    if (!"HYBRID".equals(streamClass)) {
      if ("EVENT".equals(streamClass)) {
        return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_EVENT_ONLY);
      }
      return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_ONLY);
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(definition == null ? null : definition.messageType()) == null) {
      return new ViewCapability(false, VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_NO_MESSAGE_TYPE);
    }
    String tabularValidation = validateTabularStructure(definition);
    if (tabularValidation != null) {
      return new ViewCapability(false, tabularValidation);
    }
    return new ViewCapability(true, VIEW_STATUS_HYBRID_SUPPORTED);
  }

  private static String validateTabularStructure(DefinitionStream definition) {
    return StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.validateTabularStructure(
        definition,
        VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_SERDE,
        VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_NO_KEYS,
        VIEW_STATUS_TABULAR_KEY_MISSING);
  }

  private String validateCommonViewSupport(StreamRef ref) {
    StreamRef requiredRef = Objects.requireNonNull(ref, "ref");
    DefinitionStream definition = Objects.requireNonNull(requiredRef.definition(), "ref.definition");
    if (!isEnabled(definition)) {
      return VIEW_STATUS_DISABLED;
    }
    if (!sessionGroup.equals(requiredRef.group())) {
      return VIEW_STATUS_GROUP_MISMATCH + " Current session group: " + sessionGroup + ".";
    }
    if (definition.transport() != DefinitionStream.TransportType.AMPS) {
      return VIEW_STATUS_UNSUPPORTED_TRANSPORT;
    }
    requireTopic(definition);
    requireConnectionRef(definition);
    return null;
  }

    return StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.isTabularSerdeSupported(definition);
  }

    return StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.schemaContainsAllKeys(definition, keys);
  }

    return StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.primaryConnectionRef(definition);
  }

  private StreamEvent toStreamEvent(long sequence, StreamEventContext context, StreamMessage message) {
    byte[] payload = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.cloneBytes(message == null ? null : message.payload());
    String preview = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.payloadPreview(payload);
    return new StreamEvent(
        Math.max(0L, sequence),
        Instant.now(),
        StitchStreamPayloadSupport.toInstant(message == null ? 0L : message.timestampEpochMillis()),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(message == null ? null : message.streamId()), context.streamId()),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(message == null ? null : message.topic()), context.topic(), "-"),
        context.serde(),
        context.messageType(),
        StitchStreamPayloadSupport.truncate(preview, 120),
        preview,
        StitchStreamPayloadSupport.headersAsText(message == null ? null : message.headers()),
        payload);
  }

  private List<TabularMutation> decodeTabularMutations(
      AtomicLong sequence, StreamTabularContext context, StreamMessage message) {
    if (context == null || message == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, String> headers = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.headersAsText(message.headers());
    String headerOp = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.operationFromHeaders(headers);
    String streamId =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(message.streamId()), Strings.trimToNull(context.streamId()), "-");
    String topic =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(message.topic()), Strings.trimToNull(context.topic()), "-");
    Instant observedAt = Instant.now();
    Instant eventAt = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.toInstant(message.timestampEpochMillis());
    byte[] payload = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.cloneBytes(message.payload());
    List<Map<String, Object>> rawRows =
        StitchStreamPayloadSupport.decodePayloadRows(payload, context.serde());
    if (rawRows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<TabularMutation> mutations = new ArrayList<>(rawRows.size());
    for (Map<String, Object> raw : rawRows) {
      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> projected =
          StitchStreamPayloadSupport.projectTabularValues(context, raw);
      if (projected.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      String op =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              StitchStreamPayloadSupport.operationFromValues(projected), headerOp, "upsert");
      StitchStreamPayloadSupport.removeOperationFields(projected);
      String rowId = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.rowIdFor(context.keyFields(), projected);
      if (rowId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (StitchStreamPayloadSupport.isRemoveOperation(op)) {
        mutations.add(TabularMutation.remove(rowId));
        continue;
      }
      TabularStreamRow row =
          new TabularStreamRow(
              rowId,
              sequence.incrementAndGet(),
              observedAt,
              eventAt,
              streamId,
              topic,
              op.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT),
              headers,
              StitchStreamPayloadSupport.payloadPreview(payload),
              payload,
              projected);
      mutations.add(TabularMutation.upsert(row));
    }
    return mutations.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(mutations);
  }

  private static String enumName(Enum<?> value) {
    return StitchStreamDefinitionSupport.enumName(value);
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope requireEnvelope(DefinitionStream definition) {
    DefinitionStream required = Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = required.envelope();
    if (envelope == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("stream.envelope is required");
    }
    return envelope;
  }

  private static String requireDefinitionValue(String value, String field) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(value, field);
  }

  private static String requireTopic(DefinitionStream definition) {
    DefinitionStream required = Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    if (required.address() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("stream.address is required");
    }
    return requireDefinitionValue(required.address().topic(), "stream.address.topic");
  }

  private static String requireConnectionRef(DefinitionStream definition) {
    String connectionRef = primaryConnectionRef(Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition"));
    return requireDefinitionValue(connectionRef, "stream.connectionRefs[0]");
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    return session.internal().discoveryCache();
  }

  private record StreamContextBase(
      String streamId,
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String name,
      String streamClass,
      String transport,
      String serde,
      String messageType,
      String topic,
      String sourceHint,
      String connectionRef,
      List<String> schemaColumns,
      List<String> keyFields) {
    private StreamContextBase {
      schemaColumns = schemaColumns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(schemaColumns);
      keyFields = keyFields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(keyFields);
    }

    private StreamEventContext toEventContext(ViewCapability view) {
      return new StreamEventContext(
          streamId,
          group,
          namespace,
          name,
          streamClass,
          transport,
          serde,
          messageType,
          topic,
          sourceHint,
          connectionRef,
          view != null && view.supported(),
          view == null ? "" : view.reason());
    }

    private StreamTabularContext toTabularContext(ViewCapability view) {
      return new StreamTabularContext(
          streamId,
          group,
          namespace,
          name,
          streamClass,
          transport,
          serde,
          messageType,
          topic,
          sourceHint,
          connectionRef,
          schemaColumns,
          keyFields,
          view != null && view.supported(),
          view == null ? "" : view.reason());
    }

    private StreamHybridContext toHybridContext(ViewCapability view) {
      return new StreamHybridContext(
          streamId,
          group,
          namespace,
          name,
          streamClass,
          transport,
          serde,
          messageType,
          topic,
          sourceHint,
          connectionRef,
          schemaColumns,
          keyFields,
          view != null && view.supported(),
          view == null ? "" : view.reason());
    }
  }

      long sequence,

      Instant eventTimeUtc,
      String streamId,
      String topic,
      String serde,
      String messageType,
      String summary,
      String payloadPreview,
      Map<String, String> headers,
      byte[] payload) {
    public StreamEvent {
      observedAtUtc = observedAtUtc == null ? Instant.now() : observedAtUtc;
      eventTimeUtc = eventTimeUtc == null ? observedAtUtc : eventTimeUtc;
      streamId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(streamId), "-");
      topic = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(topic), "-");
      serde = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(serde), "UNKNOWN");
      messageType = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(messageType), "-");
      summary = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(summary), "-");
      payloadPreview = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadPreview), "-");
      headers = headers == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(headers));
      payload = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.cloneBytes(payload);
    }

    public boolean hasPayload() {
      return payload != null && payload.length > 0;
    }
  }

  public record TabularStreamRow(
      String rowId,
      long sequence,
      Instant observedAtUtc,
      Instant eventTimeUtc,
      String streamId,
      String topic,
      String operation,
      Map<String, String> headers,
      String payloadPreview,
      byte[] payload,
      Map<String, Object> values) {
    public TabularStreamRow {
      rowId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rowId), "row");
      observedAtUtc = observedAtUtc == null ? Instant.now() : observedAtUtc;
      eventTimeUtc = eventTimeUtc == null ? observedAtUtc : eventTimeUtc;
      streamId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(streamId), "-");
      topic = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(topic), "-");
      operation = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(operation), "UPSERT");
      headers = headers == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(headers));
      payloadPreview = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadPreview), "-");
      payload = StitchStreamPayloadSupport.cloneBytes(payload);
      values = values == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(values));
    }

    public boolean hasPayload() {
      return payload != null && payload.length > 0;
    }
  }

  public record HybridStreamUpdate(
      StreamEvent event, StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String> tabularDelta) {
    public static HybridStreamUpdate snapshot(
        StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String> tabularSnapshot) {
      return new HybridStreamUpdate(null, tabularSnapshot);
    }

    public static HybridStreamUpdate event(StreamEvent value) {
      return new HybridStreamUpdate(value, null);
    }

    public static HybridStreamUpdate tabular(
        StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String> value) {
      return new HybridStreamUpdate(null, value);
    }
  }

  private record TabularMutation(String rowId, TabularStreamRow row, boolean remove) {
    private static TabularMutation remove(String rowId) {
      return new TabularMutation(rowId, null, true);
    }

    private static TabularMutation upsert(TabularStreamRow row) {
      return new TabularMutation(row == null ? null : row.rowId(), row, false);
    }
  }

  private static final class TabularAccumulator {
    private final int maxRows;
    private final LinkedHashMap<String, TabularStreamRow> rows =
        new LinkedHashMap<>(128, 0.75f, true);

    private TabularAccumulator(int maxRows) {
      this.maxRows = Math.max(50, maxRows);
    }

    private List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String>>> apply(
        List<TabularMutation> mutations) {
      if (mutations == null || mutations.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<TabularStreamRow> upserts = new ArrayList<>();
      List<String> removals = new ArrayList<>();
      Map<String, List<String>> changedCells = new LinkedHashMap<>();

      for (TabularMutation mutation : mutations) {
        if (mutation == null || Strings.trimToNull(mutation.rowId()) == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String rowId = mutation.rowId();
        if (mutation.remove()) {
          if (rows.remove(rowId) != null) {
            removals.add(rowId);
          }
          continue;
        }
        TabularStreamRow next = mutation.row();
        if (next == null) {
          continue;
        }
        TabularStreamRow previous = rows.get(rowId);
        if (previous != null && Objects.equals(previous.values(), next.values())) {
          continue;
        }
        rows.put(rowId, next);
        upserts.add(next);
        changedCells.put(rowId, changedColumns(previous, next));
      }

      while (rows.size() > maxRows) {
        Iterator<Map.Entry<String, TabularStreamRow>> it = rows.entrySet().iterator();
        if (!it.hasNext()) {
          break;
        }
        Map.Entry<String, TabularStreamRow> oldest = it.next();
        removals.add(oldest.getKey());
        it.remove();
      }

      List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<TabularStreamRow, String>>> updates =
          new ArrayList<>(2);
      if (!upserts.isEmpty()) {
        updates.add(
            StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(
                new StitchLiveTableDelta<>(StitchLiveTableDelta.Type.UPSERT, upserts, List.of(), changedCells)));
      }
      if (!removals.isEmpty()) {
        updates.add(StitchRealtimeUpdate.delta(StitchLiveTableDelta.remove(removals)));
      }
      return updates;
    }

    private static List<String> changedColumns(TabularStreamRow previous, TabularStreamRow next) {
      if (next == null || next.values().isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      if (previous == null || previous.values().isEmpty()) {
        return List.copyOf(next.values().keySet());
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> changed = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      LinkedHashSet<String> keys = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      keys.addAll(previous.values().keySet());
      keys.addAll(next.values().keySet());
      for (String key : keys) {
        if (!Objects.equals(previous.values().get(key), next.values().get(key))) {
          changed.add(key);
        }
      }
      return changed.isEmpty() ? List.copyOf(next.values().keySet()) : List.copyOf(changed);
    }
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  private interface StreamMessageHandler<T> {
    void onMessage(StitchRealtimeSource.Listener<T> sink, StreamMessage message);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

public record StitchStreamsRow(
    String id,
    boolean enabled,
    String group,
    String namespace,
    String name,
    String streamClass,
    String transport,
    String serde,
    String messageType,
    String schemaRef,
    String sourceHint,
    String lifecycle,
    String updatedUtc,
    boolean viewSupported,
    String viewUnavailableReason,
    boolean liveSupported,
    String liveUnavailableReason) {

  public StitchStreamsRow {
    id = normalize(id);
    group = normalize(group);
    namespace = normalize(namespace);
    name = normalize(name);
    streamClass = normalize(streamClass);
    transport = normalize(transport);
    serde = normalize(serde);
    messageType = normalize(messageType);
    schemaRef = normalize(schemaRef);
    sourceHint = normalize(sourceHint);
    lifecycle = normalize(lifecycle);
    updatedUtc = normalize(updatedUtc);
    viewUnavailableReason = normalize(viewUnavailableReason);
    liveUnavailableReason = normalize(liveUnavailableReason);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}

public class StitchStreamsScreen extends StitchGroupedResultsPage<StitchStreamsRow> {
  private final StitchStreamsProvider provider;
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry;
  private final ComboBox<String> namespaceFilter = new ComboBox<>();
  private final TextField streamNameFilter = new TextField();

  public StitchStreamsScreen(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchStreamsScreenConfig config,
      StitchStreamsProvider provider,
      StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    super(
        runtimeContext,
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(config.pageSubtitle(), ""),
        "Search streams",
        "Streams search");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.realtimeRegistry = Objects.requireNonNull(realtimeRegistry, "realtimeRegistry");

    configureFilters();
    resultsView().setPageSize(25);
    resultsView().grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Stream results grid");
    initializeResultsScreen(
        "No streams", "No matching stream definitions were found.", "Refresh stream rows");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureFiltersBar(
      StitchFiltersBar filtersBar,
      StitchGroupFilter groupFilter,
      StitchResultsSearch searchField,
      com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button refreshAction) {
    filtersBar
        .withGroupSelector(groupFilter)
        .withFilter(namespaceFilter)
        .withFilter(streamNameFilter)
        .withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchStreamsRow> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Enabled", this::enabledToggle)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.ENABLED)
            .key("enabled")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("7.8rem")
            .resizable(false)
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.group("Group", StitchStreamsRow::group)
            .key("group")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("10.5rem")
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Namespace", StitchStreamsRow::namespace)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("namespace")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("11rem")
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.name("Name", StitchStreamsRow::name)
            .key("name")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("14rem")
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Mode", this::modeBadge)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.STATUS)
            .key("mode")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("8.6rem")
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Source", this::sourceBadge)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("source")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("8.6rem")
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Schema", StitchStreamsRow::schemaRef)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("schemaRef")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("12rem")
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Summary", this::summaryText).kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP).key("summary"));

    if (grid.getColumnByKey("streams-actions") == null) {
      StitchRowActions<StitchStreamsRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
      rowActions.addAction(
          StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.PLAY, "Open", this::openStreamDialog)
              .enabledWhen(row -> row != null && row.viewSupported()));
      rowActions.addAction(StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.CODE, "JSON", this::openJson));
      rowActions.addColumn(grid).setKey("streams-actions");
    }
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchStreamsRow> loadRows() {
    return provider.loadRows();
  }

  @Override
  protected Comparator<StitchStreamsRow> rowComparator() {
    return Comparator.comparing(StitchStreamsRow::group, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(StitchStreamsRow::namespace, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(StitchStreamsRow::name, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
  }

  @Override
  protected String groupValue(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    return row == null ? null : row.group();
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesAdditionalFilters(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String namespace = normalize(namespaceFilter.getValue());
    String streamName = normalize(streamNameFilter.getValue());
    if (!namespace.isBlank() && !normalize(row.namespace()).equals(namespace)) {
      return false;
    }
    return streamName.isBlank() || normalize(row.name()).contains(streamName);
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesSearch(StitchStreamsRow row, String query) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return contains(row.group(), query)
        || contains(row.namespace(), query)
        || contains(row.name(), query)
        || contains(row.schemaRef(), query)
        || contains(row.transport(), query)
        || contains(row.sourceHint(), query)
        || contains(row.messageType(), query)
        || contains(row.lifecycle(), query)
        || contains(modeLabel(row), query);
  }

  @Override
  protected void onRowsRefreshed(List<StitchStreamsRow> rows) {
    refreshNamespaceFilter(rows);
  }

  private void configureFilters() {
    namespaceFilter.setLabel("");
    namespaceFilter.setPlaceholder("Namespace");
    namespaceFilter.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    namespaceFilter.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    namespaceFilter.setWidth("15rem");
    namespaceFilter.addClassName("stitch-streams-namespace-filter");
    namespaceFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Stream namespace filter");
    namespaceFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyCurrentFilters());

    streamNameFilter.setLabel("");
    streamNameFilter.setPlaceholder("Stream name");
    streamNameFilter.setWidth("16rem");
    streamNameFilter.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    streamNameFilter.setValueChangeMode(ValueChangeMode.EAGER);
    streamNameFilter.addClassName("stitch-streams-name-filter");
    streamNameFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Stream name filter");
    streamNameFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyCurrentFilters());
  }

  private void refreshNamespaceFilter(List<StitchStreamsRow> rows) {
    String selected = Strings.trimToNull(namespaceFilter.getValue());
    LinkedHashSet<String> namespaces = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (rows != null) {
      for (StitchStreamsRow row : rows) {
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(row.namespace());
        if (value != null) {
          namespaces.add(value);
        }
      }
    }
    namespaceFilter.setItems(namespaces.stream().sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER).toList());
    if (selected != null && namespaces.contains(selected)) {
      namespaceFilter.setValue(selected);
    } else if (selected != null) {
      namespaceFilter.clear();
    }
  }

  private void openStreamDialog(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!row.viewSupported()) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Open Not Available",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(row.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream cannot be opened for live viewing."));
      return;
    }
    new StitchStreamsLiveDialog(provider, realtimeRegistry, row).open();
  }

  private void openJson(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }
    provider
        .loadDetails(row.id())
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            details ->
                new StitchJsonDialog(
                        "Stream JSON - "
                            + Strings.firstNonBlank(
                                Strings.trimToNull(row.group()) + "/" + Strings.trimToNull(row.name()),
                                "Stream"),
                        details.sourceObject() == null ? details : details.sourceObject())
                    .open(),
            () -> new StitchJsonDialog("Stream JSON - " + row.name(), row).open());
  }

  private StitchBooleanToggle enabledToggle(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    boolean enabled = row != null && row.enabled();
    StitchBooleanToggle toggle = new StitchBooleanToggle("Enabled", enabled);
    toggle.setLabel("");
    toggle.setReadOnly(true);
    toggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled");
    return toggle;
  }

  private StitchStatusBadge modeBadge(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    String mode = modeLabel(row);
    StitchStatusBadge.Tone tone =
        switch (mode) {
          case "STREAM" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.INFO;
          case "SNAPSHOT" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL;
          case "HYBRID" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.WARNING;
          default -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL;
        };
    return new StitchStatusBadge(mode, tone);
  }

  private StitchStatusBadge sourceBadge(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    String source = Strings.firstNonBlank(row == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(row.transport()), "-");
    StitchStatusBadge.Tone tone =
        switch (source.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
          case "AMPS" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.INFO;
          case "KAFKA" -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.WARNING;
          default -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL;
        };
    return new StitchStatusBadge(source, tone);
  }

  private String summaryText(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    if (row == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    List<String> tokens = new ArrayList<>();
    String sourceHint = Strings.trimToNull(row.sourceHint());
    if (sourceHint != null) {
      tokens.add(sourceHint);
    }
    String messageType = Strings.trimToNull(row.messageType());
    if (messageType != null) {
      tokens.add("Type: " + messageType);
    }
    String lifecycle = Strings.trimToNull(row.lifecycle());
    if (lifecycle != null) {
      tokens.add("State: " + lifecycle);
    }
    return tokens.isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(" | ", tokens);
  }

  static String modeLabel(StitchStreamsRow row) {
    String streamClass = normalizeToken(row == null ? null : row.streamClass()).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (streamClass) {
      case "EVENT" -> "STREAM";
      case "TABULAR" -> "SNAPSHOT";
      case "HYBRID" -> "HYBRID";
      default -> streamClass.isBlank() ? "-" : streamClass;
    };
  }

  private static String normalizeToken(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamsScreenConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

public final class StitchStreamsScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchStreamsScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "Streams";
      this.routePath = "data/streams";
      this.pageTitle = "Data - Streams";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Browse stream definitions and inspect stream metadata.";
      this.order = 30;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchStreamsScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchStreamsScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

@Route(value = "data/streams", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStreamsView extends StitchStreamsScreen {
  public StitchStreamsView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchStreamsProvider provider,
      StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    super(runtimeContext, requireConfig(stitch), provider, realtimeRegistry);
  }

  private static StitchStreamsScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::streams)
        .filter(StitchStreamsScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/data/StitchStreamTabularViewScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.DetachEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableDelta;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableHighlightMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchLiveTableShell;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeConflationMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

@Route(value = StitchStreamTabularViewScreen.ROUTE_PATH, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStreamTabularViewScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeEnterObserver {
  public static final String ROUTE_PATH = "data/streams/view/tabular";
  public static final String QUERY_PARAM_STREAM_ID = "streamId";

  private static final List<Integer> MAX_ROWS = List.of(200, 500, 1000, 2000);
  private static final List<Integer> DISPATCH_MS = List.of(50, 100, 200, 500);
  private static final List<Integer> FLASH_SECONDS = List.of(1, 2, 5, 10);

  private final StitchStreamsProvider provider;
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry;
  private final StitchSection contextSection = new StitchSection("Stream Context");
  private final StitchSection controlsSection = new StitchSection("Tabular View Controls");
  private final FormLayout contextForm = new FormLayout();
  private final FormLayout controlsForm = new FormLayout();
  private final Span changeSummary = new Span("Changed rows: 0 | changed cells: 0");
  private final StitchLiveTableShell<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String> liveTable =
      new StitchLiveTableShell<>();
  private final Select<Integer> maxRows =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Max Rows", "Maximum tabular stream rows", MAX_ROWS, String::valueOf);
  private final Select<StitchRealtimeConflationMode> conflationMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Conflation",
          "Realtime conflation mode",
          StitchRealtimeConflationMode.values(),
          StitchRealtimeConflationMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> dispatchIntervalMs =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Dispatch ms",
          "Realtime dispatch interval milliseconds",
          DISPATCH_MS,
          String::valueOf);
  private final Select<StitchLiveTableHighlightMode> highlightMode =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Highlight",
          "Live table highlight mode",
          StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.values(),
          StitchLiveTableHighlightMode::name);
  private final Select<Integer> flashWindowSeconds =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.select(
          "Flash Seconds",
          "Temporary highlight duration seconds",
          FLASH_SECONDS,
          String::valueOf);
  private final Button applyControls =
      StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton(
          "APPLY", "Apply tabular stream control changes");

  private StitchStreamsProvider.StreamTabularContext context;
  private StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<
          StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String>>
      controller;
  private AutoCloseable controllerBinding = () -> {};
  private AutoCloseable registryBinding = () -> {};

  public StitchStreamTabularViewScreen(
      Stitch stitch, StitchStreamsProvider provider, StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry realtimeRegistry) {
    super(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.requireConfig(stitch).pageTitle() + " - View",
        "Realtime tabular-stream viewer");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.realtimeRegistry = Objects.requireNonNull(realtimeRegistry, "realtimeRegistry");
    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    configureContextSection();
    configureControlsSection();
    configureLiveTable();
    configurePageActions();

    addToBody(contextSection, controlsSection, liveTable);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, liveTable);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String streamId = StitchStreamViewSupport.queryParam(event, QUERY_PARAM_STREAM_ID);
    if (streamId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Stream Not Selected", "Open this screen from Data -> Streams using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    loadStream(streamId, true);
  }

  @Override
  protected void onDetach(DetachEvent detachEvent) {
    closeController();
    super.onDetach(detachEvent);
  }

  private void configureContextSection() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureContextForm(contextForm);
    contextSection.addToBody(contextForm);
  }

  private void configureControlsSection() {
    highlightMode.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          liveTable.setHighlightMode(event.getValue());
          liveTable.clearHighlights();
          liveTable.refreshGrid();
          updateChangeSummary();
        });
    flashWindowSeconds.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          Integer seconds = event.getValue();
          if (seconds != null) {
            liveTable.setFlashWindow(Duration.ofSeconds(seconds));
          }
        });

    applyControls.addClickListener(event -> applyControlChanges());
    controlsForm.setWidthFull();
    controlsForm.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("36em", 2),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("60em", 5));
    controlsForm.add(maxRows, conflationMode, dispatchIntervalMs, highlightMode, flashWindowSeconds);
    controlsSection.addToBody(controlsForm, new HorizontalLayout(applyControls), changeSummary);
  }

  private void configureLiveTable() {
    liveTable.withRowIdResolver(StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow::rowId);
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureLiveTableShell(
        liveTable,
        "No live rows",
        "Start the subscription to receive updates.",
        "Live tabular stream grid",
        true,
        true,
        () -> {
          liveTable.clearHighlights();
          liveTable.refreshGrid();
          updateChangeSummary();
        });
    configureGridColumns();
  }

  private void configurePageActions() {
    Button refresh =
        StitchStreamViewSupport.primaryButton("REFRESH", "Refresh tabular stream viewer");
    refresh.addClickListener(
        event ->
            loadStream(
                streamId(),
                controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state())));
    addPageAction(refresh);
  }

  private void loadStream(String requestedStreamId, boolean autoStart) {
    String streamId = Strings.trimToNull(requestedStreamId);
    if (streamId == null) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Stream Not Selected", "Open this screen from Data -> Streams using the View action.");
      return;
    }
    StitchStreamsProvider.StreamTabularContext loaded = provider.loadTabularContext(streamId).orElse(null);
    if (loaded == null) {
      applyEmptyState("Stream Not Found", "The requested stream could not be resolved.");
      return;
    }
    context = loaded;
    syncControlDefaults();
    updateContextForm();
    if (!loaded.viewSupported()) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "View Not Available",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(loaded.viewUnavailableReason()),
              "This stream does not support tabular viewing in this phase."));
      return;
    }
    bindController(autoStart);
  }

  private void applyControlChanges() {
    boolean wasActive =
        controller != null && StitchStreamViewSupport.isActive(controller.state());
    bindController(wasActive);
  }

  private void bindController(boolean autoStart) {
    if (context == null || !context.viewSupported()) {
      return;
    }
    closeController();
    liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
    configureGridColumns();
    try {
      controller =
          new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<>(
              provider.tabularSourceFor(context, optionsFromControls()),
              policyFromControls(),
              provider.defaultTabularScope(context),
              getUI().orElse(null));
      controllerBinding = liveTable.bindController(controller, this::onLiveUpdates);
      registryBinding =
          realtimeRegistry.register(
              "Data Streams Tabular View",
              context.group() + " / " + context.namespace() + " / " + context.name(),
              controller,
              getUI().orElse(null));
      liveTable.statusBar().setMessage("");
      if (autoStart) {
        controller.start();
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      applyEmptyState(
          "Tabular Viewer Setup Failed",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Tabular stream setup failed."));
    }
  }

  private void closeController() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(registryBinding);
    registryBinding = () -> {};
    StitchStreamViewSupport.safeClose(controllerBinding);
    controllerBinding = () -> {};
    if (controller != null) {
      controller.close();
      controller = null;
    }
  }

  private void onLiveUpdates(
      List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String>>>
          updates) {
    liveTable.pruneTransientHighlights();
    liveTable.refreshGrid();
    updateChangeSummary();
  }

  private void configureGridColumns() {
    List<String> dataColumns = context == null ? List.of() : context.schemaColumns();
    StitchStreamViewSupport.configureStreamTabularColumns(
        liveTable, dataColumns, "Event", "Observed", Instant::toString);
  }

  private void updateContextForm() {
    if (context == null) {
      StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, Map.of());
      return;
    }
    Map<String, String> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("Group", context.group());
    fields.put("Namespace", context.namespace());
    fields.put("Name", context.name());
    fields.put("Class", context.streamClass());
    fields.put("Transport", context.transport());
    fields.put("Serde", context.serde());
    fields.put("Message Type", context.messageType());
    fields.put("Topic", context.topic());
    fields.put("Connection", context.connectionRef());
    fields.put(
        "Key Fields",
        context.keyFields().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(", ", context.keyFields()));
    fields.put(
        "Schema Columns",
        context.schemaColumns().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.valueOf(context.schemaColumns().size()));
    fields.put("Source", context.sourceHint());
    StitchStreamViewSupport.setContextFields(contextForm, fields);
    setPageSubtitle(
        context.group()
            + "/"
            + context.namespace()
            + "/"
            + context.name()
            + " - Realtime tabular stream viewer");
  }

  private void applyEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    closeController();
    liveTable.applySnapshot(List.of());
    configureGridColumns();
    liveTable.clearHighlights();
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmptyState(title, Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    liveTable.resultsView().setItems(List.of());
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmpty(true);
    liveTable.statusBar().setMessage(Strings.firstNonBlank(message, ""));
    updateChangeSummary();
  }

  private StitchStreamsProvider.TabularViewOptions optionsFromControls() {
    return new StitchStreamsProvider.TabularViewOptions(
        StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(maxRows.getValue(), 500));
  }

  private StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyFromControls() {
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaults = provider.defaultTabularPolicy();
    return StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.builder()
        .withConflationMode(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                conflationMode.getValue(), defaults.conflationMode()))
        .withDispatchIntervalMillis(
            StitchStreamViewSupport.defaultValue(
                dispatchIntervalMs.getValue(), defaults.dispatchIntervalMillis()))
        .withMaxBatchSize(defaults.maxBatchSize())
        .withMaxQueueSize(defaults.maxQueueSize())
        .withStaleTimeoutMillis(defaults.staleTimeoutMillis())
        .build();
  }

  private void syncControlDefaults() {
    if (context == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchStreamsProvider.TabularViewOptions defaults = provider.defaultTabularOptions(context);
    StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policyDefaults = provider.defaultTabularPolicy();
    maxRows.setValue(defaults.maxRows());
    conflationMode.setValue(policyDefaults.conflationMode());
    dispatchIntervalMs.setValue(policyDefaults.dispatchIntervalMillis());
    highlightMode.setValue(StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT);
    flashWindowSeconds.setValue(2);
  }

  private void updateChangeSummary() {
    StitchStreamViewSupport.updateChangeSummary(changeSummary, liveTable);
    int changedRows = liveTable.changedRowsCount();
    int changedCells = liveTable.changedCellsCount();
    liveTable.controls().clearEnabled(changedRows > 0 || changedCells > 0);
  }

  private String streamId() {
    return context == null ? null : context.streamId();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchEventLogShell;
