final class StitchStreamViewSupport {
  private static final DateTimeFormatter UTC_SECONDS =
      DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss").withZone(ZoneOffset.UTC);

  private StitchStreamViewSupport() {}

  static StitchStreamsScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::streams)
        .filter(StitchStreamsScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  static String queryParam(BeforeEnterEvent event, String key) {
    if (event == null || Strings.trimToNull(key) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<String> values = event.getLocation().getQueryParameters().getParameters().get(key);
    return values == null || values.isEmpty() ? null : Strings.trimToNull(values.get(0));
  }

  static Button primaryButton(String text, String ariaLabel) {
    Button button = new Button(text);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(button);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    return button;
  }

  static <T> Select<T> select(String label, String ariaLabel, T[] items, Function<T, String> labelProvider) {
    return select(label, ariaLabel, List.of(items), labelProvider);
  }

  static <T> Select<T> select(
      String label, String ariaLabel, List<T> items, Function<T, String> labelProvider) {
    Select<T> select = new Select<>();
    select(label, ariaLabel, items, labelProvider, select);
    return select;
  }

  static <T> void select(
      String label,
      String ariaLabel,
      List<T> items,
      Function<T, String> labelProvider,
      Select<T> select) {
    select.setLabel(label);
    select.setItems(items);
    if (labelProvider != null) {
      select.setItemLabelGenerator(value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(labelProvider.apply(value), ""));
    }
    select.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
  }

  static void configureContextForm(FormLayout form) {
    form.setWidthFull();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("48em", 2));
  }

  static void setContextFields(FormLayout form, Map<String, String> fields) {
    form.removeAll();
    if (fields == null || fields.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    fields.forEach((label, value) -> addContextValue(form, label, value));
  }

  static void configureEventLogShell(
      StitchEventLogShell<?> eventLog,
      String emptyTitle,
      String emptyMessage,
      String gridAriaLabel,
      boolean showStatusBar,
      boolean showControls) {
    eventLog.setSizeFull();
    eventLog.statusBar().setVisible(showStatusBar);
    eventLog.controls().setVisible(showControls);
    eventLog.resultsView().setEmptyState(emptyTitle, emptyMessage);
    eventLog.resultsView().grid().setSelectionMode(Grid.SelectionMode.NONE);
    eventLog.resultsView().grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", gridAriaLabel);
  }

  static void configureStreamEventColumns(
      StitchEventLogShell<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> eventLog) {
    addEventColumn(
        eventLog,
        "Observed (UTC)",
        "observedUtc",
        StitchGridColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP,
        event -> formatUtc(event == null ? null : event.observedAtUtc()));
    addEventColumn(
        eventLog,
        "Event (UTC)",
        "eventUtc",
        StitchGridColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP,
        event -> formatUtc(event == null ? null : event.eventTimeUtc()));
    addEventColumn(
        eventLog,
        "Topic",
        "topic",
        StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP,
        event -> Strings.firstNonBlank(event == null ? null : event.topic(), "-"));
    addEventColumn(
        eventLog,
        "Summary",
        "summary",
        StitchGridColumn.Kind.NAME,
        event -> Strings.firstNonBlank(event == null ? null : event.summary(), "-"));
    addEventColumn(
        eventLog,
        "Payload",
        "payload",
        StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP,
        event -> Strings.firstNonBlank(event == null ? null : event.payloadPreview(), "-"));
  }

  static void configureLiveTableShell(
      StitchLiveTableShell<?, String> liveTable,
      String emptyTitle,
      String emptyMessage,
      String gridAriaLabel,
      boolean showStatusBar,
      boolean showControls,
      Runnable onClear) {
    liveTable.setSizeFull();
    liveTable.setHighlightMode(StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT);
    liveTable.setFlashWindow(Duration.ofSeconds(2));
    liveTable.statusBar().setVisible(showStatusBar);
    liveTable.controls().setVisible(showControls);
    liveTable.resultsView().setPaginationEnabled(false);
    liveTable.resultsView().setResultCountVisible(true);
    liveTable.resultsView().setEmptyState(emptyTitle, emptyMessage);
    liveTable.resultsView().grid().setSelectionMode(Grid.SelectionMode.NONE);
    liveTable.resultsView().grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", gridAriaLabel);
    if (onClear != null) {
      liveTable.controls().onClear(onClear);
    }
  }

  static void configureStreamTabularColumns(
      StitchLiveTableShell<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String> liveTable,
      List<String> dataColumns,
      String eventHeader,
      String observedHeader,
      Function<Instant, String> timestampFormatter) {
    Grid<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow> grid = liveTable.resultsView().grid();
    grid.removeAllColumns();

    grid.addColumn(row -> row != null && liveTable.changeTracker().isRowChanged(row.rowId()) ? "*" : "")
        .setHeader("Changed")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(false);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null ? "-" : Strings.firstNonBlank(row.rowId(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Row Id")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null ? "-" : Strings.firstNonBlank(row.operation(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Op")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null ? "-" : String.valueOf(row.sequence()))
        .setHeader("Seq")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(
            row ->
                row == null || row.eventTimeUtc() == null
                    ? "-"
                    : timestampFormatter.apply(row.eventTimeUtc()))
        .setHeader(eventHeader)
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(
            row ->
                row == null || row.observedAtUtc() == null
                    ? "-"
                    : timestampFormatter.apply(row.observedAtUtc()))
        .setHeader(observedHeader)
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(row -> row == null ? "-" : Strings.firstNonBlank(row.topic(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Topic")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setSortable(false)
        .setResizable(true);

    for (String column : dataColumns == null ? List.<String>of() : dataColumns) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      grid.addColumn(row -> trackedCellValue(liveTable, row, key))
          .setHeader(key)
          .setAutoWidth(true)
          .setSortable(false)
          .setResizable(true);
    }
  }

  static boolean isActive(StitchRealtimeConnectionState state) {
    return state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED
        || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING
        || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE;
  }

  static <T> T defaultValue(T value, T fallback) {
    return value == null ? fallback : value;
  }

  static String formatCellValue(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    if (value instanceof byte[] bytes) {
      int max = Math.min(bytes.length, 12);
      StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder("0x");
      for (int i = 0; i < max; i++) {
        builder.append(String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%02x", bytes[i]));
      }
      if (bytes.length > max) {
        builder.append("...");
      }
      return builder.toString();
    }
    return String.valueOf(value);
  }

  static String trackedCellValue(
      StitchLiveTableShell<StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow, String> liveTable,
      StitchStreamsProvider.TabularStreamRow row,
      String key) {
    if (row == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return trackedCellValue(liveTable, row.rowId(), key, row.values().get(key));
  }

  static String trackedCellValue(
      StitchLiveTableShell<?, String> liveTable, String rowId, String key, Object value) {
    String text = formatCellValue(value);
    return liveTable.changeTracker().isCellChanged(rowId, key) ? "* " + text : text;
  }

  static void updateChangeSummary(Span target, StitchLiveTableShell<?, String> liveTable) {
    int changedRows = liveTable.changedRowsCount();
    int changedCells = liveTable.changedCellsCount();
    target.setText("Changed rows: " + changedRows + " | changed cells: " + changedCells);
  }

  static String formatUtc(Instant value) {
    return value == null ? "-" : UTC_SECONDS.format(value) + " UTC";
  }

  static void safeClose(AutoCloseable handle) {
    StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(handle);
  }

  private static void addContextValue(FormLayout form, String label, String value) {
    Span content = new Span(StitchDetailsDialogSupport.displayValue(value));
    content.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label + " value");
    form.addFormItem(content, label);
  }

  private static void addEventColumn(
      StitchEventLogShell<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent> eventLog,
      String header,
      String key,
      StitchGridColumn.Kind kind,
      com.vaadin.flow.function.ValueProvider<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent, ?> provider) {
    eventLog
        .resultsView()
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.<StitchStreamsProvider.StreamEvent>text(header, provider)
                .kind(kind)
                .key(key)
                .sortable(false));
  }
}


org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.discovery

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/discovery/StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.discovery;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Command;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.MessageStream;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;

public class StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider {
  private static final List<String> PREFERRED_TOPICS =
      List.of("/fabric/discovery", "/fabric/status", "/fabric/meta", "/fabric/events");

  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter keyAdapter = new StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter();
  private final Map<String, Map<String, JsonNode>> payloadCacheByTopic = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  public StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public List<String> listTopics() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> discovered = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String topic : PREFERRED_TOPICS) {
      addTopic(discovered, topic);
    }
    discoverTopicsFromConstants(discovered);
    discoverTopicsFromServices(discovered);

    List<String> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String preferred : PREFERRED_TOPICS) {
      String normalizedPreferred = normalizeTopic(preferred);
      if (normalizedPreferred != null && discovered.remove(normalizedPreferred)) {
        ordered.add(normalizedPreferred);
      }
    }

    List<String> remainder = new ArrayList<>(discovered);
    remainder.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    ordered.addAll(remainder);
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  public List<SowRecord> querySow(String topic) {
    String resolvedTopic = requireTopic(topic);
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> payloadByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, SowRecord> recordsByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();

    Command command = new Command(Message.Command.SOW);
    command.setTopic(resolvedTopic);
    command.setOptions("oof");

    try (MessageStream stream = controlConnection().amps().client().execute(command)) {
      int generatedCounter = 0;
      for (Message message : stream) {
        if (!isDataMessage(message)) {
          continue;
        }
        JsonNode payload = parsePayload(message == null ? null : message.getData());
        String key = resolveRecordKey(message, payload, ++generatedCounter);
        payloadByKey.put(key, payload);
        recordsByKey.put(key, new SowRecord(key, payload));
      }
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to query SOW topic " + resolvedTopic + ": " + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error),
          error);
    }

    payloadCacheByTopic.put(resolvedTopic, Map.copyOf(payloadByKey));
    List<SowRecord> ordered = new ArrayList<>(recordsByKey.values());
    ordered.sort(Comparator.comparing(record -> record.key().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  public TreeModel parseKeyHierarchy(List<SowRecord> records) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, SowRecord> recordsByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    if (records != null) {
      for (SowRecord record : records) {
        if (record == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(record.key());
        if (key == null) {
          continue;
        }
        recordsByKey.put(key, new SowRecord(key, record.payload()));
        keys.add(key);
      }
    }

    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.Model model = keyAdapter.build(keys);
    return new TreeModel(model.roots(), model.byId(), Map.copyOf(recordsByKey));
  }

  public Optional<JsonNode> getPayload(String topic, String key) {
    String resolvedTopic = requireTopic(topic);
    String resolvedKey = requireKey(key);
    Map<String, JsonNode> payloadByKey = payloadCacheByTopic.get(resolvedTopic);
    if (payloadByKey != null) {
      JsonNode payload = payloadByKey.get(resolvedKey);
      if (payload != null) {
        return Optional.of(payload.deepCopy());
      }
    }

    for (SowRecord record : querySow(resolvedTopic)) {
      if (resolvedKey.equals(record.key())) {
        return Optional.of(record.payload().deepCopy());
      }
    }
    return Optional.empty();
  }

  public JsonNode publishUpdate(String topic, String key, String json) {
    String resolvedTopic = requireTopic(topic);
    String resolvedKey = requireKey(key);
    String payloadText = requireJson(json);
    JsonNode payload = parseJson(payloadText);

    Command publish = new Command(Message.Command.Publish);
    publish.setTopic(resolvedTopic);
    publish.setSowKey(resolvedKey);
    publish.setData(payloadText);

    try (MessageStream ignored = controlConnection().amps().client().execute(publish)) {
      upsertCachedPayload(resolvedTopic, resolvedKey, payload);
      return payload.deepCopy();
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to publish update to topic "
              + resolvedTopic
              + ": "
              + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error),
          error);
    }
  }

  private void discoverTopicsFromConstants(LinkedHashSet<String> topics) {
    try {
      for (java.lang.reflect.Field field : DiscoveryTopics.class.getDeclaredFields()) {
        if (!java.lang.reflect.Modifier.isStatic(field.getModifiers())
            || field.getType() != String.class) {
          continue;
        }
        addTopic(topics, (String) field.get(null));
      }
    } catch (IllegalAccessException ignored) {
      addTopic(topics, DiscoveryTopics.DISCOVERY);
      addTopic(topics, DiscoveryTopics.STATUS);
      addTopic(topics, DiscoveryTopics.HEARTBEAT);
    }
  }

  private void discoverTopicsFromServices(LinkedHashSet<String> topics) {
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      return;
    }
    for (DefinitionService service : discoveryCache.list(DefinitionService.class)) {
      if (service == null || service.amps() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      addTopic(topics, service.amps().requestTopic());
      addTopic(topics, service.amps().responseTopic());
      addTopic(topics, service.amps().inboxTopicPrefix());
      List<String> serviceTopics = service.amps().topics();
      if (serviceTopics == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (String topic : serviceTopics) {
        addTopic(topics, topic);
      }
    }
  }

  private ControlConnection controlConnection() {
    ControlConnection connection = session.internal().controlPlaneConnection();
    if (connection == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Control connection is not available");
    }
    return connection;
  }

  private void upsertCachedPayload(String topic, String key, JsonNode payload) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> updated = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    Map<String, JsonNode> existing = payloadCacheByTopic.get(topic);
    if (existing != null) {
      updated.putAll(existing);
    }
    updated.put(key, payload.deepCopy());
    payloadCacheByTopic.put(topic, Map.copyOf(updated));
  }

  private static boolean isDataMessage(Message message) {
    if (message == null || message.getData() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    int command = message.getCommand();
    return command == Message.Command.SOW || command == Message.Command.Publish;
  }

  private static JsonNode parsePayload(String payloadText) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(payloadText)) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    return parseJson(payloadText);
  }

  private static JsonNode parseJson(String payloadText) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(payloadText);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      ObjectNode fallback = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
      fallback.put("_rawPayload", payloadText);
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  private static String resolveRecordKey(Message message, JsonNode payload, int generatedCounter) {
    String candidate = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(message == null ? null : message.getSowKey());
    if (candidate != null) {
      return candidate;
    }
    String group = pointerText(payload, "/envelope/group");
    String type = pointerText(payload, "/envelope/type");
    String name = pointerText(payload, "/envelope/name");
    if (group != null && type != null && name != null) {
      return StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(group + "/" + type + "/" + name);
    }
    return "record-" + generatedCounter;
  }

  private static String pointerText(JsonNode node, String pointer) {
    if (node == null || pointer == null || pointer.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode value = node.at(pointer);
    if (value == null || value.isMissingNode() || value.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(value.isTextual() ? value.textValue() : value.asText(null));
  }

  private static void addTopic(LinkedHashSet<String> topics, String topic) {
    String normalized = normalizeTopic(topic);
    if (normalized != null) {
      topics.add(normalized);
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeTopic(String topic) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(topic);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.startsWith("/") ? normalized : "/" + normalized;
  }

  private static String requireTopic(String topic) {
    String resolved = normalizeTopic(topic);
    if (resolved == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("topic is required");
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  private static String requireKey(String key) {
    String resolved = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(key);
    if (resolved == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("key is required");
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  private static String requireJson(String json) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(json);
    if (resolved == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("json is required");
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  public record SowRecord(String key, JsonNode payload) {}

  public record TreeModel(
      List<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> roots,
      Map<String, StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> byId,
      Map<String, SowRecord> recordsByKey) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/discovery/StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.discovery;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.Icon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;

@Route(value = "admin/discovery/browser", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreen extends StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen {
  private static final StitchEmptyState NO_SELECTION =
      new StitchEmptyState("No SOW key selected", "Select a key from the browser tree to inspect payload.");
  private static final StitchEmptyState NO_PAYLOAD_NODE =
      new StitchEmptyState(
          "No payload at this node", "Select a leaf key with payload data to view or edit JSON.");

  private final StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider provider;
  private final ComboBox<String> topicSelector = new ComboBox<>();

  private StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.TreeModel treeModel =
      new StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.TreeModel(List.of(), Map.of(), Map.of());
  private Map<String, StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.SowRecord> payloadByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private String currentTopic;
  private boolean suppressTopicEvents;
  private boolean suppressEditorEvents;

  public StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider provider) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  private StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreen(
      StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig config, StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle(),
        "Refresh selected discovery topic",
        "Refresh selected discovery topic",
        "Payload",
        "Selected payload JSON");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    configureTopicSelector();
    configureInspectorPanel();

    initBrowser(
        new BrowserConfig(
            "SOW Browser",
            "Payload Inspector",
            NO_SELECTION,
            NO_PAYLOAD_NODE,
            "Search keys",
            "Search discovery keys",
            this::nodeIcon,
            node -> null,
            topicSelector),
        new EditConfig(
            () -> editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges(),
            this::saveSelectedPayload,
            this::discardSelectedPayload,
            this::isPayloadNode),
        this::detailSectionTitle,
        this::buildDetailContent,
        this::readOnlyActions,
        nodeId -> {});
    loadTopics();
  }

  @Override
  protected void refreshRequested() {
    if (currentTopic == null) {
      loadTopics();
      return;
    }
    if (editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      dirtyStateSupport()
          .guard(
              () -> {
                if (saveSelectedPayload()) {
                  loadTopic(currentTopic, true);
                  return true;
                }
                return false;
              },
              () -> {
                discardSelectedPayload();
                loadTopic(currentTopic, true);
              },
              () -> {});
      return;
    }
    loadTopic(currentTopic, true);
  }

  private static StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .discovery()
        .map(StitchDiscoveryFeature::browser)
        .filter(StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private void configureTopicSelector() {
    topicSelector.setPlaceholder("Topic");
    topicSelector.setWidth("20rem");
    topicSelector.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    topicSelector.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    topicSelector.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Discovery topic selector");
    topicSelector.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!suppressTopicEvents) {
            requestTopicChange(event.getValue());
          }
        });
  }

  private void configureInspectorPanel() {
    inspectorPanel().previewField().setHeight("30rem");
    inspectorPanel().previewField().setMinHeight("24rem");
    inspectorPanel()
        .previewField()
        .addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (!suppressEditorEvents && editorMode().isEditMode() && event.isFromClient()) {
                editorMode().markDirty();
              }
            });
  }

  private void loadTopics() {
    List<String> topics = provider.listTopics();
    topicSelector.setItems(topics);
    if (topics.isEmpty()) {
      currentTopic = null;
      clearTopicData();
      return;
    }
    String preferred =
        currentTopic != null && topics.contains(currentTopic) ? currentTopic : topics.get(0);
    setTopicSelectorValue(preferred);
    loadTopic(preferred, false);
  }

  private void requestTopicChange(String requestedTopic) {
    String resolved = normalizeTopic(requestedTopic);
    if (Objects.equals(currentTopic, resolved)) {
      return;
    }
    if (editorMode().hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      setTopicSelectorValue(currentTopic);
      dirtyStateSupport()
          .guard(
              () -> {
                if (saveSelectedPayload()) {
                  loadTopic(resolved, false);
                  return true;
                }
                return false;
              },
              () -> {
                discardSelectedPayload();
                loadTopic(resolved, false);
              },
              () -> {});
      return;
    }
    loadTopic(resolved, false);
  }

  private void loadTopic(String topic, boolean preserveSelection) {
    String resolved = normalizeTopic(topic);
    if (resolved == null) {
      currentTopic = null;
      clearTopicData();
      return;
    }
    String desiredSelection = preserveSelection ? browserShell().selectedNodeId() : null;
    try {
      List<StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.SowRecord> records = provider.querySow(resolved);
      treeModel = provider.parseKeyHierarchy(records);
      payloadByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>(treeModel.recordsByKey());
      currentTopic = resolved;
      setTopicSelectorValue(resolved);

      applyTree(
          treeModel.roots(),
          treeModel.byId(),
          NO_SELECTION,
          NO_PAYLOAD_NODE,
          desiredSelection,
          this::isPayloadNode);
      Notification.show(
          "Loaded " + records.size() + " SOW records from " + resolved, 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      clearTopicData();
      currentTopic = resolved;
      setTopicSelectorValue(resolved);
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load topic", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private void clearTopicData() {
    treeModel = new StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.TreeModel(List.of(), Map.of(), Map.of());
    payloadByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    editorMode().clear();
    clearTree(NO_SELECTION, NO_PAYLOAD_NODE);
  }

  private boolean saveSelectedPayload() {
    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node = selectedNode();
    if (!isPayloadNode(node) || currentTopic == null) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      JsonNode saved =
          provider.publishUpdate(currentTopic, node.fullKey(), inspectorPanel().previewField().getValue());
      payloadByKey.put(node.fullKey(), new StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.SowRecord(node.fullKey(), saved));
      setEditorValue(prettyJson(saved));
      Notification.show("Published update for " + node.fullKey(), 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to publish update", rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void discardSelectedPayload() {
    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node = selectedNode();
    if (!isPayloadNode(node)) {
      return;
    }
    setEditorValue(prettyJson(resolvePayload(node)));
    Notification.show("Discarded unsaved payload changes", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private List<Component> readOnlyActions(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    if (isPayloadNode(node)) {
      Button json =
          inspectorPanel().createJsonAction(() -> openJsonDialog(node), "Open payload JSON dialog");
      actions.add(json);

      Button copy =
          inspectorPanel()
              .createCopyAction("Payload copied to clipboard", "Nothing to copy", "Copy payload JSON");
      actions.add(copy);
    }

    Button close =
        inspectorPanel()
            .createCloseAction(() -> browserShell().applySelectionById(null), "Close payload inspector");
    actions.add(close);
    return List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  private String detailSectionTitle(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return "Payload Inspector";
    }
    return isPayloadNode(node) ? "Payload Inspector" : "Tree Node";
  }

  private Component buildDetailContent(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node, boolean editMode) {
    if (node == null || !isPayloadNode(node)) {
      return NO_PAYLOAD_NODE;
    }
    inspectorPanel().setContext("Key", node.fullKey());
    inspectorPanel().setMetadata(Map.of());
    inspectorPanel().setPreviewVisible(true);
    inspectorPanel().setPreviewReadOnly(!editMode);
    inspectorPanel().setPreviewAriaLabel(
        (editMode ? "Editable payload JSON for " : "Payload JSON for ") + node.fullKey());
    setEditorValue(prettyJson(resolvePayload(node)));
    return inspectorPanel();
  }

  private boolean isPayloadNode(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    return node != null && Strings.isNotBlank(node.fullKey()) && payloadByKey.containsKey(node.fullKey());
  }

  private JsonNode resolvePayload(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null || node.fullKey() == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.SowRecord cached = payloadByKey.get(node.fullKey());
    if (cached != null && cached.payload() != null) {
      return cached.payload();
    }
    if (currentTopic == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    JsonNode loaded =
        provider
            .getPayload(currentTopic, node.fullKey())
            .orElseGet(() -> DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode());
    payloadByKey.put(node.fullKey(), new StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.SowRecord(node.fullKey(), loaded));
    return loaded;
  }

  private void openJsonDialog(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    new StitchJsonDialog("Raw JSON - " + node.fullKey(), resolvePayload(node)).open();
  }

  private Component nodeIcon(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    VaadinIcon iconType =
        node != null && isPayloadNode(node) ? VaadinIcon.FILE_CODE : VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O;
    Icon icon = iconType.create();
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private void setTopicSelectorValue(String topic) {
    suppressTopicEvents = true;
    if (topic == null) {
      topicSelector.clear();
    } else {
      topicSelector.setValue(topic);
    }
    suppressTopicEvents = false;
  }

  private void setEditorValue(String value) {
    suppressEditorEvents = true;
    inspectorPanel().setPreviewValue(value);
    suppressEditorEvents = false;
  }

  private static String normalizeTopic(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.startsWith("/") ? normalized : "/" + normalized;
  }

  private static String prettyJson(JsonNode payload) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(payload);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return payload == null ? "{}" : payload.toString();
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.discovery;

public final class StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "Browser";
      this.routePath = "admin/discovery/browser";
      this.pageTitle = "Discovery Browser";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Browse and edit AMPS SOW payloads by hierarchical key.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.discovery;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchDiscoveryFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "discovery";
  public static final String BROWSER = "browser";
  public static final String ENTRY_ADMIN_DISCOVERY_BROWSER = "admin.discovery.browser";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final String discoveryLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig browser;

  private StitchDiscoveryFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.discoveryLabel = require(builder.discoveryLabel, "discoveryLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.browser = builder.browserBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig browser() {
    return browser;
  }

  public Optional<StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return BROWSER.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(browser) : Optional.empty();
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    if (!browser.enabled()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    StitchMenuEntry browserEntry =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_ADMIN_DISCOVERY_BROWSER)
            .withLabel(browser.label())
            .withRoutePath(browser.routePath())
            .withOrder(browser.order())
            .build();
    return List.of(browserEntry);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Admin";
    private String discoveryLabel = "Discovery";
    private int order = 30;
    private final StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig.Builder browserBuilder =
        StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig.builder(BROWSER);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDiscoveryLabel(String value) {
      this.discoveryLabel = require(value, "discoveryLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder browser(Consumer<StitchDiscoveryBrowserScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(browserBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDiscoveryFeature build() {
      return new StitchDiscoveryFeature(this);
    }
  }
}
