===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/docs/StitchDocsBrowserProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.docs;

import com.vladsch.flexmark.ext.tables.TablesExtension;
import com.vladsch.flexmark.html.HtmlRenderer;
import com.vladsch.flexmark.parser.Parser;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.net.URLEncoder;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import java.util.stream.Stream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;

public final class StitchDocsBrowserProvider {
  private static final String RESOURCE_URL_PREFIX = "/api/stitch/docs/resources/";

  private static final Set<String> NAV_PAGE_EXTENSIONS =
      Set.of(
          "md",
          "markdown",
          "mkd",
          "mkdown",
          "wiki",
          "txt",
          "json",
          "yaml",
          "yml",
          "xml",
          "csv",
          "adoc",
          "rst",
          "properties",
          "log",
          "sql");

  private static final Set<String> MARKDOWN_EXTENSIONS = Set.of("md", "markdown", "mkd", "mkdown");
  private static final Set<String> WIKI_EXTENSIONS = Set.of("wiki");
  private static final Set<String> CODE_BLOCK_EXTENSIONS =
      Set.of("yaml", "yml", "json", "xml", "sql", "properties", "csv", "log", "txt");

  private static final Pattern HEADING_MD_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("(?m)^\\s{0,3}#{1,6}\\s+(.+?)\\s*$");
  private static final Pattern HEADING_WIKI_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("(?m)^\\s*h([1-6])\\.\\s+(.+?)\\s*$");
  private static final Pattern LEADING_ORDER_PREFIX = Pattern.compile("^\\s*(\\d+)[._\\-\\s]*(.*)$");
  private static final Pattern IMG_SRC_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile(
          "(?i)<img\\s+[^>]*src=(\"|')(?![a-z][a-z0-9+\\-.]*:|/|#|data:)([^\"']+)\\1");
  private static final Pattern LINK_HREF_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile(
          "(?i)<a\\s+[^>]*href=(\"|')(?![a-z][a-z0-9+\\-.]*:|/|#|javascript:)([^\"']+)\\1");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_LINK_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("\\[([^\\]|]+)\\|([^\\]]+)\\]");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_DIRECT_LINK_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("(?<!\\!)\\[([^\\]|]+)\\](?!\\()");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_IMAGE_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("!([^!]+)!");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_HEADING_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("^\\s*h([1-6])\\.\\s+(.*)$");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_TOC_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("^\\s*\\{toc(?::[^}]*)?}\\s*$", Pattern.CASE_INSENSITIVE);
  private static final Pattern WIKI_CODE_OPEN_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("^\\s*\\{(code|noformat)(?::([^}]+))?}\\s*$");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_CODE_CLOSE_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("^\\s*\\{(code|noformat)}\\s*$");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_MACRO_OPEN_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("^\\s*\\{(info|note|tip|warning|panel)(?::([^}]+))?}\\s*$");
  private static final Pattern WIKI_MACRO_CLOSE_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("^\\s*\\{(info|note|tip|warning|panel)}\\s*$");
  private static final Pattern HTML_HEADING_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("(?is)<h([1-6])([^>]*)>(.*?)</h\\1>");
  private static final Pattern HTML_HEADING_ID_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("(?i)\\sid\\s*=\\s*(['\"])([^'\"]+)\\1");
  private static final Pattern HTML_TAG_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("(?is)<[^>]+>");

  private final Path root;
  private final Parser markdownParser;
  private final HtmlRenderer markdownRenderer;

  public StitchDocsBrowserProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.root = resolveRoot(runtimeContext.settings().docsRootPath());
    this.markdownParser = Parser.builder().extensions(List.of(TablesExtension.create())).build();
    this.markdownRenderer = HtmlRenderer.builder().build();
  }

  public TreeModel loadTree() {
    if (root == null || !Files.isDirectory(root)) {
      return new TreeModel(List.of(), Map.of(), null);
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, NavNode> byId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<NavNode> roots = buildChildren(root, "", byId);
    String defaultSelectionId = defaultSelectionId(roots, byId);
    return new TreeModel(List.copyOf(roots), Map.copyOf(byId), defaultSelectionId);
  }

  public DocPage loadPage(NavNode node) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(node, "node");
    if (node.directory()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot render a directory as a docs page: " + node.id());
    }
    if (root == null || node.relativePath() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Docs root is not configured");
    }
    Path file = root.resolve(node.relativePath()).normalize();
    if (!file.startsWith(root) || !Files.isRegularFile(file)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Document does not exist: " + node.relativePath());
    }
    try {
      String raw = Files.readString(file, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
      String extension = extensionOf(node.relativePath());
      RenderedPage rendered = renderPageHtml(raw, extension, node.relativePath());
      String title = resolvePageTitle(node.label(), raw, extension);
      return new DocPage(
          node.id(), title, rendered.html(), raw, node.relativePath(), rendered.headings());
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to render docs page " + node.relativePath() + ": " + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error),
          error);
    }
  }

  public DocResource loadResource(String relativePath) {
    if (root == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String sanitized = sanitizeRelativePath(relativePath);
    if (sanitized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Path file = resolveResourcePath(sanitized);
    if (file == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      byte[] bytes = Files.readAllBytes(file);
      return new DocResource(sanitized, detectContentType(sanitized, file), bytes);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to read docs resource " + sanitized + ": " + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error), error);
    }
  }

  private List<NavNode> buildChildren(Path directory, String relativePrefix, Map<String, NavNode> byId) {
    List<Path> entries = listEntries(directory);
    if (entries.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    List<NavNode> folders = new ArrayList<>();
    List<NavNode> files = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Path entry : entries) {
      String name = entry.getFileName() == null ? null : entry.getFileName().toString();
      if (Strings.isBlank(name) || name.startsWith(".")) {
        continue;
      }
      String relative = relativePrefix.isBlank() ? name : relativePrefix + "/" + name;
      if (Files.isDirectory(entry)) {
        List<NavNode> children = buildChildren(entry, relative, byId);
        if (children.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        NavNode folder = new NavNode(relative, displayName(name, true), relative, true, List.copyOf(children));
        folders.add(folder);
        byId.put(folder.id(), folder);
        continue;
      }
      if (!isNavPage(name)) {
        continue;
      }
      NavNode file = new NavNode(relative, displayName(name, false), relative, false, List.of());
      files.add(file);
      byId.put(file.id(), file);
    }

    folders.sort(Comparator.comparing(node -> sortableName(node.label())));
    files.sort(Comparator.comparing(node -> sortableName(node.label())));

    List<NavNode> merged = new ArrayList<>(folders.size() + files.size());
    merged.addAll(folders);
    merged.addAll(files);
    return List.copyOf(merged);
  }

  private static List<Path> listEntries(Path directory) {
    try (Stream<Path> stream = Files.list(directory)) {
      return stream.sorted(directoryEntryComparator()).toList();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return List.of();
    }
  }

  private static Comparator<Path> directoryEntryComparator() {
    return (left, right) -> {
      boolean leftDir = Files.isDirectory(left);
      boolean rightDir = Files.isDirectory(right);
      if (leftDir != rightDir) {
        return leftDir ? -1 : 1;
      }
      String leftName = left.getFileName() == null ? "" : left.getFileName().toString();
      String rightName = right.getFileName() == null ? "" : right.getFileName().toString();
      SortKey leftKey = sortKey(leftName);
      SortKey rightKey = sortKey(rightName);
      if (leftKey.order() != null && rightKey.order() != null) {
        int orderCompare = Integer.compare(leftKey.order(), rightKey.order());
        if (orderCompare != 0) {
          return orderCompare;
        }
      } else if (leftKey.order() != null) {
        return -1;
      } else if (rightKey.order() != null) {
        return 1;
      }
      return leftKey.normalized().compareTo(rightKey.normalized());
    };
  }

  private static SortKey sortKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToEmpty(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    Matcher matcher = LEADING_ORDER_PREFIX.matcher(normalized);
    if (matcher.matches()) {
      try {
        Integer order = Integer.parseInt(matcher.group(1));
        String remainder = Strings.trimToEmpty(matcher.group(2));
        return new SortKey(order, remainder.isBlank() ? normalized : remainder);
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
        // Fall through.
      }
    }
    return new SortKey(null, normalized);
  }

  private static String defaultSelectionId(List<NavNode> roots, Map<String, NavNode> byId) {
    if (roots == null || roots.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String candidate : List.of("README.md", "README.markdown", "README.wiki")) {
      String id = candidate.replace('\\', '/');
      NavNode rootReadme = byId.get(id);
      if (rootReadme != null && !rootReadme.directory()) {
        return rootReadme.id();
      }
    }
    for (NavNode node : roots) {
      String found = firstFile(node);
      if (found != null) {
        return found;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String firstFile(NavNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (!node.directory()) {
      return node.id();
    }
    for (NavNode child : node.children()) {
      String found = firstFile(child);
      if (found != null) {
        return found;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static boolean isNavPage(String fileName) {
    String extension = extensionOf(fileName);
    return extension != null && NAV_PAGE_EXTENSIONS.contains(extension.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
  }

  private RenderedPage renderPageHtml(String raw, String extension, String relativePath) {
    String ext = Strings.trimToNull(extension);
    if (ext == null) {
      return new RenderedPage(asCodeBlockHtml(raw, null), List.of());
    }
    String lower = ext.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (MARKDOWN_EXTENSIONS.contains(lower)) {
      return renderMarkdown(raw, relativePath, lower);
    }
    if (WIKI_EXTENSIONS.contains(lower)) {
      return renderWiki(raw, relativePath, lower);
    }
    if (CODE_BLOCK_EXTENSIONS.contains(lower)) {
      return new RenderedPage(asCodeBlockHtml(raw, lower), List.of());
    }
    return new RenderedPage(asCodeBlockHtml(raw, lower), List.of());
  }

  private RenderedPage renderWiki(String wiki, String relativePath, String extension) {
    List<TocItem> headings = extractWikiHeadings(wiki);
    String markdown = confluenceWikiToMarkdown(wiki, headings);
    return renderMarkdown(markdown, relativePath, extension);
  }

  private RenderedPage renderMarkdown(String markdown, String relativePath, String extension) {
    String rendered = markdownRenderer.render(markdownParser.parse(Strings.trimToEmpty(markdown)));
    String rewritten = rewriteRelativeResources(rendered, relativePath, extension);
    HeadingProcessing headingProcessing = ensureHeadingAnchors(rewritten);
    return new RenderedPage(headingProcessing.html(), headingProcessing.headings());
  }

  private static String asCodeBlockHtml(String raw, String language) {
    String escaped = escapeHtml(Strings.trimToEmpty(raw));
    String langClass = Strings.isBlank(language) ? "" : " class=\"language-" + language + "\"";
    return "<pre><code" + langClass + ">" + escaped + "</code></pre>";
  }

  private static String resolvePageTitle(String fallback, String raw, String extension) {
    String ext = Strings.trimToNull(extension);
    if (ext != null) {
      if (MARKDOWN_EXTENSIONS.contains(ext.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        Matcher heading = HEADING_MD_PATTERN.matcher(Strings.trimToEmpty(raw));
        if (heading.find()) {
          String candidate = Strings.trimToNull(heading.group(1));
          if (candidate != null) {
            return cleanupHeading(candidate);
          }
        }
      } else if (WIKI_EXTENSIONS.contains(ext.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        Matcher heading = HEADING_WIKI_PATTERN.matcher(Strings.trimToEmpty(raw));
        if (heading.find()) {
          String candidate = Strings.trimToNull(heading.group(2));
          if (candidate != null) {
            return cleanupHeading(candidate);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(fallback, "Document");
  }

  private static String cleanupHeading(String value) {
    String normalized = value.replaceAll("`", "").replaceAll("\\*\\*", "").trim();
    return normalized.isBlank() ? "Document" : normalized;
  }

  private static List<TocItem> extractWikiHeadings(String wiki) {
    String raw = Strings.trimToEmpty(wiki);
    if (raw.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<TocItem> headings = new ArrayList<>();
    Map<String, Integer> slugCounts = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    String[] lines = raw.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace('\r', '\n').split("\n", -1);
    for (String line : lines) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToEmpty(line);
      Matcher matcher = WIKI_HEADING_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed);
      if (!matcher.matches()) {
        continue;
      }
      int level = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, Integer.parseInt(matcher.group(1))));
      String text = normalizeWikiHeadingText(matcher.group(2));
      if (text == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = uniqueSlug(text, slugCounts);
      headings.add(new TocItem(id, text, level));
    }
    return List.copyOf(headings);
  }

  private static String normalizeWikiHeadingText(String rawHeading) {
    String value = Strings.trimToEmpty(rawHeading);
    if (value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value;
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("\\[([^\\]|]+)\\|([^\\]]+)\\]", "$1");
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("\\[([^\\]]+)\\]", "$1");
    normalized = normalized.replace("*", "").replace("_", "").replace("`", "");
    normalized = normalized.replace("{", "").replace("}", "");
    normalized = Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized;
  }

  private static String uniqueSlug(String value, Map<String, Integer> slugCounts) {
    String base = slugify(value);
    Integer next = slugCounts.get(base);
    if (next == null) {
      slugCounts.put(base, 1);
      return base;
    }
    int sequence = next + 1;
    slugCounts.put(base, sequence);
    return base + "-" + sequence;
  }

  private static String slugify(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToEmpty(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("[^a-z0-9]+", "-");
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("(^-+|-+$)", "");
    return normalized.isBlank() ? "section" : normalized;
  }

  private static String wikiTocHtml(List<TocItem> headings) {
    List<TocItem> tocItems =
        headings == null
            ? List.of()
            : headings.stream().filter(item -> item != null && item.level() <= 3).toList();
    if (tocItems.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    TocNode root = new TocNode(null);
    List<TocNode> stack = new ArrayList<>();
    stack.add(root);
    for (TocItem item : tocItems) {
      while (stack.size() > 1) {
        TocNode top = stack.get(stack.size() - 1);
        TocItem topItem = top.item();
        if (topItem != null && topItem.level() >= item.level()) {
          stack.remove(stack.size() - 1);
          continue;
        }
        break;
      }
      TocNode parent = stack.get(stack.size() - 1);
      TocNode node = new TocNode(item);
      parent.children().add(node);
      stack.add(node);
    }

    StringBuilder html = new StringBuilder();
    html.append("<div class=\"stitch-docs-toc\"><ul>");
    for (TocNode child : root.children()) {
      appendTocNode(html, child);
    }
    html.append("</ul></div>");
    return html.toString();
  }

  private static void appendTocNode(StringBuilder html, TocNode node) {
    if (node == null || node.item() == null) {
      return;
    }
    TocItem item = node.item();
    html.append("<li>");
    html.append("<a href=\"#");
    html.append(escapeHtml(item.id()));
    html.append("\">");
    html.append(escapeHtml(item.text()));
    html.append("</a>");
    if (!node.children().isEmpty()) {
      html.append("<ul>");
      for (TocNode child : node.children()) {
        appendTocNode(html, child);
      }
      html.append("</ul>");
    }
    html.append("</li>");
  }

  private static String confluenceWikiToMarkdown(String wiki, List<TocItem> headings) {
    String raw = Strings.trimToEmpty(wiki);
    if (raw.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    List<TocItem> headingItems = headings == null ? List.of() : headings;
    String tocHtml = wikiTocHtml(headingItems);
    List<String> output = new ArrayList<>();
    boolean inCodeBlock = false;
    String codeFence = "```";
    boolean inMacro = false;
    String macroName = null;
    boolean inPanelMacro = false;
    int headingIndex = 0;

    String[] lines = raw.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace('\r', '\n').split("\n", -1);
    for (String line : lines) {
      if (line == null) {
        output.add("");
        continue;
      }
      String trimmed = line.trim();

      if (inCodeBlock) {
        if (WIKI_CODE_CLOSE_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed).matches()) {
          output.add("```");
          inCodeBlock = false;
          codeFence = "```";
        } else {
          output.add(line);
        }
        continue;
      }

      if (inMacro) {
        Matcher close = WIKI_MACRO_CLOSE_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed);
        if (close.matches() && close.group(1).equalsIgnoreCase(macroName)) {
          inMacro = false;
          inPanelMacro = false;
          macroName = null;
          output.add("");
        } else if (inPanelMacro && trimmed.startsWith("h")) {
          output.add("> " + inlineWikiToMarkdown(trimmed));
        } else {
          output.add("> " + inlineWikiToMarkdown(line));
        }
        continue;
      }

      Matcher codeOpen = WIKI_CODE_OPEN_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed);
      if (codeOpen.matches()) {
        String options = Strings.trimToNull(codeOpen.group(2));
        String language = extractCodeLanguage(options);
        codeFence = Strings.isBlank(language) ? "```" : "```" + language;
        output.add(codeFence);
        inCodeBlock = true;
        continue;
      }

      Matcher macroOpen = WIKI_MACRO_OPEN_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed);
      if (macroOpen.matches()) {
        macroName = macroOpen.group(1).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        String options = Strings.trimToNull(macroOpen.group(2));
        String label = macroLabel(macroName, options);
        output.add("> **" + label + "**");
        output.add(">");
        inMacro = true;
        inPanelMacro = "panel".equals(macroName);
        continue;
      }

      if (WIKI_TOC_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed).matches()) {
        output.add(tocHtml);
        continue;
      }

      Matcher heading = WIKI_HEADING_PATTERN.matcher(trimmed);
      if (heading.matches()) {
        int level = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, Integer.parseInt(heading.group(1))));
        String text = normalizeWikiHeadingText(heading.group(2));
        String id;
        if (headingIndex < headingItems.size()) {
          TocItem item = headingItems.get(headingIndex);
          id = item == null ? null : item.id();
        } else {
          id = null;
        }
        headingIndex++;
        String safeText = Strings.firstNonBlank(text, "Section");
        String safeId = Strings.firstNonBlank(id, slugify(safeText));
        output.add(
            "<h"
                + level
                + " id=\""
                + escapeHtml(safeId)
                + "\">"
                + escapeHtml(safeText)
                + "</h"
                + level
                + ">");
        continue;
      }

      if (trimmed.startsWith("||")) {
        List<String> cells = parseWikiTableRow(trimmed, true);
        if (!cells.isEmpty()) {
          output.add(toMarkdownTableRow(cells));
          output.add(toMarkdownTableSeparator(cells.size()));
        } else {
          output.add("");
        }
        continue;
      }

      if (trimmed.startsWith("|")) {
        List<String> cells = parseWikiTableRow(trimmed, false);
        output.add(cells.isEmpty() ? "" : toMarkdownTableRow(cells));
        continue;
      }

      output.add(inlineWikiToMarkdown(line));
    }

    if (inCodeBlock) {
      output.add("```");
    }
    if (inMacro) {
      output.add("");
    }
    return String.join("\n", output);
  }

  private static String extractCodeLanguage(String options) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(options);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String token : normalized.split("\\|")) {
      String part = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (part == null) {
        continue;
      }
      int equals = part.indexOf('=');
      if (equals > 0) {
        String key = part.substring(0, equals).trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(part.substring(equals + 1));
        if (value != null && (key.equals("lang") || key.equals("language"))) {
          return value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        }
      } else {
        return part.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String macroLabel(String macroName, String options) {
    if ("panel".equals(macroName)) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(options);
      if (normalized != null) {
        for (String token : normalized.split("\\|")) {
          String part = Strings.trimToNull(token);
          if (part == null) {
            continue;
          }
          int equals = part.indexOf('=');
          if (equals > 0) {
            String key = part.substring(0, equals).trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if ("title".equals(key)) {
              String value = Strings.trimToNull(part.substring(equals + 1));
              if (value != null) {
                return value;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
      return "Panel";
    }
    return capitalizeWord(macroName);
  }

  private static List<String> parseWikiTableRow(String line, boolean header) {
    String delimiter = header ? "\\|\\|" : "\\|";
    String[] raw = line.split(delimiter, -1);
    List<String> cells = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String token : raw) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (trimmed != null) {
        cells.add(inlineWikiToMarkdown(trimmed));
      }
    }
    return cells;
  }

  private static String toMarkdownTableRow(List<String> cells) {
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder("|");
    for (String cell : cells) {
      builder.append(' ').append(cell.replace("|", "\\|")).append(" |");
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  private static String toMarkdownTableSeparator(int columns) {
    int count = Math.max(1, columns);
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder("|");
    for (int index = 0; index < count; index++) {
      builder.append(" --- |");
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  private static String inlineWikiToMarkdown(String line) {
    String value = Strings.trimToEmpty(line);
    Matcher linkMatcher = WIKI_LINK_PATTERN.matcher(value);
    StringBuffer linked = new StringBuffer();
    while (linkMatcher.find()) {
      String text = Strings.trimToEmpty(linkMatcher.group(1));
      String target = Strings.trimToEmpty(linkMatcher.group(2));
      linkMatcher.appendReplacement(
          linked, Matcher.quoteReplacement("[" + text + "](" + target + ")"));
    }
    linkMatcher.appendTail(linked);

    Matcher directLinkMatcher = WIKI_DIRECT_LINK_PATTERN.matcher(linked.toString());
    StringBuffer direct = new StringBuffer();
    while (directLinkMatcher.find()) {
      String target = Strings.trimToEmpty(directLinkMatcher.group(1));
      directLinkMatcher.appendReplacement(
          direct, Matcher.quoteReplacement("[" + target + "](" + target + ")"));
    }
    directLinkMatcher.appendTail(direct);

    Matcher imageMatcher = WIKI_IMAGE_PATTERN.matcher(direct.toString());
    StringBuffer images = new StringBuffer();
    while (imageMatcher.find()) {
      String target = Strings.trimToEmpty(imageMatcher.group(1));
      imageMatcher.appendReplacement(images, Matcher.quoteReplacement("![](" + target + ")"));
    }
    imageMatcher.appendTail(images);
    return images.toString();
  }

  private static HeadingProcessing ensureHeadingAnchors(String html) {
    String source = Strings.trimToEmpty(html);
    if (source.isBlank()) {
      return new HeadingProcessing("", List.of());
    }
    Matcher matcher = HTML_HEADING_PATTERN.matcher(source);
    StringBuffer output = new StringBuffer();
    Map<String, Integer> slugCounts = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<DocHeading> headings = new ArrayList<>();
    while (matcher.find()) {
      int level = Integer.parseInt(matcher.group(1));
      String attributes = Strings.trimToEmpty(matcher.group(2));
      String body = Strings.trimToEmpty(matcher.group(3));
      String headingText = headingText(body);
      String existingId = sanitizeAnchorId(extractHeadingId(attributes));
      String anchorId = uniqueSlug(Strings.firstNonBlank(existingId, headingText), slugCounts);
      String resolvedText = Strings.firstNonBlank(headingText, "Section");
      headings.add(new DocHeading(anchorId, resolvedText, level));
      String replacement =
          "<h"
              + level
              + upsertHeadingId(attributes, anchorId)
              + ">"
              + body
              + "</h"
              + level
              + ">";
      matcher.appendReplacement(output, Matcher.quoteReplacement(replacement));
    }
    matcher.appendTail(output);
    return new HeadingProcessing(output.toString(), List.copyOf(headings));
  }

  private static String extractHeadingId(String attributes) {
    String source = Strings.trimToEmpty(attributes);
    Matcher matcher = HTML_HEADING_ID_PATTERN.matcher(source);
    if (!matcher.find()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(matcher.group(2));
  }

  private static String upsertHeadingId(String attributes, String id) {
    String source = Strings.trimToEmpty(attributes);
    String withoutId = HTML_HEADING_ID_PATTERN.matcher(source).replaceAll("");
    String trimmed = withoutId.stripTrailing();
    if (trimmed.isBlank()) {
      return " id=\"" + escapeHtml(id) + "\"";
    }
    if (!Character.isWhitespace(trimmed.charAt(0))) {
      trimmed = " " + trimmed;
    }
    return trimmed + " id=\"" + escapeHtml(id) + "\"";
  }

  private static String headingText(String headingHtml) {
    String plain = HTML_TAG_PATTERN.matcher(Strings.trimToEmpty(headingHtml)).replaceAll(" ");
    plain = plain.replace('\u00A0', ' ');
    plain = plain.replaceAll("\\s+", " ");
    plain = decodeBasicEntities(plain);
    return Strings.trimToNull(plain);
  }

  private static String decodeBasicEntities(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToEmpty(value);
    return normalized
        .replace("&amp;", "&")
        .replace("&lt;", "<")
        .replace("&gt;", ">")
        .replace("&quot;", "\"")
        .replace("&#39;", "'");
  }

  private String rewriteRelativeResources(String html, String relativePath, String pageExtension) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(html) || Strings.isBlank(relativePath)) {
      return html;
    }
    String normalizedPath = relativePath.replace('\\', '/');
    int lastSlash = normalizedPath.lastIndexOf('/');
    Path base = lastSlash < 0 ? Path.of("") : Path.of(normalizedPath.substring(0, lastSlash + 1));

    String withImages = rewriteImageAttributes(html, base);
    String withLinks = rewriteLinkAttributes(withImages, base, pageExtension);
    return withLinks;
  }

  private static String rewriteImageAttributes(String html, Path base) {
    Matcher matcher = IMG_SRC_PATTERN.matcher(html);
    StringBuffer output = new StringBuffer();
    while (matcher.find()) {
      String quote = matcher.group(1);
      String source = matcher.group(2);
      String resolved = resolveRelativeResourcePath(base, source);
      if (resolved == null) {
        matcher.appendReplacement(output, Matcher.quoteReplacement(matcher.group(0)));
        continue;
      }
      String replacement =
          matcher
              .group(0)
              .replace("src=" + quote + source + quote, "src=" + quote + resolved + quote);
      matcher.appendReplacement(output, Matcher.quoteReplacement(replacement));
    }
    matcher.appendTail(output);
    return output.toString();
  }

  private String rewriteLinkAttributes(String html, Path base, String pageExtension) {
    Matcher matcher = LINK_HREF_PATTERN.matcher(html);
    StringBuffer output = new StringBuffer();
    while (matcher.find()) {
      String quote = matcher.group(1);
      String source = matcher.group(2);
      String replacement = rewriteLinkTag(matcher.group(0), quote, source, base, pageExtension);
      matcher.appendReplacement(output, Matcher.quoteReplacement(replacement));
    }
    matcher.appendTail(output);
    return output.toString();
  }

  private String rewriteLinkTag(
      String linkTag, String quote, String source, Path base, String pageExtension) {
    InternalDocLink internal = resolveInternalDocLink(base, source, pageExtension);
    if (internal != null) {
      StringBuilder replacement = new StringBuilder();
      replacement
          .append("href=")
          .append(quote)
          .append("#")
          .append(quote)
          .append(" data-doc-path=")
          .append(quote)
          .append(escapeHtml(internal.path()))
          .append(quote);
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(internal.anchorId())) {
        replacement
            .append(" data-doc-anchor=")
            .append(quote)
            .append(escapeHtml(internal.anchorId()))
            .append(quote);
      }
      return linkTag.replace("href=" + quote + source + quote, replacement.toString());
    }
    String resolved = resolveRelativeResourcePath(base, source);
    if (resolved == null) {
      return linkTag;
    }
    return linkTag.replace("href=" + quote + source + quote, "href=" + quote + resolved + quote);
  }

  private InternalDocLink resolveInternalDocLink(Path base, String source, String pageExtension) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(source);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    normalized = normalized.replace('\\', '/');
    if (normalized.startsWith("#") || normalized.startsWith("data:")) {
      return null;
    }
    String anchor = null;
    int hash = normalized.indexOf('#');
    if (hash >= 0) {
      anchor = normalized.substring(hash + 1);
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, hash);
    }
    int query = normalized.indexOf('?');
    if (query >= 0) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, query);
    }
    normalized = Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String docPath = resolveRelativeDocPath(base, normalized, pageExtension);
    if (docPath == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new InternalDocLink(docPath, sanitizeAnchorId(anchor));
  }

  private String resolveRelativeDocPath(Path base, String source, String pageExtension) {
    String normalized = source.replace('\\', '/');
    if (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    Path resolved = base.resolve(normalized).normalize();
    String candidate = toNormalizedRelative(resolved);
    if (candidate == null || candidate.startsWith("..")) {
      return null;
    }
    String extension = extensionOf(candidate);
    if (extension != null && NAV_PAGE_EXTENSIONS.contains(extension.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
      return isKnownDocPath(candidate) ? candidate : null;
    }
    return resolveDocPathWithImplicitExtension(candidate, pageExtension);
  }

  private String resolveDocPathWithImplicitExtension(String basePath, String pageExtension) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> extensions = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    String preferred = Strings.trimToNull(pageExtension);
    if (preferred != null && NAV_PAGE_EXTENSIONS.contains(preferred.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
      extensions.add(preferred.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
    }
    extensions.add("wiki");
    extensions.add("md");
    extensions.add("markdown");
    extensions.add("yml");
    extensions.add("yaml");

    for (String extension : extensions) {
      String withExtension = withExtension(basePath, extension);
      if (isKnownDocPath(withExtension)) {
        return withExtension;
      }
      String withIndex = withIndexExtension(basePath, extension);
      if (isKnownDocPath(withIndex)) {
        return withIndex;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private boolean isKnownDocPath(String relativeDocPath) {
    String normalized = sanitizeRelativePath(relativeDocPath);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String extension = extensionOf(normalized);
    if (extension == null || !NAV_PAGE_EXTENSIONS.contains(extension.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
      return false;
    }
    if (root == null) {
      return true;
    }
    Path file = root.resolve(normalized).normalize();
    return file.startsWith(root) && Files.isRegularFile(file);
  }

  private static String withExtension(String basePath, String extension) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(basePath);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized + "." + extension;
  }

  private static String withIndexExtension(String basePath, String extension) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(basePath);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (normalized.endsWith("/")) {
      return normalized + "index." + extension;
    }
    return normalized + "/index." + extension;
  }

  private static String sanitizeAnchorId(String anchor) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(anchor);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    while (normalized.startsWith("#")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("[^a-zA-Z0-9_\\-]", "-");
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("-{2,}", "-");
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("(^-+|-+$)", "");
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
  }

  private static String toNormalizedRelative(Path value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.toString().replace('\\', '/');
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
  }

  private static String resolveRelativeResourcePath(Path base, String source) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(source);
    if (trimmed == null || trimmed.startsWith("#") || trimmed.startsWith("data:")) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = trimmed.replace('\\', '/');
    if (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
      if (normalized.startsWith("docs/")) {
        normalized = normalized.substring("docs/".length());
      }
      return RESOURCE_URL_PREFIX + encodePath(normalized);
    }
    Path resolved = base.resolve(normalized).normalize();
    String candidate = resolved.toString().replace('\\', '/');
    if (candidate.startsWith("..")) {
      return null;
    }
    return RESOURCE_URL_PREFIX + encodePath(candidate);
  }

  private static String encodePath(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String[] segments = normalized.split("/");
    List<String> encoded = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String segment : segments) {
      if (segment == null || segment.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      encoded.add(URLEncoder.encode(segment, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    }
    return String.join("/", encoded);
  }

  private static String sanitizeRelativePath(String value) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = trimmed.replace('\\', '/');
    while (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    if (normalized.isBlank() || normalized.contains("..")) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private Path resolveResourcePath(String sanitizedRelativePath) {
    if (root == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Path direct = root.resolve(sanitizedRelativePath).normalize();
    if (direct.startsWith(root) && Files.isRegularFile(direct)) {
      return direct;
    }
    String rootName = root.getFileName() == null ? null : root.getFileName().toString();
    String normalizedRoot = Strings.trimToNull(rootName);
    if (normalizedRoot != null) {
      String prefix = normalizedRoot + "/";
      if (sanitizedRelativePath.startsWith(prefix)) {
        Path trimmed = root.resolve(sanitizedRelativePath.substring(prefix.length())).normalize();
        if (trimmed.startsWith(root) && Files.isRegularFile(trimmed)) {
          return trimmed;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String detectContentType(String relativePath, Path file) {
    try {
      String fromFs = Files.probeContentType(file);
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(fromFs)) {
        return fromFs;
      }
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      // Fall through.
    }
    String extension = extensionOf(relativePath);
    if (extension == null) {
      return "application/octet-stream";
    }
    return switch (extension.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
      case "md", "markdown", "mkd", "mkdown" -> "text/markdown; charset=utf-8";
      case "wiki", "txt", "log", "sql", "properties", "csv", "adoc", "rst" -> "text/plain; charset=utf-8";
      case "yaml", "yml" -> "application/yaml; charset=utf-8";
      case "json" -> "application/json; charset=utf-8";
      case "xml" -> "application/xml; charset=utf-8";
      case "png" -> "image/png";
      case "jpg", "jpeg" -> "image/jpeg";
      case "gif" -> "image/gif";
      case "svg" -> "image/svg+xml";
      default -> "application/octet-stream";
    };
  }

  private static Path resolveRoot(String configuredRoot) {
    String explicit = Strings.trimToNull(configuredRoot);
    if (explicit != null) {
      Path path = Path.of(explicit).toAbsolutePath().normalize();
      if (Files.isDirectory(path)) {
        return path;
      }
      return null;
    }

    Path cwd = Path.of("").toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    List<Path> defaults =
        List.of(
            cwd.resolve("docs").resolve("wiki"),
            cwd.resolve("docs"),
            cwd.resolve("..").resolve("docs").resolve("wiki"),
            cwd.resolve("..").resolve("docs"),
            cwd.resolve("..").resolve("..").resolve("docs").resolve("wiki"),
            cwd.resolve("..").resolve("..").resolve("docs"));
    LinkedHashSet<Path> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Path candidate : defaults) {
      dedup.add(candidate.toAbsolutePath().normalize());
    }
    for (Path candidate : dedup) {
      if (Files.isDirectory(candidate)) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String extensionOf(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int index = normalized.lastIndexOf('.');
    if (index < 0 || index >= normalized.length() - 1) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.substring(index + 1);
  }

  private static String displayName(String rawName, boolean directory) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(rawName);
    if (value == null) {
      return directory ? "Section" : "Page";
    }
    String base = value;
    if (!directory) {
      int dot = base.lastIndexOf('.');
      if (dot > 0) {
        base = base.substring(0, dot);
      }
    }
    Matcher matcher = LEADING_ORDER_PREFIX.matcher(base);
    if (matcher.matches()) {
      String stripped = Strings.trimToNull(matcher.group(2));
      if (stripped != null) {
        base = stripped;
      }
    }
    base = base.replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ').trim();
    if (base.isBlank()) {
      return directory ? "Section" : "Page";
    }
    List<String> words = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String token : base.split("\\s+")) {
      String part = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (part == null) {
        continue;
      }
      words.add(capitalizeWord(part));
    }
    return words.isEmpty() ? (directory ? "Section" : "Page") : String.join(" ", words);
  }

  private static String capitalizeWord(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return "";
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.length() == 1) {
      return trimmed.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    }
    return trimmed.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + trimmed.substring(1);
  }

  private static String sortableName(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToEmpty(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String escapeHtml(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    StringBuilder out = new StringBuilder(value.length() + 32);
    for (int index = 0; index < value.length(); index++) {
      char ch = value.charAt(index);
      switch (ch) {
        case '&' -> out.append("&amp;");
        case '<' -> out.append("&lt;");
        case '>' -> out.append("&gt;");
        case '"' -> out.append("&quot;");
        case '\'' -> out.append("&#39;");
        default -> out.append(ch);
      }
    }
    return out.toString();
  }

  public record TreeModel(List<NavNode> roots, Map<String, NavNode> byId, String defaultSelectionId) {}

  public record NavNode(
      String id, String label, String relativePath, boolean directory, List<NavNode> children) {}

  public record DocPage(
      String id, String title, String html, String raw, String relativePath, List<DocHeading> headings) {}

  public record DocHeading(String id, String text, int level) {}

  public record DocResource(String path, String contentType, byte[] bytes) {}

  private record TocItem(String id, String text, int level) {}

  private record TocNode(TocItem item, List<TocNode> children) {
    private TocNode(TocItem item) {
      this(item, new ArrayList<>());
    }
  }

  private record InternalDocLink(String path, String anchorId) {}

  private record RenderedPage(String html, List<DocHeading> headings) {}

  private record HeadingProcessing(String html, List<DocHeading> headings) {}

  private record SortKey(Integer order, String normalized) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/docs/StitchDocsBrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.docs;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.Icon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.dom.DomListenerRegistration;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import elemental.json.JsonObject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchTreeLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

@Route(value = "docs/browser", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchDocsBrowserScreen extends StitchPage {
  private static final String DOC_LINK_FILTER = "event.target.closest('a[data-doc-path]') != null";
  private static final String DOC_PATH_EVENT_DATA =
      "event.target.closest('a[data-doc-path]').dataset.docPath";
  private static final String DOC_ANCHOR_EVENT_DATA =
      "event.target.closest('a[data-doc-path]').dataset.docAnchor";
  private static final Pattern LEADING_ORDER_PREFIX = Pattern.compile("^\\s*(\\d+)[._\\-\\s]*(.*)$");

  private final StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig config;
  private final StitchDocsBrowserProvider provider;
  private final StitchTreeLayout<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> layout = new StitchTreeLayout<>();
  private final Map<String, StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> nodesById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final Map<String, Integer> pageIndexById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private List<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> pageOrder = List.of();

  public StitchDocsBrowserScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchDocsBrowserProvider provider) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  private StitchDocsBrowserScreen(
      StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig config, StitchDocsBrowserProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(config.pageSubtitle(), ""));
    this.config = config;
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    addClassName("stitch-docs-browser-screen");
    body().addClassName("stitch-docs-browser-body");

    Button refresh = new Button("REFRESH", event -> loadTree(true));
    refresh.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    refresh.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh docs browser");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh docs browser");
    addPageAction(refresh);

    layout
        .setNavHeaderTitle("Docs")
        .setDetailHeaderTitle("Page")
        .setChildResolver(StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode::children)
        .setLabelResolver(StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode::label)
        .setNodeIconRenderer(StitchDocsBrowserScreen::nodeIcon)
        .setNoSelectionContent(
            new StitchEmptyState(
                "No page selected", "Pick a document page from the navigation tree to read."))
        .setNoDetailsContent(
            new StitchEmptyState(
                "No page available", "The selected item does not have a renderable page."))
        .setDetailRenderer(this::renderSelection)
        .withAutoNavSizing(280, 560);
    layout.addClassName("stitch-docs-browser-layout");
    addToBody(layout);

    loadTree(false);
  }

  private static StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .docs()
        .map(StitchDocsFeature::browser)
        .filter(StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private void loadTree(boolean preserveSelection) {
    String currentSelection = preserveSelection ? selectedNodeId() : null;
    try {
      StitchDocsBrowserProvider.TreeModel model = provider.loadTree();
      nodesById.clear();
      nodesById.putAll(model.byId());
      rebuildPageOrder(model.roots());
      layout.setRoots(model.roots());
      String selection =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(currentSelection, model.defaultSelectionId(), firstPageId(model.byId()));
      StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode selected =
          selection == null ? null : model.byId().get(selection);
      layout.treeNav().select(selected);
      if (selected == null) {
        layout.treeNav().collapseAll();
      }
      Notification.show("Loaded " + countPages(model.roots()) + " docs page(s)", 1200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      nodesById.clear();
      pageIndexById.clear();
      pageOrder = List.of();
      layout.setRoots(java.util.List.of());
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load docs browser", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private Component renderSelection(StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return new StitchEmptyState(
          "No page selected", "Pick a document page from the navigation tree to read.");
    }
    if (node.directory()) {
      return new StitchEmptyState(
          node.label(),
          "Select a page under this section from the left navigation.");
    }
    try {
      StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocPage page = provider.loadPage(node);
      return renderPage(page);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return new StitchEmptyState(
          "Unable To Render Page",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(rootMessage(error), "Unable to load the selected document."));
    }
  }

  private Component renderPage(StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocPage page) {
    VerticalLayout container = new VerticalLayout();
    container.setPadding(false);
    container.setSpacing(false);
    container.setSizeFull();
    container.addClassName("stitch-docs-page");

    Span breadcrumb = new Span(breadcrumbLabel(page.relativePath()));
    breadcrumb.addClassName("stitch-docs-breadcrumb");

    Div documentLayout = new Div();
    documentLayout.addClassName("stitch-docs-document-layout");

    Div article = new Div();
    article.addClassName("stitch-docs-article");

    Div content = new Div();
    content.addClassName("stitch-docs-content");
    content.getElement().setProperty("innerHTML", Strings.trimToEmpty(page.html()));
    bindInternalDocLinks(content);
    article.add(content);

    Component pageNav = buildPageNavigation(page.id());
    if (pageNav != null) {
      article.add(pageNav);
    }

    Div inPageToc = buildInPageTocPanel(page.headings());
    if (inPageToc == null) {
      documentLayout.add(article);
    } else {
      documentLayout.addClassName("stitch-docs-document-layout-with-toc");
      documentLayout.add(article, inPageToc);
      bindInPageTocBehavior(container, content, inPageToc);
    }

    container.add(breadcrumb, documentLayout);
    container.setFlexGrow(1, documentLayout);
    return container;
  }

  private void rebuildPageOrder(Collection<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> roots) {
    List<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    flattenPages(roots, ordered);
    pageOrder = List.copyOf(ordered);
    pageIndexById.clear();
    for (int index = 0; index < pageOrder.size(); index++) {
      StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node = pageOrder.get(index);
      if (node != null) {
        pageIndexById.put(node.id(), index);
      }
    }
  }

  private static void flattenPages(
      Collection<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> nodes,
      List<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> ordered) {
    if (nodes == null || nodes.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node : nodes) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (node.directory()) {
        flattenPages(node.children(), ordered);
      } else {
        ordered.add(node);
      }
    }
  }

  private Component buildPageNavigation(String pageId) {
    DocNeighbors neighbors = resolveNeighbors(pageId);
    if (neighbors.previous() == null && neighbors.next() == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Div nav = new Div();
    nav.addClassName("stitch-docs-page-nav");

    if (neighbors.previous() != null) {
      Button previous =
          new Button(
              "\u2190 Previous: " + Strings.firstNonBlank(neighbors.previous().label(), "Previous"),
              event -> layout.treeNav().select(neighbors.previous()));
      previous.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
      previous.addClassName("stitch-docs-page-nav-link");
      nav.add(previous);
    }

    if (neighbors.next() != null) {
      Button next =
          new Button(
              "Next: " + Strings.firstNonBlank(neighbors.next().label(), "Next") + " \u2192",
              event -> layout.treeNav().select(neighbors.next()));
      next.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
      next.addClassName("stitch-docs-page-nav-link");
      nav.add(next);
    }
    return nav;
  }

  private DocNeighbors resolveNeighbors(String pageId) {
    Integer index = pageIndexById.get(pageId);
    if (index == null) {
      return new DocNeighbors(null, null);
    }
    StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode previous = index > 0 ? pageOrder.get(index - 1) : null;
    StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode next =
        index < pageOrder.size() - 1 ? pageOrder.get(index + 1) : null;
    return new DocNeighbors(previous, next);
  }

  private Div buildInPageTocPanel(List<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocHeading> headings) {
    List<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocHeading> source =
        headings == null
            ? List.of()
            : headings.stream()
                .filter(heading -> heading != null && heading.level() <= 3 && Strings.isNotBlank(heading.id()))
                .toList();
    if (source.size() < 2) {
      return null;
    }

    LinkedHashSet<String> seen = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    List<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocHeading> tocHeadings = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocHeading heading : source) {
      String id = normalizeAnchor(heading.id());
      if (id == null || !seen.add(id)) {
        continue;
      }
      tocHeadings.add(new StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocHeading(id, heading.text(), heading.level()));
    }
    if (tocHeadings.size() < 2) {
      return null;
    }

    StringBuilder html = new StringBuilder();
    html.append("<div class=\"stitch-docs-inpage-toc-title\">On This Page</div>");
    html.append("<ul class=\"stitch-docs-inpage-toc-list\">");
    for (StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocHeading heading : tocHeadings) {
      int level = Math.max(1, Math.min(3, heading.level()));
      String text = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(heading.text()), "Section");
      html.append("<li class=\"stitch-docs-inpage-toc-item level-").append(level).append("\">");
      html.append("<a class=\"stitch-docs-inpage-toc-link\" href=\"#");
      html.append(escapeHtml(heading.id()));
      html.append("\" data-anchor=\"");
      html.append(escapeHtml(heading.id()));
      html.append("\">");
      html.append(escapeHtml(text));
      html.append("</a></li>");
    }
    html.append("</ul>");

    Div panel = new Div();
    panel.addClassName("stitch-docs-inpage-toc");
    panel.getElement().setProperty("innerHTML", html.toString());
    return panel;
  }

  private void bindInPageTocBehavior(VerticalLayout scrollHost, Div content, Div tocPanel) {
    tocPanel
        .getElement()
        .executeJs(
            """
            const tocRoot = this;
            const contentRoot = $0;
            const scrollContainer = $1;
            if (!tocRoot || !contentRoot || !scrollContainer) {
              return;
            }
            const links = Array.from(tocRoot.querySelectorAll('a[data-anchor]'));
            if (!links.length) {
              return;
            }
            const headingById = new Map();
            for (const link of links) {
              const id = link.dataset.anchor;
              if (!id) {
                continue;
              }
              const heading = contentRoot.querySelector(`[id="${id}"]`);
              if (heading) {
                headingById.set(id, heading);
              }
            }
            const ids = Array.from(headingById.keys());
            if (!ids.length) {
              tocRoot.style.display = 'none';
              return;
            }
            const setActive = (id) => {
              for (const link of links) {
                link.classList.toggle('stitch-docs-inpage-toc-link-active', link.dataset.anchor === id);
              }
            };
            const computeActive = () => {
              const threshold = scrollContainer.getBoundingClientRect().top + 120;
              let active = ids[0];
              for (const id of ids) {
                const heading = headingById.get(id);
                if (!heading) {
                  continue;
                }
                if (heading.getBoundingClientRect().top <= threshold) {
                  active = id;
                } else {
                  break;
                }
              }
              setActive(active);
            };
            let ticking = false;
            const onScroll = () => {
              if (ticking) {
                return;
              }
              ticking = true;
              requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                ticking = false;
                computeActive();
              });
            };
            scrollContainer.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
            for (const link of links) {
              link.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
                event.preventDefault();
                const id = link.dataset.anchor;
                const heading = id ? headingById.get(id) : null;
                if (!heading) {
                  return;
                }
                heading.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
                setActive(id);
              });
            }
            computeActive();
            """,
            content.getElement(),
            scrollHost.getElement());
  }

  private void bindInternalDocLinks(Div content) {
    DomListenerRegistration registration =
        content
            .getElement()
            .addEventListener(
                "click",
                event -> {
                  JsonObject data = event.getEventData();
                  String docPath =
                      data.hasKey(DOC_PATH_EVENT_DATA)
                          ? Strings.trimToNull(data.getString(DOC_PATH_EVENT_DATA))
                          : null;
                  String anchor =
                      data.hasKey(DOC_ANCHOR_EVENT_DATA)
                          ? Strings.trimToNull(data.getString(DOC_ANCHOR_EVENT_DATA))
                          : null;
                  if (docPath == null) {
                    return;
                  }
                  openInternalDoc(docPath, anchor);
                });
    registration.setFilter(DOC_LINK_FILTER);
    registration.addEventData(DOC_PATH_EVENT_DATA);
    registration.addEventData(DOC_ANCHOR_EVENT_DATA);
    registration.addEventData("event.preventDefault()");
  }

  private void openInternalDoc(String relativePath, String anchor) {
    String normalizedPath = normalizeRelativePath(relativePath);
    if (normalizedPath == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node = nodesById.get(normalizedPath);
    if (node == null || node.directory()) {
      Notification.show("Document not found: " + normalizedPath, 2200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }
    layout.treeNav().select(node);
    scrollToAnchor(anchor);
  }

  private void scrollToAnchor(String anchor) {
    String normalizedAnchor = normalizeAnchor(anchor);
    if (normalizedAnchor == null) {
      return;
    }
    getUI()
        .ifPresent(
            ui ->
                ui.beforeClientResponse(
                    this,
                    ignored ->
                        ui.getPage()
                            .executeJs(
                                "const target = document.getElementById($0);"
                                    + "if (target) { target.scrollIntoView({block: 'start'}); }",
                                normalizedAnchor)));
  }

  private static String normalizeRelativePath(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    normalized = normalized.replace('\\', '/');
    while (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    if (normalized.contains("..")) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeAnchor(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    while (normalized.startsWith("#")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("[^a-zA-Z0-9_\\-]", "-");
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("-{2,}", "-");
    normalized = normalized.replaceAll("(^-+|-+$)", "");
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
  }

  private static String breadcrumbLabel(String relativePath) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(relativePath);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "Docs";
    }
    String[] rawSegments = normalized.replace('\\', '/').split("/");
    List<String> crumbs = new ArrayList<>();
    crumbs.add("Docs");
    for (String segment : rawSegments) {
      String cleaned = cleanBreadcrumbSegment(segment);
      if (cleaned != null) {
        crumbs.add(cleaned);
      }
    }
    return String.join(" / ", crumbs);
  }

  private static String cleanBreadcrumbSegment(String segment) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(segment);
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int extension = value.lastIndexOf('.');
    if (extension > 0) {
      value = value.substring(0, extension);
    }
    Matcher matcher = LEADING_ORDER_PREFIX.matcher(value);
    if (matcher.matches()) {
      String stripped = Strings.trimToNull(matcher.group(2));
      if (stripped != null) {
        value = stripped;
      }
    }
    value = value.replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ');
    value = value.replaceAll("\\s+", " ").trim();
    if (value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    StringBuilder display = new StringBuilder();
    for (String token : value.split("\\s+")) {
      if (token.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!display.isEmpty()) {
        display.append(' ');
      }
      display.append(token.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
      if (token.length() > 1) {
        display.append(token.substring(1).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      }
    }
    return display.isEmpty() ? null : display.toString();
  }

  private static String escapeHtml(String value) {
    String source = Strings.trimToEmpty(value);
    if (source.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    StringBuilder output = new StringBuilder(source.length() + 16);
    for (int index = 0; index < source.length(); index++) {
      char ch = source.charAt(index);
      switch (ch) {
        case '&' -> output.append("&amp;");
        case '<' -> output.append("&lt;");
        case '>' -> output.append("&gt;");
        case '"' -> output.append("&quot;");
        case '\'' -> output.append("&#39;");
        default -> output.append(ch);
      }
    }
    return output.toString();
  }

  private static String firstPageId(Map<String, StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> byId) {
    if (byId == null || byId.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node : byId.values()) {
      if (node != null && !node.directory()) {
        return node.id();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static int countPages(java.util.Collection<StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode> nodes) {
    if (nodes == null || nodes.isEmpty()) {
      return 0;
    }
    int count = 0;
    for (StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node : nodes) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!node.directory()) {
        count++;
      }
      count += countPages(node.children());
    }
    return count;
  }

  private String selectedNodeId() {
    StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode selected = layout.treeNav().selectedItem();
    return selected == null ? null : selected.id();
  }

  private static Component nodeIcon(StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode node) {
    VaadinIcon iconType = node != null && node.directory() ? VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O : VaadinIcon.FILE_TEXT_O;
    Icon icon = iconType.create();
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    Throwable cursor = error;
    String message = null;
    while (cursor != null) {
      String candidate = Strings.trimToNull(cursor.getMessage());
      if (candidate != null) {
        message = candidate;
      }
      cursor = cursor.getCause();
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(message, "Unexpected error");
  }

  private record DocNeighbors(
      StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode previous, StitchDocsBrowserProvider.NavNode next) {}
}

public final class StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig {

    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;

    return enabled;

    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/docs/StitchDocsFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.docs;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchDocsFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "docs";
  public static final String BROWSER = "browser";
  public static final String ENTRY_BROWSER = "docs.browser";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig browser;

  private StitchDocsFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.browser = builder.browserBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig browser() {
    return browser;
  }

  public Optional<StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return BROWSER.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(browser) : Optional.empty();
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    if (!browser.enabled()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchMenuEntry browserEntry =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_BROWSER)
            .withLabel(browser.label())
            .withRoutePath(browser.routePath())
            .withOrder(browser.order())
            .build();
    return List.of(browserEntry);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Docs";
    private int order = 50;
    private final StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig.Builder browserBuilder =
        StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig.builder(BROWSER);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder browser(Consumer<StitchDocsBrowserScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(browserBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDocsFeature build() {
      return new StitchDocsFeature(this);
    }
  }
}
