===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/StitchEntitlementsAdminRow.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Row model for the admin-wide entitlements orchestration surface. */
public record StitchEntitlementsAdminRow(
    String id,
    AssetType assetType,
    boolean enabled,
    String group,
    String namespace,
    String name,
    String lifecycle,
    String sourceHint) {

  public StitchEntitlementsAdminRow {
    id = normalize(id);
    assetType = assetType == null ? AssetType.SERVICE : assetType;
    group = normalize(group);
    namespace = normalize(namespace);
    name = normalize(name);
    lifecycle = normalize(lifecycle);
    sourceHint = normalize(sourceHint);
  }

  public boolean hasNamespace() {
    return !namespace.isBlank();
  }

  public enum AssetType {
    SERVICE,
    DATASET
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/StitchEntitlementsAdminScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchBooleanToggle;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchGroupFilter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsSearch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.StitchEntitlementsAdminRow.AssetType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component.StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component.StitchNamespaceEntitlementsDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component.StitchServiceEntitlementsDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchGroupedResultsPage;

public class StitchEntitlementsAdminScreen
    extends StitchGroupedResultsPage<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> {
  private static final String TYPE_ALL = "ALL";
  private static final String TYPE_SERVICE = "SERVICE";
  private static final String TYPE_DATASET = "DATASET";

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider provider;
  private final StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider namespaceProvider;
  private final ComboBox<String> assetTypeFilter = new ComboBox<>();
  private final TextField namespaceFilter = new TextField();

  public StitchEntitlementsAdminScreen(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig config,
      StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider provider) {
    super(
        runtimeContext,
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(config.pageSubtitle(), ""),
        "Type to filter entitlement assets...",
        "Search entitlement assets");
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.namespaceProvider = new StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider(runtimeContext);

    configureFilters();
    resultsView().setPageSize(25);
    resultsView().grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Admin entitlements asset grid");
    initializeResultsScreen(
        "No entitlement-capable assets",
        "No matching assets were found.",
        "Refresh entitlement-capable assets");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureFiltersBar(
      StitchFiltersBar filtersBar,
      StitchGroupFilter groupFilter,
      StitchResultsSearch searchField,
      com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button refreshAction) {
    filtersBar
        .withFilter(assetTypeFilter)
        .withGroupSelector(groupFilter)
        .withFilter(namespaceFilter)
        .withFilter(searchField)
        .withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Enabled", this::enabledToggle)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.ENABLED)
            .key("enabled")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("8.1rem")
            .resizable(false)
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow>status(
                "Asset Type", row -> row == null ? "" : row.assetType().name())
            .key("assetType"));
    grid.addColumn(StitchGridColumn.group("Group", StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::group).key("group"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Namespace", StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::namespace)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("namespace"));
    grid.addColumn(StitchGridColumn.name("Name", StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::name).key("name"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.status("Lifecycle/Mode", StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::lifecycle)
            .key("lifecycle"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Source", StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::sourceHint)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
            .key("sourceHint"));

    StitchRowActions<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.SHIELD, "Open Entitlements", this::openEntitlements));
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O, "Namespace Context", this::openNamespaceContext)
            .enabledWhen(this::supportsNamespaceContext));
    rowActions.addColumn(grid);
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> loadRows() {
    return provider.loadRows();
  }

  @Override
  protected Comparator<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> rowComparator() {
    return null;
  }

  @Override
  protected String groupValue(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) {
    return row == null ? null : row.group();
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesAdditionalFilters(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) {
    return matchesType(row, selectedType()) && matchesNamespace(row, normalize(namespaceFilter.getValue()));
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesSearch(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row, String query) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return contains(row.assetType().name(), query)
        || contains(row.group(), query)
        || contains(row.namespace(), query)
        || contains(row.name(), query)
        || contains(row.lifecycle(), query)
        || contains(row.sourceHint(), query);
  }

  private void configureFilters() {
    assetTypeFilter.setLabel("");
    assetTypeFilter.setItems(TYPE_ALL, TYPE_SERVICE, TYPE_DATASET);
    assetTypeFilter.setValue(TYPE_ALL);
    assetTypeFilter.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    assetTypeFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Filter by asset type");
    assetTypeFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyCurrentFilters());

    namespaceFilter.setLabel("");
    namespaceFilter.setPlaceholder("Namespace...");
    namespaceFilter.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    namespaceFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Filter by namespace");
    namespaceFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyCurrentFilters());
  }

  private void openEntitlements(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) {
    if (row == null || row.group().isBlank() || row.name().isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    if (row.assetType() == AssetType.DATASET) {
      if (row.namespace().isBlank()) {
        return;
      }
      new StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog(runtimeContext, row.group(), row.namespace(), row.name()).open();
      return;
    }
    new StitchServiceEntitlementsDialog(runtimeContext, row.group(), row.name()).open();
  }

  private void openNamespaceContext(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) {
    if (!supportsNamespaceContext(row)) {
      return;
    }
    new StitchNamespaceEntitlementsDialog(
            namespaceProvider,
            namespaceProvider.resolveNamespaceContext(row.group(), row.namespace(), row.name()))
        .open();
  }

  private boolean supportsNamespaceContext(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) {
    return row != null
        && row.assetType() == AssetType.DATASET
        && !row.group().isBlank()
        && !row.namespace().isBlank()
        && !row.name().isBlank();
  }

  private String selectedType() {
    return normalize(assetTypeFilter.getValue()).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private StitchBooleanToggle enabledToggle(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) {
    boolean enabled = row != null && row.enabled();
    StitchBooleanToggle toggle = new StitchBooleanToggle("Enabled", enabled);
    toggle.setLabel("");
    toggle.setReadOnly(true);
    toggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled");
    return toggle;
  }

  private static boolean matchesType(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row, String type) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (type.isBlank() || TYPE_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(type)) {
      return true;
    }
    return row.assetType().name().equalsIgnoreCase(type);
  }

  private boolean matchesNamespace(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row, String namespace) {
    if (row == null || namespace.isBlank()) {
      return row != null;
    }
    return contains(row.namespace(), namespace);
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/StitchEntitlementsAdminView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

@Route(value = "admin/entitlements", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchEntitlementsAdminView extends StitchEntitlementsAdminScreen {
  public StitchEntitlementsAdminView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider provider) {
    super(runtimeContext, requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  private static StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .entitlements()
        .map(StitchEntitlementsFeature::admin)
        .filter(StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/StitchEntitlementsFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchEntitlementsFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "entitlements";
  public static final String ADMIN = "admin";
  public static final String ENTRY_ADMIN_ENTITLEMENTS = "admin.entitlements";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig admin;

  private StitchEntitlementsFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.admin = builder.adminBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig admin() {
    return admin;
  }

  public Optional<StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return ADMIN.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(admin) : Optional.empty();
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    if (!admin.enabled()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchMenuEntry entitlementsEntry =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_ADMIN_ENTITLEMENTS)
            .withLabel(admin.label())
            .withRoutePath(admin.routePath())
            .withOrder(admin.order())
            .build();
    return List.of(entitlementsEntry);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Admin";
    private int order = 30;
    private final StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig.Builder adminBuilder =
        StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig.builder(ADMIN);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder admin(Consumer<StitchEntitlementsAdminScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(adminBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchEntitlementsFeature build() {
      return new StitchEntitlementsFeature(this);
    }
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.json.StitchEntitlementsJsonView;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;

/** Dataset dual-pane parity dialog based on shared Stitch entitlements primitives. */
public final class StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog {
  private final StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider provider;
  private final String group;
  private final String namespace;
  private final String datasetName;
  private final VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor inheritedEditor =
      new StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor();
  private final StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor overridesEditor =
      new StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor();
  private final StitchEntitlementsDialogShell shell;

  private StitchDatasetEntitlementsState loadedState;
  private StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy currentOverridePolicy = StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty();
  private boolean applying;
  private boolean dirty;

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    this(new StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider(runtimeContext), group, namespace, datasetName);
  }

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsDialog(
      StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider provider, String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.group = require(group, "group");
    this.namespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    this.datasetName = require(datasetName, "datasetName");
    configureContent();
    shell =
        new StitchEntitlementsDialogShell(
            "Dataset Entitlements - " + this.group + "/" + this.namespace + "/" + this.datasetName,
            org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext.of(
                "dataset:" + this.group + "/" + this.namespace + "/" + this.datasetName),
            content,
            () -> dirty,
            this::submitChanges,
            this::reload);
    shell.addPrimaryAction("NAMESPACE", this::openNamespaceContext);
    shell.addPrimaryAction("VISUALIZE", this::openGraph);
    shell.addPrimaryAction("NS JSON", this::openNamespaceJson);
    shell.addPrimaryAction("OVERRIDE JSON", this::openOverrideJson);
    reload();
  }

  public void open() {
    shell.open();
  }

  private void configureContent() {
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset entitlements dual pane editor");

    inheritedEditor.setReadOnly(true);
    inheritedEditor.setAccessOnly(true);
    inheritedEditor.setViewMode(StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor.ViewMode.BY_ACTION);
    inheritedEditor.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Inherited namespace entitlements");
    inheritedEditor.addClassName("stitch-readonly");

    overridesEditor.setReadOnly(false);
    overridesEditor.setAccessOnly(false);
    overridesEditor.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset override entitlements");
    overridesEditor.addClassName("stitch-editable");
    overridesEditor.setValueChangeListener(this::onOverridesChanged);

    StitchSection left = new StitchSection("Inherited from Namespace (Read-only)");
    left.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-pane");
    left.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-pane-left");
    left.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-left");
    StitchSummaryStrip inheritedSummary = new StitchSummaryStrip();
    inheritedSummary.setItems(
        Map.of(
            "Scope", "Namespace",
            "Mode", "Read-only",
            "Surface", "Access / Row Filters / Column Masks"));
    left.addToBody(
        inheritedSummary,
        new Span("Inherited namespace policy (read-only)."),
        inheritedEditor);

    StitchSection right = new StitchSection("Dataset Overrides (Editable)");
    right.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-pane");
    right.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-pane-right");
    right.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-right");
    StitchSummaryStrip overrideSummary = new StitchSummaryStrip();
    overrideSummary.setItems(
        Map.of(
            "Scope", "Dataset",
            "Mode", "Editable",
            "Surface", "Access / Row Filters / Column Masks"));
    right.addToBody(
        overrideSummary,
        new Span("Dataset-local policy overrides (editable)."),
        overridesEditor);

    HorizontalLayout split = new HorizontalLayout(left, right);
    split.setPadding(false);
    split.setSpacing(true);
    split.setWidthFull();
    split.setHeightFull();
    split.setAlignItems(HorizontalLayout.Alignment.START);
    split.addClassName("stitch-entitlements-split");
    split.setFlexGrow(1, left);
    split.setFlexGrow(1, right);

    content.add(split);
  }

  private void reload() {
    applying = true;
    try {
      StitchDatasetEntitlementsState loaded = provider.loadDatasetEntitlements(group, namespace, datasetName);
      loadedState = loaded;
      currentOverridePolicy = loaded.datasetOverridePolicy();

      List<String> actions = resolveActions(loaded);
      inheritedEditor.setLookupProvider(provider.lookupProvider(group));
      overridesEditor.setLookupProvider(provider.lookupProvider(group));
      inheritedEditor.setActions(actions);
      overridesEditor.setActions(actions);
      inheritedEditor.setValue(loaded.namespaceInheritedPolicy());
      overridesEditor.setValue(currentOverridePolicy);

      shell.setContext(loaded.context());
      shell.withJsonPayloadSupplier(this::combinedJsonPayload);
      dirty = false;
      refreshSubmitState();
    } catch (RuntimeException error) {
      loadedState = null;
      currentOverridePolicy = StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty();
      inheritedEditor.setValue(StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty());
      overridesEditor.setValue(StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty());
      shell.setContext(
          org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext.of(
              "dataset:" + group + "/" + namespace + "/" + datasetName));
      dirty = false;
      refreshSubmitState();
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Unable to load dataset entitlements", StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error));
    } finally {
      applying = false;
    }
  }

  private void onOverridesChanged(StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    if (applying) {
      return;
    }
    currentOverridePolicy = policy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : policy;
    StitchDatasetEntitlementsState baseline = loadedState;
    if (baseline == null) {
      return;
    }
    dirty = !Objects.equals(currentOverridePolicy, baseline.datasetOverridePolicy());
    refreshSubmitState();
  }

  private boolean submitChanges() {
    if (!dirty) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      provider.saveDatasetEntitlements(group, namespace, datasetName, currentOverridePolicy);
      Notification.show("Dataset entitlements updated", 2000, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (RuntimeException error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Unable to save dataset entitlements", StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void refreshSubmitState() {
    shell.setSubmitEnabled(dirty);
  }

  private void openNamespaceContext() {
    StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider.StitchNamespaceContext context =
        provider.resolveNamespaceContext(group, namespace, datasetName);
    new StitchNamespaceEntitlementsDialog(provider, context).open();
  }

  private void openNamespaceJson() {
    provider
        .loadNamespaceOverrideDefinition(group, namespace)
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            definition ->
                StitchEntitlementsJsonView.open(
                    "Namespace Entitlement JSON - " + group + "/" + namespace, definition),
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Namespace JSON Unavailable",
                    "No namespace override entitlement definition exists."));
  }

  private void openOverrideJson() {
    provider
        .loadDatasetOverrideDefinition(group, namespace, datasetName)
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            definition ->
                StitchEntitlementsJsonView.open(
                    "Dataset Override Entitlement JSON - "
                        + group
                        + "/"
                        + namespace
                        + "/"
                        + datasetName,
                    definition),
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Override JSON Unavailable",
                    "No dataset override entitlement definition exists."));
  }

  private void openGraph() {
    StitchDatasetEntitlementsState state = activeState();
    StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog dialog =
        new StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog(
            "Access Graph", group + "/" + namespace + "/" + datasetName);
    dialog.setActionOptions(resolveActions(state));
    dialog.setDataProvider(
        request -> {
          StitchDatasetEntitlementsState current = activeState();
          String datasetResourceId = current.context().resourceId();
          String namespaceResourceId = "namespace:" + group + "/" + namespace;
          return
            StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport.datasetData(
                datasetResourceId,
                namespaceResourceId,
                currentOverridePolicy,
                current.effectivePolicy(),
                current.namespaceInheritedPolicy(),
                request);
        });
    dialog.open();
  }

  private Map<String, Object> combinedJsonPayload() {
    StitchDatasetEntitlementsState state = activeState();
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("group", group);
    payload.put("namespace", namespace);
    payload.put("dataset", datasetName);
    payload.put("context", state.context());
    payload.put("namespaceInheritedPolicy", state.namespaceInheritedPolicy());
    payload.put("datasetOverridePolicy", currentOverridePolicy);
    payload.put("effectivePolicy", state.effectivePolicy());
    payload.put("metadata", state.metadata());
    return Map.copyOf(payload);
  }

  private static List<String> resolveActions(StitchDatasetEntitlementsState state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return StitchEntitlementPolicy.resolveActions(null);
    }
    return StitchEntitlementPolicy.resolveActions(
        state.metadata().get("actions"),
        state.namespaceInheritedPolicy().accessPolicy().actions(),
        state.datasetOverridePolicy().accessPolicy().actions(),
        state.effectivePolicy().accessPolicy().actions());
  }

  private StitchDatasetEntitlementsState activeState() {
    StitchDatasetEntitlementsState baseline = loadedState;
    if (baseline == null) {
      return new StitchDatasetEntitlementsState(
          org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext.of(
              "dataset:" + group + "/" + namespace + "/" + datasetName),
          StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty(),
          StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty(),
          StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty(),
          Map.of());
    }
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy effective =
        StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.merge(
            baseline.namespaceInheritedPolicy(), currentOverridePolicy);
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementsState(
        baseline.context(),
        baseline.namespaceInheritedPolicy(),
        currentOverridePolicy,
        effective,
        baseline.metadata());
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(value, field);
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.radiobutton.RadioButtonGroup;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.tabs.Tab;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BiFunction;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubjectType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider;

public class StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor extends VerticalLayout {
  private static final List<String> DEFAULT_ACTIONS = List.of("READ", "WRITE");
  private static final List<String> DEFAULT_MASK_EXPRESSIONS =
      List.of("NONE", "REDACT", "HASH", "NULLIFY", "NULL", "TOKENIZE");

  private final Tab accessTab = new Tab("Access");
  private final Tab rowFiltersTab = new Tab("Row Filters");
  private final Tab columnMasksTab = new Tab("Column Masks");
  private final StitchTabs tabs = new StitchTabs(accessTab, rowFiltersTab, columnMasksTab);
  private final RadioButtonGroup<ViewMode> viewModeToggle = new RadioButtonGroup<>();
  private final VerticalLayout contentHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor accessEditor = new StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor();

  private StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy value = StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty();
  private List<String> actions = DEFAULT_ACTIONS;
  private StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider lookupProvider = emptyLookupProvider();
  private Consumer<StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy> valueChangeListener = ignored -> {};
  private ViewMode viewMode = ViewMode.BY_ACTION;
  private boolean readOnly;
  private boolean accessOnly;
  private boolean syncing;

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsPolicyEditor() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset entitlements policy editor");

    tabs.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset entitlements mode tabs");
    tabs.addSelectedChangeListener(event -> refreshContent());

    viewModeToggle.setLabel("View Mode");
    viewModeToggle.setItems(ViewMode.BY_ACTION, ViewMode.BY_SUBJECT);
    viewModeToggle.setValue(ViewMode.BY_ACTION);
    viewModeToggle.setItemLabelGenerator(
        mode -> mode == null ? "" : mode == ViewMode.BY_ACTION ? "By action" : "By subject");
    viewModeToggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset entitlements view mode");
    viewModeToggle.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          viewMode = Objects.requireNonNullElse(event.getValue(), ViewMode.BY_ACTION);
          refreshContent();
        });

    accessEditor.setLookupProvider(lookupProvider);
    accessEditor.setActions(actions);
    accessEditor.setValue(StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty());
    accessEditor.setValueChangeListener(
        accessPolicy -> {
          if (syncing) {
            return;
          }
          value = value.withAccessPolicy(accessPolicy);
          emitValueChange();
          if (isAccessTabSelected() && viewMode == ViewMode.BY_SUBJECT) {
            refreshContent();
          }
        });

    contentHost.setPadding(false);
    contentHost.setSpacing(true);
    contentHost.setWidthFull();
    contentHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Dataset entitlements editor content");

    HorizontalLayout modeRow = new HorizontalLayout(viewModeToggle);
    modeRow.setPadding(false);
    modeRow.setSpacing(true);
    modeRow.setWidthFull();

    add(tabs, modeRow, contentHost);
    refreshTabVisibility();
    refreshContent();
  }

  public void setLookupProvider(StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider provider) {
    lookupProvider = provider == null ? emptyLookupProvider() : provider;
    accessEditor.setLookupProvider(lookupProvider);
    refreshContent();
  }

  public void setActions(List<String> values) {
    actions = normalizeActions(values);
    accessEditor.setActions(actions);
    refreshContent();
  }

  public void setValue(StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    syncing = true;
    try {
      value = policy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : policy;
      accessEditor.setActions(unionActions(actions, value.accessPolicy().actions()));
      accessEditor.setValue(value.accessPolicy());
      refreshContent();
    } finally {
      syncing = false;
    }
  }

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy value() {
    return value.withAccessPolicy(accessEditor.value());
  }

  public void setValueChangeListener(Consumer<StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy> listener) {
    valueChangeListener = listener == null ? ignored -> {} : listener;
  }

  public ViewMode viewMode() {
    return viewMode;
  }

  public void setViewMode(ViewMode mode) {
    viewMode = Objects.requireNonNullElse(mode, ViewMode.BY_ACTION);
    viewModeToggle.setValue(viewMode);
    refreshContent();
  }

  public void setReadOnly(boolean value) {
    readOnly = value;
    accessEditor.setReadOnly(value);
    refreshContent();
  }

  public void setAccessOnly(boolean value) {
    accessOnly = value;
    refreshTabVisibility();
    refreshContent();
  }

  public enum ViewMode {
    BY_ACTION,
    BY_SUBJECT
  }

  private void refreshTabVisibility() {
    if (accessOnly) {
      tabs.removeAll();
      tabs.add(accessTab);
      tabs.setSelectedTab(accessTab);
      return;
    }
    tabs.removeAll();
    tabs.add(accessTab, rowFiltersTab, columnMasksTab);
    if (tabs.getSelectedTab() == null) {
      tabs.setSelectedTab(accessTab);
    }
  }

  private void refreshContent() {
    contentHost.removeAll();
    if (isAccessTabSelected()) {
      contentHost.add(viewMode == ViewMode.BY_ACTION ? accessByAction() : accessBySubjectSummary());
      return;
    }
    if (isRowFiltersTabSelected()) {
      contentHost.add(viewMode == ViewMode.BY_ACTION ? rowFiltersByAction() : rowFiltersBySubject());
      return;
    }
    contentHost.add(viewMode == ViewMode.BY_ACTION ? columnMasksByAction() : columnMasksBySubject());
  }

  private boolean isAccessTabSelected() {
    Tab selected = (Tab) tabs.getSelectedTab();
    return selected == null || selected == accessTab;
  }

  private boolean isRowFiltersTabSelected() {
    return tabs.getSelectedTab() == rowFiltersTab;
  }

  private Component accessByAction() {
    accessEditor.setReadOnly(readOnly);
    accessEditor.setActions(unionActions(actions, value.accessPolicy().actions()));
    accessEditor.setValue(value.accessPolicy());
    return accessEditor;
  }

  private Component accessBySubjectSummary() {
    VerticalLayout body = sectionBody("Dataset access by subject");
    if (!readOnly) {
      body.add(
          new StitchEmptyState(
              "By-subject editing",
              "Switch to By action mode to add or remove access grants."));
    }
    Map<String, List<String>> grouped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : unionActions(actions, value.accessPolicy().actions())) {
      for (StitchEntitlementRule rule : value.accessPolicy().rulesForAction(action)) {
        for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : rule.subjects()) {
          String key =
              subject.type().name() + " " + Strings.firstNonBlank(subject.label(), subject.id());
          grouped.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> new ArrayList<>())
              .add(action + " " + rule.effect().display());
        }
      }
    }
    if (grouped.isEmpty()) {
      body.add(new StitchEmptyState("No access rules", "No access rules are currently defined."));
      return body;
    }
    grouped.entrySet().stream()
        .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .forEach(
            entry -> {
              StitchSection section = new StitchSection(entry.getKey());
              HorizontalLayout chips = new HorizontalLayout();
              chips.setPadding(false);
              chips.setSpacing(true);
              chips.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
              entry.getValue().stream()
                  .sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                  .forEach(
                      value -> {
                        StitchStatusBadge badge =
                            value.contains("DENY")
                                ? StitchStatusBadge.warning(value)
                                : StitchStatusBadge.success(value);
                        chips.add(badge);
                      });
              section.addToBody(chips);
              body.add(section);
            });
    return body;
  }

  private Component rowFiltersByAction() {
    return rulesByAction(
        "Dataset row filters by action",
        "No row filters",
        "No row filters are defined.",
        this::addRowFilterSection,
        this::rowRulesFor,
        this::rowFilterRuleLine);
  }

  private Component rowFiltersBySubject() {
    return rulesBySubject(
        "Dataset row filters by subject",
        "No row filters",
        "No row filters are currently defined.",
        this::addRowFilterSection,
        value.rowFilters(),
        StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule::subject,
        StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.sortedRowRules(value.rowFilters()),
        this::rowFilterRuleLine);
  }

  private Component columnMasksByAction() {
    return rulesByAction(
        "Dataset column masks by action",
        "No column masks",
        "No column masks are defined.",
        this::addColumnMaskSection,
        this::maskRulesFor,
        this::columnMaskRuleLine);
  }

  private Component columnMasksBySubject() {
    return rulesBySubject(
        "Dataset column masks by subject",
        "No column masks",
        "No column masks are currently defined.",
        this::addColumnMaskSection,
        value.columnMasks(),
        StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule::subject,
        StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.sortedColumnMaskRules(value.columnMasks()),
        this::columnMaskRuleLine);
  }

  private Component addRowFilterSection() {
    StitchSection section = new StitchSection("Add Row Filter");
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();

    ComboBox<String> action = actionCombo("Row filter action");
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementEffect> effect = effectCombo("Row filter effect");
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubjectType> type = subjectTypeCombo("Row filter subject type");
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> subject = subjectCombo("Row filter subject", type.getValue());
    type.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshSubjectDataProvider(subject, event.getValue()));

    Button add = new Button("ADD");
    add.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Add row filter");
    TextArea predicate = new TextArea("Predicate");
    predicate.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    predicate.setWidthFull();
    predicate.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Row filter predicate");
    add.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          StitchEntitlementSubject selected = subject.getValue();
          String expression = Strings.trimToNull(predicate.getValue());
          if (selected == null || expression == null) {
            return;
          }
          addRowFilter(action.getValue(), effect.getValue(), selected, expression);
          subject.clear();
          predicate.clear();
        });

    row.add(action, effect, type, subject, add);
    section.addToBody(row, predicate);
    return section;
  }

  private Component addColumnMaskSection() {
    StitchSection section = new StitchSection("Add Column Mask");
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();

    ComboBox<String> action = actionCombo("Column mask action");
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementEffect> effect = effectCombo("Column mask effect");
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubjectType> type = subjectTypeCombo("Column mask subject type");
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> subject = subjectCombo("Column mask subject", type.getValue());
    type.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshSubjectDataProvider(subject, event.getValue()));

    ComboBox<String> column = new ComboBox<>("Column");
    column.setWidth("14rem");
    column.setItems(value.schemaFields());
    column.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    column.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Column mask column");

    ComboBox<String> expression = new ComboBox<>("Mask");
    expression.setWidth("14rem");
    expression.setItems(resolveMaskExpressions());
    expression.setAllowCustomValue(true);
    expression.addCustomValueSetListener(event -> expression.setValue(event.getDetail()));
    expression.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Column mask expression");

    boolean schemaAvailable = !value.schemaFields().isEmpty();
    Button add = new Button("ADD");
    add.setEnabled(schemaAvailable);
    add.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Add column mask");
    add.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          StitchEntitlementSubject selected = subject.getValue();
          String selectedColumn = Strings.trimToNull(column.getValue());
          String selectedExpression = Strings.trimToNull(expression.getValue());
          if (selected == null || selectedColumn == null || selectedExpression == null) {
            return;
          }
          addColumnMask(action.getValue(), effect.getValue(), selected, selectedColumn, selectedExpression);
          subject.clear();
        });
    row.add(action, effect, type, subject, column, expression, add);
    section.addToBody(row);
    if (!schemaAvailable) {
      section.addToBody(new Span("Schema unavailable. Column mask creation is disabled."));
    }
    return section;
  }

  private Component rowFilterRuleLine(StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule rule) {
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    StitchStatusBadge badge =
        rule.effect() == StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY
            ? StitchStatusBadge.warning(rule.action() + " DENY")
            : StitchStatusBadge.success(rule.action() + " ALLOW");
    Span subject =
        new Span(rule.subject().type().name() + " " + Strings.firstNonBlank(rule.subject().label(), rule.subject().id()));
    Span predicate = new Span(rule.predicate());
    row.add(badge, subject, predicate);
    row.expand(predicate);
    if (!readOnly) {
      row.add(inlineRemove("Remove row filter", () -> removeRowFilter(rule)));
    }
    return row;
  }

  private Component columnMaskRuleLine(StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule rule) {
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    StitchStatusBadge badge =
        rule.effect() == StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY
            ? StitchStatusBadge.warning(rule.action() + " DENY")
            : StitchStatusBadge.success(rule.action() + " ALLOW");
    Span subject =
        new Span(rule.subject().type().name() + " " + Strings.firstNonBlank(rule.subject().label(), rule.subject().id()));
    Span column = new Span(rule.column());
    Span expression = new Span(rule.expression());
    row.add(badge, subject, column, expression);
    row.expand(expression);
    if (!readOnly) {
      row.add(inlineRemove("Remove column mask", () -> removeColumnMask(rule)));
    }
    return row;
  }

  private void addRowFilter(
      String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect, StitchEntitlementSubject subject, String predicate) {
    StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule rule =
        new StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule(
            normalizeAction(action),
            effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect,
            new StitchEntitlementSubject(subject.type(), subject.id(), subject.label()),
            predicate);
    List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> next = new ArrayList<>(value.rowFilters());
    if (!next.contains(rule)) {
      next.add(rule);
    }
    value = value.withRowFilters(next);
    emitValueChange();
    refreshContent();
  }

  private void removeRowFilter(StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule rule) {
    List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> next = new ArrayList<>(value.rowFilters());
    next.remove(rule);
    value = value.withRowFilters(next);
    emitValueChange();
    refreshContent();
  }

  private void addColumnMask(
      String action,
      StitchEntitlementEffect effect,
      StitchEntitlementSubject subject,
      String column,
      String expression) {
    StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule rule =
        new StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule(
            normalizeAction(action),
            effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect,
            new StitchEntitlementSubject(subject.type(), subject.id(), subject.label()),
            column,
            expression);
    List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> next = new ArrayList<>(value.columnMasks());
    if (!next.contains(rule)) {
      next.add(rule);
    }
    value = value.withColumnMasks(next);
    emitValueChange();
    refreshContent();
  }

  private void removeColumnMask(StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule rule) {
    List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> next = new ArrayList<>(value.columnMasks());
    next.remove(rule);
    value = value.withColumnMasks(next);
    emitValueChange();
    refreshContent();
  }

  private void emitValueChange() {
    if (syncing) {
      return;
    }
    valueChangeListener.accept(value());
  }

  private List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rowRulesFor(String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect) {
    String resolvedAction = normalizeAction(action);
    StitchEntitlementEffect resolvedEffect = effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect;
    return StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.sortedRowRules(
        value.rowFilters().stream()
        .filter(rule -> resolvedAction.equalsIgnoreCase(rule.action()))
        .filter(rule -> resolvedEffect == rule.effect())
        .toList());
  }

  private List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> maskRulesFor(
      String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect) {
    String resolvedAction = normalizeAction(action);
    StitchEntitlementEffect resolvedEffect = effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect;
    return StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.sortedColumnMaskRules(
        value.columnMasks().stream()
        .filter(rule -> resolvedAction.equalsIgnoreCase(rule.action()))
        .filter(rule -> resolvedEffect == rule.effect())
        .toList());
  }

  private <T> Component rulesByAction(
      String ariaLabel,
      String emptyTitle,
      String emptyBody,
      Supplier<Component> addSection,
      BiFunction<String, StitchEntitlementEffect, List<T>> rulesFor,
      Function<T, Component> lineRenderer) {
    VerticalLayout body = sectionBody(ariaLabel);
    if (!readOnly) {
      body.add(addSection.get());
    }
    for (String action : unionActions(actions, value.accessPolicy().actions())) {
      for (StitchEntitlementEffect effect :
          List.of(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)) {
        List<T> rules = rulesFor.apply(action, effect);
        if (rules.isEmpty() && readOnly) {
          continue;
        }
        StitchSection section = new StitchSection(action + " " + effect.display());
        if (rules.isEmpty()) {
          section.addToBody(new StitchEmptyState(emptyTitle, emptyBody));
        } else {
          VerticalLayout rows = sectionBody(ariaLabel + " lines");
          rules.forEach(rule -> rows.add(lineRenderer.apply(rule)));
          section.addToBody(rows);
        }
        body.add(section);
      }
    }
    return body;
  }

  private <T> Component rulesBySubject(
      String ariaLabel,
      String emptyTitle,
      String emptyBody,
      Supplier<Component> addSection,
      List<T> rawRules,
      Function<T, StitchEntitlementSubject> subjectGetter,
      List<T> sortedRules,
      Function<T, Component> lineRenderer) {
    VerticalLayout body = sectionBody(ariaLabel);
    if (!readOnly) {
      body.add(addSection.get());
    }
    Map<String, List<T>> grouped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (T rule : rawRules) {
      StitchEntitlementSubject subject = subjectGetter.apply(rule);
      String key = subjectLabel(subject);
      grouped.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> new ArrayList<>()).add(rule);
    }
    if (grouped.isEmpty()) {
      body.add(new StitchEmptyState(emptyTitle, emptyBody));
      return body;
    }
    grouped.entrySet().stream()
        .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .forEach(
            entry -> {
              StitchSection section = new StitchSection(entry.getKey());
              VerticalLayout rows = sectionBody(ariaLabel + " group");
              for (T rule : sortedRules) {
                if (entry.getValue().contains(rule)) {
                  rows.add(lineRenderer.apply(rule));
                }
              }
              section.addToBody(rows);
              body.add(section);
            });
    return body;
  }

  private static String subjectLabel(StitchEntitlementSubject subject) {
    if (subject == null) {
      return "USER unknown";
    }
    return subject.type().name() + " " + Strings.firstNonBlank(subject.label(), subject.id());
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeActions(Collection<String> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return DEFAULT_ACTIONS;
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : source) {
      String normalized = normalizeAction(value);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        dedup.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
      return DEFAULT_ACTIONS;
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static List<String> unionActions(Collection<String> first, Collection<String> second) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>(normalizeActions(first));
    merged.addAll(normalizeActions(second));
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(merged);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private List<String> resolveMaskExpressions() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>(DEFAULT_MASK_EXPRESSIONS);
    for (StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule rule : value.columnMasks()) {
      String expression = Strings.trimToNull(rule.expression());
      if (expression != null) {
        values.add(expression);
      }
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(values);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "READ" : normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private ComboBox<String> actionCombo(String ariaLabel) {
    ComboBox<String> combo = new ComboBox<>("Action");
    combo.setWidth("9rem");
    List<String> actionItems = unionActions(actions, value.accessPolicy().actions());
    combo.setItems(actionItems);
    combo.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    combo.setValue(actionItems.get(0));
    combo.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    return combo;
  }

  private ComboBox<StitchEntitlementEffect> effectCombo(String ariaLabel) {
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementEffect> combo = new ComboBox<>("Effect");
    combo.setWidth("9rem");
    combo.setItems(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY);
    combo.setItemLabelGenerator(StitchEntitlementEffect::display);
    combo.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    combo.setValue(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW);
    combo.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    return combo;
  }

  private ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubjectType> subjectTypeCombo(String ariaLabel) {
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubjectType> combo = new ComboBox<>("Subject Type");
    combo.setWidth("9rem");
    combo.setItems(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.values());
    combo.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    combo.setItemLabelGenerator(type -> type == null ? "" : type.name());
    combo.setValue(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER);
    combo.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    return combo;
  }

  private ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> subjectCombo(
      String ariaLabel, StitchEntitlementSubjectType subjectType) {
    ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> combo = new ComboBox<>("Subject");
    combo.setWidth("16rem");
    combo.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    combo.setItemLabelGenerator(
        value -> value == null ? "" : Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value.label()), value.id()));
    combo.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    refreshSubjectDataProvider(combo, subjectType);
    return combo;
  }

  private void refreshSubjectDataProvider(
      ComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> combo, StitchEntitlementSubjectType type) {
    StitchEntitlementSubjectType resolved = type == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : type;
    combo.clear();
    combo.setDataProvider(lookupProvider.dataProvider(resolved), filter -> filter);
  }

  private VerticalLayout sectionBody(String ariaLabel) {
    VerticalLayout body = new VerticalLayout();
    body.setPadding(false);
    body.setSpacing(true);
    body.setWidthFull();
    body.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    return body;
  }

  private static Button inlineRemove(String ariaLabel, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button("REMOVE");
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.addClickListener(event -> action.run());
    return button;
  }

  private static StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider emptyLookupProvider() {
    return new StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider() {
      @Override
      public LookupResult listApps(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public LookupResult listGroups(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public LookupResult listUsers(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }
    };
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider;

/** Shared by-action access editor used by service, dataset, and namespace entitlement workflows. */
public class StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor extends VerticalLayout {
  private final VerticalLayout actionHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private final Map<String, EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker>> pickersByAction =
      new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private List<String> actions = List.of("READ");
  private StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider lookupProvider = emptyLookupProvider();
  private StitchEntitlementPolicy value = StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty();
  private Consumer<StitchEntitlementPolicy> valueChangeListener = ignored -> {};
  private boolean readOnly;
  private boolean syncing;

  public StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();

    actionHost.setPadding(false);
    actionHost.setSpacing(true);
    actionHost.setWidthFull();
    actionHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Entitlement access actions");
    add(actionHost);
    render();
  }

  public void setLookupProvider(StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider provider) {
    this.lookupProvider = provider == null ? emptyLookupProvider() : provider;
    pickersByAction.values().forEach(map -> map.values().forEach(picker -> picker.setLookupProvider(this.lookupProvider)));
  }

  public void setActions(Collection<String> actions) {
    List<String> normalized = normalizeActions(actions);
    if (normalized.equals(this.actions)) {
      return;
    }
    this.actions = normalized;
    render();
    setValue(value);
  }

  public List<String> actions() {
    return actions;
  }

  public void setValue(StitchEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    syncing = true;
    try {
      value = policy == null ? StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty() : policy;
      List<String> actionUniverse = unionActions(actions, value.actions());
      if (!actionUniverse.equals(this.actions)) {
        this.actions = actionUniverse;
        render();
      }
      for (String action : this.actions) {
        EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker> effectPickers =
            pickersByAction.get(action);
        if (effectPickers == null) {
          continue;
        }
        effectPickers
            .get(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW)
            .setValue(value.subjectsFor(action, StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW));
        effectPickers
            .get(StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)
            .setValue(value.subjectsFor(action, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY));
      }
    } finally {
      syncing = false;
    }
  }

  public StitchEntitlementPolicy value() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> rules = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : actions) {
      EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker> map = pickersByAction.get(action);
      if (map == null) {
        continue;
      }
      StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker allowPicker = map.get(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW);
      StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker denyPicker = map.get(StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY);
      List<StitchEntitlementRule> actionRules = new ArrayList<>();
      actionRules.add(
          new StitchEntitlementRule(
              action, StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, allowPicker == null ? List.of() : allowPicker.value()));
      actionRules.add(
          new StitchEntitlementRule(
              action, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY, denyPicker == null ? List.of() : denyPicker.value()));
      rules.put(action, List.copyOf(actionRules));
    }
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(rules, value.metadata());
  }

  public void setValueChangeListener(Consumer<StitchEntitlementPolicy> listener) {
    this.valueChangeListener = listener == null ? ignored -> {} : listener;
  }

  public void setReadOnly(boolean value) {
    this.readOnly = value;
    pickersByAction
        .values()
        .forEach(
            map ->
                map.values()
                    .forEach(
                        picker -> {
                          if (picker != null) {
                            picker.setEnabled(!readOnly);
                          }
                        }));
  }

  private void render() {
    actionHost.removeAll();
    pickersByAction.clear();
    for (String action : actions) {
      actionHost.add(buildActionSection(action));
    }
  }

  private Component buildActionSection(String action) {
    StitchSection section = new StitchSection(action);
    section.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", action + " entitlement action");
    EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker> byEffect =
        new EnumMap<>(StitchEntitlementEffect.class);
    for (StitchEntitlementEffect effect : List.of(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)) {
      StitchSection effectSection = new StitchSection(effect.display());
      Span subtitle = new Span("Subjects granted with " + effect.display() + " effect.");
      StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker picker =
          new StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker(action + " " + effect.display() + " subjects");
      picker.setLookupProvider(lookupProvider);
      picker.setEnabled(!readOnly);
      picker.setValueChangeListener(ignored -> emitValueChange());
      effectSection.addToBody(subtitle, picker);
      section.addToBody(effectSection);
      byEffect.put(effect, picker);
    }
    pickersByAction.put(action, byEffect);
    return section;
  }

  private void emitValueChange() {
    if (syncing) {
      return;
    }
    value = value();
    valueChangeListener.accept(value);
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeActions(Collection<String> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of("READ");
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String action : source) {
      String normalized = normalizeAction(action);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        dedup.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of("READ");
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static List<String> unionActions(List<String> first, List<String> second) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    merged.addAll(normalizeActions(first));
    merged.addAll(normalizeActions(second));
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(merged);
    sorted.sort(Comparator.comparing(value -> value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider emptyLookupProvider() {
    return new StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider() {
      @Override
      public LookupResult listApps(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public LookupResult listGroups(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public LookupResult listUsers(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }
    };
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchEntitlementsDialogShell.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BooleanSupplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;

/** Shared header/action shell for all Stitch entitlements dialogs. */
public class StitchEntitlementsDialogShell extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final StitchStatusBadge resourceBadge = StitchStatusBadge.info("");
  private final StitchStatusBadge directBadge = StitchStatusBadge.neutral("");
  private final StitchStatusBadge effectiveBadge = StitchStatusBadge.success("");
  private final StitchStatusBadge inheritedBadge = StitchStatusBadge.warning("");
  private final HorizontalLayout headerBadges = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final Component content;
  private final BooleanSupplier dirtySupplier;
  private final BooleanSupplier submitHandler;
  private final Runnable reloadHandler;
  private Button submitButton;
  private StitchEntitlementContext context;

  public StitchEntitlementsDialogShell(
      String title,
      StitchEntitlementContext context,
      Component content,
      BooleanSupplier dirtySupplier,
      BooleanSupplier submitHandler,
      Runnable reloadHandler) {
    super(title == null || title.isBlank() ? "Entitlements" : title.trim());
    this.context = Objects.requireNonNullElse(context, StitchEntitlementContext.of("resource:unknown"));
    this.content = Objects.requireNonNull(content, "content");
    this.dirtySupplier = Objects.requireNonNullElse(dirtySupplier, () -> false);
    this.submitHandler = Objects.requireNonNullElse(submitHandler, () -> false);
    this.reloadHandler = Objects.requireNonNullElse(reloadHandler, () -> {});

    setWidth("86vw");
    setMaxWidth("1200px");
    setHeight("85vh");

    configureHeaderBadges();
    refreshContextBadges();
    body().setSizeFull();
    addToBody(headerBadges, this.content);

    addPrimaryAction("SUBMIT", this::handleSubmitAction);
    addSecondaryAction("CANCEL", this::handleCancelAction);
    cacheSubmitButton();
  }

  public void setContext(StitchEntitlementContext value) {
    context = Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, StitchEntitlementContext.of("resource:unknown"));
    refreshContextBadges();
  }

  public StitchEntitlementContext context() {
    return context;
  }

  public boolean triggerSubmit() {
    if (!submitHandler.getAsBoolean()) {
      return false;
    }
    reloadHandler.run();
    return true;
  }

  public void setSubmitEnabled(boolean enabled) {
    if (submitButton != null) {
      submitButton.setEnabled(enabled);
    }
  }

  private void configureHeaderBadges() {
    headerBadges.setPadding(false);
    headerBadges.setSpacing(true);
    headerBadges.setWidthFull();
    headerBadges.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    headerBadges.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Entitlement context badges");

    resourceBadge.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Entitlement resource");
    directBadge.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Direct entitlement count");
    effectiveBadge.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Effective entitlement count");
    inheritedBadge.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Inherited entitlement count");

    headerBadges.add(resourceBadge, directBadge, effectiveBadge, inheritedBadge);
  }

  private void refreshContextBadges() {
    resourceBadge.setTextValue(context.resourceId()).setTone(StitchStatusBadge.Tone.INFO);
    directBadge.setTextValue("Direct " + context.directCount()).setTone(StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL);
    effectiveBadge
        .setTextValue("Effective " + context.effectiveCount())
        .setTone(StitchStatusBadge.Tone.SUCCESS);
    Integer inherited = context.inheritedCount();
    inheritedBadge.setVisible(inherited != null);
    if (inherited != null) {
      inheritedBadge.setTextValue("Inherited " + inherited).setTone(StitchStatusBadge.Tone.WARNING);
    }
  }

  private void handleSubmitAction() {
    triggerSubmit();
  }

  private void handleCancelAction() {
    if (!dirtySupplier.getAsBoolean()) {
      close();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        () -> {
          if (!triggerSubmit()) {
            return false;
          }
          close();
          return true;
        },
        this::close,
        () -> {});
  }

  private void cacheSubmitButton() {
    footer()
        .getChildren()
        .filter(component -> component instanceof Button)
        .map(component -> (Button) component)
        .filter(button -> "SUBMIT".equalsIgnoreCase(button.getText()))
        .findFirst()
        .ifPresent(button -> submitButton = button);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.MultiSelectComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubjectType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider;

/** Shared APP/GROUP/USER multi-select picker for entitlements editing. */
public class StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker extends VerticalLayout {
  private final EnumMap<StitchEntitlementSubjectType, MultiSelectComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject>>
      selectors = new EnumMap<>(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.class);
  private final EnumMap<StitchEntitlementSubjectType, HorizontalLayout> badges =
      new EnumMap<>(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.class);
  private StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider lookupProvider = emptyLookupProvider();
  private Consumer<List<StitchEntitlementSubject>> valueChangeListener = ignored -> {};
  private boolean syncing;

  public StitchEntitlementsSubjectPicker(String ariaLabelPrefix) {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();

    String prefix = normalize(ariaLabelPrefix);
    for (StitchEntitlementSubjectType type : StitchEntitlementSubjectType.values()) {
      add(buildTypeSection(type, prefix));
    }
  }

  public void setLookupProvider(StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider provider) {
    this.lookupProvider = provider == null ? emptyLookupProvider() : provider;
    selectors.forEach(
        (type, selector) ->
            selector.setDataProvider(this.lookupProvider.dataProvider(type), filter -> filter));
  }

  public void setValueChangeListener(Consumer<List<StitchEntitlementSubject>> listener) {
    this.valueChangeListener = listener == null ? ignored -> {} : listener;
  }

  public void setValue(List<StitchEntitlementSubject> subjects) {
    syncing = true;
    try {
      Map<StitchEntitlementSubjectType, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>> byType =
          new LinkedHashMap<>();
      for (StitchEntitlementSubjectType type : StitchEntitlementSubjectType.values()) {
        byType.put(type, new LinkedHashSet<>());
      }
      for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : normalizeSubjects(subjects)) {
        byType.get(subject.type()).add(subject);
      }
      selectors.forEach(
          (type, selector) -> selector.setValue(Set.copyOf(byType.getOrDefault(type, new LinkedHashSet<>()))));
      refreshBadges();
    } finally {
      syncing = false;
    }
  }

  public List<StitchEntitlementSubject> value() {
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> merged = new ArrayList<>();
    selectors.forEach(
        (type, selector) -> {
          for (StitchEntitlementSubject selected : selector.getSelectedItems()) {
            if (selected == null) {
              continue;
            }
            merged.add(new StitchEntitlementSubject(type, selected.id(), selected.label()));
          }
        });
    return normalizeSubjects(merged);
  }

  public List<StitchEntitlementSubject> valueForType(StitchEntitlementSubjectType type) {
    StitchEntitlementSubjectType resolved = type == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : type;
    MultiSelectComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> selector = selectors.get(resolved);
    if (selector == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> out = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementSubject selected : selector.getSelectedItems()) {
      if (selected == null) {
        continue;
      }
      out.add(new StitchEntitlementSubject(resolved, selected.id(), selected.label()));
    }
    return normalizeSubjects(out);
  }

  private VerticalLayout buildTypeSection(StitchEntitlementSubjectType type, String prefix) {
    VerticalLayout section = new VerticalLayout();
    section.setPadding(false);
    section.setSpacing(false);
    section.setWidthFull();

    Span label = new Span(typeLabel(type));
    label.getElement().setAttribute("role", "heading");
    label.getElement().setAttribute("aria-level", "3");

    MultiSelectComboBox<StitchEntitlementSubject> selector = new MultiSelectComboBox<>();
    selector.setWidthFull();
    selector.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    selector.setPageSize(25);
    selector.setItemLabelGenerator(
        value -> value == null ? "" : normalize(value.label()).isBlank() ? value.id() : value.label());
    selector.setDataProvider(lookupProvider.dataProvider(type), filter -> filter);
    selector.setPlaceholder("Select " + typeLabel(type) + "...");
    selector.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", prefix + " " + typeLabel(type));
    selector.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          refreshBadges();
          emitValueChange();
        });

    HorizontalLayout badgeRow = new HorizontalLayout();
    badgeRow.setPadding(false);
    badgeRow.setSpacing(true);
    badgeRow.setWidthFull();
    badgeRow.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    badgeRow.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", typeLabel(type) + " selected subjects");

    selectors.put(type, selector);
    badges.put(type, badgeRow);

    section.add(label, selector, badgeRow);
    return section;
  }

  private void refreshBadges() {
    badges.forEach(
        (type, row) -> {
          row.removeAll();
          List<StitchEntitlementSubject> selected = valueForType(type);
          if (selected.isEmpty()) {
            return;
          }
          for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : selected) {
            StitchStatusBadge badge =
                new StitchStatusBadge(
                    type.name() + ": " + (normalize(subject.label()).isBlank() ? subject.id() : subject.label()),
                    toneForType(type));
            badge.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", typeLabel(type) + " " + subject.id());
            row.add(badge);
          }
        });
  }

  private void emitValueChange() {
    if (syncing) {
      return;
    }
    valueChangeListener.accept(value());
  }

  private static List<StitchEntitlementSubject> normalizeSubjects(
      List<StitchEntitlementSubject> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, StitchEntitlementSubject> byKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : source) {
      if (subject == null) {
        continue;
      }
      StitchEntitlementSubject normalized =
          new StitchEntitlementSubject(subject.type(), subject.id(), subject.label());
      String key = normalized.type().name() + ":" + normalized.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      byKey.put(key, normalized);
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> sorted = new ArrayList<>(byKey.values());
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparing((StitchEntitlementSubject value) -> value.type().name())
            .thenComparing(value -> value.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
            .thenComparing(value -> normalize(value.label()).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static StitchStatusBadge.Tone toneForType(StitchEntitlementSubjectType type) {
    return switch (type) {
      case APP -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.INFO;
      case GROUP -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.WARNING;
      case USER -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL;
    };
  }

  private static String typeLabel(StitchEntitlementSubjectType type) {
    return switch (type) {
      case APP -> "Apps";
      case GROUP -> "Groups";
      case USER -> "Users";
    };
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, "").trim();
  }

  private static StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider emptyLookupProvider() {
    return new StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider() {
      @Override
