      public LookupResult listApps(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public LookupResult listGroups(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public LookupResult listUsers(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
        return LookupResult.empty();
      }
    };
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchNamespaceEntitlementsDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.json.StitchEntitlementsJsonView;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider.StitchNamespaceContext;

/** Read-only namespace context dialog launched from dataset entitlements. */
public final class StitchNamespaceEntitlementsDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider provider;
  private final StitchNamespaceContext context;
  private final StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor directEditor = new StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor();
  private final StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor effectiveEditor = new StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor();
  private final StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor inheritedEditor = new StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor();

  public StitchNamespaceEntitlementsDialog(
      StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider provider, StitchNamespaceContext context) {
    super("Namespace Entitlements");
    this.provider = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.context = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    setDialogTitle("Namespace Entitlements - " + context.group() + "/" + context.namespace());
    setWidth("86vw");
    setMaxWidth("1200px");
    setHeight("85vh");

    directEditor.setReadOnly(true);
    effectiveEditor.setReadOnly(true);
    inheritedEditor.setReadOnly(true);
    directEditor.setLookupProvider(this.provider.lookupProvider(context.group()));
    effectiveEditor.setLookupProvider(this.provider.lookupProvider(context.group()));
    inheritedEditor.setLookupProvider(this.provider.lookupProvider(context.group()));

    List<String> actions = resolveActions();
    directEditor.setActions(actions);
    effectiveEditor.setActions(actions);
    inheritedEditor.setActions(actions);

    directEditor.setValue(context.namespaceState().directPolicy());
    effectiveEditor.setValue(context.namespaceState().effectivePolicy());
    inheritedEditor.setValue(context.inheritedPolicy().accessPolicy());

    StitchSection direct = new StitchSection("Namespace Direct Policy");
    direct.addToBody(new Span("Direct namespace rules."), directEditor);
    StitchSection effective = new StitchSection("Namespace Effective Policy");
    effective.addToBody(new Span("Effective namespace rules after inheritance resolution."), effectiveEditor);
    StitchSection inherited = new StitchSection("Inherited from Namespace (Dataset Context)");
    inherited.addToBody(
        new Span("Rules inherited by dataset " + context.datasetName() + "."),
        inheritedEditor);

    VerticalLayout body = new VerticalLayout(contextBadges(), direct, effective, inherited);
    body.setPadding(false);
    body.setSpacing(true);
    body.setWidthFull();
    body.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Namespace entitlements read only context");
    addToBody(body);

    addPrimaryAction("JSON", this::openNamespaceJson);
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::close);
  }

  private HorizontalLayout contextBadges() {
    StitchStatusBadge direct =
        StitchStatusBadge.neutral("Direct " + context.namespaceState().context().directCount());
    StitchStatusBadge effective =
        StitchStatusBadge.success("Effective " + context.namespaceState().context().effectiveCount());
    StitchStatusBadge inherited = StitchStatusBadge.warning("Inherited " + context.inheritedCount());
    StitchStatusBadge dataset = StitchStatusBadge.info(context.datasetResourceId());
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(direct, effective, inherited, dataset);
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    row.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Namespace direct effective inherited counts");
    return row;
  }

  private List<String> resolveActions() {
    return StitchEntitlementPolicy.resolveActions(
        context.namespaceState().metadata().get("actions"),
        context.namespaceState().directPolicy().actions(),
        context.namespaceState().effectivePolicy().actions(),
        context.inheritedPolicy().accessPolicy().actions());
  }

  private void openNamespaceJson() {
    provider
        .loadNamespaceOverrideDefinition(context.group(), context.namespace())
        .ifPresentOrElse(
            definition ->
                StitchEntitlementsJsonView.open(
                    "Namespace Entitlement JSON - " + context.group() + "/" + context.namespace(),
                    definition),
            () ->
                StitchDialogs.openInfo(
                    "Namespace JSON Unavailable",
                    "No namespace override entitlement definition exists."));
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/component/StitchServiceEntitlementsDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.details.Details;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchServiceEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider.StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;

/** Service entitlements parity dialog built on the shared Stitch entitlements primitives. */
public final class StitchServiceEntitlementsDialog {
  private static final List<String> DEFAULT_ACTIONS = List.of("START", "INVOKE");

  private final StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider provider;
  private final String group;
  private final String serviceName;
  private final VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor accessEditor = new StitchEntitlementsAccessEditor();
  private final VerticalLayout technicalRows = new VerticalLayout();
  private final Details technicalDetails = new Details("Technical Details", technicalRows);
  private final StitchEntitlementsDialogShell shell;

  private StitchServiceEntitlementsState loadedState;
  private StitchServiceEntitlementsState currentState;
  private StitchEntitlementPolicy currentDirectPolicy = StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty();
  private boolean applying;
  private boolean dirty;

  public StitchServiceEntitlementsDialog(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, String group, String serviceName) {
    this(new StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider(runtimeContext), group, serviceName);
  }

  public StitchServiceEntitlementsDialog(
      StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider provider, String group, String serviceName) {
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.group = require(group, "group");
    this.serviceName = require(serviceName, "serviceName");
    configureContent();
    shell =
        new StitchEntitlementsDialogShell(
            "Service Entitlements - " + this.group + "/" + this.serviceName,
            StitchEntitlementContext.of("service:" + this.group + "/" + this.serviceName),
            content,
            () -> dirty,
            this::submitChanges,
            this::reload);
    shell.addPrimaryAction("VISUALIZE", this::openGraph);
    reload();
  }

  public void open() {
    shell.open();
  }

  private void configureContent() {
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Service entitlements editor");

    StitchSection accessSection = new StitchSection("Access");
    accessSection.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Service access editor");
    accessSection.addToBody(accessEditor);

    technicalRows.setPadding(false);
    technicalRows.setSpacing(false);
    technicalRows.setWidthFull();
    technicalRows.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Service entitlement technical details");

    technicalDetails.setOpened(false);
    technicalDetails.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Service entitlement technical details");

    content.add(accessSection, technicalDetails);

    accessEditor.setValueChangeListener(this::onPolicyChanged);
  }

  private void reload() {
    applying = true;
    try {
      StitchServiceEntitlementsState loaded =
          provider.loadServiceEntitlements(group, serviceName);
      loadedState = loaded;
      currentState = loaded;
      currentDirectPolicy = loaded == null ? StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty() : loaded.directPolicy();
      List<String> actions = provider.actionsFor(loaded);
      StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider lookup = provider.lookupProvider(group);
      accessEditor.setLookupProvider(lookup);
      accessEditor.setActions(actions);
      accessEditor.setValue(currentDirectPolicy);
      shell.setContext(
          loaded == null
              ? StitchEntitlementContext.of("service:" + group + "/" + serviceName)
              : loaded.context());
      shell.withJsonPayloadSupplier(this::jsonPayload);
      refreshTechnicalDetails(loaded);
      dirty = false;
      refreshSubmitState();
    } catch (RuntimeException error) {
      loadedState = null;
      currentState = null;
      currentDirectPolicy = StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty();
      accessEditor.setLookupProvider(provider.lookupProvider(group));
      accessEditor.setActions(DEFAULT_ACTIONS);
      accessEditor.setValue(currentDirectPolicy);
      shell.setContext(StitchEntitlementContext.of("service:" + group + "/" + serviceName));
      technicalRows.removeAll();
      technicalRows.add(
          new StitchEmptyState(
              "Unable to load service entitlements",
              StitchTextSupport.rootMessageOrEmpty(error).isBlank()
                  ? "Unknown error"
                  : StitchTextSupport.rootMessageOrEmpty(error)));
      dirty = false;
      refreshSubmitState();
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Unable to load service entitlements", StitchTextSupport.rootMessageOrEmpty(error));
    } finally {
      applying = false;
    }
  }

  private void onPolicyChanged(StitchEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    if (applying) {
      return;
    }
    currentDirectPolicy = policy == null ? StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty() : policy;
    dirty =
        !Objects.equals(
            currentDirectPolicy.rulesByAction(),
            loadedState == null ? Map.of() : loadedState.directPolicy().rulesByAction());
    refreshSubmitState();
  }

  private boolean submitChanges() {
    if (!dirty) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      provider.saveServiceEntitlements(group, serviceName, currentDirectPolicy);
      Notification.show("Service entitlements updated", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (RuntimeException error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Unable to save service entitlements", StitchTextSupport.rootMessageOrEmpty(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void refreshSubmitState() {
    shell.setSubmitEnabled(dirty);
  }

  private void refreshTechnicalDetails(StitchServiceEntitlementsState state) {
    technicalRows.removeAll();
    if (state == null) {
      technicalRows.add(new StitchEmptyState("No details", "No technical details are available."));
      return;
    }
    Map<String, String> metadata = state.metadata();
    addTechnicalRow("Resource ID", metadata.get("resourceId"));
    addTechnicalRow("Service Type", metadata.get("serviceType"));
    addTechnicalRow("Resolved Policies", joinMetadata(metadata.get("resolvedPolicies")));
    addTechnicalRow("Overrides", joinMetadata(metadata.get("overrides")));
    addTechnicalRow("Inheritance", joinMetadata(metadata.get("inheritance")));
  }

  private void addTechnicalRow(String label, String value) {
    Span key = new Span((label == null ? "Field" : label) + ":");
    Span text = new Span(value == null || value.isBlank() ? "-" : value);
    key.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label + " label");
    text.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label + " value");
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(key, text);
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.expand(text);
    technicalRows.add(row);
  }

  private void openGraph() {
    String resourceId =
        currentState == null ? "service:" + group + "/" + serviceName : currentState.context().resourceId();
    StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog dialog =
        new StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog("Access Graph", group + "/" + serviceName);
    dialog.setActionOptions(accessEditor.actions());
    dialog.setDataProvider(
        request ->
            StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport.serviceData(
                resourceId,
                currentDirectPolicy,
                currentState == null ? StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty() : currentState.effectivePolicy(),
                request));
    dialog.open();
  }

  private Map<String, Object> jsonPayload() {
    StitchServiceEntitlementsState state = currentState;
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("group", group);
    payload.put("serviceName", serviceName);
    if (state == null) {
      payload.put("context", Map.of());
      payload.put("directPolicy", Map.of());
      payload.put("effectivePolicy", Map.of());
      payload.put("metadata", Map.of());
      return Map.copyOf(payload);
    }
    payload.put("context", state.context());
    payload.put("directPolicy", state.directPolicy());
    payload.put("effectivePolicy", state.effectivePolicy());
    payload.put("metadata", state.metadata());
    return Map.copyOf(payload);
  }

  private static String joinMetadata(String value) {
    String normalized = StitchTextSupport.trimToEmpty(value);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return "-";
    }
    return normalized.replace("\n", " | ");
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(value, field);
  }

}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/graph/StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.CheckboxGroup;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.MultiSelectComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Pre;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.tabs.Tab;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;

/** Shared entitlements graph dialog foundation (direct/effective + filter shell). */
public class StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final Tab directTab = new Tab("Direct");
  private final Tab effectiveTab = new Tab("Effective");
  private final StitchTabs modeTabs = new StitchTabs(directTab, effectiveTab);
  private final CheckboxGroup<GraphFilter> nodeFilterGroup = new CheckboxGroup<>();
  private final MultiSelectComboBox<String> actionFilter = new MultiSelectComboBox<>();
  private final CheckboxGroup<StitchEntitlementEffect> effectFilter = new CheckboxGroup<>();
  private final Span counts = new Span("Direct: 0 / Effective: 0");
  private final VerticalLayout graphHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private Function<GraphRequest, GraphData> dataProvider = ignored -> GraphData.empty();

  public StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog(String title, String resourceLabel) {
    super(title == null || title.isBlank() ? "Entitlements Graph" : title.trim(), false);
    setWidth("86vw");
    setMaxWidth("1200px");
    setHeight("85vh");

    modeTabs.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph mode");
    modeTabs.addSelectedChangeListener(event -> refreshGraphHost());

    nodeFilterGroup.setLabel("Visible node categories");
    nodeFilterGroup.setItems(GraphFilter.values());
    nodeFilterGroup.setValue(EnumSet.allOf(GraphFilter.class));
    nodeFilterGroup.setItemLabelGenerator(GraphFilter::label);
    nodeFilterGroup.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph node filters");
    nodeFilterGroup.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshGraphHost());

    actionFilter.setLabel("Actions");
    actionFilter.setWidthFull();
    actionFilter.setPlaceholder("All actions");
    actionFilter.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    actionFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph action filters");
    actionFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshGraphHost());

    effectFilter.setLabel("Effects");
    effectFilter.setItems(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY);
    effectFilter.setValue(EnumSet.of(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY));
    effectFilter.setItemLabelGenerator(StitchEntitlementEffect::display);
    effectFilter.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph effect filters");
    effectFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshGraphHost());

    graphHost.setPadding(false);
    graphHost.setSpacing(false);
    graphHost.setWidthFull();
    graphHost.setHeightFull();
    graphHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Entitlements graph viewport");

    StitchSection modeSection = new StitchSection("Mode");
    modeSection.addToBody(modeTabs);

    StitchSection filtersSection = new StitchSection("Filters");
    filtersSection.addToBody(nodeFilterGroup, actionFilter, effectFilter);

    StitchSection graphSection = new StitchSection("Graph");
    graphSection.addToBody(graphHost);

    Span resource = new Span(Objects.requireNonNullElse(resourceLabel, "").trim());
    resource.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph resource");
    counts.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph direct and effective counts");
    HorizontalLayout contextRow = new HorizontalLayout(resource, counts);
    contextRow.setPadding(false);
    contextRow.setSpacing(true);
    contextRow.setWidthFull();
    contextRow.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Graph resource context");
    contextRow.expand(resource);

    VerticalLayout layout = new VerticalLayout(contextRow, modeSection, filtersSection, graphSection);
    layout.setPadding(false);
    layout.setSpacing(true);
    layout.setWidthFull();
    layout.setHeightFull();

    addToBody(layout);
    refreshGraphHost();
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::close);
  }

  public GraphMode mode() {
    return modeTabs.getSelectedTab() == effectiveTab ? GraphMode.EFFECTIVE : GraphMode.DIRECT;
  }

  public Set<GraphFilter> filters() {
    Set<GraphFilter> selected = nodeFilterGroup.getValue();
    if (selected == null || selected.isEmpty()) {
      return EnumSet.noneOf(GraphFilter.class);
    }
    return EnumSet.copyOf(selected);
  }

  public void setActionOptions(Collection<String> actions) {
    actionFilter.setItems(actions == null ? Set.of() : actions);
  }

  public void setDataProvider(Function<GraphRequest, GraphData> provider) {
    dataProvider = provider == null ? ignored -> GraphData.empty() : provider;
    refreshGraphHost();
  }

  private void setGraphContent(GraphData data) {
    graphHost.removeAll();
    GraphData resolved = data == null ? GraphData.empty() : data;
    counts.setText(
        "Direct: " + resolved.directLines().size() + " / Effective: " + resolved.effectiveLines().size());

    List<String> lines = mode() == GraphMode.DIRECT ? resolved.directLines() : resolved.effectiveLines();
    if (lines.isEmpty()) {
      graphHost.add(
          new StitchEmptyState(
              "No graph relationships",
              "No relationships match the selected mode and filters."));
      return;
    }
    Pre pre = new Pre(String.join("\n", lines));
    pre.setWidthFull();
    pre.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Entitlements graph relationships");
    graphHost.add(pre);
  }

  private void refreshGraphHost() {
    setGraphContent(dataProvider.apply(request()));
  }

  private GraphRequest request() {
    Set<String> actions = Set.copyOf(actionFilter.getSelectedItems());
    Set<StitchEntitlementEffect> effects = effectFilter.getValue();
    return new GraphRequest(
        mode(),
        filters(),
        actions,
        effects == null || effects.isEmpty()
            ? EnumSet.noneOf(StitchEntitlementEffect.class)
            : EnumSet.copyOf(effects));
  }

  public enum GraphMode {
    DIRECT,
    EFFECTIVE
  }

  public enum GraphFilter {
    APP("Apps"),
    GROUP("Groups"),
    USER("Users"),
    ACTION("Actions"),
    RESOURCE("Resources"),
    COLUMN("Columns"),
    ROW("Rows");

    private final String label;

    GraphFilter(String label) {
      this.label = label;
    }

    public String label() {
      return label;
    }
  }

  public record GraphRequest(
      GraphMode mode,
      Set<GraphFilter> nodeFilters,
      Set<String> actionFilters,
      Set<StitchEntitlementEffect> effectFilters) {}

  public record GraphData(List<String> directLines, List<String> effectiveLines) {
    public GraphData {
      directLines = directLines == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(directLines);
      effectiveLines = effectiveLines == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(effectiveLines);
    }

    public static GraphData empty() {
      return new GraphData(List.of(), List.of());
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/graph/StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog.GraphData;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog.GraphFilter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.graph.StitchEntitlementsGraphDialog.GraphRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;

/** Shared graph relationship preparation for service and dataset entitlement dialogs. */
public final class StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport {
  private StitchEntitlementsGraphSupport() {}

  public static GraphData serviceData(
      String resourceId, StitchEntitlementPolicy direct, StitchEntitlementPolicy effective, GraphRequest request) {
    return new GraphData(
        accessLines(resourceId, direct, request, null),
        accessLines(resourceId, effective, request, null));
  }

  public static GraphData datasetData(
      String datasetResourceId,
      String namespaceResourceId,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy direct,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy effective,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy inherited,
      GraphRequest request) {
    List<String> directLines =
        join(
            accessLines(datasetResourceId, direct.accessPolicy(), request, null),
            rowLines(direct.rowFilters(), request),
            columnLines(direct.columnMasks(), request),
            List.of());
    List<String> effectiveLines =
        join(
            accessLines(datasetResourceId, effective.accessPolicy(), request, namespaceResourceId),
            rowLines(effective.rowFilters(), request),
            columnLines(effective.columnMasks(), request),
            inheritanceLines(datasetResourceId, namespaceResourceId, inherited, request));
    return new GraphData(directLines, effectiveLines);
  }

  private static List<String> accessLines(
      String resourceId,
      StitchEntitlementPolicy policy,
      GraphRequest request,
      String inheritedSourceResourceId) {
    if (policy == null || policy.rulesByAction().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<GraphFilter> nodeFilters = nodeFilters(request);
    if (!nodeFilters.contains(GraphFilter.ACTION) || !nodeFilters.contains(GraphFilter.RESOURCE)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> lines = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String action : policy.actions()) {
      if (!matchesAction(action, request)) {
        continue;
      }
      for (StitchEntitlementRule rule : policy.rulesForAction(action)) {
        if (!matchesEffect(rule.effect(), request)) {
          continue;
        }
        for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : rule.subjects()) {
          if (!matchesSubject(subject, nodeFilters)) {
            continue;
          }
          String inheritedSuffix =
              inheritedSourceResourceId == null ? "" : " (inherited from " + inheritedSourceResourceId + ")";
          lines.add(
              "SUBJECT "
                  + subject.type().name()
                  + " "
                  + Strings.firstNonBlank(subject.label(), subject.id())
                  + " -> ACTION "
                  + action
                  + " ["
                  + rule.effect().display()
                  + "] -> RESOURCE "
                  + resourceId
                  + inheritedSuffix);
        }
      }
    }
    return sorted(lines);
  }

  private static List<String> rowLines(
      List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rules, GraphRequest request) {
    Set<GraphFilter> nodeFilters = nodeFilters(request);
    if (!nodeFilters.contains(GraphFilter.ROW)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> lines = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule rule : rules) {
      if (!matchesAction(rule.action(), request)
          || !matchesEffect(rule.effect(), request)
          || !matchesSubject(rule.subject(), nodeFilters)) {
        continue;
      }
      lines.add(
          "ROW "
              + rule.action()
              + " "
              + rule.effect().display()
              + " "
              + rule.subject().type().name()
              + " "
              + rule.subject().id()
              + " :: "
              + rule.predicate());
    }
    return sorted(lines);
  }

  private static List<String> columnLines(
      List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> rules, GraphRequest request) {
    Set<GraphFilter> nodeFilters = nodeFilters(request);
    if (!nodeFilters.contains(GraphFilter.COLUMN)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> lines = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule rule : rules) {
      if (!matchesAction(rule.action(), request)
          || !matchesEffect(rule.effect(), request)
          || !matchesSubject(rule.subject(), nodeFilters)) {
        continue;
      }
      lines.add(
          "COLUMN "
              + rule.action()
              + " "
              + rule.effect().display()
              + " "
              + rule.subject().type().name()
              + " "
              + rule.subject().id()
              + " :: "
              + rule.column()
              + " -> "
              + rule.expression());
    }
    return sorted(lines);
  }

  private static List<String> inheritanceLines(
      String datasetResourceId,
      String namespaceResourceId,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy inherited,
      GraphRequest request) {
    Set<GraphFilter> nodeFilters = nodeFilters(request);
    if (!nodeFilters.contains(GraphFilter.RESOURCE)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    boolean hasInherited =
        inherited != null
            && (!inherited.accessPolicy().rulesByAction().isEmpty()
                || !inherited.rowFilters().isEmpty()
                || !inherited.columnMasks().isEmpty());
    if (!hasInherited) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return List.of(
        "RESOURCE " + namespaceResourceId + " -> RESOURCE " + datasetResourceId + " [INHERITED]");
  }

  private static boolean matchesSubject(StitchEntitlementSubject subject, Set<GraphFilter> filters) {
    return filters.contains(subjectFilter(subject));
  }

  private static boolean matchesAction(String action, GraphRequest request) {
    Set<String> selected = request.actionFilters();
    if (selected == null || selected.isEmpty()) {
      return true;
    }
    for (String candidate : selected) {
      if (Strings.firstNonBlank(candidate, "").equalsIgnoreCase(action)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static boolean matchesEffect(StitchEntitlementEffect effect, GraphRequest request) {
    Set<StitchEntitlementEffect> selected = request.effectFilters();
    if (selected == null || selected.isEmpty()) {
      return true;
    }
    return selected.contains(effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect);
  }

  private static GraphFilter subjectFilter(StitchEntitlementSubject subject) {
    if (subject == null) {
      return GraphFilter.USER;
    }
    return switch (subject.type()) {
      case APP -> GraphFilter.APP;
      case GROUP -> GraphFilter.GROUP;
      case USER -> GraphFilter.USER;
    };
  }

  private static Set<GraphFilter> nodeFilters(GraphRequest request) {
    Set<GraphFilter> selected = request.nodeFilters();
    if (selected == null || selected.isEmpty()) {
      return EnumSet.noneOf(GraphFilter.class);
    }
    return EnumSet.copyOf(selected);
  }

  private static List<String> join(
      List<String> first, List<String> second, List<String> third, List<String> fourth) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    merged.addAll(first);
    merged.addAll(second);
    merged.addAll(third);
    merged.addAll(fourth);
    return sorted(merged);
  }

  private static List<String> sorted(Set<String> source) {
    List<String> out = new ArrayList<>(source);
    out.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.json

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.json;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDialog;

/** Shared read-only JSON inspection helper for entitlements workflows. */
public final class StitchEntitlementsJsonView {
  private StitchEntitlementsJsonView() {}

  public static StitchJsonDialog open(String title, Object payload) {
    StitchJsonDialog dialog =
        new StitchJsonDialog(
            normalizeTitle(title),
            payload == null ? java.util.Map.of("value", "null") : payload);
    dialog.open();
    return dialog;
  }

  private static String normalizeTitle(String value) {
    String normalized = Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, "").trim();
    return normalized.isBlank() ? "Entitlements JSON" : normalized;
  }
}


org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;

public record StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
    StitchEntitlementPolicy accessPolicy,
    List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rowFilters,
    List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> columnMasks,
    List<String> schemaFields,
    Map<String, String> metadata) {

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy {
    accessPolicy = accessPolicy == null ? StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty() : accessPolicy;
    rowFilters = rowFilters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rowFilters);
    columnMasks = columnMasks == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(columnMasks);
    schemaFields = normalizeSchemaFields(schemaFields);
    metadata = metadata == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(metadata);
  }

  public static StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy empty() {
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), Map.of());
  }

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy withAccessPolicy(StitchEntitlementPolicy value) {
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        value, rowFilters, columnMasks, schemaFields, metadata);
  }

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy withSchemaFields(List<String> values) {
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        accessPolicy, rowFilters, columnMasks, values, metadata);
  }

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy withRowFilters(
      Collection<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> values) {
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        accessPolicy, sortedRowRules(values), columnMasks, schemaFields, metadata);
  }

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy withColumnMasks(
      Collection<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> values) {
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        accessPolicy, rowFilters, sortedColumnMaskRules(values), schemaFields, metadata);
  }

  public static StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy merge(
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy inherited, StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy overrides) {
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy base = inherited == null ? empty() : inherited;
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy local = overrides == null ? empty() : overrides;
    LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rows = new LinkedHashSet<>(base.rowFilters());
    rows.addAll(local.rowFilters());
    LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> masks = new LinkedHashSet<>(base.columnMasks());
    masks.addAll(local.columnMasks());
    LinkedHashSet<String> fields = new LinkedHashSet<>(base.schemaFields());
    fields.addAll(local.schemaFields());
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        StitchEntitlementPolicy.merge(base.accessPolicy(), local.accessPolicy()),
        sortedRowRules(rows),
        sortedColumnMaskRules(masks),
        List.copyOf(fields),
        Map.of());
  }

  public static StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy subtract(
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy effective, StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy direct) {
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy resolvedEffective = effective == null ? empty() : effective;
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy resolvedDirect = direct == null ? empty() : direct;
    List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rows = new ArrayList<>(resolvedEffective.rowFilters());
    rows.removeAll(resolvedDirect.rowFilters());
    List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> masks = new ArrayList<>(resolvedEffective.columnMasks());
    masks.removeAll(resolvedDirect.columnMasks());
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        StitchEntitlementPolicy.subtract(
            resolvedEffective.accessPolicy(), resolvedDirect.accessPolicy()),
        sortedRowRules(rows),
        sortedColumnMaskRules(masks),
        resolvedEffective.schemaFields(),
        Map.of());
  }

  public static List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> sortedRowRules(
      Collection<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return source.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).distinct().sorted(rowRuleComparator()).toList();
  }

  public static List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> sortedColumnMaskRules(
      Collection<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return source.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).distinct().sorted(maskRuleComparator()).toList();
  }

  private static Comparator<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rowRuleComparator() {
    return Comparator.comparing(
            (StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule rule) -> rule.action(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.effect().name())
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.subject().type().name())
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.subject().id(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.predicate(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
  }

  private static Comparator<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> maskRuleComparator() {
    return Comparator.comparing(
            (StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule rule) -> rule.action(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.effect().name())
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.subject().type().name())
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.subject().id(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.column(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(rule -> rule.expression(), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeSchemaFields(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String normalized = Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, "").trim();
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        dedup.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
    sorted.sort(Comparator.comparing(value -> value.toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchDatasetEntitlementsState.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Map;

public record StitchDatasetEntitlementsState(
    StitchEntitlementContext context,
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy namespaceInheritedPolicy,
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy datasetOverridePolicy,
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy effectivePolicy,
    Map<String, String> metadata) {

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsState {
    context = context == null ? StitchEntitlementContext.of("dataset:unknown") : context;
    namespaceInheritedPolicy =
        namespaceInheritedPolicy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : namespaceInheritedPolicy;
    datasetOverridePolicy =
        datasetOverridePolicy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : datasetOverridePolicy;
    effectivePolicy = effectivePolicy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : effectivePolicy;
    metadata = metadata == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(metadata);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;

public record StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule(
    String action,
    StitchEntitlementEffect effect,
    StitchEntitlementSubject subject,
    String column,
    String expression) {

  public StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule {
    action = normalizeAction(action);
    effect = effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect;
    subject = Objects.requireNonNull(subject, "subject");
    column = Objects.requireNonNullElse(column, "").trim();
    expression = Objects.requireNonNullElse(expression, "").trim();
    if (column.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("column is required");
    }
    if (expression.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("expression is required");
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "READ";
    }
    return value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementContext.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Objects;

public record StitchEntitlementContext(
    String resourceId, int directCount, int effectiveCount, Integer inheritedCount) {

  public StitchEntitlementContext {
    resourceId = Objects.requireNonNullElse(resourceId, "").trim();
    if (resourceId.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("resourceId is required");
    }
    if (directCount < 0) {
      directCount = 0;
    }
    if (effectiveCount < 0) {
      effectiveCount = 0;
    }
    if (inheritedCount != null && inheritedCount < 0) {
      inheritedCount = 0;
    }
  }

  public static StitchEntitlementContext of(String resourceId) {
    return new StitchEntitlementContext(resourceId, 0, 0, null);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementEffect.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Locale;

public enum StitchEntitlementEffect {
  ALLOW,
  DENY;

  public static StitchEntitlementEffect from(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return ALLOW;
    }
    return "DENY".equalsIgnoreCase(value.trim()) ? DENY : ALLOW;
  }

  public String display() {
    return name().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementPolicy.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class StitchEntitlementPolicy {
  private final Map<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> rulesByAction;
  private final Map<String, String> metadata;

  public StitchEntitlementPolicy(
      Map<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> rulesByAction, Map<String, String> metadata) {
    this.rulesByAction = normalizeRules(rulesByAction);
    this.metadata = normalizeMetadata(metadata);
  }

  public static StitchEntitlementPolicy empty() {
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(Map.of(), Map.of());
  }

  public Map<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> rulesByAction() {
    return rulesByAction;
  }

  public Map<String, String> metadata() {
    return metadata;
  }

  public List<String> actions() {
    return List.copyOf(rulesByAction.keySet());
  }

  public List<StitchEntitlementRule> rulesForAction(String action) {
    String key = normalizeAction(action);
    return rulesByAction.getOrDefault(key, List.of());
  }

  public List<StitchEntitlementSubject> subjectsFor(String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect) {
    for (StitchEntitlementRule rule : rulesForAction(action)) {
      if (rule.effect() == effect) {
        return rule.subjects();
      }
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  public StitchEntitlementPolicy withRules(String action, Collection<StitchEntitlementRule> rules) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> next = new LinkedHashMap<>(rulesByAction);
    String key = normalizeAction(action);
    next.put(key, normalizeRuleList(rules == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rules)));
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(next, metadata);
  }

  public StitchEntitlementPolicy withMetadata(Map<String, String> nextMetadata) {
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(rulesByAction, nextMetadata);
  }

  public static StitchEntitlementPolicy merge(
      StitchEntitlementPolicy inherited, StitchEntitlementPolicy overrides) {
    StitchEntitlementPolicy base = inherited == null ? empty() : inherited;
    StitchEntitlementPolicy local = overrides == null ? empty() : overrides;
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> merged = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : resolveActions(null, base.actions(), local.actions())) {
      List<StitchEntitlementRule> rules = new ArrayList<>();
      for (StitchEntitlementEffect effect :
          List.of(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)) {
        LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject> subjects = new LinkedHashSet<>();
        subjects.addAll(base.subjectsFor(action, effect));
        subjects.addAll(local.subjectsFor(action, effect));
        rules.add(new StitchEntitlementRule(action, effect, List.copyOf(subjects)));
      }
      merged.put(action, List.copyOf(rules));
    }
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(merged, Map.of());
  }

  public static StitchEntitlementPolicy subtract(
      StitchEntitlementPolicy effective, StitchEntitlementPolicy direct) {
    StitchEntitlementPolicy resolvedEffective = effective == null ? empty() : effective;
    StitchEntitlementPolicy resolvedDirect = direct == null ? empty() : direct;
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : resolveActions(null, resolvedEffective.actions(), resolvedDirect.actions())) {
      List<StitchEntitlementRule> rules = new ArrayList<>();
      for (StitchEntitlementEffect effect :
          List.of(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)) {
        LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject> subjects =
            new LinkedHashSet<>(resolvedEffective.subjectsFor(action, effect));
        subjects.removeAll(resolvedDirect.subjectsFor(action, effect));
        rules.add(new StitchEntitlementRule(action, effect, List.copyOf(subjects)));
      }
      out.put(action, List.copyOf(rules));
    }
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(out, Map.of());
  }

  @SafeVarargs
  public static List<String> resolveActions(
      String metadataCsv, Collection<String>... actionSets) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = parseActions(metadataCsv);
    if (merged.isEmpty()) {
      for (Collection<String> source : actionSets) {
        if (source == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (String value : source) {
          String normalized = normalizeAction(value);
          if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
            merged.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    if (merged.isEmpty()) {
      merged.add("READ");
      merged.add("WRITE");
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(merged);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static LinkedHashSet<String> parseActions(String csv) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> parsed = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (csv == null || csv.isBlank()) {
      return parsed;
    }
    for (String token : csv.split(",")) {
      String normalized = normalizeAction(token);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        parsed.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    return parsed;
  }

  private static Map<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> normalizeRules(
      Map<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    source.forEach(
        (action, rules) -> normalized.put(normalizeAction(action), normalizeRuleList(rules == null ? List.of() : rules)));
    List<Map.Entry<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>>> sorted =
        normalized.entrySet().stream()
            .sorted(Map.Entry.comparingByKey(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
            .toList();
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> entry : sorted) {
      out.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
    }
    return Map.copyOf(out);
  }

  private static List<StitchEntitlementRule> normalizeRuleList(Collection<StitchEntitlementRule> rules) {
    if (rules == null || rules.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, StitchEntitlementRule> byEffect = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementRule rule : rules) {
      if (rule == null) {
        continue;
      }
      byEffect.put(rule.effect(), rule);
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementRule> sorted = new ArrayList<>(byEffect.values());
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparing((StitchEntitlementRule value) -> normalizeAction(value.action()))
            .thenComparing(value -> value.effect().name().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> normalizeMetadata(Map<String, String> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    source.forEach(
        (key, value) -> {
          String normalizedKey = Objects.requireNonNullElse(key, "").trim();
          if (!normalizedKey.isBlank()) {
            normalized.put(normalizedKey, Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, "").trim());
          }
        });
    return Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "READ";
    }
    return value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;

public record StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule(
    String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect, StitchEntitlementSubject subject, String predicate) {

  public StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule {
    action = normalizeAction(action);
    effect = effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect;
    subject = Objects.requireNonNull(subject, "subject");
    predicate = Objects.requireNonNullElse(predicate, "").trim();
    if (predicate.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("predicate is required");
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "READ";
    }
    return value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementRule.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;

public record StitchEntitlementRule(
    String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect, List<StitchEntitlementSubject> subjects) {

  public StitchEntitlementRule {
    action = normalizeAction(action);
    effect = effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect;
    subjects = normalizeSubjects(subjects);
  }

  public StitchEntitlementRule(String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect) {
    this(action, effect, List.of());
  }

  public StitchEntitlementRule withSubjects(Collection<StitchEntitlementSubject> value) {
    return new StitchEntitlementRule(action, effect, value == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(value));
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "READ";
    }
    return value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static List<StitchEntitlementSubject> normalizeSubjects(List<StitchEntitlementSubject> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, StitchEntitlementSubject> byKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : source) {
      if (subject == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = subject.type().name() + ":" + subject.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      byKey.put(key, subject);
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> sorted = new ArrayList<>(byKey.values());
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparing((StitchEntitlementSubject value) -> value.type().name())
            .thenComparing(value -> value.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
            .thenComparing(value -> Objects.requireNonNullElse(value.label(), "").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementSubject.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Objects;

public record StitchEntitlementSubject(StitchEntitlementSubjectType type, String id, String label) {

  public StitchEntitlementSubject {
    type = type == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : type;
    id = normalize(id);
    if (id.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Subject id is required");
    }
    label = normalize(label);
    if (label.isBlank()) {
      label = id;
    }
  }

  public StitchEntitlementSubject withLabel(String value) {
    return new StitchEntitlementSubject(type, id, value);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, "").trim();
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/model/StitchEntitlementSubjectType.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model;

import java.util.Locale;

public enum StitchEntitlementSubjectType {
  APP,
  GROUP,
  USER;

  public static StitchEntitlementSubjectType from(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return USER;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "APP" -> APP;
      case "GROUP" -> GROUP;
      default -> USER;
    };
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/provider/StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.CanonicalIds;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEntitlement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
