import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubjectType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchServiceEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Dataset entitlements provider used by the dataset dual-pane parity dialog. */
public class StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider implements StitchEntitlementsProvider {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider lookupDelegate;

  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.lookupDelegate = new StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider(runtimeContext);
  }

  public StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider lookupProvider(String group) {
    return lookupDelegate.lookupProvider(normalize(group));
  }

  @Override
  public StitchServiceEntitlementsState loadServiceEntitlements(String group, String serviceName) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Service entitlements are not provided by this provider");
  }

  @Override
  public StitchServiceEntitlementsState saveServiceEntitlements(
      String group, String serviceName, StitchEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Service entitlements are not provided by this provider");
  }

  @Override
  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsState loadDatasetEntitlements(
      String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedNamespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    String normalizedDatasetName = require(datasetName, "datasetName");

    String datasetResourceId =
        DataEntitlements.canonicalDatasetResourceId(
            normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDatasetName);
    String namespaceResourceId = namespaceScopeId(datasetResourceId);

    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct = directDatasetEntitlements(datasetResourceId, normalizedGroup);
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> effective =
        effectiveDatasetEntitlements(datasetResourceId, namespaceResourceId, normalizedGroup);

    List<String> actions = actionsFor(direct, effective);
    List<String> schemaFields = loadSchemaFields(normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDatasetName);
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy directPolicy = extractDatasetPolicy(direct, actions, schemaFields, normalizedGroup);
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy effectivePolicy =
        extractDatasetPolicy(effective, actions, schemaFields, normalizedGroup);
    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy inheritedPolicy =
        StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.subtract(effectivePolicy, directPolicy);

    int directCount = policyCount(direct);
    int effectiveCount = policyCount(effective);
    int inheritedCount = Math.max(0, effectiveCount - directCount);

    StitchEntitlementContext context =
        new StitchEntitlementContext(datasetResourceId, directCount, effectiveCount, inheritedCount);
    Map<String, String> metadata =
        Map.of(
            "group", normalizedGroup,
            "namespace", normalizedNamespace,
            "dataset", normalizedDatasetName,
            "actions", String.join(",", actions));
    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementsState(
        context, inheritedPolicy, directPolicy, effectivePolicy, metadata);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchDatasetEntitlementsState saveDatasetEntitlements(
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String datasetName,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedNamespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    String normalizedDatasetName = require(datasetName, "datasetName");

    String datasetResourceId =
        DataEntitlements.canonicalDatasetResourceId(
            normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDatasetName);

    StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy incoming =
        policy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : policy;
    List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> bindings =
        toBindings(normalizedGroup, incoming.accessPolicy(), incoming.rowFilters(), incoming.columnMasks());

    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct = directDatasetEntitlements(datasetResourceId, normalizedGroup);
    DiscoveryCache cache = discoveryCache();
    if (bindings.isEmpty()) {
      StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.deleteDefinitions(cache, direct);
      return loadDatasetEntitlements(normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDatasetName);
    }

    DefinitionEntitlement existing =
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.pickPrimaryOverride(
                direct, "overrides/datasets/" + normalizedNamespace + "/" + normalizedDatasetName)
            .orElse(null);
    DefinitionEntitlement updated =
        buildDatasetDefinition(
            normalizedGroup,
            normalizedNamespace,
            normalizedDatasetName,
            datasetResourceId,
            bindings,
            existing);
    cache.upsert(updated);
    StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.pruneDuplicateDefinitions(cache, direct, updated);
    return loadDatasetEntitlements(normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDatasetName);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState loadNamespaceEntitlements(String group, String namespace) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedNamespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    String resourceId = "namespace:" + normalizedGroup + "/" + normalizedNamespace;

    List<DefinitionEntitlement> effective = effectiveNamespaceEntitlements(resourceId, normalizedGroup);
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct = directNamespaceEntitlements(resourceId, normalizedGroup);
    List<String> actions = actionsFor(direct, effective);

    StitchEntitlementPolicy directPolicy = extractAccessPolicy(direct, actions, normalizedGroup);
    StitchEntitlementPolicy effectivePolicy = extractAccessPolicy(effective, actions, normalizedGroup);

    int directCount = policyCount(direct);
    int effectiveCount = policyCount(effective);
    return new StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState(
        new StitchEntitlementContext(resourceId, directCount, effectiveCount, null),
        directPolicy,
        effectivePolicy,
        Map.of(
            "group", normalizedGroup,
            "namespace", normalizedNamespace,
            "actions", String.join(",", actions)));
  }

  public StitchNamespaceContext resolveNamespaceContext(
      String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedNamespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    String normalizedDataset = require(datasetName, "datasetName");

    StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState namespaceState =
        loadNamespaceEntitlements(normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace);
    StitchDatasetEntitlementsState datasetState =
        loadDatasetEntitlements(normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDataset);
    int inheritedCount =
        datasetState.context().inheritedCount() == null ? 0 : datasetState.context().inheritedCount();
    return new StitchNamespaceContext(
        normalizedGroup,
        normalizedNamespace,
        normalizedDataset,
        namespaceState,
        datasetState.namespaceInheritedPolicy(),
        inheritedCount,
        datasetState.context().resourceId());
  }

  public Optional<DefinitionEntitlement> loadDatasetOverrideDefinition(
      String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedNamespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    String normalizedDatasetName = require(datasetName, "datasetName");
    String datasetResourceId =
        DataEntitlements.canonicalDatasetResourceId(
            normalizedGroup, normalizedNamespace, normalizedDatasetName);
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct = directDatasetEntitlements(datasetResourceId, normalizedGroup);
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.pickPrimaryOverride(
        direct, "overrides/datasets/" + normalizedNamespace + "/" + normalizedDatasetName);
  }

  public Optional<DefinitionEntitlement> loadNamespaceOverrideDefinition(String group, String namespace) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedNamespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
    String resourceId = "namespace:" + normalizedGroup + "/" + normalizedNamespace;
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct = directNamespaceEntitlements(resourceId, normalizedGroup);
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.pickPrimaryOverride(
        direct, "overrides/namespaces/" + normalizedNamespace);
  }

  private StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy extractDatasetPolicy(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> source,
      List<String> actions,
      List<String> schemaFields,
      String group) {
    StitchEntitlementPolicy access = extractAccessPolicy(source, actions, group);
    List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> masks = new ArrayList<>();

    for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding binding :
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.activeBindings(source)) {
      String action = normalizeDatasetAction(binding.action());
      StitchEntitlementEffect effect = StitchEntitlementEffect.from(binding.effect());
      StitchEntitlementSubject subject = toSubject(binding.subject(), group);
      if (subject == null) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet obligations = binding.obligations();
      if (obligations == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (obligations.rowFilters() != null) {
        for (DefinitionEntitlement.RowFilter rowFilter : obligations.rowFilters()) {
          String predicate = normalize(rowFilter == null ? null : rowFilter.expression());
          if (!predicate.isBlank()) {
            rows.add(new StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule(action, effect, subject, predicate));
          }
        }
      }
      if (obligations.columnsMask() != null) {
        for (DefinitionEntitlement.ColumnMask columnMask : obligations.columnsMask()) {
          String column = normalize(columnMask == null ? null : columnMask.column());
          String expression =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  normalize(columnMask == null ? null : columnMask.replacement()),
                  normalize(columnMask == null ? null : columnMask.strategy()));
          if (!column.isBlank() && !expression.isBlank()) {
            masks.add(new StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule(action, effect, subject, column, expression));
          }
        }
      }
    }

    return new StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy(
        access,
        StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.sortedRowRules(rows),
        StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.sortedColumnMaskRules(masks),
        schemaFields,
        Map.of());
  }

  private StitchEntitlementPolicy extractAccessPolicy(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> source, List<String> actions, String group) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>>> byAction =
        new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : actions) {
      byAction.put(action, emptyEffectMap());
    }

    for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding binding :
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.activeBindings(source)) {
      String action = normalizeDatasetAction(binding.action());
      StitchEntitlementSubject subject = toSubject(binding.subject(), group);
      if (subject == null) {
        continue;
      }
      byAction.computeIfAbsent(action, ignored -> emptyEffectMap());
      byAction
          .get(action)
          .get(StitchEntitlementEffect.from(binding.effect()))
          .add(subject);
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> rules = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : sortedActions(byAction.keySet())) {
      EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>> map =
          byAction.getOrDefault(action, emptyEffectMap());
      rules.put(
          action,
          List.of(
              new StitchEntitlementRule(
                  action,
                  StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW,
                  sortedSubjects(map.get(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW))),
              new StitchEntitlementRule(
                  action,
                  StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY,
                  sortedSubjects(map.get(StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)))));
    }
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(rules, Map.of());
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> toBindings(
      String group,
      StitchEntitlementPolicy accessPolicy,
      List<StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule> rowRules,
      List<StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule> maskRules) {
    LinkedHashMap<BindingKey, BindingAccumulator> byKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : accessPolicy.actions()) {
      for (StitchEntitlementRule rule : accessPolicy.rulesForAction(action)) {
        for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : rule.subjects()) {
          bindingAccumulator(byKey, group, action, rule.effect(), subject);
        }
      }
    }
    for (StitchEntitlementRowFilterRule rowRule : rowRules) {
      BindingAccumulator accumulator =
          bindingAccumulator(byKey, group, rowRule.action(), rowRule.effect(), rowRule.subject());
      accumulator.rowPredicates().add(rowRule.predicate());
    }
    for (StitchEntitlementColumnMaskRule maskRule : maskRules) {
      BindingAccumulator accumulator =
          bindingAccumulator(byKey, group, maskRule.action(), maskRule.effect(), maskRule.subject());
      accumulator.columnMasks().put(maskRule.column(), maskRule.expression());
    }

    List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> out = new ArrayList<>();
    int index = 0;
    for (Map.Entry<BindingKey, BindingAccumulator> entry : byKey.entrySet()) {
      BindingKey key = entry.getKey();
      String subject = toCanonicalSubject(group, key.subject());
      if (subject == null) {
        continue;
      }
      BindingAccumulator value = entry.getValue();
      List<DefinitionEntitlement.RowFilter> filters = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String predicate : value.rowPredicates()) {
        String normalized = normalize(predicate);
        if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
          filters.add(new DefinitionEntitlement.RowFilter(normalized, Boolean.FALSE, Map.of()));
        }
      }
      List<DefinitionEntitlement.ColumnMask> columnMasks = new ArrayList<>();
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> mask : value.columnMasks().entrySet()) {
        String column = normalize(mask.getKey());
        String expression = normalize(mask.getValue());
        if (!column.isBlank() && !expression.isBlank()) {
          columnMasks.add(new DefinitionEntitlement.ColumnMask(column, expression, null, expression));
        }
      }
      DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet obligations =
          new DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet(
              List.copyOf(filters), List.of(), List.copyOf(columnMasks), List.of(), List.of(), Map.of());
      out.add(
          new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding(
              "stitch-dataset-"
                  + normalizeToken(key.action())
                  + "-"
                  + normalizeToken(key.effect().name())
                  + "-"
                  + normalizeToken(key.subject().type().name())
                  + "-"
                  + index++,
              subject,
              wireAction(key.action()),
              key.effect().display(),
              true,
              obligations,
              Map.of(),
              Map.of()));
    }
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }

  private BindingAccumulator bindingAccumulator(
      Map<BindingKey, BindingAccumulator> byKey,
      String group,
      String action,
      StitchEntitlementEffect effect,
      StitchEntitlementSubject subject) {
    StitchEntitlementSubject normalized =
        new StitchEntitlementSubject(
            subject == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : subject.type(),
            subject == null ? "" : subject.id(),
            subject == null ? "" : subject.label());
    BindingKey key =
        new BindingKey(
            normalize(group),
            normalizeDatasetAction(action),
            effect == null ? StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW : effect,
            normalized);
    return byKey.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> new BindingAccumulator());
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement> directDatasetEntitlements(String datasetResourceId, String group) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.directEntitlementsByGroup(
        scopedEntitlements(group, Set.of(datasetResourceId), Set.of("dataset")), group);
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement> effectiveDatasetEntitlements(
      String datasetResourceId, String namespaceResourceId, String group) {
    return scopedEntitlements(
        group,
        namespaceResourceId.isBlank()
            ? Set.of(datasetResourceId)
            : Set.of(datasetResourceId, namespaceResourceId),
        Set.of("dataset", "namespace"));
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement> effectiveNamespaceEntitlements(String resourceId, String group) {
    return scopedEntitlements(group, Set.of(resourceId), Set.of("namespace"));
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement> directNamespaceEntitlements(String resourceId, String group) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.directEntitlementsByGroup(
        scopedEntitlements(group, Set.of(resourceId), Set.of("namespace")), group);
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement> scopedEntitlements(
      String group, Set<String> scopeIds, Set<String> allowedScopeTypes) {
    Set<String> normalizedScopes = scopeIds.stream().map(StitchDatasetEntitlementsProvider::normalize).collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toSet());
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> out = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : discoveryCache().list(DefinitionEntitlement.class)) {
      if (!enabled(entitlement == null || entitlement.envelope() == null ? null : entitlement.envelope().enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      String sourceGroup = StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.envelopeGroup(entitlement);
      if (!sourceGroup.equals(normalize(group)) && !PLATFORM_GROUP.equals(sourceGroup)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!normalizedScopes.contains(canonicalScope(entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.scopeId()))) {
        continue;
      }
      String scopeType = normalize(entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.scopeType());
      if (!scopeType.isBlank() && !allowedScopeTypes.contains(scopeType)) {
        continue;
      }
      out.add(entitlement);
    }
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }

  private List<String> loadSchemaFields(String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    DefinitionDataset dataset = requireDataset(group, namespace, datasetName);
    String schemaName =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            normalize(dataset == null || dataset.view() == null ? null : dataset.view().schemaName()),
            schemaFromIngest(group, namespace, datasetName));
    if (schemaName == null || schemaName.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Optional<SchemaModel> schema = session.schemas().get(group, schemaName);
    if (schema.isEmpty()) {
      schema = session.schemas().get(schemaName);
    }
    if (schema.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return schema.get().getFields().stream()
        .map(field -> normalize(field == null ? null : field.name()))
        .filter(value -> !value.isBlank())
        .sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .distinct()
        .toList();
  }

  private String schemaFromIngest(String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    String datasetResourceId = DataEntitlements.canonicalDatasetResourceId(group, namespace, datasetName);
    for (DefinitionIngest ingest : discoveryCache().list(DefinitionIngest.class)) {
      String ingestDatasetId = canonicalScope(ingest == null ? null : ingest.datasetId());
      if (Objects.equals(ingestDatasetId, datasetResourceId)) {
        return normalize(ingest.outputSchemaId());
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  private DefinitionDataset requireDataset(String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    return discoveryCache()
        .get(DefinitionDataset.class, group, namespace + "/" + datasetName)
        .orElseThrow(
            () ->
                new IllegalArgumentException(
                    "Dataset not found: " + group + "/" + namespace + "/" + datasetName));
  }

  private DefinitionEntitlement buildDatasetDefinition(
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String datasetName,
      String resourceId,
      List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> bindings,
      DefinitionEntitlement existing) {
    String actor = Strings.firstNonBlank(StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject(), "service:stitch");
    String now = Instant.now().toString();
    DefinitionEnvelope previous = existing == null ? null : existing.envelope();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT,
            "overrides/datasets/" + namespace + "/" + datasetName,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(
                previous == null ? null : previous.uuid(), "ent-dataset-" + namespace + "-" + datasetName),
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.createdTimeUtc(), now),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.createdBy(), actor),
            now,
            actor);
    DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument policy =
        new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument(
            "1.0",
            resourceId,
            group,
            namespace + "/" + datasetName,
            "DATASET",
            "DATASET",
            resourceId,
            "DATASET",
            "dataset-" + datasetName,
            "Dataset entitlements managed by Stitch",
            "1",
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            Map.of(),
            List.copyOf(bindings));
    return new DefinitionEntitlement(
        envelope,
        "dataset",
        resourceId,
        List.of(policy),
        List.of(),
        Map.of("managedBy", "stitch"),
        List.of("Stitch managed dataset entitlements"));
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Discovery cache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private static int policyCount(List<DefinitionEntitlement> definitions) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.policyCount(definitions);
  }

  private static EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>> emptyEffectMap() {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.emptyEffectMap();
  }

  private static List<StitchEntitlementSubject> sortedSubjects(Set<StitchEntitlementSubject> source) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.sortedSubjects(source);
  }

  private static List<String> actionsFor(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct, List<DefinitionEntitlement> effective) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> actions = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    collectActions(direct, actions);
    collectActions(effective, actions);
    return StitchEntitlementPolicy.resolveActions(null, actions);
  }

  private static void collectActions(List<DefinitionEntitlement> definitions, Set<String> sink) {
    for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding binding :
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.activeBindings(definitions)) {
      sink.add(normalizeDatasetAction(binding.action()));
    }
  }

  private static List<String> sortedActions(Set<String> source) {
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(source == null ? Set.of() : source);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static String normalizeDatasetAction(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset entitlement action is required.");
    }
    if ("READ".equals(normalized) || "WRITE".equals(normalized)) {
      return normalized;
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("Unsupported dataset entitlement action: " + value);
  }

  private static String wireAction(String action) {
    return switch (normalizeDatasetAction(action)) {
      case "WRITE" -> EntitlementsAction.WRITE.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      case "READ" -> EntitlementsAction.READ.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported dataset entitlement action: " + action);
    };
  }

  private static StitchEntitlementSubject toSubject(String subject, String group) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.toSubject(subject, group, false);
  }

  private static String toCanonicalSubject(String group, StitchEntitlementSubject subject) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.toCanonicalSubject(group, subject, true);
  }

  private static String namespaceScopeId(String datasetScopeId) {
    CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed = CanonicalIds.parse(datasetScopeId);
    return "namespace:" + parsed.group() + "/" + parsed.namespace();
  }

  private static String canonicalScope(String scopeId) {
    return CanonicalIds.parse(require(scopeId, "scopeId")).canonical();
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.normalize(value);
  }

  private static boolean enabled(Boolean value) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.enabled(value);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.require(value, fieldName);
  }

  private static String normalizeToken(String value) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.normalizeToken(value);
  }

  private record BindingKey(
      String group, String action, StitchEntitlementEffect effect, StitchEntitlementSubject subject) {}

  private record BindingAccumulator(
      LinkedHashSet<String> rowPredicates, LinkedHashMap<String, String> columnMasks) {
    private BindingAccumulator() {
      this(new LinkedHashSet<>(), new LinkedHashMap<>());
    }
  }

  public record StitchNamespaceContext(
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String datasetName,
      StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState namespaceState,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy inheritedPolicy,
      int inheritedCount,
      String datasetResourceId) {
    public StitchNamespaceContext {
      group = require(group, "group");
      namespace = require(namespace, "namespace");
      datasetName = require(datasetName, "datasetName");
      namespaceState =
          namespaceState == null
              ? new StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState(
                  StitchEntitlementContext.of("namespace:" + group + "/" + namespace),
                  StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty(),
                  StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty(),
                  Map.of())
              : namespaceState;
      inheritedPolicy = inheritedPolicy == null ? StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy.empty() : inheritedPolicy;
      inheritedCount = Math.max(0, inheritedCount);
      datasetResourceId = require(datasetResourceId, "datasetResourceId");
    }

    public String namespaceResourceId() {
      return "namespace:" + group + "/" + namespace;
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/provider/StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets.StitchAssetsDataProviders;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets.StitchAssetsFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets.StitchAssetsRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data.StitchDatasetsProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data.StitchDatasetsRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.StitchEntitlementsAdminRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.StitchEntitlementsAdminRow.AssetType;

/** Admin entitlements browser provider that orchestrates service + dataset assets. */
public class StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider {
  private final StitchAssetsDataProviders assetsDataProviders;
  private final StitchDatasetsProvider datasetsProvider;

  public StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider(
      StitchAssetsDataProviders assetsDataProviders, StitchDatasetsProvider datasetsProvider) {
    this.assetsDataProviders = Objects.requireNonNull(assetsDataProviders, "assetsDataProviders");
    this.datasetsProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(datasetsProvider, "datasetsProvider");
  }

  public List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> loadRows() {
    List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    rows.addAll(loadServiceRows());
    rows.addAll(loadDatasetRows());
    rows.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(
                (StitchEntitlementsAdminRow row) -> row.assetType().name(),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::group, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::namespace, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(StitchEntitlementsAdminRow::name, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> loadServiceRows() {
    List<StitchAssetsRow> services =
        assetsDataProviders.provider(StitchAssetsFeature.SERVICES).loadRows();
    if (services == null || services.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(services.size());
    for (StitchAssetsRow service : services) {
      if (service == null || service.group().isBlank() || service.name().isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      String namespace = service.field("namespace");
      String lifecycle = lifecycle(service.sourceObject());
      String hint = Strings.firstNonBlank(service.field("serviceType"), service.field("resourceId"));
      rows.add(
          new StitchEntitlementsAdminRow(
              "service::" + service.group() + "::" + service.name(),
              AssetType.SERVICE,
              service.enabled(),
              service.group(),
              namespace,
              service.name(),
              lifecycle,
              hint));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> loadDatasetRows() {
    List<StitchDatasetsRow> datasets = datasetsProvider.loadRows();
    if (datasets == null || datasets.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementsAdminRow> rows = new ArrayList<>(datasets.size());
    for (StitchDatasetsRow dataset : datasets) {
      if (dataset == null
          || dataset.group().isBlank()
          || dataset.namespace().isBlank()
          || dataset.name().isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      rows.add(
          new StitchEntitlementsAdminRow(
              "dataset::" + dataset.group() + "::" + dataset.namespace() + "::" + dataset.name(),
              AssetType.DATASET,
              dataset.enabled(),
              dataset.group(),
              dataset.namespace(),
              dataset.name(),
              dataset.mode(),
              Strings.firstNonBlank(dataset.datasetType(), dataset.sourceType())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static String lifecycle(Object sourceObject) {
    if (sourceObject instanceof DefinitionService service) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = service.envelope();
      return normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.lifecycleStatus());
    }
    if (sourceObject instanceof DefinitionDataset dataset) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = dataset.envelope();
      return normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.lifecycleStatus());
    }
    return "";
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/provider/StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider;

import com.vaadin.flow.data.provider.CallbackDataProvider;
import com.vaadin.flow.data.provider.Query;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.stream.Stream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubjectType;

/**
 * Shared data-driven lookup contract for entitlement subject pickers.
 *
 * <p>Implementations are expected to return stable, sorted results and support lazy query windows.
 */
public interface StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider {

  LookupResult listApps(String filterText, int offset, int limit);

  LookupResult listGroups(String filterText, int offset, int limit);

  LookupResult listUsers(String filterText, int offset, int limit);

  default CallbackDataProvider<StitchEntitlementSubject, String> dataProvider(
      StitchEntitlementSubjectType type) {
    StitchEntitlementSubjectType resolvedType =
        type == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : type;
    return new CallbackDataProvider<>(
        query -> fetchForType(resolvedType, query), query -> countForType(resolvedType, query));
  }

  default LookupResult lookup(
      StitchEntitlementSubjectType type, String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
    StitchEntitlementSubjectType resolvedType =
        type == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : type;
    return switch (resolvedType) {
      case APP -> listApps(filterText, offset, limit);
      case GROUP -> listGroups(filterText, offset, limit);
      case USER -> listUsers(filterText, offset, limit);
    };
  }

  static LookupResult sortedDistinct(
      Collection<StitchEntitlementSubject> source,
      StitchEntitlementSubjectType expectedType,
      String filterText,
      int offset,
      int limit) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return LookupResult.empty();
    }
    String filter = normalizeFilter(filterText);
    StitchEntitlementSubjectType resolvedType =
        expectedType == null ? StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER : expectedType;
    Map<String, StitchEntitlementSubject> dedup = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchEntitlementSubject candidate : source) {
      if (candidate == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (candidate.type() != resolvedType) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = normalize(candidate.id());
      if (id.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!filter.isBlank()) {
        String haystack =
            (normalize(candidate.id()) + " " + normalize(candidate.label())).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (!haystack.contains(filter)) {
          continue;
        }
      }
      dedup.put(id.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), candidate);
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup.values());
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(
                (StitchEntitlementSubject value) -> normalize(value.label()).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
            .thenComparing(value -> normalize(value.id()).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    int safeOffset = Math.max(0, offset);
    int safeLimit = limit <= 0 ? sorted.size() : limit;
    if (safeOffset >= sorted.size()) {
      return new LookupResult(List.of(), sorted.size());
    }
    int end = Math.min(sorted.size(), safeOffset + safeLimit);
    return new LookupResult(sorted.subList(safeOffset, end), sorted.size());
  }

  private Stream<StitchEntitlementSubject> fetchForType(
      StitchEntitlementSubjectType type, Query<StitchEntitlementSubject, String> query) {
    String filter = query.getFilter().orElse("");
    LookupResult result = lookup(type, filter, query.getOffset(), query.getLimit());
    return result.items().stream();
  }

  private int countForType(
      StitchEntitlementSubjectType type, Query<StitchEntitlementSubject, String> query) {
    String filter = query.getFilter().orElse("");
    return lookup(type, filter, 0, 1).totalCount();
  }

  private static String normalizeFilter(String value) {
    return normalize(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, "").trim();
  }

  record LookupResult(List<StitchEntitlementSubject> items, int totalCount) {
    public LookupResult {
      items = items == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(items);
      totalCount = Math.max(totalCount, items.size());
    }

    public static LookupResult empty() {
      return new LookupResult(List.of(), 0);
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/provider/StitchEntitlementsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider;

import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchDatasetEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchServiceEntitlementsState;

/** Shared backend contract for Stitch entitlements workflows. */
public interface StitchEntitlementsProvider {

  StitchServiceEntitlementsState loadServiceEntitlements(String group, String serviceName);

  default StitchDatasetEntitlementsState loadDatasetEntitlements(
      String group, String namespace, String datasetName) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Dataset entitlements are not implemented");
  }

  StitchServiceEntitlementsState saveServiceEntitlements(
      String group, String serviceName, StitchEntitlementPolicy policy);

  default StitchDatasetEntitlementsState saveDatasetEntitlements(
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String datasetName,
      StitchDatasetEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Dataset entitlements are not implemented");
  }

  default StitchNamespaceEntitlementsState loadNamespaceEntitlements(String group, String namespace) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Namespace entitlements are not implemented");
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/provider/StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEntitlement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubjectType;

final class StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport {
  private StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport() {}

  static int policyCount(List<DefinitionEntitlement> entitlements) {
    int count = 0;
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : entitlements == null ? List.<DefinitionEntitlement>of() : entitlements) {
      count += entitlement == null || entitlement.policies() == null ? 0 : entitlement.policies().size();
    }
    return count;
  }

  static EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>> emptyEffectMap() {
    EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>> map =
        new EnumMap<>(StitchEntitlementEffect.class);
    map.put(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW, new LinkedHashSet<>());
    map.put(StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY, new LinkedHashSet<>());
    return map;
  }

  static List<StitchEntitlementSubject> sortedSubjects(Collection<StitchEntitlementSubject> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return values.stream()
        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing((StitchEntitlementSubject value) -> value.type().name())
                .thenComparing(value -> value.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
                .thenComparing(value -> value.label().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)))
        .toList();
  }

  static StitchEntitlementSubject toSubject(String wireSubject, String group, boolean rejectBlankPrefixedId) {
    String value = normalize(wireSubject);
    if (value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (value.startsWith("app:")) {
      String path = value.substring("app:".length());
      int slash = path.indexOf('/');
      if (slash <= 0 || slash >= path.length() - 1) {
        return null;
      }
      String id = path.substring(slash + 1);
      if (rejectBlankPrefixedId && id.isBlank()) {
        return null;
      }
      return new StitchEntitlementSubject(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.APP, id, id);
    }
    if (value.startsWith("group:")) {
      String id = value.substring("group:".length());
      if (rejectBlankPrefixedId && id.isBlank()) {
        return null;
      }
      return new StitchEntitlementSubject(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.GROUP, id, id);
    }
    if (value.startsWith("user:")) {
      String id = value.substring("user:".length());
      if (rejectBlankPrefixedId && id.isBlank()) {
        return null;
      }
      return new StitchEntitlementSubject(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER, id, id);
    }
    return null;
  }

  static String toCanonicalSubject(
      String group, StitchEntitlementSubject subject, boolean prefixPlainUserIds) {
    if (subject == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String id = normalize(subject.id());
    if (id.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (subject.type()) {
      case APP -> id.startsWith("app:") ? id : "app:" + (id.contains("/") ? id : normalize(group) + "/" + id);
      case GROUP -> id.startsWith("group:") ? id : "group:" + id;
      case USER -> {
        if (!prefixPlainUserIds) {
          yield id;
        }
        if (id.startsWith("user:") || id.contains(":")) {
          yield id;
        }
        yield "user:" + id;
      }
    };
  }

  static boolean enabled(Boolean value) {
    return value == null || value.booleanValue();
  }

  static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(value, fieldName);
  }

  static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  static String normalizeToken(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).replaceAll("[^a-z0-9_-]", "-");
    return normalized.isBlank() ? "x" : normalized;
  }

  static String envelopeGroup(DefinitionEntitlement entitlement) {
    if (entitlement == null || entitlement.envelope() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("entitlement.envelope is required");
    }
    return require(entitlement.envelope().group(), "entitlement.envelope.group");
  }

  static List<DefinitionEntitlement> directEntitlementsByGroup(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> source, String group) {
    String expected = require(group, "group");
    return (source == null ? List.<DefinitionEntitlement>of() : source).stream()
        .filter(entitlement -> Objects.equals(expected, envelopeGroup(entitlement)))
        .toList();
  }

  static List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> activeBindings(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> definitions) {
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> out = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : definitions) {
      if (entitlement == null || entitlement.policies() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument policy : entitlement.policies()) {
        if (policy == null || !enabled(policy.enabled()) || policy.bindings() == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding binding : policy.bindings()) {
          if (binding != null && enabled(binding.enabled())) {
            out.add(binding);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }

  static void deleteDefinitions(DiscoveryCache cache, List<DefinitionEntitlement> definitions) {
    if (cache == null || definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : definitions) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.envelope();
      if (envelope != null) {
        cache.delete(DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT, envelope.group(), envelope.name());
      }
    }
  }

  static void pruneDuplicateDefinitions(
      DiscoveryCache cache, List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct, DefinitionEntitlement updated) {
    if (cache == null || direct == null || direct.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope updatedEnvelope = updated == null ? null : updated.envelope();
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : direct) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.envelope();
      if (envelope == null || updatedEnvelope == null) {
        continue;
      }
      boolean sameId =
          Objects.equals(envelope.group(), updatedEnvelope.group())
              && Objects.equals(envelope.name(), updatedEnvelope.name());
      if (!sameId) {
        cache.delete(DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT, envelope.group(), envelope.name());
      }
    }
  }

  static Optional<DefinitionEntitlement> pickPrimaryOverride(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct, String expectedName) {
    String expected = normalize(expectedName);
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : direct == null ? List.<DefinitionEntitlement>of() : direct) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.envelope();
      if (Objects.equals(expected, normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name()))) {
        return Optional.of(entitlement);
      }
    }
    return direct == null || direct.isEmpty() ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(direct.get(0));
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/entitlements/provider/StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.provider;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEntitlement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementEffect;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementPolicy;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementRule;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchEntitlementSubjectType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.model.StitchServiceEntitlementsState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchSsoUsers;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Service entitlements provider + lookup implementation for the assets/services flow. */
public class StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider
    implements StitchEntitlementsProvider, StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String PLATFORM_NAME = "platform";
  private static final List<String> DEFAULT_ACTIONS = List.of("START", "INVOKE");

  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchSsoUsers ssoUsers;
  private volatile String lookupGroup = "";

  public StitchServiceEntitlementsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    session = resolved;
    ssoUsers = new StitchSsoUsers(runtimeContext.settings());
  }

  public StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider lookupProvider(String group) {
    lookupGroup = normalize(group);
    return this;
  }

  public List<String> actionsFor(StitchServiceEntitlementsState state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return DEFAULT_ACTIONS;
    }
    List<String> fromMetadata = parseActions(state.metadata().get("actions"));
    if (!fromMetadata.isEmpty()) {
      return fromMetadata;
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    merged.addAll(state.directPolicy().actions());
    merged.addAll(state.effectivePolicy().actions());
    return orderedActions(merged);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchServiceEntitlementsState loadServiceEntitlements(String group, String serviceName) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedServiceName = require(serviceName, "serviceName");
    DefinitionService service = requireService(normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName);
    String resourceId = serviceResourceId(service, normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName);

    List<DefinitionEntitlement> effective = scopedEntitlements(resourceId);
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct =
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.directEntitlementsByGroup(effective, normalizedGroup);
    List<String> actions = actionsForEntitlements(direct, effective);
    StitchEntitlementPolicy directPolicy = toPolicy(direct, actions, normalizedGroup);
    StitchEntitlementPolicy effectivePolicy = toPolicy(effective, actions, normalizedGroup);

    StitchEntitlementContext context =
        new StitchEntitlementContext(resourceId, policyCount(direct), policyCount(effective), null);
    Map<String, String> metadata =
        metadata(
            normalizedGroup,
            normalizedServiceName,
            Objects.requireNonNull(service.serviceType(), "service.serviceType").name(),
            resourceId,
            actions,
            direct,
            effective);
    return new StitchServiceEntitlementsState(context, directPolicy, effectivePolicy, metadata);
  }

  @Override
  public StitchServiceEntitlementsState saveServiceEntitlements(
      String group, String serviceName, StitchEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    String normalizedGroup = require(group, "group");
    String normalizedServiceName = require(serviceName, "serviceName");
    DefinitionService service = requireService(normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName);
    String resourceId = serviceResourceId(service, normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName);

    StitchEntitlementPolicy incoming = policy == null ? StitchEntitlementPolicy.empty() : policy;
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct =
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.directEntitlementsByGroup(
            scopedEntitlements(resourceId), normalizedGroup);
    List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> bindings = toBindings(normalizedGroup, incoming);

    if (bindings.isEmpty()) {
      StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.deleteDefinitions(discoveryCache(), direct);
      return loadServiceEntitlements(normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName);
    }

    DefinitionEntitlement existing =
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.pickPrimaryOverride(
                direct, "overrides/services/" + normalizedServiceName)
            .orElse(null);
    DefinitionEntitlement updated =
        buildDefinition(normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName, resourceId, bindings, existing);
    DiscoveryCache cache = discoveryCache();
    cache.upsert(updated);
    StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.pruneDuplicateDefinitions(cache, direct, updated);
    return loadServiceEntitlements(normalizedGroup, normalizedServiceName);
  }

  @Override
  public LookupResult listApps(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
    String group = normalize(lookupGroup);
    if (group.isBlank()) {
      return LookupResult.empty();
    }
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionApp app : discoveryCache().list(DefinitionApp.class, group)) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = app == null ? null : app.envelope();
      if (!enabled(envelope == null ? null : envelope.enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name());
      if (id.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      options.add(
          new StitchEntitlementSubject(
              StitchEntitlementSubjectType.APP,
              id,
              Strings.firstNonBlank(normalize(app.displayName()), id)));
    }
    return StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider.sortedDistinct(
        options, StitchEntitlementSubjectType.APP, filterText, offset, limit);
  }

  @Override
  public LookupResult listGroups(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> ids = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    platformModel().ifPresent(model -> collectGroups(model.root(), ids));
    List<StitchEntitlementSubject> options =
        ids.stream()
            .filter(id -> id != null && !id.isBlank())
            .map(id -> new StitchEntitlementSubject(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.GROUP, id, id))
            .toList();
    return StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider.sortedDistinct(
        options, StitchEntitlementSubjectType.GROUP, filterText, offset, limit);
  }

  @Override
  public LookupResult listUsers(String filterText, int offset, int limit) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchEntitlementSubject> usersById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    platformModel()
        .ifPresent(
            model -> {
              Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> users = model.users();
              if (users == null) {
                return;
              }
              users.forEach(
                  (key, value) -> {
                    String id = Strings.firstNonBlank(normalize(value == null ? null : value.id()), normalize(key));
                    if (id == null || id.isBlank()) {
                      return;
                    }
                    usersById.put(
                        id.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT),
                        new StitchEntitlementSubject(
                            StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER, id, userLabel(value, id)));
                  });
            });
    for (String user : ssoUsers.listUsers()) {
      String id = normalize(user);
      if (id.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      usersById.putIfAbsent(
          id.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT),
          new StitchEntitlementSubject(StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER, id, id));
    }
    return StitchEntitlementsLookupProvider.sortedDistinct(
        usersById.values(), StitchEntitlementSubjectType.USER, filterText, offset, limit);
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement> scopedEntitlements(String resourceId) {
    List<DefinitionEntitlement> out = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : discoveryCache().list(DefinitionEntitlement.class)) {
      if (matchesScope(entitlement, resourceId)) {
        out.add(entitlement);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }

  private List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> toBindings(
      String group, StitchEntitlementPolicy policy) {
    List<String> actions = orderedActions(policy == null ? List.of() : policy.actions());
    List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> out = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String action : actions) {
      for (StitchEntitlementRule rule : policy.rulesForAction(action)) {
        for (StitchEntitlementSubject subject : rule.subjects()) {
          String canonical = toCanonicalSubject(group, subject);
          if (canonical == null) {
            continue;
          }
          out.add(
              new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding(
                  "stitch-"
                      + normalizeToken(action)
                      + "-"
                      + normalizeToken(rule.effect().name())
                      + "-"
                      + normalizeToken(subject.type().name())
                      + "-"
                      + out.size(),
                  canonical,
                  toWireAction(action),
                  rule.effect().display(),
                  true,
                  emptyObligations(),
                  Map.of(),
                  Map.of()));
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }

  private StitchEntitlementPolicy toPolicy(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> entitlements, List<String> actions, String group) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>>> matrix =
        new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String action : actions) {
      matrix.put(action, emptyEffectMap());
    }
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : entitlements) {
      if (entitlement == null || entitlement.policies() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument policy : entitlement.policies()) {
        if (policy == null || !enabled(policy.enabled()) || policy.bindings() == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding binding : policy.bindings()) {
          if (binding == null || !enabled(binding.enabled())) {
            continue;
          }
          String action = serviceAction(binding.action());
          StitchEntitlementSubject subject = toSubject(binding.subject(), group);
          if (subject == null) {
            continue;
          }
          matrix.computeIfAbsent(action, ignored -> emptyEffectMap());
          matrix
              .get(action)
              .get(StitchEntitlementEffect.from(binding.effect()))
              .add(subject);
        }
      }
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, List<StitchEntitlementRule>> rules = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>>> entry :
        matrix.entrySet()) {
      rules.put(
          entry.getKey(),
          List.of(
              new StitchEntitlementRule(
                  entry.getKey(),
                  StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW,
                  sortedSubjects(entry.getValue().get(StitchEntitlementEffect.ALLOW))),
              new StitchEntitlementRule(
                  entry.getKey(),
                  StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY,
                  sortedSubjects(entry.getValue().get(StitchEntitlementEffect.DENY)))));
    }
    return new StitchEntitlementPolicy(rules, Map.of());
  }

  private List<String> actionsForEntitlements(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct, List<DefinitionEntitlement> effective) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> actions = new LinkedHashSet<>(DEFAULT_ACTIONS);
    collectActions(direct, actions);
    collectActions(effective, actions);
    return orderedActions(actions);
  }

  private static void collectActions(
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> entitlements, Set<String> actions) {
    for (DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding binding :
        StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.activeBindings(entitlements)) {
      actions.add(serviceAction(binding.action()));
    }
  }

  private static List<String> orderedActions(Collection<String> source) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> actions = new LinkedHashSet<>(DEFAULT_ACTIONS);
    for (String action : source == null ? List.<String>of() : source) {
      String normalized = serviceAction(action);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        actions.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    List<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
    if (actions.remove("START")) {
      out.add("START");
    }
    if (actions.remove("INVOKE")) {
      out.add("INVOKE");
    }
    List<String> remainder = new ArrayList<>(actions);
    remainder.sort(Comparator.comparing(value -> value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    out.addAll(remainder);
    return List.copyOf(out);
  }

  private Map<String, String> metadata(
      String group,
      String serviceName,
      String serviceType,
      String resourceId,
      List<String> actions,
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> direct,
      List<DefinitionEntitlement> effective) {
    List<String> resolved = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> overrides = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> inheritance = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : effective) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.envelope();
      String fromGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group(), "entitlement.envelope.group");
      String fromName = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name(), "entitlement.envelope.name");
      int policies = entitlement == null || entitlement.policies() == null ? 0 : entitlement.policies().size();
      resolved.add(fromGroup + "/" + fromName + " policies=" + policies);
      if (!Objects.equals(normalize(group), normalize(fromGroup))) {
        inheritance.add("Inherited from " + fromGroup + " (" + fromName + ")");
      }
    }
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : direct) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = entitlement == null ? null : entitlement.envelope();
      String name = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name(), "entitlement.envelope.name");
      int policies = entitlement == null || entitlement.policies() == null ? 0 : entitlement.policies().size();
      overrides.add(name + " policies=" + policies);
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    metadata.put("group", group);
    metadata.put("serviceName", serviceName);
    metadata.put("serviceType", Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceType, "serviceType"));
    metadata.put("resourceId", resourceId);
    metadata.put("actions", String.join(",", actions));
    metadata.put("resolvedPolicies", String.join("\n", resolved));
    metadata.put("overrides", String.join("\n", overrides));
    metadata.put("inheritance", String.join("\n", inheritance));
    metadata.put("savedBy", Strings.firstNonBlank(StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject(), "service:stitch"));
    return Map.copyOf(metadata);
  }

  private DefinitionEntitlement buildDefinition(
      String group,
      String serviceName,
      String resourceId,
      List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> bindings,
      DefinitionEntitlement existing) {
    String actor = Strings.firstNonBlank(StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject(), "service:stitch");
    String now = Instant.now().toString();
    DefinitionEnvelope previous = existing == null ? null : existing.envelope();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT,
            "overrides/services/" + serviceName,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.uuid(), "ent-service-" + serviceName),
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.createdTimeUtc(), now),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.createdBy(), actor),
            now,
            actor);
    DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument policy =
        new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument(
            "1.0",
            resourceId,
            group,
            serviceName,
            "SERVICE",
            "SERVICE",
            resourceId,
            "SERVICE",
            "service-" + serviceName,
            "Service entitlements managed by Stitch",
            "1",
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            Map.of(),
            List.copyOf(bindings));
    return new DefinitionEntitlement(
        envelope,
        "service",
        resourceId,
        List.of(policy),
        List.of(),
        Map.of("managedBy", "stitch"),
        List.of("Stitch managed service entitlements"));
  }

  private DefinitionService requireService(String group, String serviceName) {
    return discoveryCache()
        .get(DefinitionService.class, group, serviceName)
        .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalArgumentException("Service not found: " + group + "/" + serviceName));
  }

  private String serviceResourceId(DefinitionService service, String group, String serviceName) {
    String explicit = Strings.requireNonBlank(service == null ? null : service.resourceId(), "service.resourceId");
    return ServiceEntitlements.requireServiceResourceId(explicit);
  }

  private static boolean matchesScope(DefinitionEntitlement entitlement, String resourceId) {
    if (entitlement == null) {
      return false;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = entitlement.envelope();
    if (!enabled(envelope == null ? null : envelope.enabled())) {
      return false;
    }
    String canonicalScopeId = Strings.requireNonBlank(entitlement.scopeId(), "entitlement.scopeId");
    String expectedScopeId = Strings.requireNonBlank(resourceId, "resourceId");
    if (!canonicalScopeId.equals(expectedScopeId)) {
      return false;
    }
    return "service".equals(Strings.requireNonBlank(entitlement.scopeType(), "entitlement.scopeType"));
  }

  private Optional<DefinitionPlatform> platformModel() {
    return discoveryCache().get(DefinitionPlatform.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, PLATFORM_NAME);
  }

  private void collectGroups(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, LinkedHashSet<String> groups) {
    if (node == null) {
      return;
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> orgGroups = node.groups();
    if (orgGroups != null) {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : orgGroups) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String id = Strings.requireNonBlank(group.name(), "platform.group.name");
        groups.add(id);
      }
    }
    if (node.ous() != null) {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : node.ous()) {
        collectGroups(child, groups);
      }
    }
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private static int policyCount(List<DefinitionEntitlement> entitlements) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.policyCount(entitlements);
  }

  private static DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet emptyObligations() {
    return new DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet(
        List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), Map.of());
  }

  private static String toWireAction(String action) {
    return switch (serviceAction(action)) {
      case "START" -> "service.start";
      case "INVOKE" -> "service.invoke";
      default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported service entitlement action: " + action);
    };
  }

  private static String serviceAction(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Service entitlement action is required.");
    }
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "SERVICE.START", "START" -> "START";
      case "SERVICE.INVOKE", "INVOKE" -> "INVOKE";
      default -> normalized;
    };
  }

  private static StitchEntitlementSubject toSubject(String wireSubject, String group) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.toSubject(wireSubject, group, true);
  }

  private static String toCanonicalSubject(String group, StitchEntitlementSubject subject) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.toCanonicalSubject(group, subject, false);
  }

  private static EnumMap<StitchEntitlementEffect, LinkedHashSet<StitchEntitlementSubject>>
      emptyEffectMap() {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.emptyEffectMap();
  }

  private static List<StitchEntitlementSubject> sortedSubjects(
      Collection<StitchEntitlementSubject> values) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.sortedSubjects(values);
  }

  private static List<String> parseActions(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String token : normalized.split(",")) {
      String action = serviceAction(token);
      if (!action.isBlank()) {
        out.add(action);
      }
    }
    return orderedActions(out);
  }

  private static String userLabel(DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user, String fallbackId) {
    if (user == null) {
      return fallbackId;
    }
    String full = (normalize(user.firstName()) + " " + normalize(user.lastName())).trim();
    if (!full.isBlank()) {
      return full;
    }
    String email = normalize(user.email());
    if (!email.isBlank()) {
      return email;
    }
    String id = normalize(user.id());
    return id.isBlank() ? fallbackId : id;
  }

  private static boolean enabled(Boolean value) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.enabled(value);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.require(value, field);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.normalize(value);
  }

  private static String normalizeToken(String value) {
    return StitchEntitlementsProviderSupport.normalizeToken(value);
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/platform/StitchGroupsGroupEditor.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
