public class StitchGroupsGroupEditor extends VerticalLayout {

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface ChangeListener {
    void onChange(GroupDraft draft);
  }

  public record GroupDraft(
      String name, String description, List<String> humanUsers, List<String> serviceUsers) {
    public GroupDraft {
      humanUsers = humanUsers == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(humanUsers);
      serviceUsers = serviceUsers == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(serviceUsers);
    }
  }

  private record MemberOption(String id, String label) {}

  private record MemberPresentation(String id, String initials, String primary, String secondary) {}

  private final TextField nameField = new TextField("Name");
  private final TextArea descriptionField = new TextArea("Description");
  private final TextField idField = readOnlyField("Id");
  private final TextField pathField = readOnlyField("Path");
  private final TextField typeField = readOnlyField("Type");
  private final TextField humanCountField = readOnlyField("Human Members");
  private final TextField serviceCountField = readOnlyField("Service Members");

  private final ComboBox<MemberOption> addHumanSelect = new ComboBox<>();
  private final ComboBox<MemberOption> addServiceSelect = new ComboBox<>();
  private final TextField serviceFallbackInput = new TextField();
  private final Grid<MemberPresentation> humanGrid = new Grid<>(MemberPresentation.class, false);
  private final Grid<MemberPresentation> serviceGrid = new Grid<>(MemberPresentation.class, false);
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final Div humanControls = new Div();
  private final Div serviceSelectRow = new Div();
  private final Div serviceFallbackRow = new Div();

  private final List<String> humanUsers = new ArrayList<>();
  private final List<String> serviceUsers = new ArrayList<>();
  private Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> userDirectory = Map.of();
  private Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> serviceDirectory = Map.of();

  private ChangeListener changeListener;
  private boolean muteEvents;
  private boolean readOnly = true;

  public StitchGroupsGroupEditor() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.72rem");
    addClassName("stitch-groups-editor");

    FormLayout metadata = new FormLayout();
    metadata.setWidthFull();
    metadata.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("46em", 2));
    metadata.addClassName("stitch-groups-basic-form");

    nameField.setWidthFull();
    nameField.addClassName("stitch-groups-editable-field");
    nameField.addValueChangeListener(event -> emitChange());

    descriptionField.setWidthFull();
    descriptionField.setMinHeight("120px");
    descriptionField.addClassName("stitch-groups-editable-field");
    descriptionField.addClassName("stitch-groups-description");
    descriptionField.addValueChangeListener(event -> emitChange());

    metadata.add(nameField, idField, pathField, typeField, humanCountField, serviceCountField);

    configureHumanSelectors();
    configureServiceSelectors();
    configureMemberGrid(humanGrid, true);
    configureMemberGrid(serviceGrid, false);

    humanControls.add(serviceControlRow(addHumanSelect, this::addHumanFromSelect));
    serviceSelectRow.add(serviceControlRow(addServiceSelect, this::addServiceFromSelect));
    serviceFallbackRow.add(serviceFallbackControl());

    summaryStrip.addClassName("stitch-groups-summary");
    summaryStrip.setItems(Map.of("Type", "Group", "Human Members", "0", "Service Members", "0"));

    StitchSection basicInfo = new StitchSection("Basic Info");
    basicInfo.addClassName("stitch-groups-basic-section");
    basicInfo.addToBody(metadata, descriptionField);

    StitchSection members = new StitchSection("Members");
    members.addClassName("stitch-groups-members-section");
    members.addToBody(
        memberSection("Human Members", humanControls, humanGrid),
        memberSection("Service Members", new Div(serviceSelectRow, serviceFallbackRow), serviceGrid));

    add(summaryStrip, basicInfo, members);
    setReadOnly(true);
  }

  public void setNode(
      StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node,
      Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> users,
      Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> services,
      ChangeListener listener) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(node, "node");
    if (node.kind() != StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.GROUP) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group editor requires a GROUP node");
    }
    this.changeListener = listener;
    this.userDirectory = users == null ? Map.of() : users;
    this.serviceDirectory = services == null ? Map.of() : services;
    muteEvents = true;
    humanUsers.clear();
    serviceUsers.clear();
    humanUsers.addAll(node.userIds());
    serviceUsers.addAll(node.serviceIds());

    nameField.setValue(emptySafe(node.name()));
    descriptionField.setValue(emptySafe(node.description()));
    idField.setValue(emptySafe(node.id()));
    pathField.setValue(emptySafe(node.pathLabel()));
    typeField.setValue(emptySafe(node.type()));
    serviceFallbackInput.clear();
    refreshSelects();
    refreshMemberLists();
    muteEvents = false;
  }

  public void setReadOnly(boolean value) {
    this.readOnly = value;
    nameField.setReadOnly(value);
    descriptionField.setReadOnly(value);
    humanControls.setVisible(true);
    refreshSelects();
    refreshMemberLists();
  }

  public GroupDraft draft() {
    return new GroupDraft(
        trimToNull(nameField.getValue()),
        trimToNull(descriptionField.getValue()),
        List.copyOf(humanUsers),
        List.copyOf(serviceUsers));
  }

  private void configureHumanSelectors() {
    addHumanSelect.setWidthFull();
    addHumanSelect.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    addHumanSelect.setPlaceholder("Search human users");
    addHumanSelect.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    addHumanSelect.setItemLabelGenerator(option -> option == null ? "" : option.label());
  }

  private void configureServiceSelectors() {
    addServiceSelect.setWidthFull();
    addServiceSelect.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    addServiceSelect.setPlaceholder("Search service accounts");
    addServiceSelect.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    addServiceSelect.setItemLabelGenerator(option -> option == null ? "" : option.label());

    serviceFallbackInput.setWidthFull();
    serviceFallbackInput.setPlaceholder("service id, app:<group>/<name>, or service:<group>/<name>");
    serviceFallbackInput.setClearButtonVisible(true);
  }

  private HorizontalLayout serviceControlRow(ComboBox<MemberOption> select, Runnable addAction) {
    Button add = secondaryButton("Add", addAction);
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(select, add);
    row.setAlignItems(Alignment.END);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.expand(select);
    return row;
  }

  private HorizontalLayout serviceFallbackControl() {
    Button add =
        secondaryButton(
            "Add",
            () -> {
              String normalized = normalizeServiceInput(serviceFallbackInput.getValue());
              if (normalized == null) {
                toast("Invalid service user id format.");
                return;
              }
              if (!dedupeAdd(serviceUsers, normalized, StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalServiceKey)) {
                toast("Service user already exists.");
                return;
              }
              serviceFallbackInput.clear();
              refreshMemberLists();
              emitChange();
            });
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(serviceFallbackInput, add);
    row.setAlignItems(Alignment.END);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.expand(serviceFallbackInput);
    return row;
  }

  private Button secondaryButton(String label, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button(label, event -> action.run());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    return button;
  }

  private void addHumanFromSelect() {
    MemberOption option = addHumanSelect.getValue();
    if (option == null || option.id() == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!dedupeAdd(humanUsers, option.id(), StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalHumanKey)) {
      toast("Human user already exists.");
      return;
    }
    refreshSelects();
    refreshMemberLists();
    emitMembershipChange();
  }

  private void addServiceFromSelect() {
    MemberOption option = addServiceSelect.getValue();
    if (option == null || option.id() == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!dedupeAdd(serviceUsers, option.id(), StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalServiceKey)) {
      toast("Service user already exists.");
      return;
    }
    refreshSelects();
    refreshMemberLists();
    emitMembershipChange();
  }

  private void refreshSelects() {
    List<MemberOption> humanOptions = availableHumanOptions();
    addHumanSelect.setItems(humanOptions);
    addHumanSelect.clear();

    List<MemberOption> serviceOptions = availableServiceOptions();
    boolean hasServiceDirectory = !serviceOptions.isEmpty() || !serviceDirectory.isEmpty();
    serviceSelectRow.setVisible(hasServiceDirectory);
    serviceFallbackRow.setVisible(!hasServiceDirectory);
    if (hasServiceDirectory) {
      addServiceSelect.setItems(serviceOptions);
      addServiceSelect.clear();
    }
  }

  private List<MemberOption> availableHumanOptions() {
    Set<String> existing = canonicalSet(humanUsers, StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalHumanKey);
    List<MemberOption> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> entry : userDirectory.entrySet()) {
      String id = trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user = entry.getValue();
      if (id == null && user != null) {
        id = trimToNull(user.id());
      }
      if (id == null || existing.contains(canonicalHumanKey(id))) {
        continue;
      }
      options.add(new MemberOption(id, humanOptionLabel(id, user)));
    }
    options.sort((left, right) -> left.label().compareToIgnoreCase(right.label()));
    return List.copyOf(options);
  }

  private List<MemberOption> availableServiceOptions() {
    Set<String> existing = canonicalSet(serviceUsers, StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalServiceKey);
    List<MemberOption> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> entry : serviceDirectory.entrySet()) {
      String id = trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service = entry.getValue();
      if (id == null && service != null) {
        id = trimToNull(service.id());
      }
      if (id == null || existing.contains(canonicalServiceKey(id))) {
        continue;
      }
      options.add(new MemberOption(id, serviceOptionLabel(id, service)));
    }
    options.sort((left, right) -> left.label().compareToIgnoreCase(right.label()));
    return List.copyOf(options);
  }

  private static Set<String> canonicalSet(List<String> values, Function<String, String> canonicalizer) {
    Set<String> canonical = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (values == null) {
      return canonical;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      String key = canonicalizer.apply(value);
      if (!key.isBlank()) {
        canonical.add(key);
      }
    }
    return canonical;
  }

  private void refreshMemberLists() {
    List<MemberPresentation> humans = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : humanUsers) {
      humans.add(presentHuman(value));
    }
    humans.sort((left, right) -> left.primary().compareToIgnoreCase(right.primary()));
    humanGrid.setItems(humans);

    List<MemberPresentation> services = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : serviceUsers) {
      services.add(presentService(value));
    }
    services.sort((left, right) -> left.primary().compareToIgnoreCase(right.primary()));
    serviceGrid.setItems(services);

    humanCountField.setValue(String.valueOf(humanUsers.size()));
    serviceCountField.setValue(String.valueOf(serviceUsers.size()));
    summaryStrip.setItems(
        Map.of(
            "Type",
            "Group",
            "Human Members",
            String.valueOf(humanUsers.size()),
            "Service Members",
            String.valueOf(serviceUsers.size())));
  }

  private MemberPresentation presentHuman(String raw) {
    String id = normalizeHumanInput(raw);
    DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user = id == null ? null : resolveUser(id);
    String primary = humanPrimaryLabel(id, user);
    String secondary = humanSecondaryLabel(id, user);
    String stableId = id == null ? emptySafe(raw) : id;
    return new MemberPresentation(stableId, initials(primary, stableId), primary, secondary);
  }

  private MemberPresentation presentService(String raw) {
    String id = normalizeServiceInput(raw);
    DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service = id == null ? null : resolveService(id);
    String primary = servicePrimaryLabel(id, service);
    String secondary = serviceSecondaryLabel(id);
    String stableId = id == null ? emptySafe(raw) : id;
    return new MemberPresentation(stableId, initials(primary, stableId), primary, secondary);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser resolveUser(String id) {
    DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser exact = userDirectory.get(id);
    if (exact != null) {
      return exact;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> entry : userDirectory.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      if (key != null && key.equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        return entry.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService resolveService(String id) {
    DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService exact = serviceDirectory.get(id);
    if (exact != null) {
      return exact;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> entry : serviceDirectory.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      if (key != null && key.equalsIgnoreCase(id)) {
        return entry.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private void removeHuman(String value) {
    if (removeByCanonical(humanUsers, value, StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalHumanKey)) {
      refreshSelects();
      refreshMemberLists();
      emitMembershipChange();
    }
  }

  private void removeService(String value) {
    if (removeByCanonical(serviceUsers, value, StitchGroupsGroupEditor::canonicalServiceKey)) {
      refreshSelects();
      refreshMemberLists();
      emitMembershipChange();
    }
  }

  private Div memberSection(String title, Component addControl, Component list) {
    Span sectionTitle = new Span(title);
    sectionTitle.addClassName("stitch-groups-members-subtitle");
    VerticalLayout wrapper = new VerticalLayout(sectionTitle, addControl, list);
    wrapper.setPadding(false);
    wrapper.setSpacing(false);
    wrapper.getStyle().set("gap", "0.56rem");
    wrapper.setWidthFull();
    return new Div(wrapper);
  }

  private void configureMemberGrid(Grid<MemberPresentation> grid, boolean human) {
    grid.addClassNames("stitch-results-grid", "stitch-groups-member-grid");
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_NO_BORDER);
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.setAllRowsVisible(true);
    if (human) {
      grid.addComponentColumn(row -> avatar(row.initials())).setHeader("Avatar").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
      grid.addColumn(MemberPresentation::primary).setHeader("Name").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
      grid.addColumn(MemberPresentation::secondary).setHeader("Email").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    } else {
      grid.addColumn(MemberPresentation::primary).setHeader("Service").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
      grid.addColumn(MemberPresentation::secondary).setHeader("Id").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    }
    grid.addComponentColumn(
            row -> {
              Button remove = new Button(VaadinIcon.TRASH.create(), event -> {
                if (human) {
                  removeHuman(row.id());
                } else {
                  removeService(row.id());
                }
              });
              remove.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE, ButtonVariant.LUMO_ICON, ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
              remove.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Remove member");
              return remove;
            })
        .setHeader("Actions")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
  }

  private Component avatar(String initials) {
    Span avatar = new Span(initials == null || initials.isBlank() ? "?" : initials);
    avatar.addClassName("stitch-groups-member-avatar");
    return avatar;
  }

  private void emitChange() {
    if (muteEvents || readOnly || changeListener == null) {
      return;
    }
    changeListener.onChange(draft());
  }

  private void emitMembershipChange() {
    if (muteEvents || changeListener == null) {
      return;
    }
    changeListener.onChange(draft());
  }

  private void toast(String message) {
    Notification.show(message, 2200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private static boolean dedupeAdd(
      List<String> values, String value, Function<String, String> canonicalizer) {
    if (values == null || value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String target = canonicalizer.apply(value);
    for (String existing : values) {
      if (Objects.equals(target, canonicalizer.apply(existing))) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    values.add(value);
    return true;
  }

  private static boolean removeByCanonical(
      List<String> values, String value, Function<String, String> canonicalizer) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String target = canonicalizer.apply(value);
    for (int i = 0; i < values.size(); i++) {
      if (Objects.equals(target, canonicalizer.apply(values.get(i)))) {
        values.remove(i);
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String humanOptionLabel(String id, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user) {
    String name = humanName(user);
    if (name != null) {
      return name + " (" + id + ")";
    }
    return id;
  }

  private static String serviceOptionLabel(String id, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service) {
    String display = trimToNull(service == null ? null : service.displayName());
    if (display != null) {
      return display + " (" + id + ")";
    }
    return id;
  }

  private static String humanPrimaryLabel(String id, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user) {
    String full = humanName(user);
    if (full != null) {
      return full;
    }
    return id == null ? "Unknown user" : id;
  }

  private static String humanSecondaryLabel(String id, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user) {
    String email = trimToNull(user == null ? null : user.email());
    if (email != null) {
      return email;
    }
    return id == null ? "user:unknown" : "user:" + id;
  }

  private static String servicePrimaryLabel(String id, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service) {
    String display = trimToNull(service == null ? null : service.displayName());
    if (display != null) {
      return display;
    }
    return id == null ? "Unknown service" : id;
  }

  private static String serviceSecondaryLabel(String id) {
    return id == null ? "service:unknown" : "service:" + id;
  }

  private static String humanName(DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user) {
    String first = trimToNull(user == null ? null : user.firstName());
    String last = trimToNull(user == null ? null : user.lastName());
    if (first == null && last == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (first == null) {
      return last;
    }
    if (last == null) {
      return first;
    }
    return first + " " + last;
  }

  private static String initials(String primary, String fallbackId) {
    String base = trimToNull(primary);
    if (base == null) {
      base = trimToNull(fallbackId);
    }
    if (base == null) {
      return "?";
    }
    String[] tokens = base.split("\\s+");
    if (tokens.length == 1) {
      String one = tokens[0].replaceAll("[^A-Za-z0-9]", "");
      if (one.isBlank()) {
        return "?";
      }
      return one.substring(0, Math.min(2, one.length())).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    }
    String left = tokens[0].isBlank() ? "" : tokens[0].substring(0, 1);
    String right = tokens[tokens.length - 1].isBlank() ? "" : tokens[tokens.length - 1].substring(0, 1);
    String combined = (left + right).replaceAll("[^A-Za-z0-9]", "");
    return combined.isBlank() ? "?" : combined.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String normalizeHumanInput(String raw) {
    String value = trimToNull(raw);
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value;
    if (value.regionMatches(true, 0, "user:", 0, "user:".length())) {
      normalized = trimToNull(value.substring("user:".length()));
    }
    if (normalized == null || normalized.contains(" ")) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String normalizeServiceInput(String raw) {
    String value = trimToNull(raw);
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value;
    if (value.regionMatches(true, 0, "service:", 0, "service:".length())) {
      normalized = trimToNull(value.substring("service:".length()));
    } else if (value.regionMatches(true, 0, "app:", 0, "app:".length())) {
      normalized = trimToNull(value.substring("app:".length()));
    }
    if (normalized == null || normalized.contains(" ")) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String canonicalHumanKey(String raw) {
    String normalized = normalizeHumanInput(raw);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String canonicalServiceKey(String raw) {
    String normalized = normalizeServiceInput(raw);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static TextField readOnlyField(String label) {
    TextField field = new TextField(label);
    field.setReadOnly(true);
    field.setWidthFull();
    field.addClassName("stitch-groups-readonly-field");
    return field;
  }

  private static String emptySafe(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;

public class StitchGroupsOuEditor extends VerticalLayout {

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface ChangeListener {
    void onChange(OuDraft draft);
  }

  public record OuDraft(String name, String description) {}

  private final TextField nameField = new TextField("Name");
  private final TextArea descriptionField = new TextArea("Description");
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final StitchSection basicInfo = new StitchSection("Basic Info");
  private final VerticalLayout viewRows = new VerticalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout editFields = new VerticalLayout();

  private final Span nameValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Name");
  private final Span idValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Id");
  private final Span pathValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Path");
  private final Span typeValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Type");
  private final Span descriptionValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Description");
  private final Span childOuValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Child OUs");
  private final Span childGroupValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Child Groups");
  private final Span subtreeGroupValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Subtree Groups");
  private final Span subtreeMemberValue = propertyRow(viewRows, "Subtree Members");

  private ChangeListener changeListener;
  private boolean muteEvents;
  private boolean readOnly = true;

  public StitchGroupsOuEditor() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.72rem");
    addClassName("stitch-groups-ou-editor");

    summaryStrip.addClassName("stitch-groups-summary");
    summaryStrip.setItems(
        Map.of("Type", "OU", "Child OUs", "0", "Subtree Groups", "0", "Subtree Members", "0"));

    viewRows.setPadding(false);
    viewRows.setSpacing(false);
    viewRows.setWidthFull();
    viewRows.getStyle().set("gap", "0.48rem");
    viewRows.addClassName("stitch-groups-property-list");

    nameField.setWidthFull();
    nameField.addValueChangeListener(event -> emitChange());
    descriptionField.setWidthFull();
    descriptionField.setMinHeight("120px");
    descriptionField.addValueChangeListener(event -> emitChange());

    editFields.setPadding(false);
    editFields.setSpacing(false);
    editFields.setWidthFull();
    editFields.getStyle().set("gap", "0.56rem");
    editFields.addClassName("stitch-groups-edit-fields");
    editFields.add(nameField, descriptionField);

    basicInfo.addClassName("stitch-groups-basic-section");
    basicInfo.addToBody(viewRows, editFields);

    add(summaryStrip, basicInfo);
    setReadOnly(true);
  }

  public void setNode(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node, ChangeListener listener) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(node, "node");
    if (node.kind() != StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU editor requires an OU node");
    }
    this.changeListener = listener;
    muteEvents = true;
    nameField.setValue(emptySafe(node.name()));
    descriptionField.setValue(emptySafe(node.description()));
    nameValue.setText(valueOrDash(node.name()));
    idValue.setText(valueOrDash(node.id()));
    pathValue.setText(valueOrDash(node.pathLabel()));
    typeValue.setText("OU");
    descriptionValue.setText(valueOrDash(node.description()));
    childOuValue.setText(String.valueOf(node.childOuCount()));
    childGroupValue.setText(String.valueOf(node.childGroupCount()));
    subtreeGroupValue.setText(String.valueOf(node.groupCountInSubtree()));
    subtreeMemberValue.setText(String.valueOf(node.principalCountInSubtree()));

    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Type", "OU");
    summary.put("Child OUs", String.valueOf(node.childOuCount()));
    summary.put("Subtree Groups", String.valueOf(node.groupCountInSubtree()));
    summary.put("Subtree Members", String.valueOf(node.principalCountInSubtree()));
    summaryStrip.setItems(summary);
    muteEvents = false;
  }

  public void setReadOnly(boolean value) {
    this.readOnly = value;
    viewRows.setVisible(true);
    editFields.setVisible(!value);
  }

  public OuDraft draft() {
    return new OuDraft(trimToNull(nameField.getValue()), trimToNull(descriptionField.getValue()));
  }

  private void emitChange() {
    if (muteEvents || readOnly || changeListener == null) {
      return;
    }
    changeListener.onChange(draft());
  }

  private static Span propertyRow(VerticalLayout host, String label) {
    Div row = new Div();
    row.addClassName("stitch-groups-property-row");

    Span labelValue = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(label), "-"));
    labelValue.addClassName("stitch-groups-property-label");
    Span value = new Span("-");
    value.addClassName("stitch-groups-property-value");

    row.add(labelValue, value);
    host.add(row);
    return value;
  }

  private static String emptySafe(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }

  private static String valueOrDash(String value) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(value), "-");
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/platform/StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;

public class StitchGroupsTreeAdapter {

  public enum NodeKind {
    OU,
    GROUP
  }

  public record TreeSnapshot(List<TreeNode> roots, Map<String, TreeNode> byId) {
    public TreeSnapshot {
      roots = roots == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(roots);
      byId = byId == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(byId);
    }
  }

  public record TreeNode(
      String id,
      NodeKind kind,
      String title,
      String name,
      String nodeName,
      String displayName,
      String type,
      String description,
      List<String> userIds,
      List<String> serviceIds,
      String pathLabel,
      int childOuCount,
      int childGroupCount,
      int groupCountInSubtree,
      int principalCountInSubtree,
      List<TreeNode> children) {

    public TreeNode {
      title = trimToEmpty(title);
      name = trimToEmpty(name);
      nodeName = trimToEmpty(nodeName);
      displayName = trimToEmpty(displayName);
      type = trimToEmpty(type);
      description = description == null ? "" : description;
      userIds = userIds == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(userIds);
      serviceIds = serviceIds == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(serviceIds);
      pathLabel = trimToEmpty(pathLabel);
      children = children == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(children);
    }

    public TreeNode withChildren(List<TreeNode> nextChildren) {
      return new TreeNode(
          id,
          kind,
          title,
          name,
          nodeName,
          displayName,
          type,
          description,
          userIds,
          serviceIds,
          pathLabel,
          childOuCount,
          childGroupCount,
          groupCountInSubtree,
          principalCountInSubtree,
          nextChildren);
    }
  }

  public record OuUpdate(String name, String description) {}

  public record GroupUpdate(
      String name, String description, List<String> humanUsers, List<String> serviceUsers) {
    public GroupUpdate {
      humanUsers = normalizeIds(humanUsers);
      serviceUsers = normalizeIds(serviceUsers);
    }
  }

  private record GroupTarget(List<Integer> ouPath, int groupIndex) {}

  public DefinitionPlatform deepCopy(DefinitionPlatform source) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(source, "source");
    return new DefinitionPlatform(
        copyEnvelope(source.envelope()),
        copyUsers(source.users()),
        copyServices(source.services()),
        copyOu(source.root()),
        source.configId(),
        source.effectiveConfigId());
  }

  public TreeSnapshot snapshot(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    if (model == null || model.root() == null) {
      return new TreeSnapshot(List.of(), Map.of());
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, TreeNode> byId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    TreeNode root = buildOuNode(model.root(), List.of(), "root", byId);
    return new TreeSnapshot(List.of(root), byId);
  }

  public List<TreeNode> filter(List<TreeNode> roots, String query) {
    if (roots == null || roots.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String normalized = trimToEmpty(query).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return roots;
    }
    List<TreeNode> filtered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (TreeNode root : roots) {
      TreeNode keep = filterNode(root, normalized);
      if (keep != null) {
        filtered.add(keep);
      }
    }
    return filtered;
  }

  public DefinitionPlatform applyOuEdits(DefinitionPlatform model, String ouNodeId, OuUpdate update) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    Objects.requireNonNull(update, "update");
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
    List<Integer> targetPath = parseOuPath(ouNodeId);
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot = rewriteOu(root, targetPath, 0, update);
    return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
  }

  public DefinitionPlatform applyGroupEdits(
      DefinitionPlatform model, String groupNodeId, GroupUpdate update) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    Objects.requireNonNull(update, "update");
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
    GroupTarget target = parseGroupTarget(groupNodeId);
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot =
        rewriteGroup(root, target.ouPath(), 0, target.groupIndex(), update);
    return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
  }

  public DefinitionPlatform createOu(
      DefinitionPlatform model, String parentOuNodeId, String name, String description) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    String parentId = trimToNull(parentOuNodeId);
    if (parentId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Parent OU node id is required");
    }
    String normalizedName = trimToNull(name);
    if (normalizedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU name is required");
    }
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
    List<Integer> parentPath = parseOuPath(parentId);
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot =
        rewriteCreateOu(root, parentPath, 0, normalizedName, trimToNull(description));
    return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
  }

  public DefinitionPlatform createGroup(
      DefinitionPlatform model,
      String parentOuNodeId,
      String name,
      String type,
      String description) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    String parentId = trimToNull(parentOuNodeId);
    if (parentId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Parent OU node id is required");
    }
    String normalizedName = trimToNull(name);
    if (normalizedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group name is required");
    }
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
    List<Integer> parentPath = parseOuPath(parentId);
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot =
        rewriteCreateGroup(
            root, parentPath, 0, normalizedName, trimToNull(type), trimToNull(description));
    return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
  }

  public DefinitionPlatform renameNode(
      DefinitionPlatform model, String nodeId, String newName, String description) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    String normalizedName = trimToNull(newName);
    if (normalizedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Name is required");
    }
    String normalizedNodeId = trimToNull(nodeId);
    if (normalizedNodeId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Node id is required");
    }
    if (normalizedNodeId.startsWith("ou:")) {
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
      List<Integer> targetPath = parseOuPath(normalizedNodeId);
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot =
          rewriteRenameOu(root, targetPath, 0, normalizedName, description);
      return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
    }
    if (normalizedNodeId.startsWith("group:")) {
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
      GroupTarget target = parseGroupTarget(normalizedNodeId);
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot =
          rewriteRenameGroup(root, target.ouPath(), 0, target.groupIndex(), normalizedName, description);
      return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
    }
    throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported node id: " + nodeId);
  }

  public DefinitionPlatform deleteNode(DefinitionPlatform model, String nodeId) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    String normalizedNodeId = trimToNull(nodeId);
    if (normalizedNodeId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Node id is required");
    }
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = requireRoot(model);
    if (normalizedNodeId.startsWith("ou:")) {
      List<Integer> targetPath = parseOuPath(normalizedNodeId);
      if (targetPath.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Root OU cannot be deleted");
      }
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot = rewriteDeleteOu(root, targetPath, 0);
      return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
    }
    if (normalizedNodeId.startsWith("group:")) {
      GroupTarget target = parseGroupTarget(normalizedNodeId);
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewrittenRoot =
          rewriteDeleteGroup(root, target.ouPath(), 0, target.groupIndex());
      return withRoot(model, rewrittenRoot);
    }
    throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported node id: " + nodeId);
  }

  public String parentOuNodeId(String nodeId) {
    String normalizedNodeId = trimToNull(nodeId);
    if (normalizedNodeId == null) {
      return "ou:";
    }
    if (normalizedNodeId.startsWith("group:")) {
      GroupTarget target = parseGroupTarget(normalizedNodeId);
      return toOuId(target.ouPath());
    }
    if (normalizedNodeId.startsWith("ou:")) {
      List<Integer> path = parseOuPath(normalizedNodeId);
      if (path.isEmpty()) {
        return "ou:";
      }
      return toOuId(path.subList(0, path.size() - 1));
    }
    return "ou:";
  }

  private TreeNode filterNode(TreeNode node, String query) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (matches(node, query)) {
      return node;
    }
    List<TreeNode> childMatches = new ArrayList<>();
    for (TreeNode child : node.children()) {
      TreeNode filteredChild = filterNode(child, query);
      if (filteredChild != null) {
        childMatches.add(filteredChild);
      }
    }
    if (childMatches.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return node.withChildren(childMatches);
  }

  private static boolean matches(TreeNode node, String query) {
    return contains(node.title(), query)
        || contains(node.description(), query)
        || contains(node.pathLabel(), query)
        || contains(node.name(), query)
        || contains(node.nodeName(), query)
        || contains(node.displayName(), query);
  }

  private static boolean contains(String value, String query) {
    return value != null && value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains(query);
  }

  private TreeNode buildOuNode(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode ou,
      List<Integer> path,
      String pathLabel,
      Map<String, TreeNode> byId) {
    if (ou == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<TreeNode> children = new ArrayList<>();
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> ous = safeOus(ou.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups = safeGroups(ou.groups());

    for (int index = 0; index < ous.size(); index++) {
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = ous.get(index);
      if (child == null) {
        continue;
      }
      List<Integer> nextPath = append(path, index);
      String childPathLabel = pathLabel + "/" + resolveNodeLabel(child);
      TreeNode childNode = buildOuNode(child, nextPath, childPathLabel, byId);
      if (childNode != null) {
        children.add(childNode);
      }
    }
    for (int index = 0; index < groups.size(); index++) {
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group = groups.get(index);
      if (group == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = toGroupId(path, index);
      String groupTitle = buildGroupTitle(group);
      TreeNode groupNode =
          new TreeNode(
              id,
              NodeKind.GROUP,
              groupTitle,
              group.name(),
              group.nodeName(),
              group.displayName(),
              group.type(),
              group.description(),
              safeIds(group.userIds()),
              safeIds(group.serviceIds()),
              pathLabel + "/" + resolveGroupLabel(group),
              0,
              0,
              0,
              safeIds(group.userIds()).size() + safeIds(group.serviceIds()).size(),
              List.of());
      byId.put(id, groupNode);
      children.add(groupNode);
    }

    int groupCount = countGroups(ou);
    int principals = countPrincipals(ou, new LinkedHashSet<>());
    String id = toOuId(path);
    TreeNode node =
        new TreeNode(
            id,
            NodeKind.OU,
            buildOuTitle(ou, groupCount, principals),
            ou.name(),
            ou.nodeName(),
            ou.displayName(),
            ou.type(),
            ou.description(),
            List.of(),
            List.of(),
            pathLabel,
            ous.size(),
            groups.size(),
            groupCount,
            principals,
            children);
    byId.put(id, node);
    return node;
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteOu(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, List<Integer> targetPath, int depth, OuUpdate update) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTarget = depth == targetPath.size();
    String name = atTarget ? applyNonBlank(update.name(), node.name()) : node.name();
    String description = atTarget ? update.description() : node.description();

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size());
    if (depth < targetPath.size()) {
      int targetChild = targetPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU path is not valid: " + targetPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(rewriteOu(child, targetPath, depth + 1, update));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    } else {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
    }

    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        name,
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        description,
        copyGroups(node.groups()),
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteGroup(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node,
      List<Integer> targetOuPath,
      int depth,
      int groupIndex,
      GroupUpdate update) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTargetOu = depth == targetOuPath.size();

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> rewrittenGroups;
    if (atTargetOu) {
      List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups = safeGroups(node.groups());
      if (groupIndex < 0 || groupIndex >= groups.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group path is not valid: " + targetOuPath + "#" + groupIndex);
      }
      rewrittenGroups = new ArrayList<>(groups.size());
      for (int index = 0; index < groups.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group = groups.get(index);
        if (index == groupIndex) {
          rewrittenGroups.add(
              new DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup(
                  applyNonBlank(update.name(), group.name()),
                  group.nodeName(),
                  group.displayName(),
                  group.type(),
                  update.description(),
                  normalizeIds(update.humanUsers()),
                  normalizeIds(update.serviceUsers())));
        } else {
          rewrittenGroups.add(copyGroup(group));
        }
      }
    } else {
      rewrittenGroups = copyGroups(node.groups());
    }

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size());
    if (depth < targetOuPath.size()) {
      int targetChild = targetOuPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group OU path is not valid: " + targetOuPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(rewriteGroup(child, targetOuPath, depth + 1, groupIndex, update));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    } else {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
    }

    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        node.name(),
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        node.description(),
        rewrittenGroups,
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteCreateOu(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node,
      List<Integer> targetPath,
      int depth,
      String name,
      String description) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTarget = depth == targetPath.size();
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size() + (atTarget ? 1 : 0));
    if (atTarget) {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
      rewrittenChildren.add(
          new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
              name,
              null,
              null,
              "OU",
              description,
              List.of(),
              List.of()));
    } else {
      int targetChild = targetPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU path is not valid: " + targetPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(
              rewriteCreateOu(child, targetPath, depth + 1, name, description));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    }
    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        node.name(),
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        node.description(),
        copyGroups(node.groups()),
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteCreateGroup(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node,
      List<Integer> targetPath,
      int depth,
      String name,
      String type,
      String description) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTarget = depth == targetPath.size();

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> rewrittenGroups = copyGroups(node.groups());
    if (atTarget) {
      if (rewrittenGroups == null) {
        rewrittenGroups = new ArrayList<>();
      } else {
        rewrittenGroups = new ArrayList<>(rewrittenGroups);
      }
      rewrittenGroups.add(
          new DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup(
              name,
              null,
              null,
              trimToNull(type),
              description,
              List.of(),
              List.of()));
    }

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size());
    if (!atTarget) {
      int targetChild = targetPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU path is not valid: " + targetPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(
              rewriteCreateGroup(child, targetPath, depth + 1, name, type, description));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    } else {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
    }

    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        node.name(),
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        node.description(),
        rewrittenGroups,
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteRenameOu(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node,
      List<Integer> targetPath,
      int depth,
      String name,
      String description) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTarget = depth == targetPath.size();
    String nextName = atTarget ? name : node.name();
    String nextDescription = atTarget ? description : node.description();

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size());
    if (depth < targetPath.size()) {
      int targetChild = targetPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU path is not valid: " + targetPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(
              rewriteRenameOu(child, targetPath, depth + 1, name, description));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    } else {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
    }

    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        nextName,
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        nextDescription,
        copyGroups(node.groups()),
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteRenameGroup(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node,
      List<Integer> targetOuPath,
      int depth,
      int groupIndex,
      String name,
      String description) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTargetOu = depth == targetOuPath.size();
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> rewrittenGroups;
    if (atTargetOu) {
      List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups = safeGroups(node.groups());
      if (groupIndex < 0 || groupIndex >= groups.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group path is not valid: " + targetOuPath + "#" + groupIndex);
      }
      rewrittenGroups = new ArrayList<>(groups.size());
      for (int index = 0; index < groups.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group = groups.get(index);
        if (index == groupIndex) {
          rewrittenGroups.add(
              new DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup(
                  name,
                  group.nodeName(),
                  group.displayName(),
                  group.type(),
                  description,
                  safeIds(group.userIds()),
                  safeIds(group.serviceIds())));
        } else {
          rewrittenGroups.add(copyGroup(group));
        }
      }
    } else {
      rewrittenGroups = copyGroups(node.groups());
    }

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size());
    if (depth < targetOuPath.size()) {
      int targetChild = targetOuPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group OU path is not valid: " + targetOuPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(
              rewriteRenameGroup(child, targetOuPath, depth + 1, groupIndex, name, description));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    } else {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
    }

    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        node.name(),
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        node.description(),
        rewrittenGroups,
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteDeleteOu(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, List<Integer> targetPath, int depth) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(Math.max(0, children.size() - 1));
    int targetIndex = targetPath.get(depth);
    if (targetIndex < 0 || targetIndex >= children.size()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU path is not valid: " + targetPath);
    }
    boolean removeAtCurrentDepth = depth == targetPath.size() - 1;
    for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
      if (index != targetIndex) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        continue;
      }
      if (!removeAtCurrentDepth) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(rewriteDeleteOu(child, targetPath, depth + 1));
      }
    }
    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        node.name(),
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        node.description(),
        copyGroups(node.groups()),
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode rewriteDeleteGroup(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, List<Integer> targetOuPath, int depth, int groupIndex) {
    if (node == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is required");
    }
    boolean atTargetOu = depth == targetOuPath.size();
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> rewrittenGroups;
    if (atTargetOu) {
      List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups = safeGroups(node.groups());
      if (groupIndex < 0 || groupIndex >= groups.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group path is not valid: " + targetOuPath + "#" + groupIndex);
      }
      rewrittenGroups = new ArrayList<>(Math.max(0, groups.size() - 1));
      for (int index = 0; index < groups.size(); index++) {
        if (index != groupIndex) {
          rewrittenGroups.add(copyGroup(groups.get(index)));
        }
      }
    } else {
      rewrittenGroups = copyGroups(node.groups());
    }

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = safeOus(node.ous());
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> rewrittenChildren = new ArrayList<>(children.size());
    if (depth < targetOuPath.size()) {
      int targetChild = targetOuPath.get(depth);
      if (targetChild < 0 || targetChild >= children.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group OU path is not valid: " + targetOuPath);
      }
      for (int index = 0; index < children.size(); index++) {
        DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child = children.get(index);
        if (index == targetChild) {
          rewrittenChildren.add(rewriteDeleteGroup(child, targetOuPath, depth + 1, groupIndex));
        } else {
          rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
        }
      }
    } else {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
        rewrittenChildren.add(copyOu(child));
      }
    }

    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        node.name(),
        node.nodeName(),
        node.displayName(),
        node.type(),
        node.description(),
        rewrittenGroups,
        rewrittenChildren);
  }

  private static DefinitionPlatform withRoot(DefinitionPlatform source, DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root) {
    return new DefinitionPlatform(
        copyEnvelope(source.envelope()),
        copyUsers(source.users()),
        copyServices(source.services()),
        root,
        source.configId(),
        source.effectiveConfigId());
  }

  private static DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode requireRoot(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    if (model == null || model.root() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Platform model root is missing");
    }
    return model.root();
  }

  private static List<Integer> parseOuPath(String nodeId) {
    if (nodeId == null || !nodeId.startsWith("ou:")) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("OU node id is invalid: " + nodeId);
    }
    String body = nodeId.substring("ou:".length());
    if (body.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String[] tokens = body.split("/");
    List<Integer> path = new ArrayList<>(tokens.length);
    for (String token : tokens) {
      path.add(Integer.parseInt(token));
    }
    return path;
  }

  private static GroupTarget parseGroupTarget(String nodeId) {
    if (nodeId == null || !nodeId.startsWith("group:")) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group node id is invalid: " + nodeId);
    }
    String body = nodeId.substring("group:".length());
    int marker = body.lastIndexOf('#');
    if (marker < 0 || marker == body.length() - 1) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Group node id is invalid: " + nodeId);
    }
    String pathPart = body.substring(0, marker);
    String groupIndexPart = body.substring(marker + 1);
    List<Integer> path = pathPart.isBlank() ? List.of() : parsePath(pathPart);
    int groupIndex = Integer.parseInt(groupIndexPart);
    return new GroupTarget(path, groupIndex);
  }

  private static List<Integer> parsePath(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String[] tokens = value.split("/");
    List<Integer> path = new ArrayList<>(tokens.length);
    for (String token : tokens) {
      path.add(Integer.parseInt(token));
    }
    return path;
  }

  private static String toOuId(List<Integer> path) {
    if (path == null || path.isEmpty()) {
      return "ou:";
    }
    StringBuilder id = new StringBuilder("ou:");
    for (int i = 0; i < path.size(); i++) {
      if (i > 0) {
        id.append('/');
      }
      id.append(path.get(i));
    }
    return id.toString();
  }

  private static String toGroupId(List<Integer> ouPath, int groupIndex) {
    StringBuilder id = new StringBuilder("group:");
    if (ouPath != null && !ouPath.isEmpty()) {
      for (int i = 0; i < ouPath.size(); i++) {
        if (i > 0) {
          id.append('/');
        }
        id.append(ouPath.get(i));
      }
    }
    id.append('#').append(groupIndex);
    return id.toString();
  }

  private static List<Integer> append(List<Integer> path, int index) {
    List<Integer> appended = new ArrayList<>(path == null ? 1 : path.size() + 1);
    if (path != null && !path.isEmpty()) {
      appended.addAll(path);
    }
    appended.add(index);
    return appended;
  }

  private static String resolveNodeLabel(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node) {
    String display = trimToNull(node == null ? null : node.displayName());
    if (display != null) {
      return display;
    }
    String name = trimToNull(node == null ? null : node.name());
    if (name != null) {
      return name;
    }
    String nodeName = trimToNull(node == null ? null : node.nodeName());
    return nodeName == null ? "ou" : nodeName;
  }

  private static String resolveGroupLabel(DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group) {
    String display = trimToNull(group == null ? null : group.displayName());
    if (display != null) {
      return display;
    }
    String name = trimToNull(group == null ? null : group.name());
    if (name != null) {
      return name;
    }
    String nodeName = trimToNull(group == null ? null : group.nodeName());
    return nodeName == null ? "group" : nodeName;
  }

  private static String buildOuTitle(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, int groupCount, int principalCount) {
    String label = resolveNodeLabel(node);
    return label + "  [" + groupCount + " groups, " + principalCount + " members]";
  }

  private static String buildGroupTitle(DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group) {
    String label = resolveGroupLabel(group);
    int users = safeIds(group == null ? null : group.userIds()).size();
    int services = safeIds(group == null ? null : group.serviceIds()).size();
    return label + "  [" + users + " users, " + services + " services]";
  }

  private static int countGroups(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return 0;
    }
    int count = safeGroups(node.groups()).size();
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : safeOus(node.ous())) {
      count += countGroups(child);
    }
    return count;
  }

  private static int countPrincipals(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, LinkedHashSet<String> distinct) {
    if (node == null) {
      return 0;
    }
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : safeGroups(node.groups())) {
      distinct.addAll(safeIds(group == null ? null : group.userIds()));
      distinct.addAll(safeIds(group == null ? null : group.serviceIds()));
    }
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : safeOus(node.ous())) {
      countPrincipals(child, distinct);
    }
    return distinct.size();
  }

  private static List<String> safeIds(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> cleaned = new ArrayList<>(values.size());
    for (String value : values) {
      String trimmed = trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed != null) {
        cleaned.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
    return cleaned.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(cleaned);
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeIds(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String trimmed = trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed != null) {
        deduped.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
    return deduped.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(deduped);
  }

  private static List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> safeOus(List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> ous) {
    if (ous == null || ous.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> copy = new ArrayList<>(ous.size());
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : ous) {
      if (child != null) {
        copy.add(child);
      }
    }
    return copy;
  }

  private static List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> safeGroups(List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups) {
    if (groups == null || groups.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> copy = new ArrayList<>(groups.size());
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : groups) {
      if (group != null) {
        copy.add(group);
      }
    }
    return copy;
  }

  private static String applyNonBlank(String preferred, String fallback) {
    String trimmed = trimToNull(preferred);
    return trimmed == null ? fallback : trimmed;
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  private static String trimToEmpty(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim();
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope copyEnvelope(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new DefinitionEnvelope(
        envelope.group(),
        envelope.type(),
        envelope.name(),
        envelope.uuid(),
        envelope.enabled(),
        envelope.lifecycleStatus(),
        envelope.createdTimeUtc(),
        envelope.createdBy(),
        envelope.updatedTimeUtc(),
        envelope.updatedBy());
  }

  private static Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> copyUsers(
      Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> users) {
    if (users == null) {
      return null;
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> copy = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> entry : users.entrySet()) {
      DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user = entry.getValue();
      copy.put(
          entry.getKey(),
          user == null
              ? null
              : new DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser(
                  user.id(), user.firstName(), user.lastName(), user.email()));
    }
    return copy;
  }

  private static Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> copyServices(
      Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> services) {
    if (services == null) {
      return null;
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> copy = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> entry : services.entrySet()) {
      DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service = entry.getValue();
      copy.put(
          entry.getKey(),
          service == null ? null : new DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService(service.id(), service.displayName()));
    }
    return copy;
  }

  private static DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode copyOu(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode ou) {
    if (ou == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : safeOus(ou.ous())) {
      children.add(copyOu(child));
    }
    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode(
        ou.name(),
        ou.nodeName(),
        ou.displayName(),
        ou.type(),
        ou.description(),
        copyGroups(ou.groups()),
        children);
  }

  private static List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> copyGroups(List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups) {
    if (groups == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> copy = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : groups) {
      copy.add(copyGroup(group));
    }
    return copy;
  }

  private static DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup copyGroup(DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group) {
    if (group == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup(
        group.name(),
        group.nodeName(),
        group.displayName(),
        group.type(),
        group.description(),
        safeIds(group.userIds()),
        safeIds(group.serviceIds()));
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/platform/StitchPlatformFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchPlatformFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "platform";
  public static final String GROUPS = "groups";
  public static final String ENTRY_SECURITY_GROUPS = "admin.security.groups";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final String securityLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig groups;

  private StitchPlatformFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.securityLabel = require(builder.securityLabel, "securityLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.groups = builder.groupsBuilder.build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public String menuLabel() {
    return menuLabel;
  }

  public String securityLabel() {
    return securityLabel;
  }

  public StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig groups() {
    return groups;
  }

  public Optional<StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig> screen(String screenId) {
    if (screenId == null || screenId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return GROUPS.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId.trim()) ? Optional.of(groups) : Optional.empty();
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    if (!groups.enabled()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchMenuEntry groupsEntry =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_SECURITY_GROUPS)
            .withLabel(groups.label())
            .withRoutePath(groups.routePath())
            .withOrder(groups.order())
            .build();
    return List.of(groupsEntry);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Admin";
    private String securityLabel = "Security";
    private int order = 30;
    private final StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig.Builder groupsBuilder =
        StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig.builder(GROUPS);

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSecurityLabel(String value) {
      this.securityLabel = require(value, "securityLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder groups(Consumer<StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(groupsBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchPlatformFeature build() {
      return new StitchPlatformFeature(this);
    }
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/platform/StitchPlatformGroupsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchPlatformGroupsProvider {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String PLATFORM_NAME = "platform";

  private final SessionImpl session;

  public StitchPlatformGroupsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public Optional<DefinitionPlatform> loadPlatformModel() {
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = discoveryCache();
    return discoveryCache == null
        ? Optional.empty()
        : discoveryCache.get(DefinitionPlatform.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, PLATFORM_NAME);
  }

  public void savePlatformModel(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = discoveryCache();
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    discoveryCache.upsert(model);
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    return session.internal().discoveryCache();
  }
}
